  const albumUrl =
    sanitizeBandcampHttpUrl(payload.albumUrl || BANDCAMP_CONFIG.defaultAlbumUrl, 900) ||
    BANDCAMP_CONFIG.defaultAlbumUrl;
  const fetched = fetchBandcampTextViaSup(albumUrl, 18000);
  let parsed = {
    albumTitle: "Polygon Island",
    artworkUrl: BANDCAMP_CONFIG.defaultArtworkUrl,
    tracks: [],
  };
  let source = "fallback";
  let error = "";
  if (fetched.ok && fetched.text) {
    parsed = parseBandcampAlbumHtml(fetched.text, albumUrl);
    source = parsed.tracks.length ? "bandcamp-live" : "fallback";
  } else {
    error = sanitizeBandcampText(fetched.error || "Unable to fetch album page", 260);
  }
  if (!parsed.tracks.length) {
    parsed.tracks = [
      {
        id: "polygon-island-album",
        title: parsed.albumTitle || "Polygon Island",
        streamUrl: "",
        trackUrl: albumUrl,
        duration: 0,
      },
    ];
  }
  return {
    ok: true,
    albumUrl,
    albumTitle: sanitizeBandcampText(parsed.albumTitle || "Polygon Island", 120) || "Polygon Island",
    artworkUrl: sanitizeBandcampHttpUrl(parsed.artworkUrl || BANDCAMP_CONFIG.defaultArtworkUrl, 900),
    tracks: normalizeBandcampTracks(parsed.tracks),
    source,
    error,
  };
}

async function loadBandcampArtistAlbums(event) {
  const payload = asObject(event && event.value);
  const artistUrl =
    sanitizeBandcampHttpUrl(payload.artistUrl || BANDCAMP_CONFIG.defaultArtistUrl, 900) ||
    BANDCAMP_CONFIG.defaultArtistUrl;
  const fetched = fetchBandcampTextViaSup(artistUrl, 16000);
  let albums = [];
  let source = "fallback";
  let error = "";
  if (fetched.ok && fetched.text) {
    albums = parseBandcampArtistAlbumsHtml(fetched.text, artistUrl);
    source = albums.length ? "artist-live" : "fallback";
  } else {
    error = sanitizeBandcampText(fetched.error || "Unable to fetch artist albums", 260);
  }
  if (!albums.length) {
    albums = [fallbackBandcampAlbum()];
  }
  return {
    ok: true,
    artistUrl,
    albums,
    source,
    error,
  };
}

async function searchBandcampAlbums(event) {
  const payload = asObject(event && event.value);
  const query = sanitizeBandcampText(payload.query || "", 120);
  if (!query) {
    return {
      ok: true,
      query: "",
      searchUrl: "",
      albums: [],
      source: "empty",
      error: "Query required",
    };
  }
  const searchUrl = `https://bandcamp.com/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(query)}&item_type=a`;
  const fetched = fetchBandcampTextViaSup(searchUrl, 17000);
  let albums = [];
  let source = "fallback";
  let error = "";
  if (fetched.ok && fetched.text) {
    albums = parseBandcampSearchAlbumsHtml(fetched.text, searchUrl).slice(0, 48);
    source = albums.length ? "search-live" : "fallback";
  } else {
    error = sanitizeBandcampText(fetched.error || "Bandcamp search failed", 260);
  }
  return {
    ok: true,
    query,
    searchUrl,
    albums,
    source,
    error,
  };
}

function getTransitSecretsBag() {
  const primary = asObject(safeGlobalGet("TRANSIT_REALTIME_SECRETS", {}));
  const secondary = asObject(safeGlobalGet("transitRealtimeSecrets", {}));
  return {
    ...primary,
    ...secondary,
  };
}

function getTransitSecretValue(secretKey, payload) {
  const key = String(secretKey || "").trim();
  if (!key) {
    return "";
  }
  const requestSecrets = asObject(payload && payload.secrets);
  const requestValue = requestSecrets[key];
  if (typeof requestValue === "string" && requestValue.trim()) {
    return requestValue.trim();
  }
  const bag = getTransitSecretsBag();
  const bagValue = bag[key];
  if (typeof bagValue === "string" && bagValue.trim()) {
    return bagValue.trim();
  }
  const directCandidates = [key, "secret:" + key, "secret." + key];
  for (const candidate of directCandidates) {
    const value = safeGlobalGet(candidate, "");
    if (typeof value === "string" && value.trim()) {
      return value.trim();
    }
  }
  return "";
}

function stripOdptPrefix(value) {
  const text = String(value || "").trim();
  if (!text) {
    return "";
  }
  const colonIndex = text.indexOf(":");
  return colonIndex >= 0 ? text.slice(colonIndex + 1) : text;
}

function normalizeTransitStationKey(value) {
  return String(value || "")
    .toLowerCase()
    .replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "");
}

function lookupTransitFallbackStationCoord(stationName) {
  const key = normalizeTransitStationKey(stationName);
  if (!key) {
    return null;
  }
  for (const [name, coord] of Object.entries(TRANSIT_STATION_COORDS)) {
    if (normalizeTransitStationKey(name) === key && Array.isArray(coord) && coord.length >= 2) {
      const lng = Number(coord[0]);
      const lat = Number(coord[1]);
      if (Number.isFinite(lng) && Number.isFinite(lat)) {
        return [lng, lat];
      }
    }
  }
  return null;
}

function getTransitStationCoordByRef(value) {
  const raw = Array.isArray(value) ? value[0] : value;
  const text = stripOdptPrefix(raw);
  if (!text) {
    return null;
  }
  const parts = text.split(".").filter(Boolean);
  const candidates = [];
  if (parts.length > 0) {
    candidates.push(parts[parts.length - 1]);
  }
  candidates.push(text);
  for (const candidate of candidates) {
    const coord = lookupTransitFallbackStationCoord(candidate);
    if (coord) {
      return coord;
    }
  }
  return null;
}

function appendQueryParam(url, key, value) {
  const cleanUrl = String(url || "").trim();
  if (!cleanUrl) {
    return "";
  }
  const paramKey = String(key || "").trim();
  const paramValue = String(value || "").trim();
  if (!paramKey || !paramValue) {
    return cleanUrl;
  }
  try {
    const parsed = new URL(cleanUrl);
    parsed.searchParams.set(paramKey, paramValue);
    return parsed.toString();
  } catch (_error) {
    return cleanUrl + (cleanUrl.indexOf("?") >= 0 ? "&" : "?") + encodeURIComponent(paramKey) + "=" + encodeURIComponent(paramValue);
  }
}

function fetchTransitViaSup(url, options) {
  const settings = asObject(options);
  const request = {
    method: settings.method ? String(settings.method) : "GET",
    timeout: clamp(toInt(settings.timeoutMs, 9000), 1200, 35000),
    headers: asObject(settings.headers),
  };
  if (settings.body !== undefined) {
    request.body = settings.body;
  }
  try {
    const response = sup.fetch(String(url || ""), request);
    const status = toInt(response && response.status, 200);
    const ok = response
      ? response.ok !== false && status >= 200 && status < 300
      : false;
    return {
      ok,
      status,
      response: response || null,
      error: ok ? "" : "http_" + String(status),
    };
  } catch (error) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      status: 0,
      response: null,
      error: error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error),
    };
  }
}

function parseTransitJsonResponse(response) {
  if (!response) {
    return null;
  }
  try {
    if (typeof response.json === "function") {
      const payload = response.json();
      if (payload && typeof payload === "object") {
        return payload;
      }
    }
  } catch (_error) {
    // continue
  }
  try {
    if (typeof response.text === "function") {
      const text = String(response.text() || "");
      if (!text) {
        return null;
      }
      const parsed = JSON.parse(text);
      return parsed && typeof parsed === "object" ? parsed : null;
    }
  } catch (_error) {
    // continue
  }
  return null;
}

function textToByteArray(text) {
  const input = String(text || "");
  const bytes = new Uint8Array(input.length);
  for (let i = 0; i < input.length; i += 1) {
    bytes[i] = input.charCodeAt(i) & 0xff;
  }
  return bytes;
}

function parseTransitByteResponse(response) {
  if (!response) {
    return new Uint8Array(0);
  }
  try {
    if (typeof response.bytes === "function") {
      const value = response.bytes();
      if (value instanceof Uint8Array) {
        return value;
      }
      if (value && value.buffer && Number.isFinite(value.byteLength)) {
        return new Uint8Array(value.buffer, value.byteOffset || 0, value.byteLength);
      }
      if (value instanceof ArrayBuffer) {
        return new Uint8Array(value);
      }
    }
  } catch (_error) {
    // continue
  }
  try {
    if (typeof response.arrayBuffer === "function") {
      const ab = response.arrayBuffer();
      if (ab instanceof ArrayBuffer) {
        return new Uint8Array(ab);
      }
    }
  } catch (_error) {
    // continue
  }
  try {
    if (response.data && response.data instanceof Uint8Array) {
      return response.data;
    }
  } catch (_error) {
    // continue
  }
  try {
    if (typeof response.text === "function") {
      return textToByteArray(response.text());
    }
  } catch (_error) {
    // continue
  }
  return new Uint8Array(0);
}

function getTransitProviderCache(cacheKey, ttlMs, loader) {
  const key = String(cacheKey || "");
  const now = Date.now();
  if (key) {
    const cached = TRANSIT_SERVER_CACHE.providers.get(key);
    if (cached && Number(cached.expiresAt) > now) {
      return {
        ok: true,
        cached: true,
        value: cached.value,
      };
    }
  }
  try {
    const value = loader();
    if (key) {
      TRANSIT_SERVER_CACHE.providers.set(key, {
        expiresAt: now + Math.max(1200, toInt(ttlMs, 10000)),
        value,
      });
    }
    return {
      ok: true,
      cached: false,
      value,
    };
  } catch (error) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      cached: false,
      value: null,
      error: error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error),
    };
  }
}

function decodeProtoVarint(bytes, startIndex) {
  let index = toInt(startIndex, 0);
  let shift = 0;
  let value = 0;
  while (index < bytes.length && shift <= 63) {
    const byte = bytes[index];
    value += (byte & 0x7f) * Math.pow(2, shift);
    index += 1;
    if ((byte & 0x80) === 0) {
      return {
        ok: true,
        value,
        next: index,
      };
    }
    shift += 7;
  }
  return {
    ok: false,
    value: 0,
    next: startIndex,
  };
}

function skipProtoField(bytes, index, wireType) {
  if (wireType === 0) {
    const parsed = decodeProtoVarint(bytes, index);
    return parsed.ok ? parsed.next : -1;
  }
  if (wireType === 1) {
    return index + 8 <= bytes.length ? index + 8 : -1;
  }
  if (wireType === 2) {
    const len = decodeProtoVarint(bytes, index);
    if (!len.ok) {
      return -1;
    }
    const next = len.next + len.value;
    return next <= bytes.length ? next : -1;
  }
  if (wireType === 5) {
    return index + 4 <= bytes.length ? index + 4 : -1;
  }
  return -1;
}

function readProtoLengthDelimited(bytes, index) {
  const parsed = decodeProtoVarint(bytes, index);
  if (!parsed.ok) {
    return null;
  }
  const length = toInt(parsed.value, 0);
  const from = parsed.next;
  const to = from + length;
  if (length < 0 || to > bytes.length) {
    return null;
  }
  return {
    bytes: bytes.subarray(from, to),
    next: to,
  };
}

function decodeUtf8Bytes(bytes) {
  if (!bytes || bytes.length <= 0) {
    return "";
  }
  try {
    if (typeof TextDecoder !== "undefined") {
      return new TextDecoder("utf-8").decode(bytes);
    }
  } catch (_error) {
    // continue
  }
  let out = "";
  for (let i = 0; i < bytes.length; i += 1) {
    out += String.fromCharCode(bytes[i]);
  }
  return out;
}

function readProtoFloat32(bytes, index) {
  if (index + 4 > bytes.length) {
    return Number.NaN;
  }
  try {
    const view = new DataView(bytes.buffer, bytes.byteOffset + index, 4);
    return view.getFloat32(0, true);
  } catch (_error) {
    return Number.NaN;
  }
}

function readProtoFloat64(bytes, index) {
  if (index + 8 > bytes.length) {
    return Number.NaN;
  }
  try {
    const view = new DataView(bytes.buffer, bytes.byteOffset + index, 8);
    return view.getFloat64(0, true);
  } catch (_error) {
    return Number.NaN;
  }
}

function parseGtfsTripDescriptor(bytes) {
  const out = {
    tripId: "",
    routeId: "",
  };
  let index = 0;
  while (index < bytes.length) {
    const tag = decodeProtoVarint(bytes, index);
    if (!tag.ok) {
      break;
    }
    index = tag.next;
    const field = Math.floor(tag.value / 8);
    const wireType = tag.value & 0x7;
    if ((field === 1 || field === 5) && wireType === 2) {
      const value = readProtoLengthDelimited(bytes, index);
      if (!value) {
        break;
      }
      const text = decodeUtf8Bytes(value.bytes);
      if (field === 1) {
        out.tripId = text;
      } else {
        out.routeId = text;
      }
      index = value.next;
      continue;
    }
    const skipped = skipProtoField(bytes, index, wireType);
    if (skipped < 0) {
      break;
    }
    index = skipped;
  }
  return out;
}

function parseGtfsVehicleDescriptor(bytes) {
  const out = {
    id: "",
  };
  let index = 0;
  while (index < bytes.length) {
    const tag = decodeProtoVarint(bytes, index);
    if (!tag.ok) {
      break;
    }
    index = tag.next;
    const field = Math.floor(tag.value / 8);
    const wireType = tag.value & 0x7;
    if (field === 1 && wireType === 2) {
      const value = readProtoLengthDelimited(bytes, index);
      if (!value) {
        break;
      }
      out.id = decodeUtf8Bytes(value.bytes);
      index = value.next;
      continue;
    }
    const skipped = skipProtoField(bytes, index, wireType);
    if (skipped < 0) {
      break;
    }
    index = skipped;
  }
  return out;
}

function parseGtfsPosition(bytes) {
  const out = {
    lat: Number.NaN,
    lng: Number.NaN,
    bearingDeg: Number.NaN,
  };
  let index = 0;
  while (index < bytes.length) {
    const tag = decodeProtoVarint(bytes, index);
    if (!tag.ok) {
      break;
    }
    index = tag.next;
    const field = Math.floor(tag.value / 8);
    const wireType = tag.value & 0x7;
    if (wireType === 5 && (field === 1 || field === 2 || field === 3)) {
      const value = readProtoFloat32(bytes, index);
      if (field === 1) {
        out.lat = value;
      } else if (field === 2) {
        out.lng = value;
      } else {
        out.bearingDeg = value;
      }
      index += 4;
      continue;
    }
    if (wireType === 1 && (field === 1 || field === 2 || field === 3)) {
      const value = readProtoFloat64(bytes, index);
      if (field === 1) {
        out.lat = value;
      } else if (field === 2) {
        out.lng = value;
      } else {
        out.bearingDeg = value;
      }
      index += 8;
      continue;
    }
    const skipped = skipProtoField(bytes, index, wireType);
    if (skipped < 0) {
      break;
    }
    index = skipped;
  }
  return out;
}

function parseGtfsVehiclePosition(bytes) {
  const out = {
    vehicleId: "",
    tripId: "",
    routeId: "",
    lng: Number.NaN,
    lat: Number.NaN,
    bearingDeg: Number.NaN,
    timestampSec: 0,
  };
  let index = 0;
  while (index < bytes.length) {
    const tag = decodeProtoVarint(bytes, index);
    if (!tag.ok) {
      break;
    }
    index = tag.next;
    const field = Math.floor(tag.value / 8);
    const wireType = tag.value & 0x7;
    if (field === 1 && wireType === 2) {
      const value = readProtoLengthDelimited(bytes, index);
      if (!value) {
        break;
      }
      const trip = parseGtfsTripDescriptor(value.bytes);
      out.tripId = trip.tripId || out.tripId;
      out.routeId = trip.routeId || out.routeId;
      index = value.next;
      continue;
    }
    if (field === 2 && wireType === 2) {
      const value = readProtoLengthDelimited(bytes, index);
      if (!value) {
        break;
      }
      const pos = parseGtfsPosition(value.bytes);
      out.lat = pos.lat;
      out.lng = pos.lng;
      out.bearingDeg = pos.bearingDeg;
      index = value.next;
      continue;
    }
    if (field === 5 && wireType === 0) {
      const value = decodeProtoVarint(bytes, index);
      if (!value.ok) {
        break;
      }
      out.timestampSec = toInt(value.value, 0);
      index = value.next;
      continue;
    }
    if (field === 8 && wireType === 2) {
      const value = readProtoLengthDelimited(bytes, index);
      if (!value) {
        break;
      }
      const vehicle = parseGtfsVehicleDescriptor(value.bytes);
      out.vehicleId = vehicle.id || out.vehicleId;
      index = value.next;
      continue;
    }
    const skipped = skipProtoField(bytes, index, wireType);
    if (skipped < 0) {
      break;
    }
    index = skipped;
  }
  return out;
}

function parseGtfsRealtimeVehiclePositions(bytes) {
  const out = [];
  let index = 0;
  while (index < bytes.length) {
    const tag = decodeProtoVarint(bytes, index);
    if (!tag.ok) {
      break;
    }
    index = tag.next;
    const field = Math.floor(tag.value / 8);
    const wireType = tag.value & 0x7;
    if (field === 2 && wireType === 2) {
      const entity = readProtoLengthDelimited(bytes, index);
      if (!entity) {
        break;
      }
      index = entity.next;
      let entityIndex = 0;
      let vehicleBytes = null;
      let entityId = "";
      while (entityIndex < entity.bytes.length) {
        const entityTag = decodeProtoVarint(entity.bytes, entityIndex);
        if (!entityTag.ok) {
          break;
        }
        entityIndex = entityTag.next;
        const entityField = Math.floor(entityTag.value / 8);
        const entityWireType = entityTag.value & 0x7;
        if (entityField === 1 && entityWireType === 2) {
          const idValue = readProtoLengthDelimited(entity.bytes, entityIndex);
          if (!idValue) {
            break;
          }
          entityId = decodeUtf8Bytes(idValue.bytes);
          entityIndex = idValue.next;
          continue;
        }
        if (entityField === 4 && entityWireType === 2) {
          const vehicleValue = readProtoLengthDelimited(entity.bytes, entityIndex);
          if (!vehicleValue) {
            break;
          }
          vehicleBytes = vehicleValue.bytes;
          entityIndex = vehicleValue.next;
          continue;
        }
        const skippedEntity = skipProtoField(entity.bytes, entityIndex, entityWireType);
        if (skippedEntity < 0) {
          break;
        }
        entityIndex = skippedEntity;
      }
      if (vehicleBytes && vehicleBytes.length > 0) {
        const vehicle = parseGtfsVehiclePosition(vehicleBytes);
        if (!vehicle.vehicleId && entityId) {
          vehicle.vehicleId = entityId;
        }
        if (Number.isFinite(vehicle.lng) && Number.isFinite(vehicle.lat)) {
          out.push(vehicle);
        }
      }
      continue;
    }
    const skipped = skipProtoField(bytes, index, wireType);
    if (skipped < 0) {
      break;
    }
    index = skipped;
  }
  return out;
}

function normalizeOdptTrainRows(rows, sourceLabel) {
  const out = [];
  for (const row of Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : []) {
    if (!row || typeof row !== "object") {
      continue;
    }
    const id = stripOdptPrefix(row["owl:sameAs"] || row.id || row.trainId || "");
    const operator = stripOdptPrefix(row["odpt:operator"] || row.operator || row.o || "");
    const railway = stripOdptPrefix(row["odpt:railway"] || row.railway || row.r || "");
    const fromStation = row["odpt:fromStation"] || row.fs || row.fromStation || "";
    const toStation = row["odpt:toStation"] || row.ts || row.toStation || row["odpt:destinationStation"] || "";
    const stationCoord =
      getTransitStationCoordByRef(fromStation) ||
      getTransitStationCoordByRef(toStation) ||
      getTransitStationCoordByRef(row["odpt:originStation"] || row.os || "");
    let lng = Number(row.lng);
    let lat = Number(row.lat);
    if (!Number.isFinite(lng)) lng = Number(row.lon);
    if (!Number.isFinite(lat)) lat = Number(row.latitude);
    if (!Number.isFinite(lng)) lng = Number(row.longitude);
    if (!Number.isFinite(lat)) lat = Number(row.y);
    if (!Number.isFinite(lng)) lng = Number(row.x);
    if (!Number.isFinite(lng) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
      if (stationCoord) {
        lng = Number(stationCoord[0]);
        lat = Number(stationCoord[1]);
      }
    }
    if (!Number.isFinite(lng) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
      continue;
    }
    const delayRaw = Number(row["odpt:delay"] || row.delay || 0);
    const delaySec = Number.isFinite(delayRaw)
      ? (Math.abs(delayRaw) > 10000 ? Math.round(delayRaw / 1000) : Math.round(delayRaw))
      : 0;
    const headingDeg = Number(row.headingDeg || row.heading || row.bearingDeg || row.bearing);
    const statusTextRaw = row["odpt:trainType"] || row.statusText || row.status || row.text || "";
    out.push({
      id: id || (railway ? railway + ":" + String(out.length + 1) : "odpt:" + String(out.length + 1)),
      source: sourceLabel || "odpt",
      operator,
      railway,
      lng,
      lat,
      headingDeg: Number.isFinite(headingDeg) ? headingDeg : null,
      delaySec,
      statusText: stripOdptPrefix(statusTextRaw),
    });
  }
  return out;
}

function normalizeMiniTokyoTrainRows(rows, sourceLabel) {
  const out = [];
  for (const row of Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : []) {
    if (!row || typeof row !== "object") {
      continue;
    }
    const id = stripOdptPrefix(row.id || row.trainId || row["owl:sameAs"] || "");
    const operator = stripOdptPrefix(row.o || row.operator || row["odpt:operator"] || "");
    const railway = stripOdptPrefix(row.r || row.railway || row["odpt:railway"] || "");
    let lng = Number(row.lng);
    let lat = Number(row.lat);
    if (!Number.isFinite(lng)) lng = Number(row.lon);
    if (!Number.isFinite(lat)) lat = Number(row.latitude);
    if (!Number.isFinite(lng)) lng = Number(row.longitude);
    if (!Number.isFinite(lat)) lat = Number(row.y);
    if (!Number.isFinite(lng)) lng = Number(row.x);
    const stationCoord =
      getTransitStationCoordByRef(row.fs || row.fromStation || "") ||
      getTransitStationCoordByRef(row.ts || row.toStation || "") ||
      getTransitStationCoordByRef(row.os || row.originStation || "");
    if ((!Number.isFinite(lng) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) && stationCoord) {
      lng = Number(stationCoord[0]);
      lat = Number(stationCoord[1]);
    }
    if (!Number.isFinite(lng) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
      continue;
    }
    const delayRaw = Number(row.delay || 0);
    const delaySec = Number.isFinite(delayRaw)
      ? (Math.abs(delayRaw) > 10000 ? Math.round(delayRaw / 1000) : Math.round(delayRaw))
      : 0;
    const headingDeg = Number(row.headingDeg || row.heading || row.bearingDeg || row.bearing);
    out.push({
      id: id || ("miniTokyo:" + String(out.length + 1)),
      source: sourceLabel || "mini_tokyo",
      operator,
      railway,
      lng,
      lat,
      headingDeg: Number.isFinite(headingDeg) ? headingDeg : null,
      delaySec,
      statusText: String(row.statusText || row.status || row.text || "").slice(0, 160),
    });
  }
  return out;
}

function mergeNormalizedTrains(trainLists, maxItems) {
  const out = [];
  const seen = new Set();
  for (const list of Array.isArray(trainLists) ? trainLists : []) {
    for (const train of Array.isArray(list) ? list : []) {
      if (!train || !Number.isFinite(Number(train.lng)) || !Number.isFinite(Number(train.lat))) {
        continue;
      }
      const idKey = String(train.id || "").trim();
      const geoKey = Number(train.lng).toFixed(5) + ":" + Number(train.lat).toFixed(5);
      const key = idKey || (String(train.railway || "") + "|" + geoKey);
      if (seen.has(key)) {
        continue;
      }
      seen.add(key);
      out.push({
        id: idKey || key,
        source: String(train.source || "unknown"),
        operator: String(train.operator || ""),
        railway: String(train.railway || ""),
        lng: Number(train.lng),
        lat: Number(train.lat),
        headingDeg: Number.isFinite(Number(train.headingDeg)) ? Number(train.headingDeg) : undefined,
        delaySec: Number.isFinite(Number(train.delaySec)) ? Number(train.delaySec) : undefined,
        statusText: train.statusText ? String(train.statusText).slice(0, 180) : undefined,
      });
      if (maxItems > 0 && out.length >= maxItems) {
        return out;
      }
    }
  }
  return out;
}

function normalizeGtfsBusRows(rows, sourceLabel, feedId) {
  const out = [];
  for (const row of Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : []) {
    if (!row || !Number.isFinite(Number(row.lng)) || !Number.isFinite(Number(row.lat))) {
      continue;
    }
    const id = String(row.vehicleId || row.tripId || "").trim() || String(feedId || "bus") + ":" + String(out.length + 1);
    const bearingDeg = Number(row.bearingDeg);
    out.push({
      id,
      source: sourceLabel || "toei_gtfs_rt",
      feedId: String(feedId || "toei"),
      routeId: row.routeId ? String(row.routeId) : undefined,
      tripId: row.tripId ? String(row.tripId) : undefined,
      lng: Number(row.lng),
      lat: Number(row.lat),
      bearingDeg: Number.isFinite(bearingDeg) ? bearingDeg : undefined,
    });
  }
  return out;
}

function fetchTransitJsonCached(url, cacheKey, timeoutMs, ttlMs) {
  const cached = getTransitProviderCache(cacheKey, ttlMs, () => {
    const fetched = fetchTransitViaSup(url, { method: "GET", timeoutMs });
    if (!fetched.ok) {
      throw new Error(fetched.error || "fetch_failed");
    }
    const payload = parseTransitJsonResponse(fetched.response);
    if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object") {
      throw new Error("invalid_json_payload");
    }
    return payload;
  });
  if (!cached.ok) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      payload: null,
      error: cached.error || "json_fetch_failed",
    };
  }
  return {
    ok: true,
    payload: cached.value,
    cached: cached.cached,
  };
}

function fetchTransitBytesCached(url, cacheKey, timeoutMs, ttlMs) {
  const cached = getTransitProviderCache(cacheKey, ttlMs, () => {
    const fetched = fetchTransitViaSup(url, { method: "GET", timeoutMs });
    if (!fetched.ok) {
      throw new Error(fetched.error || "fetch_failed");
    }
    const bytes = parseTransitByteResponse(fetched.response);
    if (!(bytes instanceof Uint8Array) || bytes.length <= 0) {
      throw new Error("empty_binary_payload");
    }
    return bytes;
  });
  if (!cached.ok) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      payload: new Uint8Array(0),
      error: cached.error || "bytes_fetch_failed",
    };
  }
  return {
    ok: true,
    payload: cached.value instanceof Uint8Array ? cached.value : new Uint8Array(0),
    cached: cached.cached,
  };
}

function buildOdptTrainUrls(payload, warnings) {
  const config = TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG && TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.trainSources
    ? asObject(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.trainSources.odpt)
    : {};
  if (config.enabled === false) {
    return [];
  }
  const urls = Array.isArray(config.urls) ? config.urls : [];
  const railwayFilter = Array.isArray(config.railwayFilter) ? config.railwayFilter : [];
  const filterValue = railwayFilter
    .map((item) => stripOdptPrefix(item))
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((item) => "odpt.Railway:" + item)
    .join(",");
  const tokenKeys = Array.isArray(config.tokenKeys) ? config.tokenKeys : [];
  const consumerKeyParam = config.consumerKeyParam
    ? String(config.consumerKeyParam)
    : "acl:consumerKey";
  const out = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < urls.length; i += 1) {
    const rawUrl = String(urls[i] || "").trim();
    if (!rawUrl) {
      continue;
    }
    let url = rawUrl;
    if (filterValue) {
      url = appendQueryParam(url, "odpt:railway", filterValue);
    }
    const tokenKey = tokenKeys[i] || tokenKeys[0] || "";
    const token = getTransitSecretValue(tokenKey, payload);
    if (!token && tokenKey) {
      warnings.push("Missing transit secret: " + tokenKey);
      continue;
    }
    if (token) {
      url = appendQueryParam(url, consumerKeyParam, token);
    }
    out.push(url);
  }
  return out;
}

function loadOdptRealtimeTrains(payload, warnings) {
  const out = [];
  const urls = buildOdptTrainUrls(payload, warnings);
  const timeoutMs = Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.requestTimeoutMs) || 9000;
  const cacheTtlMs = Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.cacheTtlMs) || 10000;
  for (const url of urls) {
    const cacheKey = "train:odpt:" + url;
    const fetched = fetchTransitJsonCached(url, cacheKey, timeoutMs, cacheTtlMs);
    if (!fetched.ok) {
      warnings.push("ODPT train feed failed: " + fetched.error);
      continue;
    }
    const rows = Array.isArray(fetched.payload) ? fetched.payload : [];
    out.push(...normalizeOdptTrainRows(rows, "odpt"));
  }
  return out;
}

function loadMiniTokyoRealtimeTrains(warnings) {
  const config = TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG && TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.trainSources
    ? asObject(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.trainSources.miniTokyo)
    : {};
  if (config.enabled === false) {
    return [];
  }
  const urls = Array.isArray(config.urls) ? config.urls : [];
  const timeoutMs = Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.requestTimeoutMs) || 9000;
  const cacheTtlMs = Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.cacheTtlMs) || 10000;
  const trainRows = [];
  const infoRows = [];
  for (const rawUrl of urls) {
    const url = String(rawUrl || "").trim();
    if (!url) {
      continue;
    }
    const fetched = fetchTransitJsonCached(url, "train:mini:" + url, timeoutMs, cacheTtlMs);
    if (!fetched.ok) {
      warnings.push("MiniTokyo feed failed: " + fetched.error);
      continue;
    }
    const rows = Array.isArray(fetched.payload) ? fetched.payload : [];
    if (/traininfo/i.test(url)) {
      infoRows.push(...rows);
    } else {
      trainRows.push(...rows);
    }
  }
  const normalized = normalizeMiniTokyoTrainRows(trainRows, "mini_tokyo");
  if (infoRows.length > 0 && normalized.length > 0) {
    const infoByRailway = new Map();
    for (const item of infoRows) {
      if (!item || typeof item !== "object") {
        continue;
      }
      const railway = stripOdptPrefix(item.railway || item.r || item["odpt:railway"] || "");
      const text = String(item.text || item.status || item["odpt:trainInformationText"] || "").trim();
      if (!railway || !text) {
        continue;
      }
      infoByRailway.set(railway, text);
    }
    for (const row of normalized) {
      if (!row || row.statusText) {
        continue;
      }
      const text = infoByRailway.get(String(row.railway || ""));
      if (text) {
        row.statusText = text;
      }
    }
  }
  return normalized;
}

function resolveToeiBusFeedList(payload) {
  const config = TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG && TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.busSources
    ? asObject(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.busSources.toei)
    : {};
  const defaults = Array.isArray(config.feedDefaults) ? config.feedDefaults : [];
  const overrides = Array.isArray(payload && payload.busFeeds) ? payload.busFeeds : null;
  const rows = overrides && overrides.length > 0 ? overrides : defaults;
  const out = [];
  for (const row of rows) {
    if (!row || typeof row !== "object") {
      continue;
    }
    const id = String(row.id || row.feedId || "toei_feed").trim();
    const url = String(row.url || "").trim();
    if (!url) {
      continue;
    }
    out.push({
      id: id || "toei_feed",
      url,
      tokenKey: row.tokenKey ? String(row.tokenKey) : "",
      consumerKeyParam: row.consumerKeyParam ? String(row.consumerKeyParam) : "acl:consumerKey",
    });
  }
  return out;
}

function loadToeiRealtimeBuses(payload, warnings) {
  const config = TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG && TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.busSources
    ? asObject(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.busSources.toei)
    : {};
  if (config.enabled === false) {
    return [];
  }
  const feeds = resolveToeiBusFeedList(payload);
  if (feeds.length <= 0) {
    warnings.push("No Toei realtime bus feeds configured.");
    return [];
  }
  const timeoutMs = Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.requestTimeoutMs) || 9000;
  const cacheTtlMs = Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.cacheTtlMs) || 10000;
  const out = [];
  for (const feed of feeds) {
    let url = String(feed.url || "").trim();
    if (!url) {
      continue;
    }
    const token = getTransitSecretValue(feed.tokenKey, payload);
    if (!token && feed.tokenKey) {
      warnings.push("Missing transit secret: " + feed.tokenKey);
      continue;
    }
    if (token) {
      url = appendQueryParam(url, feed.consumerKeyParam || "acl:consumerKey", token);
    }
    const fetched = fetchTransitBytesCached(url, "bus:toei:" + url, timeoutMs, cacheTtlMs);
    if (!fetched.ok) {
      warnings.push("Toei bus feed failed (" + feed.id + "): " + fetched.error);
      continue;
    }
    const vehicles = parseGtfsRealtimeVehiclePositions(fetched.payload);
    out.push(...normalizeGtfsBusRows(vehicles, "toei_gtfs_rt", feed.id));
  }
  return out;
}

async function loadTransitRealtime(event) {
  const payload = asObject(event && event.value);
  const enabled = !(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG && TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.enabled === false);
  const now = Date.now();
  const timestamp = new Date(now).toISOString();
  if (!enabled) {
    return {
      ok: true,
      timestamp,
      trains: [],
      buses: [],
      warnings: ["Transit realtime disabled by config."],
    };
  }

  const cacheTtlMs = Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.cacheTtlMs) || 10000;
  const forceRefresh = !!payload.forceRefresh;
  if (!forceRefresh && TRANSIT_SERVER_CACHE.combined && TRANSIT_SERVER_CACHE.combined.payload) {
    if (Number(TRANSIT_SERVER_CACHE.combined.expiresAt) > now) {
      return TRANSIT_SERVER_CACHE.combined.payload;
    }
  }

  const warnings = [];
  let trains = [];
  let buses = [];
  try {
    const odptTrains = loadOdptRealtimeTrains(payload, warnings);
    const miniTokyoTrains = loadMiniTokyoRealtimeTrains(warnings);
    trains = mergeNormalizedTrains(
      [odptTrains, miniTokyoTrains],
      Math.max(0, toInt(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.maxTrains, 420))
    );
  } catch (error) {
    warnings.push("Train realtime error: " + (error && error.message ? error.message : String(error)));
  }
  try {
    buses = loadToeiRealtimeBuses(payload, warnings);
    const maxBuses = Math.max(0, toInt(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.maxBuses, 420));
    if (maxBuses > 0 && buses.length > maxBuses) {
      buses = buses.slice(0, maxBuses);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    warnings.push("Bus realtime error: " + (error && error.message ? error.message : String(error)));
  }

  const response = {
    ok: true,
    timestamp,
    trains,
    buses,
    warnings: Array.from(new Set(warnings.map((row) => String(row || "").slice(0, 220)).filter(Boolean))),
  };
  TRANSIT_SERVER_CACHE.combined = {
    expiresAt: now + Math.max(1200, cacheTtlMs),
    payload: response,
  };
  return response;
}

    const CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX = "[PLATEAU_MVP][client]";
    const uiLogLines = [];
    let tilesModulePromise = null;
    let tilesPluginsModulePromise = null;
    const tilesetPreflightCache = new Map();
    const transportTileFeatureCache = new Map();
    const transitTileFeatureCache = new Map();
    const transportSimplifiedCoordinateCache = new Map();
    const streetLayerTileFeatureCache = new Map();
    const parkLayerTileFeatureCache = new Map();
    const waterLayerTileFeatureCache = new Map();
    const realtimeClientPayloadCache = {
      payload: null,
      expiresAt: 0,
    };
    const tileIndexZoomCache = new WeakMap();
    let gltfLoaderClassPromise = null;
    let dracoLoaderClassPromise = null;

    function normalizeAssetPath(value) {
      if (!value || typeof value !== "string") {
        return "";
      }
      let out = String(value).split("\\\\").join("/");
      while (out.endsWith("/")) {
        out = out.slice(0, -1);
      }
      return out;
    }

    function trimLeadingSlashes(value) {
      let out = String(value || "");
      while (out.startsWith("/")) {
        out = out.slice(1);
      }
      return out;
    }

    function joinAssetPath(base, leaf) {
      const b = normalizeAssetPath(base);
      const l = trimLeadingSlashes(normalizeAssetPath(leaf));
      if (!b) {
        return l ? "./" + l : "";
      }
      if (!l) {
        return b;
      }
      return b + "/" + l;
    }
    const originalConsole = {
      log: console.log.bind(console),
      info: console.info.bind(console),
      warn: console.warn.bind(console),
      error: console.error.bind(console),
    };
    const warnCounters = Object.create(null);

    function formatLogArg(arg) {
      if (arg === null) {
        return "null";
      }
      if (arg === undefined) {
        return "undefined";
      }
      if (typeof arg === "string") {
        return arg;
      }
      if (arg instanceof Error) {
        return arg.name + ": " + arg.message;
      }
      try {
        const json = JSON.stringify(arg);
        if (json && json.length > 800) {
          return json.slice(0, 800) + "...";
        }
        return json;
      } catch (_error) {
        try {
          return String(arg);
        } catch (_error2) {
          return "[unprintable]";
        }
      }
    }

    function pushUiLog(level, args) {
      const ts = new Date().toISOString().slice(11, 19);
      const rendered = Array.from(args || []).map(formatLogArg).join(" ");
      const line = ts + " [" + level + "] " + rendered;
      uiLogLines.push(line);
      if (uiLogLines.length > 220) {
        uiLogLines.shift();
      }
      if (dom.logBox) {
        dom.logBox.textContent = uiLogLines.join("\\n");
        dom.logBox.scrollTop = dom.logBox.scrollHeight;
      }
    }

    console.log = (...args) => {
      originalConsole.log(...args);
      pushUiLog("log", args);
    };
    console.info = (...args) => {
      originalConsole.info(...args);
      pushUiLog("info", args);
    };

    function classifyNoisyWarning(args) {
      const msg = Array.from(args || []).map(formatLogArg).join(" ");
      if (msg.includes("Unknown extension \\\"CESIUM_RTC\\\"")) {
        return "cesium_rtc";
      }
      if (msg.includes("Multiple instances of Three.js being imported")) {
        return "multiple_three_instances";
      }
      return "";
    }

    console.warn = (...args) => {
      const noisyKey = classifyNoisyWarning(args);
      if (noisyKey) {
        warnCounters[noisyKey] = (warnCounters[noisyKey] || 0) + 1;
        const seen = warnCounters[noisyKey];
        if (seen <= 2) {
          originalConsole.warn(...args);
          pushUiLog("warn", args);
        } else if (seen === 3) {
          const note = [
            CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX,
            "suppressed_repeated_warning",
            { key: noisyKey, repeats: seen - 1 },
          ];
          originalConsole.warn(...note);
          pushUiLog("warn", note);
        }
        return;
      }

      originalConsole.warn(...args);
      pushUiLog("warn", args);
    };
    console.error = (...args) => {
      originalConsole.error(...args);
      pushUiLog("error", args);
    };

    function debugLog(...args) {
      try {
        console.log(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, ...args);
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
    }

    const globalErrorThrottle = {
      map: new Map(),
      windowMs: 1200,
      maxPerWindow: 2,
    };
    function shouldLogGlobalError(kind, message) {
      const key = String(kind || "error") + ":" + String(message || "unknown");
      const now = Date.now();
      const prev = globalErrorThrottle.map.get(key);
      if (!prev || now - prev.startMs > globalErrorThrottle.windowMs) {
        globalErrorThrottle.map.set(key, { startMs: now, count: 1, suppressed: 0 });
        return { allow: true, flushSuppressed: 0 };
      }
      prev.count += 1;
      if (prev.count <= globalErrorThrottle.maxPerWindow) {
        return { allow: true, flushSuppressed: 0 };
      }
      prev.suppressed += 1;
      if (prev.count === globalErrorThrottle.maxPerWindow + 1) {
        return { allow: true, flushSuppressed: 0 };
      }
      if (prev.suppressed % 20 === 0) {
        return { allow: true, flushSuppressed: prev.suppressed };
      }
      return { allow: false, flushSuppressed: 0 };
    }

    window.addEventListener("error", (event) => {
      const message = event && event.message ? event.message : "unknown";
      const decision = shouldLogGlobalError("window_error", message);
      if (!decision.allow) {
        return;
      }
      if (decision.flushSuppressed > 0) {
        console.error(
          CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX,
          "window_error_suppressed",
          { message, suppressed: decision.flushSuppressed }
        );
      }
      console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "window_error", {
        message,
        filename: event && event.filename ? String(event.filename) : "",
        lineno: event && Number.isFinite(Number(event.lineno)) ? Number(event.lineno) : null,
        colno: event && Number.isFinite(Number(event.colno)) ? Number(event.colno) : null,
      });
    });
    window.addEventListener("unhandledrejection", (event) => {
      const reason = event && event.reason ? event.reason : "unknown";
      const message = typeof reason === "string"
        ? reason
        : (reason && reason.message ? reason.message : String(reason));
      const decision = shouldLogGlobalError("unhandled_rejection", message);
      if (!decision.allow) {
        return;
      }
      if (decision.flushSuppressed > 0) {
        console.error(
          CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX,
          "unhandled_rejection_suppressed",
          { message, suppressed: decision.flushSuppressed }
        );
      }
      console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "unhandled_rejection", reason);
    });

    function withTimeout(promise, timeoutMs, label) {
      const ms = Math.max(200, Number(timeoutMs) || 0);
      if (!ms) {
        return promise;
      }
      let timeoutId = null;
      return Promise.race([
        promise,
        new Promise((_, reject) => {
          timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
            reject(new Error((label || "operation") + " timed out after " + String(ms) + "ms"));
          }, ms);
        }),
      ]).finally(() => {
        if (timeoutId) {
          clearTimeout(timeoutId);
        }
      });
    }

    function dynamicImport(url, timeoutMs) {
      return withTimeout(
        Function("u", "return import(u)")(url),
        Number.isFinite(Number(timeoutMs)) ? Number(timeoutMs) : 8000,
        "dynamic import: " + String(url)
      );
    }

    function loadScript(src, timeoutMs) {
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        const tag = document.createElement("script");
        const timeout = Math.max(300, Number(timeoutMs) || 8000);
        let settled = false;
        let timerId = null;
        const done = (fn, value) => {
          if (settled) return;
          settled = true;
          try {
            if (timerId) {
              clearTimeout(timerId);
            }
          } catch (_error) {
            // no-op
          }
          fn(value);
        };
        timerId = setTimeout(() => {
          done(reject, new Error("Script load timed out: " + src));
        }, timeout);
        tag.src = src;
        tag.async = true;
        tag.crossOrigin = "anonymous";
        tag.onload = () => done(resolve, src);
        tag.onerror = () => done(reject, new Error("Failed to load script: " + src));
        document.head.appendChild(tag);
      });
    }

    async function loadThreeCore() {
      const moduleCandidates = [
        "https://esm.sh/three@0.182.0",
        "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/three@0.182.0/build/three.module.js",
      ];
      for (const url of moduleCandidates) {
        try {
          debugLog("three:module_try", { url });
          const mod = await dynamicImport(url);
          if (mod && mod.Vector3 && mod.WebGLRenderer) {
            debugLog("three:module_ok", { url });
            return mod;
          }
          debugLog("three:module_bad_shape", { url, keys: Object.keys(mod || {}) });
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "three:module_fail", { url, message: error.message });
        }
      }

      const scriptCandidates = [
        "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/three@0.182.0/build/three.min.js",
        "https://unpkg.com/three@0.182.0/build/three.min.js",
      ];
      for (const src of scriptCandidates) {
        try {
          debugLog("three:script_try", { src });
          await loadScript(src);
          if (window.THREE && window.THREE.Vector3 && window.THREE.WebGLRenderer) {
            debugLog("three:script_ok", { src });
            return window.THREE;
          }
          debugLog("three:script_missing_global", { src });
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "three:script_fail", { src, message: error.message });
        }
      }

      throw new Error("Failed to load Three.js from module and script candidates.");
    }

    async function loadSkyClass() {
      const candidates = [
        "https://esm.sh/three@0.182.0/examples/jsm/objects/Sky.js?deps=three@0.182.0",
        "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/three@0.182.0/examples/jsm/objects/Sky.js",
      ];
      for (const url of candidates) {
        try {
          debugLog("sky:module_try", { url });
          const mod = await dynamicImport(url);
          const SkyClass = mod && (mod.Sky || (mod.default && mod.default.Sky) || mod.default);
          if (SkyClass) {
            debugLog("sky:module_ok", { url });
            return SkyClass;
          }
          debugLog("sky:module_bad_shape", { url, keys: Object.keys(mod || {}) });
        } catch (error) {
          debugLog("sky:module_fail", {
            url,
            message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
          });
        }
      }
      return null;
    }

    async function loadGLTFLoaderClass() {
      if (gltfLoaderClassPromise) {
        return gltfLoaderClassPromise;
      }
      const candidates = [
        "https://esm.sh/three@0.182.0/examples/jsm/loaders/GLTFLoader.js?deps=three@0.182.0",
        "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/three@0.182.0/examples/jsm/loaders/GLTFLoader.js",
      ];
      gltfLoaderClassPromise = (async () => {
        for (const url of candidates) {
          try {
            debugLog("gltf_loader:module_try", { url });
            const mod = await dynamicImport(url);
            const LoaderClass = mod && (mod.GLTFLoader || mod.default);
            if (typeof LoaderClass === "function") {
              debugLog("gltf_loader:module_ok", { url });
              return LoaderClass;
            }
            debugLog("gltf_loader:module_bad_shape", {
              url,
              keys: Object.keys(mod || {}),
            });
          } catch (error) {
            debugLog("gltf_loader:module_fail", {
              url,
              message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
            });
          }
        }
        throw new Error("Failed to load GLTFLoader module.");
      })();
      return gltfLoaderClassPromise;
    }

    async function loadDracoLoaderClass() {
      if (dracoLoaderClassPromise) {
        return dracoLoaderClassPromise;
      }
      const candidates = [
        "https://esm.sh/three@0.182.0/examples/jsm/loaders/DRACOLoader.js?deps=three@0.182.0",
        "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/three@0.182.0/examples/jsm/loaders/DRACOLoader.js",
      ];
      dracoLoaderClassPromise = (async () => {
        for (const url of candidates) {
          try {
            debugLog("draco_loader:module_try", { url });
            const mod = await dynamicImport(url);
            const LoaderClass = mod && (mod.DRACOLoader || mod.default);
            if (typeof LoaderClass === "function") {
              debugLog("draco_loader:module_ok", { url });
              return LoaderClass;
            }
            debugLog("draco_loader:module_bad_shape", {
              url,
              keys: Object.keys(mod || {}),
            });
          } catch (error) {
            debugLog("draco_loader:module_fail", {
              url,
              message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
            });
          }
        }
        return null;
      })();
      return dracoLoaderClassPromise;
    }

    async function loadCannonModule() {
      const candidates = [
        "https://esm.sh/cannon-es@0.19.0",
        "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/cannon-es@0.19.0/+esm",
      ];
      for (const url of candidates) {
        try {
          debugLog("cannon:module_try", { url });
          const mod = await dynamicImport(url);
          const candidate = mod && mod.World
            ? mod
            : (mod && mod.default && mod.default.World ? mod.default : null);
          if (candidate && candidate.World && candidate.Body && candidate.RigidVehicle) {
            debugLog("cannon:module_ok", { url });
            return candidate;
          }
          debugLog("cannon:module_bad_shape", {
            url,
            keys: Object.keys(mod || {}),
            defaultKeys: mod && mod.default ? Object.keys(mod.default) : [],
          });
        } catch (error) {
          debugLog("cannon:module_fail", {
            url,
            message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
          });
        }
      }
      throw new Error("Failed to load cannon-es module from CDN candidates.");
    }

    function createClientSessionId() {
      try {
        if (window.crypto && typeof window.crypto.randomUUID === "function") {
          return window.crypto.randomUUID();
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      return "sess-" + Date.now() + "-" + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
    }

    function buildJsonAssetUrlCandidates(url) {
      const normalized = normalizeAssetPath(url);
      if (!normalized) {
        return [];
      }
      const stripped = trimLeadingSlashes(normalized.replace(/^\\.\\/+/, ""));
      const patchFolder = trimLeadingSlashes(
        normalizeAssetPath(
          PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.folder
            ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.folder)
            : "patch_assets"
        ).replace(/^\\.\\/+/, "")
      ) || "patch_assets";
      const seeds = [];
      const seenSeeds = new Set();
      const pushSeed = (value) => {
        const candidate = normalizeAssetPath(value);
        if (!candidate) {
          return;
        }
        const key = candidate.toLowerCase();
        if (seenSeeds.has(key)) {
          return;
        }
        seenSeeds.add(key);
        seeds.push(candidate);
      };
      pushSeed(normalized);
      pushSeed(stripped);
      if (stripped) {
        pushSeed("./" + stripped);
        pushSeed("/" + stripped);
      }
      if (stripped && !stripped.startsWith("patch_assets/")) {
        pushSeed("patch_assets/" + stripped);
        pushSeed("./patch_assets/" + stripped);
        pushSeed("/patch_assets/" + stripped);
      }
      if (stripped && !stripped.startsWith(patchFolder + "/")) {
        pushSeed(patchFolder + "/" + stripped);
        pushSeed("./" + patchFolder + "/" + stripped);
        pushSeed("/" + patchFolder + "/" + stripped);
      }

      const out = [];
      const seen = new Set();
      const push = (value) => {
        const candidate = normalizeAssetPath(value);
        if (!candidate) {
          return;
        }
        const key = candidate.toLowerCase();
        if (seen.has(key)) {
          return;
        }
        seen.add(key);
        out.push(candidate);
      };
      for (const seed of seeds) {
        push(seed);
        if (typeof resolveAssetUrlCandidates === "function") {
          const resolved = resolveAssetUrlCandidates(seed);
          for (const value of resolved) {
            push(value);
          }
        }
      }
      return out;
    }

    function isObjectRecord(value) {
      return !!value && typeof value === "object" && !Array.isArray(value);
    }

    function isFeatureCollectionPayload(value) {
      return isObjectRecord(value) && Array.isArray(value.features);
    }

    function isGeoidManifestPayload(value) {
      if (!isObjectRecord(value)) {
        return false;
      }
      if (Array.isArray(value.grid)) {
        return true;
      }
      if (isObjectRecord(value.fallbackWardOffsets)) {
        return true;
      }
      return isObjectRecord(value.gridBounds);
    }

    function isTransportManifestPayload(value) {
      if (!isObjectRecord(value)) {
        return false;
      }
      if (value.format === "geojson_tiles") {
        return true;
      }
      if (isObjectRecord(value.plateauTiles)) {
        return true;
      }
      return isObjectRecord(value.tileIndex);
    }

    function isTransitManifestPayload(value) {
      if (!isObjectRecord(value)) {
        return false;
      }
      if (String(value.format || "").toLowerCase() === "geojson_tiles") {
        return true;
      }
      if (Array.isArray(value.featureClasses) && value.featureClasses.length > 0) {
        return true;
      }
      return isObjectRecord(value.tileIndex);
    }

    function isStreetLayersManifestPayload(value) {
      return isObjectRecord(value) && isObjectRecord(value.layers);
    }

    function isParksManifestPayload(value) {
      if (!isObjectRecord(value)) {
        return false;
      }
      if (String(value.featureClass || "").toLowerCase() === "park") {
        return true;
      }
      return isObjectRecord(value.tileIndex);
    }

    function isWaterwaysManifestPayload(value) {
      if (!isObjectRecord(value)) {
        return false;
      }
      const cls = String(value.featureClass || "").toLowerCase();
      if (cls === "water" || cls === "waterway") {
        return true;
      }
      if (Array.isArray(value.featureClasses) && value.featureClasses.length > 0) {
        return true;
      }
      return isObjectRecord(value.tileIndex);
    }

    async function tryFetchJson(url, validatePayload, timeoutMs) {
      if (!url) {
        return null;
      }
      const candidates = buildJsonAssetUrlCandidates(url).slice(0, 10);
      const TIMEOUT_MS = Math.max(320, Number(timeoutMs) || 2600);
      const validator = typeof validatePayload === "function" ? validatePayload : null;

      const decodeSupJson = async (response) => {
        if (!response || response.ok === false) {
          return null;
        }
        const parseJsonText = (value) => {
          if (typeof value !== "string") {
            return null;
          }
          try {
            const parsed = JSON.parse(value);
            return parsed && typeof parsed === "object" ? parsed : null;
          } catch (_error) {
            return null;
          }
        };
        const decodeBytesToJson = (value) => {
          if (!value) {
            return null;
          }
          try {
            const bytes = value instanceof Uint8Array
              ? value
              : value.buffer && value.byteLength !== undefined
                ? new Uint8Array(value.buffer, value.byteOffset || 0, value.byteLength)
                : value instanceof ArrayBuffer
                  ? new Uint8Array(value)
                  : null;
            if (!bytes || bytes.byteLength <= 0) {
              return null;
            }
            const text = typeof TextDecoder !== "undefined"
              ? new TextDecoder().decode(bytes)
              : String.fromCharCode.apply(null, Array.from(bytes.slice(0, Math.min(bytes.length, 65536))));
            return parseJsonText(text);
          } catch (_error) {
            return null;
          }
        };
        if (typeof response.json === "function") {
          try {
            const parsed = await response.json();
            if (parsed && typeof parsed === "object") {
              return parsed;
            }
          } catch (_error) {
            // continue
          }
        }
        if (typeof response.text === "function") {
          try {
            const parsed = parseJsonText(String(await response.text() || ""));
            if (parsed) return parsed;
          } catch (_error) {
            // continue
          }
        }
        if (typeof response.bytes === "function") {
          try {
            const parsed = decodeBytesToJson(await response.bytes());
            if (parsed) return parsed;
          } catch (_error) {
            // continue
          }
        }
        if (typeof response.arrayBuffer === "function") {
          try {
            const parsed = decodeBytesToJson(await response.arrayBuffer());
            if (parsed) return parsed;
          } catch (_error) {
            // continue
          }
        }
        if (response.data) {
          const parsed = decodeBytesToJson(response.data);
          if (parsed) return parsed;
        }
        if (response.body) {
          const parsed = decodeBytesToJson(response.body);
          if (parsed) return parsed;
        }
        return null;
      };

      const fetchJsonWithTimeout = async (targetUrl) => {
        if (!targetUrl || typeof fetch !== "function") {
          return null;
        }
        const controller = typeof AbortController === "function" ? new AbortController() : null;
        let timeoutId = null;
        if (controller) {
          timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
            try {
              controller.abort();
            } catch (_error) {
              // no-op
            }
          }, TIMEOUT_MS);
        }
        try {
          const response = await fetch(targetUrl, {
            method: "GET",
            credentials: "omit",
            cache: "no-store",
            signal: controller ? controller.signal : undefined,
          });
          if (!response || !response.ok) {
            return null;
          }
          const payload = await response.json();
          return payload && typeof payload === "object" ? payload : null;
        } catch (_error) {
          return null;
        } finally {
          if (timeoutId) {
            clearTimeout(timeoutId);
          }
        }
      };

      const supFetchJsonWithTimeout = async (targetUrl) => {
        if (!(window.sup && typeof window.sup.fetch === "function") || !targetUrl) {
          return null;
        }
        try {
          const response = await Promise.race([
            Promise.resolve(
              window.sup.fetch(targetUrl, {
                method: "GET",
                cache: "no-store",
              })
            ),
            new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(() => resolve(null), TIMEOUT_MS)),
          ]);
          return await decodeSupJson(response);
        } catch (_error) {
          return null;
        }
      };

      for (const candidate of candidates) {
        const direct = await fetchJsonWithTimeout(candidate);
        if (direct && (!validator || validator(direct))) {
          return direct;
        }
        const supValue = await supFetchJsonWithTimeout(candidate);
        if (supValue && (!validator || validator(supValue))) {
          return supValue;
        }
      }

      return null;
    }

    async function tryFetchJsonCandidate(url, timeoutMs, validatePayload) {
      if (!url) {
        return null;
      }
      const TIMEOUT_MS = Math.max(320, Number(timeoutMs) || 2400);
      const candidates = buildJsonAssetUrlCandidates(url).slice(0, 12);
      const validator = typeof validatePayload === "function" ? validatePayload : null;
      const decodeSupJson = async (response) => {
        if (!response || response.ok === false) {
          return null;
        }
        const parseJsonText = (value) => {
          if (typeof value !== "string") {
            return null;
          }
          try {
            const parsed = JSON.parse(value);
            return parsed && typeof parsed === "object" ? parsed : null;
          } catch (_error) {
            return null;
          }
        };
        const decodeBytesToJson = (value) => {
          if (!value) {
            return null;
          }
          try {
            const bytes = value instanceof Uint8Array
              ? value
              : value.buffer && value.byteLength !== undefined
                ? new Uint8Array(value.buffer, value.byteOffset || 0, value.byteLength)
                : value instanceof ArrayBuffer
                  ? new Uint8Array(value)
                  : null;
            if (!bytes || bytes.byteLength <= 0) {
              return null;
            }
            const text = typeof TextDecoder !== "undefined"
              ? new TextDecoder().decode(bytes)
              : String.fromCharCode.apply(null, Array.from(bytes.slice(0, Math.min(bytes.length, 65536))));
            return parseJsonText(text);
          } catch (_error) {
            return null;
          }
        };
        if (typeof response.json === "function") {
          try {
            const parsed = await response.json();
            if (parsed && typeof parsed === "object") {
              return parsed;
            }
          } catch (_error) {
            // continue
          }
        }
        if (typeof response.text === "function") {
          try {
            const parsed = parseJsonText(String(await response.text() || ""));
            if (parsed) return parsed;
          } catch (_error) {
            // continue
          }
        }
        if (typeof response.bytes === "function") {
          try {
            const parsed = decodeBytesToJson(await response.bytes());
            if (parsed) return parsed;
          } catch (_error) {
            // continue
          }
        }
        if (typeof response.arrayBuffer === "function") {
          try {
            const parsed = decodeBytesToJson(await response.arrayBuffer());
            if (parsed) return parsed;
          } catch (_error) {
            // continue
          }
        }
        if (response.data) {
          const parsed = decodeBytesToJson(response.data);
          if (parsed) return parsed;
        }
        if (response.body) {
          const parsed = decodeBytesToJson(response.body);
          if (parsed) return parsed;
        }
        return null;
      };

      const fetchJsonWithTimeout = async (targetUrl) => {
        if (!targetUrl || typeof fetch !== "function") {
          return null;
        }
        const controller = typeof AbortController === "function" ? new AbortController() : null;
        let timeoutId = null;
        if (controller) {
          timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
            try {
              controller.abort();
            } catch (_error) {
              // no-op
            }
          }, TIMEOUT_MS);
        }
        try {
          const response = await fetch(targetUrl, {
            method: "GET",
            credentials: "omit",
            cache: "no-store",
            signal: controller ? controller.signal : undefined,
          });
          if (!response || !response.ok) {
            return null;
          }
          const payload = await response.json();
          return payload && typeof payload === "object" ? payload : null;
        } catch (_error) {
          return null;
        } finally {
          if (timeoutId) {
            clearTimeout(timeoutId);
          }
        }
      };

      const supFetchJsonWithTimeout = async (targetUrl) => {
        if (!(window.sup && typeof window.sup.fetch === "function") || !targetUrl) {
          return null;
        }
        try {
          const response = await Promise.race([
            Promise.resolve(
              window.sup.fetch(targetUrl, {
                method: "GET",
                cache: "no-store",
              })
            ),
            new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(() => resolve(null), TIMEOUT_MS)),
          ]);
          return await decodeSupJson(response);
        } catch (_error) {
          return null;
        }
      };

      for (const candidate of candidates) {
        const direct = await fetchJsonWithTimeout(candidate);
        if (direct && (!validator || validator(direct))) {
          return direct;
        }
      }
      for (const candidate of candidates) {
        const viaSup = await supFetchJsonWithTimeout(candidate);
        if (viaSup && (!validator || validator(viaSup))) {
          return viaSup;
        }
      }
      return null;
    }

    async function loadExternalPatchAssetManifests() {
      const folder = PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.folder
        ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.folder)
        : "./patch_assets";
      const geoidFile = PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.geoidManifestFile
        ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.geoidManifestFile)
        : "geoid_tokyo23.json";
      const transportFile = PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.transportManifestFile
        ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.transportManifestFile)
        : "transport_manifest_minato.json";
      const transitFile = PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.transitManifestFile
        ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.transitManifestFile)
        : "transit_manifest_minato.json";
      const streetFile = PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.streetLayersManifestFile
        ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.streetLayersManifestFile)
        : "street_layers_manifest_minato.json";
      const parksFile = PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.parksManifestFile
        ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.parksManifestFile)
        : "parks_manifest_minato.json";
      const waterwaysFile = PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.waterwaysManifestFile
        ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.waterwaysManifestFile)
        : "waterways_manifest_minato.json";
      const geoidUrl = joinAssetPath(folder, geoidFile);
      const transportUrl = joinAssetPath(folder, transportFile);
      const transitUrl = joinAssetPath(folder, transitFile);
      const streetUrl = joinAssetPath(folder, streetFile);
      const parksUrl = joinAssetPath(folder, parksFile);
      const waterwaysUrl = joinAssetPath(folder, waterwaysFile);

      let externalGeoid = null;
      let externalTransport = null;
      let externalTransit = null;
      let externalStreetLayers = null;
      let externalParks = null;
      let externalWaterways = null;
      const loadState = {
        geoid: false,
        transport: false,
        transit: false,
        streetLayers: false,
        parks: false,
        waterways: false,
      };
      try {
        const settled = await Promise.allSettled([
          tryFetchJson(geoidUrl, isGeoidManifestPayload, 3200),
          tryFetchJson(transportUrl, isTransportManifestPayload, 3200),
          tryFetchJson(transitUrl, isTransitManifestPayload, 3200),
          tryFetchJson(streetUrl, isStreetLayersManifestPayload, 3200),
          tryFetchJson(parksUrl, isParksManifestPayload, 3200),
          tryFetchJson(waterwaysUrl, isWaterwaysManifestPayload, 3200),
        ]);
        externalGeoid = settled[0] && settled[0].status === "fulfilled" ? settled[0].value : null;
        externalTransport = settled[1] && settled[1].status === "fulfilled" ? settled[1].value : null;
        externalTransit = settled[2] && settled[2].status === "fulfilled" ? settled[2].value : null;
        externalStreetLayers = settled[3] && settled[3].status === "fulfilled" ? settled[3].value : null;
        externalParks = settled[4] && settled[4].status === "fulfilled" ? settled[4].value : null;
        externalWaterways = settled[5] && settled[5].status === "fulfilled" ? settled[5].value : null;
      } catch (error) {
        debugLog("assets:external_manifest_load_error", {
          message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
        });
      }

      if (externalGeoid) {
        Object.assign(GEOID_MANIFEST, externalGeoid);
        state.geoidManager = null;
        loadState.geoid = true;
        debugLog("assets:external_geoid_manifest_loaded", { url: geoidUrl });
      } else {
        debugLog("assets:external_geoid_manifest_missing", { url: geoidUrl });
      }

      if (externalTransport) {
        Object.assign(TRANSPORT_MANIFEST, externalTransport);
        if (!TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.basePath) {
          TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.basePath = folder;
        }
        loadState.transport = true;
        debugLog("assets:external_transport_manifest_loaded", { url: transportUrl });
      } else {
        debugLog("assets:external_transport_manifest_missing", { url: transportUrl });
      }

      if (externalTransit) {
        Object.assign(TRANSIT_MANIFEST, externalTransit);
        if (!TRANSIT_MANIFEST.basePath) {
          TRANSIT_MANIFEST.basePath = folder;
        }
        loadState.transit = true;
        debugLog("assets:external_transit_manifest_loaded", { url: transitUrl });
      } else {
        debugLog("assets:external_transit_manifest_missing", { url: transitUrl });
      }

      if (externalStreetLayers) {
        Object.assign(STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST, externalStreetLayers);
        if (!STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.basePath) {
          STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.basePath = folder;
        }
        loadState.streetLayers = true;
        debugLog("assets:external_street_layers_manifest_loaded", { url: streetUrl });
      } else {
        debugLog("assets:external_street_layers_manifest_missing", { url: streetUrl });
      }

      if (externalParks) {
        Object.assign(PARKS_MANIFEST, externalParks);
        if (!PARKS_MANIFEST.basePath) {
          PARKS_MANIFEST.basePath = folder;
        }
        loadState.parks = true;
        debugLog("assets:external_parks_manifest_loaded", { url: parksUrl });
      } else {
        debugLog("assets:external_parks_manifest_missing", { url: parksUrl });
      }

      if (externalWaterways) {
        Object.assign(WATERWAYS_MANIFEST, externalWaterways);
        if (!WATERWAYS_MANIFEST.basePath) {
          WATERWAYS_MANIFEST.basePath = folder;
        }
        loadState.waterways = true;
        debugLog("assets:external_waterways_manifest_loaded", { url: waterwaysUrl });
      } else {
        debugLog("assets:external_waterways_manifest_missing", { url: waterwaysUrl });
      }
      return loadState;
    }

    function setStatus(message, mode) {
      dom.status.textContent = String(message);
      dom.status.classList.remove("error", "ok");
      if (mode === "error") {
        dom.status.classList.add("error");
      }
      if (mode === "ok") {
        dom.status.classList.add("ok");
      }
      debugLog("status", { mode: mode || "none", message: String(message) });
    }

    function setSummary(text) {
      dom.summaryBox.textContent = String(text || "");
    }

    function setDetails(text) {
      dom.detailBox.textContent = String(text || "");
    }

    function setVmState(text) {
      if (!dom.vmBox) {
        return;
      }
      dom.vmBox.textContent = String(text || "");
    }

    function updateVmStateFromBootstrap(response) {
      if (!response) {
        setVmState("No bootstrap response.");
        return;
      }

      const vm = response.vm || {};
      const prev = response.previousVm || {};
      const lines = [
        "phase: " + (response.phase || "n/a"),
        "id: " + (vm.id || "n/a"),
        "url: " + (vm.url || "n/a"),
        "sessionId: " + (vm.sessionId || "n/a"),
        "createdAt: " + (vm.createdAt || "n/a"),
        "replacedPrevious: " + (vm.replacedPrevious ? "yes" : "no"),
        "stage: " + ((response.debug && response.debug.currentStage) || "n/a"),
      ];

      if (prev && (prev.id || prev.hadVm)) {
        lines.push("prev.id: " + (prev.id || "n/a"));
        lines.push("prev.url: " + (prev.url || "n/a"));
        lines.push("prev.deleted: " + (prev.deleted ? "yes" : "no"));
        lines.push("prev.deleteError: " + (prev.deleteError || "none"));
      }

      if (response.debug && response.debug.vmError) {
        lines.push("vmError: " + response.debug.vmError);
      }
      if (response.debug && response.debug.semanticError) {
        lines.push("semanticError: " + response.debug.semanticError);
      }
      if (response.vmProbe && response.vmProbe.attempted) {
        lines.push("vmProbe.ok: " + (response.vmProbe.ok ? "yes" : "no"));
        lines.push("vmProbe.elapsedMs: " + (Number.isFinite(response.vmProbe.elapsedMs) ? response.vmProbe.elapsedMs : "n/a"));
        lines.push("vmProbe.output: " + (response.vmProbe.output || response.vmProbe.error || "n/a"));
      }
      const vmDiag = response.debug && response.debug.vmRotationDiagnostics
        ? response.debug.vmRotationDiagnostics
        : null;
      if (vmDiag) {
        lines.push("vmCreateError: " + (vmDiag.vmCreateError || "none"));
        if (Array.isArray(vmDiag.vmCreateAttempts) && vmDiag.vmCreateAttempts.length > 0) {
          const compact = vmDiag.vmCreateAttempts
            .map((attempt) => {
              const num = Number.isFinite(attempt.attempt) ? attempt.attempt : "?";
              const elapsed = Number.isFinite(attempt.elapsedMs) ? attempt.elapsedMs : 0;
              const ok = attempt.ok ? "ok" : "fail";
              const detail = attempt.ok ? (attempt.vmId || "no-id") : (attempt.error || "error");
              return "#" + num + ":" + ok + ":" + elapsed + "ms:" + detail;
            })
            .join(" | ");
          lines.push("vmCreateAttempts: " + compact);
        }
      }

      setVmState(lines.join("\\n"));
    }

    function setResultsList(results) {
      if (!Array.isArray(results) || results.length === 0) {
        dom.resultsBox.textContent = "No results.";
        return;
      }

      const rows = results.slice(0, 10).map((item, index) => {
        const id = item.id ? String(item.id).slice(0, 28) : "unknown";
        const h = Number.isFinite(item.heightM) ? item.heightM.toFixed(1) + "m" : "n/a";
        const y = Number.isFinite(item.year) ? String(item.year) : "n/a";
        const risk = Number.isFinite(item.fireRisk) ? item.fireRisk.toFixed(2) : "n/a";
        return String(index + 1).padStart(2, "0") + ". id=" + id + " | h=" + h + " | y=" + y + " | risk=" + risk;
      });

      dom.resultsBox.textContent = rows.join("\\n");
    }

    function clamp(value, min, max) {
      return Math.min(Math.max(value, min), max);
    }

    function toRad(value) {
      return value * Math.PI / 180;
    }

    function toDeg(value) {
      return value * 180 / Math.PI;
    }

    function sleepMs(ms) {
      return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, Math.max(0, ms)));
    }

    function parseRetryAfterMs(value) {
      if (!value) {
        return 0;
      }
      const asNumber = Number(value);
      if (Number.isFinite(asNumber) && asNumber >= 0) {
        return Math.floor(asNumber * 1000);
      }
      const asDate = Date.parse(String(value));
      if (Number.isFinite(asDate)) {
        return Math.max(0, asDate - Date.now());
      }
      return 0;
    }

    async function parseJsonResponseWithContext(response, errorPrefix) {
      const status = response ? Number(response.status) || 0 : 0;
      const retryAfterMs = parseRetryAfterMs(response && response.headers ? response.headers.get("retry-after") : null);
      if (!response) {
        const error = new Error(String(errorPrefix || "json_response") + "_missing");
        error.status = 0;
        error.retryAfterMs = retryAfterMs;
        throw error;
      }
      let text = "";
      try {
        text = typeof response.text === "function" ? String(await response.text() || "") : "";
      } catch (_error) {
        text = "";
      }
      const trimmed = text.trim();
      if (!trimmed) {
        const error = new Error(String(errorPrefix || "json_response") + "_empty");
        error.status = status || 503;
        error.retryAfterMs = retryAfterMs;
        throw error;
      }
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(trimmed);
        if (parsed && typeof parsed === "object") {
          return parsed;
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // handled below with a categorized error
      }
      const snippet = trimmed.slice(0, 180).replace(/\s+/g, " ");
      const error = new Error(String(errorPrefix || "json_response") + "_non_json");
      error.status = status >= 400 ? status : 503;
      error.retryAfterMs = retryAfterMs;
      error.snippet = snippet;
      throw error;
    }

    function lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, height) {
      const a = 6378137.0;
      const e2 = 6.69437999014e-3;
      const lonR = toRad(lon);
      const latR = toRad(lat);
      const sinLat = Math.sin(latR);
      const cosLat = Math.cos(latR);
      const cosLon = Math.cos(lonR);
      const sinLon = Math.sin(lonR);
      const n = a / Math.sqrt(1 - e2 * sinLat * sinLat);

      const h = Number.isFinite(height) ? height : 0;
      const x = (n + h) * cosLat * cosLon;
      const y = (n + h) * cosLat * sinLon;
      const z = (n * (1 - e2) + h) * sinLat;
      return new THREE.Vector3(x, y, z);
    }

    function ecefToLonLat(vector) {
      const x = vector.x;
      const y = vector.y;
      const z = vector.z;
      const a = 6378137.0;
      const e = 8.1819190842622e-2;

      const b = Math.sqrt(a * a * (1 - e * e));
      const ep = Math.sqrt((a * a - b * b) / (b * b));
      const p = Math.sqrt(x * x + y * y);
      const th = Math.atan2(a * z, b * p);
      const lon = Math.atan2(y, x);
      const lat = Math.atan2(
        z + ep * ep * b * Math.pow(Math.sin(th), 3),
        p - e * e * a * Math.pow(Math.cos(th), 3)
      );
      const n = a / Math.sqrt(1 - e * e * Math.sin(lat) * Math.sin(lat));
      const alt = p / Math.cos(lat) - n;

      return {
        lng: toDeg(lon),
        lat: toDeg(lat),
        altitudeM: alt,
      };
    }

    function isWithinMinato(lng, lat) {
      const b = MINATO.bounds;
      return lng >= b.west && lng <= b.east && lat >= b.south && lat <= b.north;
    }

    function isWithinBounds(lng, lat, bounds) {
      if (!bounds) {
        return false;
      }
      return (
        lng >= Number(bounds.west) &&
        lng <= Number(bounds.east) &&
        lat >= Number(bounds.south) &&
        lat <= Number(bounds.north)
      );
    }

    function boundsIntersect(a, b) {
      if (!a || !b) {
        return false;
      }
      const aw = Number(a.west);
      const ae = Number(a.east);
      const as = Number(a.south);
      const an = Number(a.north);
      const bw = Number(b.west);
      const be = Number(b.east);
      const bs = Number(b.south);
      const bn = Number(b.north);
      if (
        !Number.isFinite(aw) || !Number.isFinite(ae) || !Number.isFinite(as) || !Number.isFinite(an) ||
        !Number.isFinite(bw) || !Number.isFinite(be) || !Number.isFinite(bs) || !Number.isFinite(bn)
      ) {
        return false;
      }
      return !(ae <= bw || aw >= be || an <= bs || as >= bn);
    }

    function getActiveWardBounds() {
      const boundsList = [];
      const manager = state && state.tilesManager ? state.tilesManager : null;
      const activeIds =
        manager && manager.activeWardIds instanceof Set
          ? Array.from(manager.activeWardIds)
          : [];
      if (activeIds.length > 0) {
        for (const wardId of activeIds) {
          const ward = getWardById(wardId);
          if (ward && ward.bounds) {
            boundsList.push(ward.bounds);
          }
        }
      }
      if (boundsList.length <= 0) {
        if (TOKYO23 && TOKYO23.bounds) {
          boundsList.push(TOKYO23.bounds);
        } else if (MINATO && MINATO.bounds) {
          boundsList.push(MINATO.bounds);
        }
      }
      return boundsList;
    }

    function isWithinAnyBounds(lng, lat, boundsList) {
      if (!Array.isArray(boundsList) || boundsList.length <= 0) {
        return false;
      }
      for (const bounds of boundsList) {
        if (isWithinBounds(lng, lat, bounds)) {
          return true;
        }
      }
      return false;
    }

    function haversineDistanceM(lon1, lat1, lon2, lat2) {
      const r = 6371008.8;
      const dLat = toRad(lat2 - lat1);
      const dLon = toRad(lon2 - lon1);
      const la1 = toRad(lat1);
      const la2 = toRad(lat2);
      const a = Math.sin(dLat / 2) ** 2 +
        Math.cos(la1) * Math.cos(la2) * Math.sin(dLon / 2) ** 2;
