      const c = 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(Math.max(0, 1 - a)));
      return r * c;
    }

    function lonLatToLocalMeters(lon, lat, refLon, refLat) {
      const kx = 111320 * Math.cos(toRad(refLat));
      const ky = 110540;
      return {
        x: (Number(lon) - Number(refLon)) * kx,
        y: (Number(lat) - Number(refLat)) * ky,
      };
    }

    function pointLineDistanceM(point, lineStart, lineEnd) {
      const px = Number(point.x);
      const py = Number(point.y);
      const ax = Number(lineStart.x);
      const ay = Number(lineStart.y);
      const bx = Number(lineEnd.x);
      const by = Number(lineEnd.y);
      if (
        !Number.isFinite(px) || !Number.isFinite(py) ||
        !Number.isFinite(ax) || !Number.isFinite(ay) ||
        !Number.isFinite(bx) || !Number.isFinite(by)
      ) {
        return Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY;
      }
      const abx = bx - ax;
      const aby = by - ay;
      const abLen2 = abx * abx + aby * aby;
      if (!Number.isFinite(abLen2) || abLen2 <= 1e-8) {
        const dx = px - ax;
        const dy = py - ay;
        return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
      }
      const apx = px - ax;
      const apy = py - ay;
      const t = clamp((apx * abx + apy * aby) / abLen2, 0, 1);
      const qx = ax + abx * t;
      const qy = ay + aby * t;
      const dx = px - qx;
      const dy = py - qy;
      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
    }

    function simplifyLineDouglasPeucker(coords, toleranceM) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length <= 2) {
        return Array.isArray(coords) ? coords : [];
      }
      const tolerance = Number.isFinite(toleranceM) ? Math.max(0, toleranceM) : 0;
      if (tolerance <= 0.0001) {
        return coords;
      }
      const first = coords[0];
      if (!Array.isArray(first) || first.length < 2) {
        return coords;
      }
      const refLon = Number(first[0]);
      const refLat = Number(first[1]);
      if (!Number.isFinite(refLon) || !Number.isFinite(refLat)) {
        return coords;
      }
      const planar = coords.map((coord) => {
        if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) return null;
        const lon = Number(coord[0]);
        const lat = Number(coord[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) return null;
        return lonLatToLocalMeters(lon, lat, refLon, refLat);
      });
      if (planar.some((item) => !item)) {
        return coords;
      }
      const keep = new Uint8Array(coords.length);
      keep[0] = 1;
      keep[coords.length - 1] = 1;
      const stack = [[0, coords.length - 1]];
      while (stack.length > 0) {
        const range = stack.pop();
        if (!range) continue;
        const start = range[0];
        const end = range[1];
        if (end - start <= 1) {
          continue;
        }
        let maxDist = -1;
        let maxIdx = -1;
        const lineStart = planar[start];
        const lineEnd = planar[end];
        for (let i = start + 1; i < end; i += 1) {
          const dist = pointLineDistanceM(planar[i], lineStart, lineEnd);
          if (dist > maxDist) {
            maxDist = dist;
            maxIdx = i;
          }
        }
        if (maxIdx > start && maxIdx < end && maxDist > tolerance) {
          keep[maxIdx] = 1;
          stack.push([start, maxIdx], [maxIdx, end]);
        }
      }
      const simplified = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < coords.length; i += 1) {
        if (keep[i]) {
          simplified.push(coords[i]);
        }
      }
      return simplified.length >= 2 ? simplified : [coords[0], coords[coords.length - 1]];
    }

    function median(values) {
      if (!Array.isArray(values) || values.length === 0) {
        return Number.NaN;
      }
      const sorted = values
        .filter((v) => Number.isFinite(v))
        .sort((a, b) => a - b);
      if (sorted.length === 0) {
        return Number.NaN;
      }
      const mid = Math.floor(sorted.length / 2);
      if (sorted.length % 2 === 0) {
        return (sorted[mid - 1] + sorted[mid]) * 0.5;
      }
      return sorted[mid];
    }

    function quantile(values, q) {
      if (!Array.isArray(values) || values.length === 0) {
        return Number.NaN;
      }
      const sorted = values
        .filter((value) => Number.isFinite(value))
        .sort((a, b) => a - b);
      if (sorted.length === 0) {
        return Number.NaN;
      }
      const qq = clamp(Number.isFinite(q) ? q : 0.5, 0, 1);
      const pos = (sorted.length - 1) * qq;
      const lo = Math.floor(pos);
      const hi = Math.ceil(pos);
      if (lo === hi) {
        return sorted[lo];
      }
      const t = pos - lo;
      return sorted[lo] + (sorted[hi] - sorted[lo]) * t;
    }

    function matrixFromUnknown(value) {
      if (!value) {
        return null;
      }
      if (value.isMatrix4) {
        return value.clone();
      }
      if (Array.isArray(value) && value.length >= 16) {
        const matrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
        matrix.fromArray(value.slice(0, 16));
        return matrix;
      }
      if (value && Array.isArray(value.elements) && value.elements.length >= 16) {
        const matrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
        matrix.fromArray(value.elements.slice(0, 16));
        return matrix;
      }
      if (value && value.matrix) {
        return matrixFromUnknown(value.matrix);
      }
      return null;
    }

    function getMatrixTranslationNorm(matrix) {
      const pos = extractPositionFromMatrix(matrix);
      return pos ? pos.length() : 0;
    }

    function getTileBoundingVolume(tile) {
      if (!tile || typeof tile !== "object") {
        return null;
      }
      const candidates = [
        tile.boundingVolume,
        tile.cached && tile.cached.boundingVolume,
        tile.cached && tile.cached.tile && tile.cached.tile.boundingVolume,
        tile.content && tile.content.boundingVolume,
      ];
      for (const candidate of candidates) {
        if (!candidate) {
          continue;
        }
        if (Array.isArray(candidate) || typeof candidate === "object") {
          return candidate;
        }
      }
      return null;
    }

    function getTileAnchorFromBoundingVolume(tile) {
      const volume = getTileBoundingVolume(tile);
      if (!volume) {
        return null;
      }

      const sphere = Array.isArray(volume.sphere) ? volume.sphere : null;
      if (sphere && sphere.length >= 3) {
        const x = Number(sphere[0]);
        const y = Number(sphere[1]);
        const z = Number(sphere[2]);
        if (Number.isFinite(x) && Number.isFinite(y) && Number.isFinite(z)) {
          return {
            point: new THREE.Vector3(x, y, z),
            source: "sphere",
          };
        }
      }

      const box = Array.isArray(volume.box) ? volume.box : null;
      if (box && box.length >= 3) {
        const x = Number(box[0]);
        const y = Number(box[1]);
        const z = Number(box[2]);
        if (Number.isFinite(x) && Number.isFinite(y) && Number.isFinite(z)) {
          return {
            point: new THREE.Vector3(x, y, z),
            source: "box",
          };
        }
      }

      const region = Array.isArray(volume.region)
        ? volume.region
        : (Array.isArray(volume) && volume.length >= 6 ? volume : null);
      if (region && region.length >= 6) {
        const west = Number(region[0]);
        const south = Number(region[1]);
        const east = Number(region[2]);
        const north = Number(region[3]);
        const minH = Number(region[4]);
        const maxH = Number(region[5]);
        if (
          Number.isFinite(west) &&
          Number.isFinite(south) &&
          Number.isFinite(east) &&
          Number.isFinite(north)
        ) {
          const lonRaw = (west + east) * 0.5;
          const latRaw = (south + north) * 0.5;
          const lonDeg = Math.abs(lonRaw) <= Math.PI * 2 + 1e-6 ? toDeg(lonRaw) : lonRaw;
          const latDeg = Math.abs(latRaw) <= Math.PI + 1e-6 ? toDeg(latRaw) : latRaw;
          const h = Number.isFinite(minH) && Number.isFinite(maxH)
            ? (minH + maxH) * 0.5
            : (Number.isFinite(minH) ? minH : (Number.isFinite(maxH) ? maxH : 0));
          return {
            point: lonLatToECEF(lonDeg, latDeg, h),
            source: "region_mid",
            lonDeg,
            latDeg,
          };
        }
      }

      return null;
    }

    function buildEcefFromLocalBasisAtPoint(anchorEcef) {
      if (!anchorEcef || !anchorEcef.isVector3 || anchorEcef.lengthSq() < 1e-6) {
        return null;
      }
      const llh = ecefToLonLat(anchorEcef);
      if (!llh || !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) || !Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) {
        return null;
      }
      const lonR = toRad(llh.lng);
      const latR = toRad(llh.lat);
      const east = new THREE.Vector3(-Math.sin(lonR), Math.cos(lonR), 0).normalize();
      const up = new THREE.Vector3(
        Math.cos(latR) * Math.cos(lonR),
        Math.cos(latR) * Math.sin(lonR),
        Math.sin(latR)
      ).normalize();
      // Use a right-handed local frame: east (x), up (y), north (z).
      const north = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(east, up).normalize();
      if (
        east.lengthSq() < 1e-8 ||
        up.lengthSq() < 1e-8 ||
        north.lengthSq() < 1e-8
      ) {
        return null;
      }
      return new THREE.Matrix4().makeBasis(east, up, north);
    }

    function estimateModelWorldPlacement(modelScene, tile) {
      const localMatrix = modelScene && modelScene.matrix
        ? modelScene.matrix.clone()
        : new THREE.Matrix4();
      const localCenter = computeObjectCenter(modelScene);
      const localCenterNorm = localCenter ? localCenter.length() : NaN;
      if (Number.isFinite(localCenterNorm) && localCenterNorm > 1000000) {
        // Some PLATEAU b3dm payloads carry absolute ECEF-like vertex positions
        // even when node transforms are identity. In that case, do not add
        // bounding-volume anchor translation again.
        return {
          matrix: localMatrix,
          source: "model_geometry_ecef",
          referencePoint: localCenter.clone(),
          localCenterNorm,
          localTranslationNorm: 0,
          useLocalTranslation: true,
          localTranslationMode: "geometry_ecef",
        };
      }
      const directWorld = modelScene && modelScene.matrixWorld
        ? modelScene.matrixWorld.clone()
        : new THREE.Matrix4();
      const directNorm = getMatrixTranslationNorm(directWorld);
      if (directNorm > 1e-3) {
        return {
          matrix: directWorld,
          source: "model_matrixWorld",
          referencePoint: extractPositionFromMatrix(directWorld),
          localCenterNorm: Number.isFinite(localCenterNorm) ? localCenterNorm : null,
        };
      }

      const tileMatrixCandidates = [
        tile && tile.cached && tile.cached.scene && tile.cached.scene.matrixWorld,
        tile && tile.cached && tile.cached.scene && tile.cached.scene.matrix,
        tile && tile.cached && tile.cached.transform,
        tile && tile.cached && tile.cached.matrixWorld,
        tile && tile.cached && tile.cached.matrix,
        tile && tile.transform,
        tile && tile.matrixWorld,
        tile && tile.matrix,
      ];
      for (const candidateRaw of tileMatrixCandidates) {
        const candidate = matrixFromUnknown(candidateRaw);
        if (!candidate) {
          continue;
        }
        const world = candidate.clone().multiply(localMatrix);
        const norm = getMatrixTranslationNorm(world);
        if (norm > 1e-3) {
          return {
            matrix: world,
            source: "tile_matrix",
            referencePoint: extractPositionFromMatrix(world),
            localCenterNorm: Number.isFinite(localCenterNorm) ? localCenterNorm : null,
          };
        }
      }

      const anchor = getTileAnchorFromBoundingVolume(tile);
      if (anchor && anchor.point && anchor.point.lengthSq() > 1e4) {
        // Anchor fallback with local-ENU interpretation:
        // convert model-local translation through ENU-at-anchor into ECEF before geo frame.
        // This avoids treating local tile offsets as raw global ECEF XYZ.
        const MAX_ANCHOR_LOCAL_TRANSLATION = 50000;
        const localTranslation = extractPositionFromMatrix(localMatrix);
        const localTranslationNorm = localTranslation ? localTranslation.length() : 0;
        const anchorNorm = anchor.point.length();
        const hasFiniteLocalTranslation =
          Number.isFinite(localTranslationNorm) &&
          localTranslationNorm > 1e-3;
        const looksAbsoluteEcefTranslation =
          hasFiniteLocalTranslation &&
          localTranslationNorm > 1000000 &&
          Number.isFinite(anchorNorm) &&
          anchorNorm > 1000000 &&
          Math.abs(localTranslationNorm - anchorNorm) / anchorNorm < 0.35;
        const useLocalTranslation =
          hasFiniteLocalTranslation &&
          (
            localTranslationNorm <= MAX_ANCHOR_LOCAL_TRANSLATION ||
            looksAbsoluteEcefTranslation
          );
        const anchoredLocalMatrix = localMatrix.clone();
        const localBasisToEcef = buildEcefFromLocalBasisAtPoint(anchor.point);
        if (localBasisToEcef) {
          let localTranslationMode = "clamped";
          if (!useLocalTranslation) {
            anchoredLocalMatrix.setPosition(0, 0, 0);
          } else if (looksAbsoluteEcefTranslation && localTranslation) {
            const ecefToLocal = localBasisToEcef.clone().invert();
            const rebasedLocalOffset = localTranslation.clone().sub(anchor.point).applyMatrix4(ecefToLocal);
            if (
              Number.isFinite(rebasedLocalOffset.x) &&
              Number.isFinite(rebasedLocalOffset.y) &&
              Number.isFinite(rebasedLocalOffset.z) &&
              rebasedLocalOffset.length() <= 200000
            ) {
              anchoredLocalMatrix.setPosition(rebasedLocalOffset);
              localTranslationMode = "ecef_rebased";
            } else {
              anchoredLocalMatrix.setPosition(0, 0, 0);
            }
          } else {
            localTranslationMode = "local";
          }
          const translate = new THREE.Matrix4().makeTranslation(anchor.point.x, anchor.point.y, anchor.point.z);
          const world = translate
            .clone()
            .multiply(localBasisToEcef)
            .multiply(anchoredLocalMatrix);
          let enuSourceSuffix = "_enu_translate_clamped_local";
          if (localTranslationMode === "local") {
            enuSourceSuffix = "_enu_translate_with_local";
          } else if (localTranslationMode === "ecef_rebased") {
            enuSourceSuffix = "_enu_ecef_rebased";
          }
          return {
            matrix: world,
            source:
              "tile_bounding_volume_" +
              (anchor.source || "unknown") +
              enuSourceSuffix,
            referencePoint: anchor.point.clone(),
            localCenterNorm: Number.isFinite(localCenterNorm) ? localCenterNorm : null,
            localTranslationNorm,
            useLocalTranslation: localTranslationMode !== "clamped",
            localTranslationMode,
          };
        }
        if (!useLocalTranslation) {
          anchoredLocalMatrix.setPosition(0, 0, 0);
        }
        const translate = new THREE.Matrix4().makeTranslation(anchor.point.x, anchor.point.y, anchor.point.z);
        const world = translate.clone().multiply(anchoredLocalMatrix);
        return {
          matrix: world,
          source:
            "tile_bounding_volume_" +
            (anchor.source || "unknown") +
            (useLocalTranslation ? "_translate_with_local" : "_translate_clamped_local"),
          referencePoint: anchor.point.clone(),
          localCenterNorm: Number.isFinite(localCenterNorm) ? localCenterNorm : null,
          localTranslationNorm,
          useLocalTranslation,
          localTranslationMode: useLocalTranslation ? "local" : "clamped",
        };
      }

      return {
        matrix: directWorld,
        source: "direct_fallback",
        referencePoint: extractPositionFromMatrix(directWorld),
        localCenterNorm: Number.isFinite(localCenterNorm) ? localCenterNorm : null,
      };
    }

    function isRenderableObject(object) {
      if (!object || typeof object !== "object") {
        return false;
      }
      if (object.geometry) {
        return true;
      }
      return !!(
        object.isMesh ||
        object.isSkinnedMesh ||
        object.isInstancedMesh ||
        object.isBatchedMesh ||
        object.isPoints ||
        object.isLine ||
        object.isLineSegments ||
        object.isLineLoop ||
        object.isSprite
      );
    }

    function isAnchorPlacementSource(source) {
      if (!source || typeof source !== "string") {
        return false;
      }
      // Treat absolute ECEF-geometry placements as geo-anchored as well.
      // Applying extra axis/plane leveling on these causes false ~46deg tilts.
      return (
        source.startsWith("tile_bounding_volume_") ||
        source === "model_geometry_ecef"
      );
    }

    function initThree() {
      debugLog("initThree:start");
      state.renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({
        canvas: dom.viewport,
        antialias: true,
        alpha: false,
        preserveDrawingBuffer: true,
      });
      state.renderer.setPixelRatio(Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 2));
      state.renderer.setSize(dom.viewport.clientWidth, dom.viewport.clientHeight, false);
      state.renderer.outputColorSpace = THREE.SRGBColorSpace;
      state.renderer.toneMapping = THREE.NoToneMapping;
      state.renderer.toneMappingExposure = 1;

      state.scene = new THREE.Scene();
      state.scene.background = new THREE.Color(0xd8e3f0);
      state.scene.fog = new THREE.Fog(0xd8e3f0, 12000, 180000);

      state.camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(
        60,
        dom.viewport.clientWidth / Math.max(1, dom.viewport.clientHeight),
        1,
        100000000
      );

      state.raycaster = new THREE.Raycaster();

      const ambient = new THREE.AmbientLight(0xffffff, 0.95);
      const hemi = new THREE.HemisphereLight(0xeaf2ff, 0xa8b3c2, 0.72);
      const keyLight = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xffffff, 0.78);
      keyLight.position.set(0.45, 1.0, 0.28);
      const fillLight = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xc9dbf2, 0.42);
      fillLight.position.set(-0.82, 0.42, -0.45);
      state.scene.add(ambient, hemi, keyLight, fillLight);
      function createFallbackSkyDome() {
        const geometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(2000000, 36, 20);
        const material = new THREE.ShaderMaterial({
          side: THREE.BackSide,
          depthWrite: false,
          depthTest: false,
          uniforms: {
            topColor: { value: new THREE.Color(0x87a8ce) },
            horizonColor: { value: new THREE.Color(0xc7d6e8) },
            bottomColor: { value: new THREE.Color(0xe5ebf1) },
            offset: { value: 0.1 },
            exponent: { value: 0.9 },
          },
          vertexShader: [
            "varying vec3 vWorldPosition;",
            "void main() {",
            "  vec4 worldPosition = modelMatrix * vec4(position, 1.0);",
            "  vWorldPosition = worldPosition.xyz;",
            "  gl_Position = projectionMatrix * viewMatrix * worldPosition;",
            "}",
          ].join("\\n"),
          fragmentShader: [
            "uniform vec3 topColor;",
            "uniform vec3 horizonColor;",
            "uniform vec3 bottomColor;",
            "uniform float offset;",
            "uniform float exponent;",
            "varying vec3 vWorldPosition;",
            "void main() {",
            "  float h = normalize(vWorldPosition).y;",
            "  float t = pow(max(h + offset, 0.0), exponent);",
            "  vec3 col = mix(horizonColor, topColor, clamp(t, 0.0, 1.0));",
            "  float below = smoothstep(-0.6, 0.0, h);",
            "  col = mix(bottomColor, col, below);",
            "  gl_FragColor = vec4(col, 1.0);",
            "}",
          ].join("\\n"),
        });
        const dome = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, material);
        dome.frustumCulled = false;
        dome.renderOrder = -1000;
        return dome;
      }
      if (SkyClass) {
        try {
          const sky = new SkyClass();
          sky.scale.setScalar(2000000);
          const uniforms = sky.material && sky.material.uniforms ? sky.material.uniforms : null;
          if (uniforms) {
            uniforms.turbidity.value = 2.6;
            uniforms.rayleigh.value = 1.6;
            uniforms.mieCoefficient.value = 0.0012;
            uniforms.mieDirectionalG.value = 0.72;
            const sun = new THREE.Vector3();
            const phi = THREE.MathUtils.degToRad(90 - 42);
            const theta = THREE.MathUtils.degToRad(188);
            sun.setFromSphericalCoords(1, phi, theta);
            uniforms.sunPosition.value.copy(sun);
          }
          if (sky.material) {
            sky.material.depthWrite = false;
            sky.material.depthTest = false;
          }
          sky.frustumCulled = false;
          sky.renderOrder = -1000;
          state.scene.add(sky);
          state.sky = sky;
          debugLog("sky:init_ok");
        } catch (error) {
          debugLog("sky:init_fail", {
            message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
          });
        }
      }
      if (!state.sky) {
        const fallbackSky = createFallbackSkyDome();
        state.scene.add(fallbackSky);
        state.sky = fallbackSky;
        debugLog("sky:fallback_enabled");
      }
      state.mirrorGroup = new THREE.Group();
      state.mirrorGroup.name = "localModelMirrorGroup";
      state.mirrorGroup.visible = !!state.useMirrorFallback;
      state.mirrorGroup.matrixAutoUpdate = false;
      if (DEBUG_LOCAL_CONTROLS) {
        applyLocalAxisTransform(0, { silent: true });
      }
      state.scene.add(state.mirrorGroup);

      focusCameraOn(TOKYO23.centroid.lng, TOKYO23.centroid.lat, 1600);
      buildGeoidManager();
      buildTerrainManager();
      buildTransportManager();
      buildTransitLayerManager();
      buildRealtimeTransitManager();
      buildStreetLayerManager();
      buildTrafficManager();
      void prepareKartModelTemplate().catch((error) => {
        debugLog("kart:model_prepare_error", {
          message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
        });
      });
      void initKartRuntime().catch((error) => {
        debugLog("kart:init_background_error", {
          message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
        });
      });
      setupInputEvents();
      window.addEventListener("resize", onResize);
      debugLog("initThree:ready", {
        viewportWidth: dom.viewport.clientWidth,
        viewportHeight: dom.viewport.clientHeight,
      });
    }

    function axisKeyToVector(axisKey) {
      if (axisKey === "z") {
        return new THREE.Vector3(0, 0, 1);
      }
      if (axisKey === "x") {
        return new THREE.Vector3(1, 0, 0);
      }
      return new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0);
    }

    function getAxisTransformEntry(index) {
      const transforms = LOCAL_AXIS_TRANSFORMS;
      const count = transforms.length;
      if (count <= 0) {
        return null;
      }
      const normalizedIndex = ((index % count) + count) % count;
      return transforms[normalizedIndex];
    }

    function getAxisTransformQuaternion(entry) {
      const quat = new THREE.Quaternion();
      if (!entry) {
        return quat;
      }
      const euler = new THREE.Euler(
        Number(entry.rotationX) || 0,
        Number(entry.rotationY) || 0,
        Number(entry.rotationZ) || 0,
        "XYZ"
      );
      quat.setFromEuler(euler);
      return quat;
    }

    function applyMirrorGroupOrientation() {
      if (!state.mirrorGroup) {
        return;
      }
      const entry = getAxisTransformEntry(state.axisTransformIndex);
      const axisQuat = getAxisTransformQuaternion(entry);
      const axisMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4().makeRotationFromQuaternion(axisQuat);
      const levelMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4().makeRotationFromQuaternion(state.localLevelQuat);
      const total = state.localGeoMatrix.clone();
      total.premultiply(axisMatrix);
      total.premultiply(levelMatrix);
      state.mirrorGroup.matrixAutoUpdate = false;
      state.mirrorGroup.matrix.copy(total);
      state.mirrorGroup.matrixWorldNeedsUpdate = true;
      state.mirrorGroup.updateMatrixWorld(true);
    }

    function extractAxisDirectionFromMatrix(matrix, axisKey) {
      if (!matrix) {
        return null;
      }
      const basis = axisKeyToVector(axisKey);
      const rotationOnly = new THREE.Matrix4().extractRotation(matrix);
      basis.applyMatrix4(rotationOnly);
      if (basis.lengthSq() <= 1e-9) {
        return null;
      }
      basis.normalize();
      return basis;
    }

    function collectLocalLevelReferences(maxItems) {
      const out = [];
      const max = Number.isFinite(maxItems) ? Math.max(1, Math.floor(maxItems)) : 24;
      if (state.mirrorClonesByModelId && state.mirrorClonesByModelId.size > 0) {
        for (const [modelId, entry] of state.mirrorClonesByModelId.entries()) {
          if (!entry || !entry.clone || !entry.clone.matrix) {
            continue;
          }
          const point = resolveReferencePoint(
            entry.clone,
            entry.referencePoint,
            entry.clone.matrixWorld || entry.clone.matrix
          );
          if (point && !isUsableReferencePoint(readReferencePoint(entry.referencePoint), 1e-6)) {
            entry.referencePoint = point.clone();
            entry.clone.userData = entry.clone.userData || {};
            entry.clone.userData.__referencePoint = [point.x, point.y, point.z];
          }
          out.push({
            source: "mirror_clone",
            modelId: modelId || "unknown_clone",
            matrix: entry.clone.matrixWorld || entry.clone.matrix,
            point,
            object: entry.clone,
          });
          if (out.length >= max) {
            return out;
          }
        }
      }
      if (state.mirrorGroup && state.mirrorGroup.children && state.mirrorGroup.children.length > 0) {
        for (const child of state.mirrorGroup.children) {
          if (!child || !child.matrix) {
            continue;
          }
          const point = resolveReferencePoint(
            child,
            child.userData && child.userData.__referencePoint,
            child.matrixWorld || child.matrix
          );
          if (point) {
            child.userData = child.userData || {};
            if (!isUsableReferencePoint(readReferencePoint(child.userData.__referencePoint), 1e-6)) {
              child.userData.__referencePoint = [point.x, point.y, point.z];
            }
          }
          out.push({
            source: "mirror_child",
            modelId: child.uuid || "__mirror_child__",
            matrix: child.matrixWorld || child.matrix,
            point,
            object: child,
          });
          if (out.length >= max) {
            return out;
          }
        }
      }
      if (out.length === 0 && state.tiles && state.tiles.group && state.tiles.group.matrixWorld) {
        out.push({
          source: "tiles_group",
          modelId: "__tiles_group__",
          matrix: state.tiles.group.matrixWorld,
          point:
            computeObjectCenter(state.tiles.group) ||
            extractPositionFromMatrix(state.tiles.group.matrixWorld),
          object: state.tiles.group,
        });
      }
      return out;
    }

    function detectBestUpAxis(references, axisQuat, targetUp) {
      const candidates = ["x", "y", "z"];
      let best = null;
      for (const axisKey of candidates) {
        const mean = new THREE.Vector3();
        let used = 0;
        for (const ref of references) {
          if (!ref || !ref.matrix) {
            continue;
          }
          const sourceDir = extractAxisDirectionFromMatrix(ref.matrix, axisKey);
          if (!sourceDir) {
            continue;
          }
          sourceDir.applyQuaternion(axisQuat).normalize();
          if (mean.lengthSq() > 1e-8 && sourceDir.dot(mean) < 0) {
            sourceDir.multiplyScalar(-1);
          }
          mean.add(sourceDir);
          used += 1;
        }
        if (used <= 0 || mean.lengthSq() <= 1e-8) {
          continue;
        }
        mean.normalize();
        const rawDot = clamp(mean.dot(targetUp), -1, 1);
        const absDot = Math.abs(rawDot);
        if (!best || absDot > best.absDot) {
          best = {
            axisKey,
            absDot,
            transformed: rawDot < 0 ? mean.clone().multiplyScalar(-1) : mean,
            inverted: rawDot < 0,
            used,
          };
        }
      }
      if (!best) {
        return null;
      }
      best.absDot = clamp(best.absDot, -1, 1);
      return best;
    }

    function extractPositionFromMatrix(matrix) {
      if (!matrix || !matrix.elements || matrix.elements.length < 16) {
        return null;
      }
      const e = matrix.elements;
      const x = Number(e[12]);
      const y = Number(e[13]);
      const z = Number(e[14]);
      if (!Number.isFinite(x) || !Number.isFinite(y) || !Number.isFinite(z)) {
        return null;
      }
      return new THREE.Vector3(x, y, z);
    }

    function readReferencePoint(value) {
      if (!value) {
        return null;
      }
      if (value.isVector3) {
        if (Number.isFinite(value.x) && Number.isFinite(value.y) && Number.isFinite(value.z)) {
          return value.clone();
        }
        return null;
      }
      if (Array.isArray(value) && value.length >= 3) {
        const x = Number(value[0]);
        const y = Number(value[1]);
        const z = Number(value[2]);
        if (Number.isFinite(x) && Number.isFinite(y) && Number.isFinite(z)) {
          return new THREE.Vector3(x, y, z);
        }
      }
      return null;
    }

    function isUsableReferencePoint(point, minNormSq) {
      if (!point || !point.isVector3) {
        return false;
      }
      if (!Number.isFinite(point.x) || !Number.isFinite(point.y) || !Number.isFinite(point.z)) {
        return false;
      }
      const threshold = Number.isFinite(minNormSq) ? Math.max(0, minNormSq) : 1e-6;
      if (threshold > 0 && point.lengthSq() <= threshold) {
        return false;
      }
      return true;
    }

    function computeObjectCenter(object) {
      if (!object || typeof object !== "object") {
        return null;
      }
      try {
        object.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      const box = new THREE.Box3().setFromObject(object);
      if (!box || box.isEmpty()) {
        return null;
      }
      const sphere = box.getBoundingSphere(new THREE.Sphere());
      if (
        !sphere ||
        !sphere.center ||
        !Number.isFinite(sphere.center.x) ||
        !Number.isFinite(sphere.center.y) ||
        !Number.isFinite(sphere.center.z)
      ) {
        return null;
      }
      return sphere.center.clone();
    }

    function resolveReferencePoint(object, fallbackPoint, fallbackMatrix) {
      const candidates = [
        readReferencePoint(fallbackPoint),
        readReferencePoint(object && object.userData ? object.userData.__referencePoint : null),
        computeObjectCenter(object),
        extractPositionFromMatrix(object && object.matrixWorld ? object.matrixWorld : null),
        extractPositionFromMatrix(fallbackMatrix),
      ];
      for (const candidate of candidates) {
        if (isUsableReferencePoint(candidate, 1e-6)) {
          return candidate;
        }
      }
      for (const candidate of candidates) {
        if (isUsableReferencePoint(candidate, 0)) {
          return candidate;
        }
      }
      return null;
    }

    function extractReferencePosition(ref) {
      if (!ref) {
        return null;
      }
      const point = resolveReferencePoint(ref.object, ref.point, ref.matrix);
      if (point && (!ref.point || !isUsableReferencePoint(readReferencePoint(ref.point), 1e-6))) {
        ref.point = point.clone();
      }
      return point;
    }

    function updateLocalGeoFrame(references) {
      state.localGeoEnabled = false;
      state.localGeoFrame = "none";
      state.localGeoMedianPosNorm = 0;
      state.localGeoAnchor.set(0, 0, 0);
      state.localGeoQuat.identity();
      state.localGeoMatrix.identity();

      if (!Array.isArray(references) || references.length < 3) {
        return false;
      }

      const rawPositions = [];
      for (const ref of references) {
        if (!ref) {
          continue;
        }
        const pos = extractReferencePosition(ref);
        if (!pos || !Number.isFinite(pos.lengthSq())) {
          continue;
        }
        rawPositions.push(pos);
      }
      if (rawPositions.length < 3) {
        return false;
      }

      // Ignore origin-clamped placeholders if we have enough true samples.
      let positions = rawPositions;
      const nonZero = rawPositions.filter((p) => p.lengthSq() > 1e-4);
      if (nonZero.length >= 3) {
        positions = nonZero;
      }
      if (positions.length < 3) {
        return false;
      }

      const norms = positions
        .map((p) => p.length())
        .filter((value) => Number.isFinite(value))
        .sort((a, b) => a - b);
      if (norms.length === 0) {
        return false;
      }
      const medianNorm = norms[Math.floor(norms.length / 2)];
      state.localGeoMedianPosNorm = medianNorm;

      // ECEF coordinates have Earth-radius scale (~6.3e6m). Lower norms are already local.
      if (!Number.isFinite(medianNorm) || medianNorm < 1000000) {
        state.localGeoFrame = "local_passthrough";
        return false;
      }

      const anchor = new THREE.Vector3();
      for (const pos of positions) {
        anchor.add(pos);
      }
      anchor.multiplyScalar(1 / positions.length);

      const llh = ecefToLonLat(anchor);
      if (
        !llh ||
        !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) ||
        !Number.isFinite(llh.lat)
      ) {
        state.localGeoFrame = "ecef_invalid";
        return false;
      }

      const lonR = toRad(llh.lng);
      const latR = toRad(llh.lat);

      const east = new THREE.Vector3(-Math.sin(lonR), Math.cos(lonR), 0).normalize();
      const up = new THREE.Vector3(
        Math.cos(latR) * Math.cos(lonR),
        Math.cos(latR) * Math.sin(lonR),
        Math.sin(latR)
      ).normalize();
      // Use a right-handed local frame: east (x), up (y), north (z).
      const north = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(east, up).normalize();
      if (
        east.lengthSq() < 1e-8 ||
        up.lengthSq() < 1e-8 ||
        north.lengthSq() < 1e-8
      ) {
        state.localGeoFrame = "ecef_basis_invalid";
        return false;
      }

      const ecefFromLocal = new THREE.Matrix4().makeBasis(east, up, north);
      const localFromEcef = ecefFromLocal.clone().invert();
      const translateToAnchor = new THREE.Matrix4().makeTranslation(-anchor.x, -anchor.y, -anchor.z);

      state.localGeoMatrix.multiplyMatrices(localFromEcef, translateToAnchor);
      state.localGeoQuat.setFromRotationMatrix(new THREE.Matrix4().extractRotation(localFromEcef));
      state.localGeoAnchor.copy(anchor);
      state.localGeoEnabled = true;
      state.localGeoFrame = "ecef_to_enu";
      return true;
    }

    function detectGroundPlaneUp(references, frameQuat, targetUp) {
      const points = [];
      for (const ref of references) {
        if (!ref) {
          continue;
        }
        const pos = extractReferencePosition(ref);
        if (pos) {
          points.push(pos);
        }
      }
      if (points.length < 4) {
        return null;
      }

      const center = new THREE.Vector3();
      for (const pos of points) {
        center.add(pos);
      }
      center.multiplyScalar(1 / points.length);

      const deltas = [];
      for (const pos of points) {
        const delta = pos.clone().sub(center).applyQuaternion(frameQuat);
        if (delta.lengthSq() > 1e-4) {
          deltas.push(delta);
        }
      }
      if (deltas.length < 4) {
        return null;
      }
      deltas.sort((a, b) => b.lengthSq() - a.lengthSq());
      const sampled = deltas.slice(0, Math.min(18, deltas.length));
      if (sampled.length < 4) {
        return null;
      }

      const normal = new THREE.Vector3();
      let pairCount = 0;
      for (let i = 0; i < sampled.length; i += 1) {
        for (let j = i + 1; j < sampled.length; j += 1) {
          const cross = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(sampled[i], sampled[j]);
          const areaSq = cross.lengthSq();
          if (areaSq < 1e-8) {
            continue;
          }
          const area = Math.sqrt(areaSq);
          cross.multiplyScalar(1 / area);
          if (normal.lengthSq() > 1e-8 && cross.dot(normal) < 0) {
            cross.multiplyScalar(-1);
          }
          normal.addScaledVector(cross, area);
          pairCount += 1;
        }
      }

      if (pairCount < 4 || normal.lengthSq() < 1e-8) {
        return null;
      }
      normal.normalize();
      if (normal.dot(targetUp) < 0) {
        normal.multiplyScalar(-1);
      }

      const dot = clamp(normal.dot(targetUp), -1, 1);
      return {
        normal,
        tiltDeg: Math.acos(dot) * (180 / Math.PI),
        pairCount,
        pointCount: sampled.length,
      };
    }

    function refreshLocalLevelAlignment(reason) {
      if (!LOCAL_ONLY_MODE || !state.mirrorGroup) {
        return false;
      }
      const entry = getAxisTransformEntry(state.axisTransformIndex);
      if (!entry) {
        state.localLevelQuat.identity();
        state.localLevelTiltDeg = 0;
        state.localDetectedSourceUpAxis = "n/a";
        state.localLevelReferenceCount = 0;
        state.localPlaneTiltDeg = 0;
        state.localLevelMode = "none";
        state.localGeoEnabled = false;
        state.localGeoFrame = "none";
        state.localGeoMedianPosNorm = 0;
        state.localGeoAnchor.set(0, 0, 0);
        state.localGeoQuat.identity();
        state.localGeoMatrix.identity();
        applyMirrorGroupOrientation();
        return false;
      }

      const targetUp = axisKeyToVector(state.localMoveUpAxis || entry.moveUpAxis || "y").normalize();
      const references = collectLocalLevelReferences(24);
      if (!references || references.length <= 0) {
        state.localLevelQuat.identity();
        state.localLevelTiltDeg = 0;
        state.localDetectedSourceUpAxis = "n/a";
        state.localLevelReferenceCount = 0;
        state.localPlaneTiltDeg = 0;
        state.localLevelMode = "none";
        state.localGeoEnabled = false;
        state.localGeoFrame = "none";
        state.localGeoMedianPosNorm = 0;
        state.localGeoAnchor.set(0, 0, 0);
        state.localGeoQuat.identity();
        state.localGeoMatrix.identity();
        applyMirrorGroupOrientation();
        return false;
      }

      const axisQuat = getAxisTransformQuaternion(entry);
      updateLocalGeoFrame(references);
      let anchorPlacementCount = 0;
      for (const ref of references) {
        const source =
          ref &&
          ref.object &&
          ref.object.userData &&
          typeof ref.object.userData.__placementSource === "string"
            ? ref.object.userData.__placementSource
            : "";
        if (isAnchorPlacementSource(source)) {
          anchorPlacementCount += 1;
        }
      }
      const anchorThreshold =
        references.length < 3
          ? references.length
          : Math.max(3, Math.floor(references.length * 0.5));
      const anchorPlacementMajority =
        state.localGeoEnabled &&
        anchorPlacementCount >= anchorThreshold;
      if (anchorPlacementMajority) {
        state.localDetectedSourceUpAxis = "anchor";
        state.localLevelReferenceCount = references.length;
        state.localPlaneTiltDeg = 0;
        state.localLevelMode = "geo_anchor_no_level";
        state.localLevelQuat.identity();
        state.localLevelTiltDeg = 0;
        applyMirrorGroupOrientation();
        debugLog("tiles:local_level_alignment", {
          reason: reason || "unknown",
          transform: entry.id || "none",
          source: references[0] && references[0].source ? references[0].source : "unknown",
          modelId: references[0] && references[0].modelId ? references[0].modelId : "unknown",
          referenceCount: state.localLevelReferenceCount,
          sourceUpAxis: state.localDetectedSourceUpAxis,
          targetUpAxis: state.localMoveUpAxis || entry.moveUpAxis || "y",
          mode: state.localLevelMode,
          geoFrame: state.localGeoFrame,
          geoMedianNorm: Number.isFinite(state.localGeoMedianPosNorm)
            ? Math.round(state.localGeoMedianPosNorm)
            : 0,
          planeTiltDeg: Number.isFinite(state.localPlaneTiltDeg) ? Number(state.localPlaneTiltDeg.toFixed(3)) : 0,
          tiltDeg: Number.isFinite(state.localLevelTiltDeg) ? Number(state.localLevelTiltDeg.toFixed(3)) : 0,
          anchorPlacementCount,
        });
        return true;
      }
      const frameQuat = axisQuat.clone().multiply(state.localGeoQuat);
      const detected = detectBestUpAxis(references, frameQuat, targetUp);
      if (!detected) {
        state.localLevelQuat.identity();
        state.localLevelTiltDeg = 0;
        state.localDetectedSourceUpAxis = "n/a";
        state.localLevelReferenceCount = 0;
        state.localPlaneTiltDeg = 0;
        state.localLevelMode = "none";
        state.localGeoEnabled = false;
        state.localGeoFrame = "none";
        state.localGeoMedianPosNorm = 0;
        state.localGeoAnchor.set(0, 0, 0);
        state.localGeoQuat.identity();
        state.localGeoMatrix.identity();
        applyMirrorGroupOrientation();
        return false;
      }
      state.localDetectedSourceUpAxis = detected.axisKey + (detected.inverted ? "(-)" : "(+)");
      state.localLevelReferenceCount = detected.used || references.length;
      const plane = detectGroundPlaneUp(references, frameQuat, targetUp);
      state.localPlaneTiltDeg = plane && Number.isFinite(plane.tiltDeg) ? plane.tiltDeg : 0;

      let chosenUp = detected.transformed;
      state.localLevelMode = state.localGeoEnabled ? "axis+geo" : "axis";
      const planeTiltLimitDeg = state.localGeoEnabled ? 12 : 35;
      const usePlane =
        plane &&
        plane.pointCount >= 4 &&
        plane.pairCount >= 4 &&
        Number.isFinite(plane.tiltDeg) &&
        plane.tiltDeg <= planeTiltLimitDeg;
      if (usePlane) {
        chosenUp = plane.normal;
        state.localLevelMode = state.localGeoEnabled ? "plane+geo" : "plane";
      } else if (plane && Number.isFinite(plane.tiltDeg) && plane.tiltDeg > planeTiltLimitDeg) {
        state.localLevelMode = state.localGeoEnabled ? "axis+geo_plane_reject" : "axis_plane_reject";
      }

      const chosenDot = clamp(chosenUp.dot(targetUp), -1, 1);
      const tiltDeg = Math.acos(chosenDot) * (180 / Math.PI);

      if (!Number.isFinite(tiltDeg) || tiltDeg < 0.01) {
        state.localLevelQuat.identity();
        state.localLevelTiltDeg = 0;
      } else {
        state.localLevelQuat.setFromUnitVectors(chosenUp, targetUp);
        state.localLevelTiltDeg = tiltDeg;
      }
      applyMirrorGroupOrientation();
      debugLog("tiles:local_level_alignment", {
        reason: reason || "unknown",
        transform: entry.id || "none",
        source: references[0] && references[0].source ? references[0].source : "unknown",
        modelId: references[0] && references[0].modelId ? references[0].modelId : "unknown",
        referenceCount: state.localLevelReferenceCount,
        sourceUpAxis: state.localDetectedSourceUpAxis,
        targetUpAxis: state.localMoveUpAxis || entry.moveUpAxis || "y",
        mode: state.localLevelMode,
        geoFrame: state.localGeoFrame,
        geoMedianNorm: Number.isFinite(state.localGeoMedianPosNorm)
          ? Math.round(state.localGeoMedianPosNorm)
          : 0,
        planeTiltDeg: Number.isFinite(state.localPlaneTiltDeg) ? Number(state.localPlaneTiltDeg.toFixed(3)) : 0,
        tiltDeg: Number.isFinite(state.localLevelTiltDeg) ? Number(state.localLevelTiltDeg.toFixed(3)) : 0,
      });
      return true;
    }

    function applyLocalAxisTransform(nextIndex, options) {
      const opts = options || {};
      const transforms = LOCAL_AXIS_TRANSFORMS;
      const count = transforms.length;
      if (count === 0 || !state.mirrorGroup) {
        return;
      }
      const normalizedIndex = ((nextIndex % count) + count) % count;
      const entry = transforms[normalizedIndex];
      state.axisTransformIndex = normalizedIndex;
      state.localAxisTransform = entry.id;
      state.localMoveUpAxis = entry.moveUpAxis || state.localMoveUpAxis || "y";
      refreshLocalLevelAlignment("axis_transform_change");
      if (!opts.silent) {
        setStatus(
          "Axis transform: " + entry.id + " | moveUp=" + state.localMoveUpAxis +
            " | levelTilt=" + state.localLevelTiltDeg.toFixed(2) + "deg",
          "ok"
        );
      }
      debugLog("tiles:axis_transform", {
        transform: entry.id,
        index: normalizedIndex,
      });
    }

    function cycleLocalAxisTransform() {
      if (!LOCAL_ONLY_MODE) {
        setStatus("Axis transform toggle is only available in local-only mode.", "error");
        return;
      }
      applyLocalAxisTransform(state.axisTransformIndex + 1, { silent: false });
    }

    function getLocalMoveUpVector() {
      if (state.localMoveUpAxis === "z") {
        return new THREE.Vector3(0, 0, 1);
      }
      return new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0);
    }

    function getNavigationUpVector() {
      if (state.navigationMode === "ecef" && state.camera) {
        const radial = state.camera.position.clone();
        if (radial.lengthSq() > 1e-6) {
          return radial.normalize();
        }
      }
      return getLocalMoveUpVector();
    }

    function getNavigationBasis(up) {
      const safeUp = up && up.lengthSq() > 1e-12
        ? up.clone().normalize()
        : new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0);
      const reference = Math.abs(safeUp.z) > 0.92
        ? new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0)
        : new THREE.Vector3(0, 0, 1);
      const east = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(reference, safeUp);
      if (east.lengthSq() <= 1e-12) {
        east.set(1, 0, 0);
      }
      east.normalize();
      const north = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(safeUp, east).normalize();
      return { east, north, up: safeUp };
    }

    function syncYawPitchFromCamera() {
      if (!state.camera) {
        return;
      }
      const up = getNavigationUpVector();
      const basis = getNavigationBasis(up);
      const forward = new THREE.Vector3();
      state.camera.getWorldDirection(forward);
      if (forward.lengthSq() <= 1e-12) {
        return;
      }
      forward.normalize();
      const dotUp = clamp(forward.dot(basis.up), -0.999, 0.999);
      const pitch = Math.asin(dotUp);
      const flat = forward.clone().addScaledVector(basis.up, -dotUp);
      if (flat.lengthSq() <= 1e-12) {
        state.pitch = clamp(pitch, -Math.PI / 2.05, Math.PI / 2.05);
        return;
      }
      flat.normalize();
      state.yaw = Math.atan2(flat.dot(basis.east), flat.dot(basis.north));
      state.pitch = clamp(pitch, -Math.PI / 2.05, Math.PI / 2.05);
    }

    function setMirrorFallbackEnabled(enabled) {
      if (!DEBUG_LOCAL_CONTROLS && enabled) {
        debugLog("tiles:mirror_toggle_ignored", { reason: "debug_controls_disabled" });
        return;
      }
      const next = !!enabled;
      state.useMirrorFallback = next;
      if (state.mirrorGroup) {
        state.mirrorGroup.visible = next;
      }
      if (state.tiles && state.tiles.group) {
        state.tiles.group.visible = !next;
      }
      if (next) {
        // Stability mode: do not rebuild from full snapshot on toggle.
        // Mixing snapshot replacement with per-model mirroring causes visible popping.
        debugLog("tiles:mirror_snapshot_disabled", {
          reason: "stability_incremental_mirror_only",
          existingMirrors: state.mirroredModelIds ? state.mirroredModelIds.size : 0,
        });
      }
      refreshLocalLevelAlignment(next ? "mirror_fallback_enable" : "mirror_fallback_disable");
      debugLog("tiles:mirror_fallback_mode", { enabled: next });
      setStatus("Mirror fallback " + (next ? "enabled" : "disabled"), "ok");
    }

    function cycleLocalMoveUpAxis() {
      if (!LOCAL_ONLY_MODE) {
        setStatus("Move-axis toggle is only available in local-only mode.", "error");
        return;
      }
      state.localMoveUpAxis = state.localMoveUpAxis === "z" ? "y" : "z";
      refreshLocalLevelAlignment("manual_move_up_toggle");
      debugLog("camera:local_move_up_axis", { axis: state.localMoveUpAxis });
      setStatus("Move up-axis: " + state.localMoveUpAxis.toUpperCase(), "ok");
    }

    function markUserNavigation(reason) {
      if (!state.userHasNavigated) {
        debugLog("camera:user_navigation_lock", { reason: reason || "unknown" });
      }
      state.userHasNavigated = true;
      if (state.tileProgress) {
        state.tileProgress.needsAutoFocusCheck = false;
      }
    }

    function requestAutoRefocus(reason) {
      state.userHasNavigated = false;
      if (state.tileProgress) {
        state.tileProgress.firstModelFocused = false;
        state.tileProgress.needsAutoFocusCheck = true;
      }
      if (state.tilesManager && state.tilesManager.enabled && state.camera) {
        const llh = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
        if (llh && Number.isFinite(llh.lng) && Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) {
          let bestWard = null;
          let bestDistance = Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY;
          const wards = Array.isArray(state.tilesManager.wardManifest)
            ? state.tilesManager.wardManifest
            : [];
          for (const ward of wards) {
            const center = getWardCenter(ward);
            const distance = haversineDistanceM(llh.lng, llh.lat, center.lng, center.lat);
            if (distance < bestDistance) {
              bestDistance = distance;
              bestWard = ward;
            }
          }
          if (bestWard) {
            const center = getWardCenter(bestWard);
            focusCameraOn(center.lng, center.lat, Math.max(900, llh.altitudeM || 1400));
            return;
          }
        }
      }
      maybeAutoFocusFromModel(
        (state.tiles && state.tiles.group) ? state.tiles.group : (state.mirrorGroup || null),
        reason || "manual_refocus",
        true
      );
    }

    function onResize() {
      if (!state.renderer || !state.camera) {
        return;
      }
      const w = dom.viewport.clientWidth;
      const h = dom.viewport.clientHeight;
      state.renderer.setSize(w, h, false);
      state.camera.aspect = w / Math.max(1, h);
      state.camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
    }

    function focusCameraOn(lng, lat, altitudeM) {
      if (!state.camera) {
        return;
      }

      const target = lonLatToECEF(lng, lat, 0);
      const up = target.clone().normalize();
      const offset = up.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.max(150, altitudeM));
      const east = new THREE.Vector3(-Math.sin(toRad(lng)), Math.cos(toRad(lng)), 0).normalize();
      const side = east.multiplyScalar(220);

      state.camera.position.copy(target.clone().add(offset).add(side));
      state.camera.up.copy(up);
      state.camera.lookAt(target);
      syncYawPitchFromCamera();
    }

    function countTilesInTree(root) {
      if (!root || typeof root !== "object") {
        return 0;
      }
      const stack = [root];
      let count = 0;
      while (stack.length > 0) {
        const node = stack.pop();
        if (!node || typeof node !== "object") {
          continue;
        }
        count += 1;
        const children = Array.isArray(node.children) ? node.children : [];
        for (const child of children) {
          stack.push(child);
        }
      }
      return count;
    }

    function extractTilesRoot(tiles, event) {
      if (event && event.tileSet && event.tileSet.root) {
        return event.tileSet.root;
      }
      if (event && event.tileSet && Array.isArray(event.tileSet.children)) {
        return event.tileSet;
      }
      if (tiles && tiles.root) {
        return tiles.root;
      }
      if (tiles && tiles.tileSet && tiles.tileSet.root) {
        return tiles.tileSet.root;
      }
      return null;
    }

    function readTileUrlLike(tile) {
      if (!tile || typeof tile !== "object") {
        return "";
      }
      const directCandidates = [
        tile.contentUri,
        tile.contentURL,
        tile.contentUrl,
        tile.uri,
        tile.url,
        tile.baseUrl,
      ];
      for (const value of directCandidates) {
        if (typeof value === "string" && value.length > 0) {
          return value;
        }
      }
      const content = tile.content;
      if (content && typeof content === "object") {
        const contentCandidates = [
          content.uri,
          content.url,
          content.baseUrl,
          content.contentUri,
          content.contentURL,
        ];
        for (const value of contentCandidates) {
          if (typeof value === "string" && value.length > 0) {
            return value;
          }
        }
      }
      return "";
    }

    function deriveTileKey(event, modelScene) {
      const tile = event && event.tile ? event.tile : null;
      const tileUrl = readTileUrlLike(tile);
      if (tileUrl) {
        return tileUrl;
      }
      if (tile && (Number.isFinite(tile.level) || Number.isFinite(tile.depth))) {
        const lv = Number.isFinite(tile.level) ? tile.level : tile.depth;
        const e = tile.boundingVolume || tile.sphere || tile.box || "";
        return "tile_level_" + String(lv) + "_" + String(e);
      }
      if (modelScene && modelScene.uuid) {
        return "model:" + String(modelScene.uuid);
      }
      return "";
    }

    function getAncestorTileKeys(tile, maxDepth) {
      const out = [];
      const max = Number.isFinite(maxDepth) ? Math.max(0, maxDepth) : 10;
      let cursor = tile && tile.parent ? tile.parent : null;
      while (cursor && out.length < max) {
        const key = readTileUrlLike(cursor);
        if (key) {
          out.push(key);
        }
        cursor = cursor.parent || null;
      }
      return out;
    }

    function getTileStatsSnapshot() {
      if (state.tilesManager && state.tilesManager.enabled) {
        return computeTilesManagerStats();
      }
      const stats = state.tiles && state.tiles.stats ? state.tiles.stats : null;
      if (!stats || typeof stats !== "object") {
        return {};
      }
      const keys = [
        "inFrustum",
        "used",
        "active",
        "visible",
        "downloading",
        "parsing",
        "failed",
        "cached",
      ];
      const out = {};
      for (const key of keys) {
        if (Number.isFinite(stats[key])) {
          out[key] = stats[key];
        }
      }
      return out;
    }

    function computeTileLoadedPercent() {
      if (state.tilesManager && state.tilesManager.enabled) {
        const manager = state.tilesManager;
        let known = 0;
        let loaded = 0;
        let hasKnown = false;
        let hasLoaded = false;
        for (const entry of manager.wards.values()) {
          if (!entry) {
            continue;
          }
          if (Number.isFinite(entry.knownTiles) && entry.knownTiles > 0) {
            known += entry.knownTiles;
            hasKnown = true;
          }
          if (Number.isFinite(entry.loadedModels)) {
            loaded += entry.loadedModels;
            hasLoaded = true;
          }
        }
        if (hasKnown && known > 0) {
          return clamp((loaded / known) * 100, 0, 100);
        }
        const stats = getTileStatsSnapshot();
        const used = Number.isFinite(stats.used) ? stats.used : Number.NaN;
        const inFrustum = Number.isFinite(stats.inFrustum) ? stats.inFrustum : Number.NaN;
        if (Number.isFinite(used) && Number.isFinite(inFrustum) && inFrustum > 0) {
          return clamp((used / inFrustum) * 100, 0, 100);
        }
        return hasLoaded && loaded > 0 ? 100 : 0;
      }
      const progress = state.tileProgress;
      if (!progress) {
        return 0;
      }
      if (progress.knownTiles > 0) {
        return clamp((progress.loadedModels / progress.knownTiles) * 100, 0, 100);
      }

      const stats = getTileStatsSnapshot();
      const used = Number.isFinite(stats.used) ? stats.used : NaN;
      const inFrustum = Number.isFinite(stats.inFrustum) ? stats.inFrustum : NaN;
      if (Number.isFinite(used) && Number.isFinite(inFrustum) && inFrustum > 0) {
        return clamp((used / inFrustum) * 100, 0, 100);
      }
      return progress.loadedModels > 0 ? 100 : 0;
    }

    function formatPercent(value) {
      const safe = Number.isFinite(value) ? value : 0;
      return (Math.round(safe * 10) / 10).toFixed(1);
    }

    function logTileProgress(force) {
      if (state.tilesManager && state.tilesManager.enabled) {
        const progress = state.tileProgress;
        if (!progress) {
          return;
        }
        const nowMs = Date.now();
        const percent = computeTileLoadedPercent();
        const shouldLog =
          !!force ||
          Math.round(percent) !== progress.lastLoggedPercent ||
          nowMs - progress.lastLoggedMs >= 2500;
        if (!shouldLog) {
          return;
        }
        progress.lastLoggedPercent = Math.round(percent);
        progress.lastLoggedMs = nowMs;
        let loadedModels = 0;
        let knownTiles = 0;
        let failedModels = 0;
        for (const entry of state.tilesManager.wards.values()) {
          loadedModels += Number.isFinite(entry.loadedModels) ? entry.loadedModels : 0;
          knownTiles += Number.isFinite(entry.knownTiles) ? entry.knownTiles : 0;
          failedModels += Number.isFinite(entry.failedModels) ? entry.failedModels : 0;
        }
        debugLog("tiles:progress", {
          loadedPercent: formatPercent(percent),
          loadedModels,
          knownTiles,
          failedModels,
          wardsActive: state.tilesManager.activeWardIds.size,
          tierDistribution: state.tilesManager.tierDistribution,
          stats: getTileStatsSnapshot(),
        });
        return;
      }
      if (!state.tiles || !state.tileProgress) {
        return;
      }
      const nowMs = Date.now();
      const percent = computeTileLoadedPercent();
      const progress = state.tileProgress;
      const shouldLog =
        !!force ||
        Math.round(percent) !== progress.lastLoggedPercent ||
        nowMs - progress.lastLoggedMs >= 3000;
      if (!shouldLog) {
        return;
      }
      progress.lastLoggedPercent = Math.round(percent);
      progress.lastLoggedMs = nowMs;
      debugLog("tiles:progress", {
        loadedPercent: formatPercent(percent),
        loadedModels: progress.loadedModels,
        knownTiles: progress.knownTiles,
        failedModels: progress.failedModels,
        stats: getTileStatsSnapshot(),
      });
    }

    function maybeAutoFocusFromModel(modelScene, source, force) {
      const progress = state.tileProgress;
      if (!progress || !state.camera || !modelScene) {
        return;
      }
      const nowMs = Date.now();
      if (!force && progress.firstModelFocused) {
        return;
      }
      if (state.userHasNavigated) {
        return;
      }
      if (force && state.lastAutoFocusAtMs > 0 && nowMs - state.lastAutoFocusAtMs < 2500) {
        return;
      }
      const candidates = [];
      const preferMirrorInLocalOnly =
        LOCAL_ONLY_MODE &&
        state.useMirrorFallback &&
        state.mirrorGroup &&
        state.mirrorGroup.children &&
        state.mirrorGroup.children.length > 0;
      if (!preferMirrorInLocalOnly && state.tiles && state.tiles.group) {
        candidates.push({ name: "tiles_group", object: state.tiles.group, priority: 3 });
      }
      if (modelScene) {
        candidates.push({ name: "model_scene", object: modelScene, priority: 2 });
      }
      if (state.mirrorGroup && state.mirrorGroup.children && state.mirrorGroup.children.length > 0) {
        candidates.push({
          name: "mirror_group",
          object: state.mirrorGroup,
          priority: preferMirrorInLocalOnly ? 4 : 1,
        });
      }

      let selected = null;
      let selectedSphere = null;
      for (const candidate of candidates) {
        if (!candidate || !candidate.object) {
          continue;
        }
        try {
          candidate.object.updateMatrixWorld(true);
        } catch (_error) {
          // no-op
        }
        const box = new THREE.Box3().setFromObject(candidate.object);
        if (box.isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        const sphere = box.getBoundingSphere(new THREE.Sphere());
        if (!sphere || !Number.isFinite(sphere.radius) || sphere.radius <= 0) {
          continue;
        }

        if (!selected) {
          selected = candidate;
          selectedSphere = sphere;
          continue;
        }
        if ((candidate.priority || 0) > (selected.priority || 0)) {
          selected = candidate;
          selectedSphere = sphere;
          continue;
        }
        if (
          (candidate.priority || 0) === (selected.priority || 0) &&
          sphere.radius > selectedSphere.radius
        ) {
          selected = candidate;
          selectedSphere = sphere;
        }
      }
      if (!selected || !selectedSphere) {
        return;
      }

      const sphere = selectedSphere;
      if (!sphere || !Number.isFinite(sphere.radius) || sphere.radius <= 0) {
        return;
      }

      const oldDistance = state.camera.position.distanceTo(sphere.center);
      const stats = getTileStatsSnapshot();
      const looksMismatched =
        oldDistance > Math.max(4000, sphere.radius * 8) ||
        ((stats.inFrustum === 0 || stats.visible === 0) && progress.loadedModels > 0);
      if (!looksMismatched) {
        return;
      }

      // Keep a fixed global frame to avoid camera-mode oscillation and culling churn.
      state.navigationMode = "ecef";

      const offset = new THREE.Vector3(1.0, 0.6, 1.0)
        .normalize()
        .multiplyScalar(
          Math.max(250, sphere.radius * 3)
        );
      const up = sphere.center.clone().normalize().multiplyScalar(Math.max(120, sphere.radius * 0.8));
      offset.add(up);
      state.camera.position.copy(sphere.center.clone().add(offset));
      state.camera.up.copy(sphere.center.clone().normalize());
      state.camera.lookAt(sphere.center);
      state.camera.near = 1;
      state.camera.far = 100000000;
      state.camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
      syncYawPitchFromCamera();

      progress.firstModelFocused = true;
      state.lastAutoFocusAtMs = nowMs;
      debugLog("tiles:auto_focus_on_model", {
        source,
        force: !!force,
        focusObject: selected.name,
        navigationMode: state.navigationMode,
        oldCameraDistance: Math.round(oldDistance),
        modelRadius: Math.round(sphere.radius),
        modelCenter: {
          x: Math.round(sphere.center.x),
          y: Math.round(sphere.center.y),
          z: Math.round(sphere.center.z),
        },
      });
      setStatus("Auto-focused camera on first loaded tile model.", "ok");
    }

    function findCesiumRtcExtension(modelScene) {
      if (!modelScene || typeof modelScene !== "object") {
        return null;
      }
      const direct = modelScene.userData && modelScene.userData.gltfExtensions
        ? modelScene.userData.gltfExtensions.CESIUM_RTC
        : null;
      if (direct && Array.isArray(direct.center) && direct.center.length >= 3) {
        return direct;
      }

      let found = null;
      try {
        modelScene.traverse((obj) => {
          if (found || !obj || !obj.userData || !obj.userData.gltfExtensions) {
            return;
          }
          const ext = obj.userData.gltfExtensions.CESIUM_RTC;
          if (ext && Array.isArray(ext.center) && ext.center.length >= 3) {
            found = ext;
          }
        });
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      return found;
    }

    function applyCesiumRtcOffset(modelScene) {
      if (!modelScene || typeof modelScene !== "object") {
        return false;
      }
      if (modelScene.userData && (modelScene.userData.__cesiumRtcApplied || modelScene.userData.__cesiumRtcSkipped)) {
        return false;
      }

      const rtc = findCesiumRtcExtension(modelScene);
      if (!rtc || !Array.isArray(rtc.center) || rtc.center.length < 3) {
        return false;
      }

      const cx = Number(rtc.center[0]) || 0;
      const cy = Number(rtc.center[1]) || 0;
      const cz = Number(rtc.center[2]) || 0;
      if (!Number.isFinite(cx) || !Number.isFinite(cy) || !Number.isFinite(cz)) {
        return false;
      }

      try {
        modelScene.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }

      const rtcCenter = new THREE.Vector3(cx, cy, cz);
      const rtcNorm = rtcCenter.length();
      const worldPos = extractPositionFromMatrix(modelScene.matrixWorld);
      const worldNorm = worldPos ? worldPos.length() : NaN;
      const center = computeObjectCenter(modelScene);
      const centerNorm = center ? center.length() : NaN;
      const positionNorm =
        modelScene.position && Number.isFinite(modelScene.position.lengthSq())
          ? Math.sqrt(modelScene.position.lengthSq())
          : NaN;

      const looksAlreadyPositioned =
        (Number.isFinite(worldNorm) && rtcNorm > 1000 && worldNorm > 100 &&
          Math.abs(worldNorm - rtcNorm) / rtcNorm < 0.35) ||
        (Number.isFinite(centerNorm) && rtcNorm > 1000 && centerNorm > 100 &&
          Math.abs(centerNorm - rtcNorm) / rtcNorm < 0.35) ||
        (rtcNorm > 100000 &&
          Number.isFinite(centerNorm) &&
          Number.isFinite(positionNorm) &&
          centerNorm > 25 &&
          positionNorm > 1);

      modelScene.userData = modelScene.userData || {};
      modelScene.userData.__cesiumRtcCenter = [cx, cy, cz];

      if (looksAlreadyPositioned) {
        modelScene.userData.__cesiumRtcSkipped = true;
        debugLog("tiles:skipped_cesium_rtc", {
          reason: "already_positioned",
          center: [Math.round(cx), Math.round(cy), Math.round(cz)],
          worldNorm: Number.isFinite(worldNorm) ? Math.round(worldNorm) : null,
          centerNorm: Number.isFinite(centerNorm) ? Math.round(centerNorm) : null,
        });
        return false;
      }

      modelScene.position.add(rtcCenter);
      modelScene.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      modelScene.userData.__cesiumRtcApplied = true;
      debugLog("tiles:applied_cesium_rtc", {
        center: [Math.round(cx), Math.round(cy), Math.round(cz)],
      });
      return true;
    }

    function removeMirrorCloneByModelId(modelId, reason) {
      if (!modelId || !state.mirrorClonesByModelId || !state.mirrorGroup) {
        return false;
      }
      const entry = state.mirrorClonesByModelId.get(modelId);
      if (!entry || !entry.clone) {
        return false;
      }
      const clone = entry.clone;
      if (clone.parent) {
        clone.parent.remove(clone);
      }
      state.mirrorClonesByModelId.delete(modelId);
      state.mirroredModelIds.delete(modelId);
      if (entry.tileKey && state.mirrorClonesByTileKey) {
        const mappedId = state.mirrorClonesByTileKey.get(entry.tileKey);
        if (mappedId === modelId) {
          state.mirrorClonesByTileKey.delete(entry.tileKey);
        }
      }
      debugLog("tiles:model_unmirrored", {
        modelId,
        reason: reason || "remove",
        mirroredCount: state.mirroredModelIds.size,
      });
      return true;
    }

    function sanitizeSurfaceMaterial(mat) {
      if (!mat) {
        return;
      }
      mat.depthTest = true;
      mat.depthWrite = true;
      if ("metalness" in mat && Number.isFinite(mat.metalness)) {
        mat.metalness = 0;
      }
      if ("roughness" in mat && Number.isFinite(mat.roughness)) {
        mat.roughness = 1;
      }
      if ("envMapIntensity" in mat && Number.isFinite(mat.envMapIntensity)) {
        mat.envMapIntensity = 0;
      }
      if ("shininess" in mat && Number.isFinite(mat.shininess)) {
        mat.shininess = 0;
      }
      if (mat.specular && typeof mat.specular.setRGB === "function") {
        mat.specular.setRGB(0, 0, 0);
      }
      mat.needsUpdate = true;
    }

    function forceFlatBuildingMaterial(mesh) {
      if (!mesh || !mesh.isMesh || !state.buildingFlatMaterial) {
        return;
      }
      mesh.material = state.buildingFlatMaterial;
      mesh.renderOrder = 12;
    }

    function cloneTextureDeep(texture) {
      if (!texture || typeof texture.clone !== "function") {
        return texture || null;
      }
      const cloned = texture.clone();
      cloned.needsUpdate = true;
      return cloned;
    }

    function cloneMaterialDeep(material) {
      if (!material || typeof material.clone !== "function") {
        return material || null;
      }
      if (state.buildingFlatMaterial && material === state.buildingFlatMaterial) {
        return state.buildingFlatMaterial;
      }
      const cloned = material.clone();
      const textureKeys = [
        "map",
        "normalMap",
        "roughnessMap",
        "metalnessMap",
        "aoMap",
        "emissiveMap",
        "alphaMap",
        "bumpMap",
        "displacementMap",
        "specularMap",
        "lightMap",
        "envMap",
      ];
      for (const key of textureKeys) {
        if (cloned[key]) {
          cloned[key] = cloneTextureDeep(cloned[key]);
        }
      }
      sanitizeSurfaceMaterial(cloned);
      return cloned;
    }

    function detachMeshResources(mesh) {
      if (!mesh || !mesh.isMesh) {
        return;
      }
      if (state.buildingFlatMaterial && mesh.material === state.buildingFlatMaterial) {
        return;
      }
      if (mesh.geometry && typeof mesh.geometry.clone === "function") {
        mesh.geometry = mesh.geometry.clone();
      }
      if (Array.isArray(mesh.material)) {
        mesh.material = mesh.material.map((mat) => cloneMaterialDeep(mat));
      } else if (mesh.material) {
        mesh.material = cloneMaterialDeep(mesh.material);
      }
    }

    function mirrorSnapshotFromTilesGroup(reason) {
      if (!LOCAL_ONLY_MODE || !state.useMirrorFallback || !state.tiles || !state.tiles.group || !state.mirrorGroup) {
        return 0;
      }
      try {
        state.tiles.group.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }

      const snapshot = state.tiles.group.clone(true);
      snapshot.name = "mirror_tiles_snapshot";
      snapshot.matrixAutoUpdate = false;
      snapshot.matrix.copy(state.tiles.group.matrixWorld);
      snapshot.matrixWorld.copy(state.tiles.group.matrixWorld);
      snapshot.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      const snapshotReferencePoint =
        computeObjectCenter(state.tiles.group) ||
        extractPositionFromMatrix(state.tiles.group.matrixWorld);
      let renderableCount = 0;
      snapshot.traverse((obj) => {
        obj.visible = true;
        if (!isRenderableObject(obj)) {
          return;
        }
        renderableCount += 1;
        if (obj.isMesh) {
          detachMeshResources(obj);
        }
      });

      if (renderableCount <= 0) {
        debugLog("tiles:mirror_snapshot_skipped", {
          reason: reason || "unknown",
          renderableCount,
          existingChildren: state.mirrorGroup.children.length,
        });
        return 0;
      }

      while (state.mirrorGroup.children.length > 0) {
        const child = state.mirrorGroup.children.pop();
        if (child && child.parent) {
          child.parent.remove(child);
        }
      }
      state.mirrorGroup.add(snapshot);
      state.mirroredModelIds = new Set(["__snapshot__"]);
      state.mirrorClonesByModelId = new Map([
        [
          "__snapshot__",
          {
            clone: snapshot,
            tileKey: "",
            referencePoint: snapshotReferencePoint ? snapshotReferencePoint.clone() : null,
          },
        ],
      ]);
      state.mirrorClonesByTileKey = new Map();
      snapshot.userData = snapshot.userData || {};
      snapshot.userData.__referencePoint =
        snapshotReferencePoint && snapshotReferencePoint.isVector3
          ? [snapshotReferencePoint.x, snapshotReferencePoint.y, snapshotReferencePoint.z]
          : null;
      refreshLocalLevelAlignment("mirror_snapshot");
      debugLog("tiles:mirror_snapshot", {
        reason: reason || "unknown",
        renderableCount,
        hasReferencePoint: !!snapshotReferencePoint,
        referenceNorm: snapshotReferencePoint && Number.isFinite(snapshotReferencePoint.lengthSq())
          ? Math.round(Math.sqrt(snapshotReferencePoint.lengthSq()))
          : 0,
      });
      return renderableCount;
    }

    function prepareLoadedModelScene(modelScene) {
      if (!modelScene || typeof modelScene.traverse !== "function") {
        return;
      }
      modelScene.traverse((obj) => {
        if (!obj || !obj.isMesh) {
          return;
        }
        obj.castShadow = false;
        obj.receiveShadow = false;
        forceFlatBuildingMaterial(obj);
        if (Array.isArray(obj.material)) {
          for (const mat of obj.material) {
            sanitizeSurfaceMaterial(mat);
          }
        } else if (obj.material) {
          sanitizeSurfaceMaterial(obj.material);
        }
      });
    }

    function mirrorLoadedModel(modelScene, source, tileKey, tile) {
      if (!LOCAL_ONLY_MODE || !state.scene || !state.mirrorGroup || !modelScene) {
        return;
      }
      const modelId = modelScene.uuid ? String(modelScene.uuid) : "";
      if (!modelId) {
        return;
      }

      if (tileKey && state.mirrorClonesByTileKey && state.mirrorClonesByTileKey.has(tileKey)) {
        const existingModelId = state.mirrorClonesByTileKey.get(tileKey);
        if (existingModelId && existingModelId !== modelId) {
          removeMirrorCloneByModelId(existingModelId, "replace_by_tile_key");
        }
      }
      if (state.mirroredModelIds.has(modelId)) {
        return;
      }

      try {
        if (state.tiles && state.tiles.group) {
          state.tiles.group.updateMatrixWorld(true);
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      try {
        modelScene.updateWorldMatrix(true, true);
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      try {
        modelScene.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      const placement = estimateModelWorldPlacement(modelScene, tile);
      const placementMatrix = placement && placement.matrix
        ? placement.matrix
        : (modelScene.matrixWorld ? modelScene.matrixWorld.clone() : new THREE.Matrix4());
      const modelReferencePoint =
        (placement && placement.referencePoint ? placement.referencePoint.clone() : null) ||
        computeObjectCenter(modelScene) ||
        extractPositionFromMatrix(placementMatrix) ||
        extractPositionFromMatrix(modelScene.matrixWorld);

      const clone = modelScene.clone(true);
      clone.matrixAutoUpdate = false;
      clone.matrix.copy(placementMatrix);
      clone.matrixWorld.copy(placementMatrix);
      clone.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      clone.userData = clone.userData || {};
      clone.userData.__referencePoint =
        modelReferencePoint && modelReferencePoint.isVector3
          ? [modelReferencePoint.x, modelReferencePoint.y, modelReferencePoint.z]
          : null;
      clone.userData.__placementSource = placement && placement.source ? placement.source : "unknown";
      clone.traverse((obj) => {
        if (!obj.isMesh) {
          return;
        }
        detachMeshResources(obj);
      });
      state.mirrorGroup.add(clone);
      state.mirroredModelIds.add(modelId);
      if (state.mirrorClonesByModelId) {
        state.mirrorClonesByModelId.set(modelId, {
          clone,
          tileKey: tileKey || "",
          referencePoint: modelReferencePoint ? modelReferencePoint.clone() : null,
        });
      }
      if (tileKey && state.mirrorClonesByTileKey) {
        state.mirrorClonesByTileKey.set(tileKey, modelId);
      }
      refreshLocalLevelAlignment("model_mirrored");
      debugLog("tiles:model_mirrored", {
        source,
        modelId,
        tileKey: tileKey || null,
        mirroredCount: state.mirroredModelIds.size,
        hasReferencePoint: !!modelReferencePoint,
        referenceNorm: modelReferencePoint && Number.isFinite(modelReferencePoint.lengthSq())
          ? Math.round(Math.sqrt(modelReferencePoint.lengthSq()))
          : 0,
        placementSource: placement && placement.source ? placement.source : "unknown",
        placementLocalTranslationNorm:
          placement && Number.isFinite(placement.localTranslationNorm)
            ? Number(placement.localTranslationNorm.toFixed(3))
            : null,
        placementUsedLocalTranslation:
          placement && typeof placement.useLocalTranslation === "boolean"
            ? placement.useLocalTranslation
            : null,
        placementLocalTranslationMode:
          placement && typeof placement.localTranslationMode === "string"
            ? placement.localTranslationMode
            : null,
        placementLocalCenterNorm:
          placement && Number.isFinite(placement.localCenterNorm)
            ? Math.round(placement.localCenterNorm)
            : null,
      });
    }

    function markModelLoaded(modelScene, source, tileKey, tile) {
      const progress = state.tileProgress;
      if (!progress) {
        return;
      }
      const key =
        modelScene && modelScene.uuid
          ? String(modelScene.uuid)
          : "model_" + String(progress.loadedModels + progress.failedModels + 1);

      if (progress.seenModelIds.has(key)) {
        return;
      }
      progress.seenModelIds.add(key);
      progress.loadedModels += 1;
      mirrorLoadedModel(modelScene, source, tileKey || "", tile || null);
      progress.needsAutoFocusCheck = true;
      logTileProgress(false);
    }

    function isEditableTarget(target) {
      if (!target || typeof target !== "object") {
        return false;
      }
      const tag = target.tagName ? String(target.tagName).toLowerCase() : "";
      if (tag === "input" || tag === "textarea" || tag === "select") {
        return true;
      }
      return !!target.isContentEditable;
    }

    function isFullscreenActive() {
      return !!(
        document.fullscreenElement ||
        document.webkitFullscreenElement
      );
    }

    function toggleFullscreen() {
      const target = dom.viewportWrap || dom.viewport || document.documentElement;
      const request =
        (target && target.requestFullscreen) ||
        (target && target.webkitRequestFullscreen);
      const exit = document.exitFullscreen || document.webkitExitFullscreen;

      if (!isFullscreenActive()) {
        if (request) {
          try {
            request.call(target);
            setStatus("Fullscreen enabled.", "ok");
          } catch (error) {
            setStatus("Failed to enter fullscreen: " + (error && error.message ? error.message : String(error)), "error");
          }
        }
        return;
      }

      if (exit) {
        try {
          exit.call(document);
          setStatus("Fullscreen disabled.", "ok");
        } catch (error) {
          setStatus("Failed to exit fullscreen: " + (error && error.message ? error.message : String(error)), "error");
        }
      }
    }

    function setupInputEvents() {
