      dom.viewport.addEventListener("contextmenu", (event) => event.preventDefault());
      const pointerLockTarget = dom.viewportWrap || dom.viewport;
      const requestPointerLock = (target) => {
        if (!target || typeof target.requestPointerLock !== "function") {
          return false;
        }
        try {
          target.requestPointerLock();
          return true;
        } catch (_error) {
          return false;
        }
      };
      const updatePointerLockState = () => {
        state.pointerLocked = document.pointerLockElement === pointerLockTarget;
      };
      document.addEventListener("pointerlockchange", updatePointerLockState);
      document.addEventListener("pointerlockerror", () => {
        debugLog("input:pointerlock_error");
      });

      const handleKeyDown = (event) => {
        const targetIsEditable = isEditableTarget(event.target);
        if (
          event.code === "KeyG" &&
          !event.repeat &&
          !event.metaKey &&
          !event.ctrlKey &&
          !event.altKey &&
          !targetIsEditable
        ) {
          const nowMs = Date.now();
          if (nowMs - (state.kart.lastToggleAtMs || 0) < 120) {
            return;
          }
          state.kart.lastToggleAtMs = nowMs;
          event.preventDefault();
          event.stopPropagation();
          debugLog("kart:key_toggle", {
            from: state.driveMode ? "drive" : "fly",
            kartReady: !!(state.kart && state.kart.ready),
            cannonReady: !!(state.cannon && state.cannon.ready),
          });
          void setDriveMode(!state.driveMode);
          return;
        }

        if (
          event.code === "KeyF" &&
          !event.metaKey &&
          !event.ctrlKey &&
          !event.altKey &&
          !targetIsEditable
        ) {
          event.preventDefault();
          toggleFullscreen();
          return;
        }

        if (
          event.code === "KeyL" &&
          !event.repeat &&
          !event.metaKey &&
          !event.ctrlKey &&
          !event.altKey &&
          !targetIsEditable
        ) {
          event.preventDefault();
          void toggleMusicPlayback();
          return;
        }

        if (
          DEBUG_LOCAL_CONTROLS &&
          event.code === "KeyX" &&
          !event.repeat &&
          !event.metaKey &&
          !event.ctrlKey &&
          !event.altKey &&
          !targetIsEditable
        ) {
          event.preventDefault();
          cycleLocalAxisTransform();
          return;
        }

        if (
          DEBUG_LOCAL_CONTROLS &&
          event.code === "KeyM" &&
          !event.repeat &&
          !event.metaKey &&
          !event.ctrlKey &&
          !event.altKey &&
          !targetIsEditable
        ) {
          event.preventDefault();
          setMirrorFallbackEnabled(!state.useMirrorFallback);
          return;
        }

        if (
          DEBUG_LOCAL_CONTROLS &&
          event.code === "KeyV" &&
          !event.repeat &&
          !event.metaKey &&
          !event.ctrlKey &&
          !event.altKey &&
          !targetIsEditable
        ) {
          event.preventDefault();
          cycleLocalMoveUpAxis();
          return;
        }

        if (
          event.code === "KeyR" &&
          !event.repeat &&
          !event.metaKey &&
          !event.ctrlKey &&
          !event.altKey &&
          !targetIsEditable
        ) {
          event.preventDefault();
          if (state.driveMode) {
            resetKartPose();
            return;
          }
          requestAutoRefocus("manual_key_r");
          setStatus("Camera refocus requested.", "ok");
          return;
        }

        if (
          state.driveMode &&
          !event.metaKey &&
          !event.ctrlKey &&
          !event.altKey &&
          !targetIsEditable
        ) {
          if (event.code === "Space") {
            event.preventDefault();
            if (!event.repeat) {
              tryKartJump();
            }
            return;
          }
          if (event.code === "KeyB") {
            event.preventDefault();
            if (!event.repeat) {
              applyKartBoost();
            }
            return;
          }
          if (event.code === "KeyC") {
            event.preventDefault();
            if (!event.repeat) {
              cycleKartColor();
            }
            return;
          }
        }

        if (
          !event.metaKey &&
          !event.ctrlKey &&
          !event.altKey &&
          !targetIsEditable &&
          (
            event.code === "Space" ||
            event.code === "KeyQ" ||
            event.code === "KeyC" ||
            event.code === "ArrowUp" ||
            event.code === "ArrowDown" ||
            event.code === "ArrowLeft" ||
            event.code === "ArrowRight"
          )
        ) {
          event.preventDefault();
        }

        if (targetIsEditable) {
          return;
        }

        state.keys[event.code] = true;
        if (
          event.code === "KeyW" ||
          event.code === "KeyS" ||
          event.code === "KeyA" ||
          event.code === "KeyD" ||
          event.code === "ArrowUp" ||
          event.code === "ArrowDown" ||
          event.code === "ArrowLeft" ||
          event.code === "ArrowRight" ||
          event.code === "Space" ||
          event.code === "KeyQ" ||
          event.code === "KeyC" ||
          event.code === "ControlLeft" ||
          event.code === "ControlRight" ||
          event.code === "ShiftLeft" ||
          event.code === "ShiftRight"
        ) {
          markUserNavigation("keyboard");
        }
        if (
          event.code.startsWith("Arrow") ||
          event.code === "Space" ||
          event.code === "ShiftLeft" ||
          event.code === "ShiftRight"
        ) {
          event.preventDefault();
        }
      };
      window.addEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown, true);

      window.addEventListener("keyup", (event) => {
        state.keys[event.code] = false;
      });

      window.addEventListener("blur", () => {
        state.keys = {};
        state.looking = false;
        state.pointerLocked = false;
      });

      dom.viewport.addEventListener("mousedown", (event) => {
        if (event.button === 0 && !isEditableTarget(event.target)) {
          requestPointerLock(pointerLockTarget);
        }
        if (event.button === 2 && !state.driveMode) {
          state.looking = true;
          state.lastMouseX = event.clientX;
          state.lastMouseY = event.clientY;
        }
      });

      window.addEventListener("mouseup", () => {
        state.looking = false;
      });

      window.addEventListener("mousemove", (event) => {
        if (state.driveMode) {
          state.lastMouseX = event.clientX;
          state.lastMouseY = event.clientY;
          return;
        }
        let dx = 0;
        let dy = 0;
        if (state.pointerLocked) {
          dx = Number(event.movementX) || 0;
          dy = Number(event.movementY) || 0;
        } else {
          if (!state.looking) {
            return;
          }
          dx = event.clientX - state.lastMouseX;
          dy = event.clientY - state.lastMouseY;
          state.lastMouseX = event.clientX;
          state.lastMouseY = event.clientY;
        }

        state.yaw -= dx * state.mouseSensitivity;
        state.pitch = clamp(state.pitch - dy * state.mouseSensitivity, -Math.PI / 2.05, Math.PI / 2.05);
        if (dx !== 0 || dy !== 0) {
          markUserNavigation("mouse_look");
        }
      });

      dom.viewport.addEventListener("click", onCanvasClick);
    }

    function updateFlyMode(deltaSec) {
      if (!state.camera || state.driveMode) {
        return;
      }

      const navUp = getNavigationUpVector();
      const basis = getNavigationBasis(navUp);
      state.camera.up.copy(basis.up);

      const cp = Math.cos(state.pitch);
      const sp = Math.sin(state.pitch);
      const cy = Math.cos(state.yaw);
      const sy = Math.sin(state.yaw);
      const forward = new THREE.Vector3()
        .addScaledVector(basis.east, sy * cp)
        .addScaledVector(basis.north, cy * cp)
        .addScaledVector(basis.up, sp);
      if (forward.lengthSq() <= 1e-10) {
        forward.copy(basis.north);
      } else {
        forward.normalize();
      }

      const lookTarget = state.camera.position.clone().add(forward);
      const lookMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4().lookAt(state.camera.position, lookTarget, basis.up);
      state.camera.quaternion.setFromRotationMatrix(lookMatrix);

      const forwardFlat = forward.clone().addScaledVector(basis.up, -forward.dot(basis.up));
      if (forwardFlat.lengthSq() < 1e-6) {
        forwardFlat.copy(basis.north);
      } else {
        forwardFlat.normalize();
      }
      const rightFlat = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(forwardFlat, basis.up).normalize();

      const move = new THREE.Vector3();
      const verticalMoveScale = 0.7;

      if (state.keys.KeyW || state.keys.ArrowUp) {
        move.add(forwardFlat);
      }
      if (state.keys.KeyS || state.keys.ArrowDown) {
        move.sub(forwardFlat);
      }
      if (state.keys.KeyA || state.keys.ArrowLeft) {
        move.sub(rightFlat);
      }
      if (state.keys.KeyD || state.keys.ArrowRight) {
        move.add(rightFlat);
      }
      if (state.keys.Space) {
        move.addScaledVector(basis.up, verticalMoveScale);
      }
      if (state.keys.KeyQ || state.keys.ControlLeft || state.keys.ControlRight || state.keys.KeyC) {
        move.addScaledVector(basis.up, -verticalMoveScale);
      }

      const speedMultiplier = state.keys.ShiftLeft || state.keys.ShiftRight
        ? state.fpsSprintMultiplier
        : 1;
      const moveSpeed = state.fpsMoveSpeed * speedMultiplier;

      if (move.lengthSq() > 0) {
        move.normalize().multiplyScalar(moveSpeed * deltaSec);
        state.camera.position.add(move);
        markUserNavigation("movement_step");
      }
    }

    async function loadTilesModule() {
      if (tilesModulePromise) {
        return tilesModulePromise;
      }
      const candidates = [
        "https://esm.sh/3d-tiles-renderer@0.4.11?deps=three@0.182.0",
        "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/3d-tiles-renderer@0.4.11/+esm",
      ];
      tilesModulePromise = (async () => {
        for (const url of candidates) {
          try {
            debugLog("tiles:module_try", { url });
            const mod = await dynamicImport(url);
            const Candidate = mod.TilesRenderer || (mod.default && mod.default.TilesRenderer) || mod.default;
            if (Candidate) {
              debugLog("tiles:module_ok", { url });
              return mod;
            }
          } catch (_error) {
            debugLog("tiles:module_fail", { url });
            // keep trying
          }
        }
        throw new Error("Could not load 3d-tiles-renderer module from CDN candidates.");
      })();
      try {
        return await tilesModulePromise;
      } catch (error) {
        tilesModulePromise = null;
        throw error;
      }
    }

    async function loadTilesPluginsModule() {
      if (tilesPluginsModulePromise) {
        return tilesPluginsModulePromise;
      }
      const candidates = [
        "https://esm.sh/3d-tiles-renderer@0.4.11/plugins?deps=three@0.182.0",
        "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/3d-tiles-renderer@0.4.11/plugins/+esm",
      ];
      tilesPluginsModulePromise = (async () => {
        for (const url of candidates) {
          try {
            debugLog("tiles:plugins_module_try", { url });
            const mod = await dynamicImport(url);
            const Candidate =
              mod.GLTFExtensionsPlugin ||
              (mod.default && mod.default.GLTFExtensionsPlugin);
            if (Candidate) {
              debugLog("tiles:plugins_module_ok", { url });
              return mod;
            }
            debugLog("tiles:plugins_module_missing_export", {
              url,
              keys: Object.keys(mod || {}),
            });
          } catch (_error) {
            debugLog("tiles:plugins_module_fail", { url });
            // keep trying
          }
        }
        return null;
      })();
      try {
        return await tilesPluginsModulePromise;
      } catch (error) {
        tilesPluginsModulePromise = null;
        throw error;
      }
    }

    async function preflightTilesetUrl(url) {
      if (!url || typeof url !== "string" || typeof fetch !== "function") {
        return {
          ok: false,
          reason: "invalid_url",
          status: 0,
        };
      }
      const cached = tilesetPreflightCache.get(url);
      if (cached && cached.expiresAt > Date.now()) {
        return cached.result;
      }
      let timer = null;
      let controller = null;
      try {
        if (typeof AbortController === "function") {
          controller = new AbortController();
          timer = setTimeout(() => {
            try {
              controller.abort();
            } catch (_error) {
              // no-op
            }
          }, 7000);
        }
        const response = await fetch(url, {
          method: "GET",
          mode: "cors",
          credentials: "omit",
          cache: "no-store",
          signal: controller ? controller.signal : undefined,
        });
        if (!response || !response.ok) {
          return {
            ok: false,
            reason: "http_error",
            status: response ? Number(response.status) || 0 : 0,
          };
        }
        try {
          const payload = await response.clone().json();
          if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object" || !payload.root) {
            const result = {
              ok: false,
              reason: "invalid_tileset_json",
              status: Number(response.status) || 200,
            };
            tilesetPreflightCache.set(url, {
              result,
              expiresAt: Date.now() + 30000,
            });
            return result;
          }
        } catch (_error) {
          const result = {
            ok: false,
            reason: "invalid_tileset_json",
            status: Number(response.status) || 200,
          };
          tilesetPreflightCache.set(url, {
            result,
            expiresAt: Date.now() + 30000,
          });
          return result;
        }
        const result = {
          ok: true,
          reason: "ok",
          status: Number(response.status) || 200,
        };
        tilesetPreflightCache.set(url, {
          result,
          expiresAt: Date.now() + 120000,
        });
        return result;
      } catch (error) {
        const result = {
          ok: false,
          reason: error && error.name === "AbortError" ? "timeout" : "fetch_exception",
          status: 0,
          message: error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error),
        };
        tilesetPreflightCache.set(url, {
          result,
          expiresAt: Date.now() + 8000,
        });
        return result;
      } finally {
        if (timer) {
          clearTimeout(timer);
        }
      }
    }

    function getWardCenter(ward) {
      if (ward && ward.centroid && Number.isFinite(ward.centroid.lng) && Number.isFinite(ward.centroid.lat)) {
        return ward.centroid;
      }
      if (ward && ward.bounds) {
        return {
          lng: (Number(ward.bounds.west) + Number(ward.bounds.east)) * 0.5,
          lat: (Number(ward.bounds.south) + Number(ward.bounds.north)) * 0.5,
        };
      }
      return TOKYO23 && TOKYO23.centroid ? TOKYO23.centroid : MINATO.centroid;
    }

    function classifyWardTier(distanceM, altitudeM, currentTier, policy) {
      const p = policy || {};
      const bPromoteM = Number.isFinite(p.bPromoteM) ? p.bPromoteM : 5000;
      const bDemoteM = Number.isFinite(p.bDemoteM) ? p.bDemoteM : 5600;
      const cPromoteM = Number.isFinite(p.cPromoteM) ? p.cPromoteM : 1800;
      const cDemoteM = Number.isFinite(p.cDemoteM) ? p.cDemoteM : 2300;
      const cAltPromoteM = Number.isFinite(p.cAltPromoteM) ? p.cAltPromoteM : 700;
      const cAltDemoteM = Number.isFinite(p.cAltDemoteM) ? p.cAltDemoteM : 850;

      if (currentTier === "C") {
        if (distanceM <= cDemoteM && altitudeM < cAltDemoteM) {
          return "C";
        }
        return distanceM <= bDemoteM ? "B" : "A";
      }

      if (currentTier === "B") {
        if (distanceM <= cPromoteM && altitudeM < cAltPromoteM) {
          return "C";
        }
        if (distanceM <= bDemoteM) {
          return "B";
        }
        return "A";
      }

      if (distanceM <= cPromoteM && altitudeM < cAltPromoteM) {
        return "C";
      }
      if (distanceM <= bPromoteM) {
        return "B";
      }
      return "A";
    }

    function tierOrder(tier) {
      if (tier === "C") {
        return 3;
      }
      if (tier === "B") {
        return 2;
      }
      return 1;
    }

    function tierErrorTarget(tier) {
      if (tier === "C") {
        return 4;
      }
      if (tier === "B") {
        return 6;
      }
      return 9;
    }

    function tierCacheBytes(tier) {
      if (tier === "C") {
        return 512 * 1024 * 1024;
      }
      if (tier === "B") {
        return 384 * 1024 * 1024;
      }
      return 256 * 1024 * 1024;
    }

    function getTierUrlCandidates(ward, _tier) {
      const urls = ward && ward.urls ? ward.urls : {};
      const preferNoTexture =
        !!LOCAL_ONLY_MODE ||
        !!(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.preferNoTextureTiles);
      const lod2 = preferNoTexture
        ? [urls.notexture, urls.texture].filter(Boolean)
        : [urls.texture, urls.notexture].filter(Boolean);
      return Array.from(new Set(lod2));
    }

    function getWardById(wardId) {
      const manifest = state.tilesManager && Array.isArray(state.tilesManager.wardManifest)
        ? state.tilesManager.wardManifest
        : [];
      for (const ward of manifest) {
        if (ward && ward.wardCode === wardId) {
          return ward;
        }
      }
      return null;
    }

    function getWardCodeAtLonLat(lng, lat) {
      const manifest = state.tilesManager && Array.isArray(state.tilesManager.wardManifest)
        ? state.tilesManager.wardManifest
        : [];
      for (const ward of manifest) {
        if (ward && ward.bounds && isWithinBounds(lng, lat, ward.bounds)) {
          return ward.wardCode || "";
        }
      }
      return "";
    }

    function buildGeoidManager() {
      if (state.geoidManager) {
        return state.geoidManager;
      }
      const manifest = GEOID_MANIFEST && typeof GEOID_MANIFEST === "object"
        ? GEOID_MANIFEST
        : {};
      const fallbackWardOffsets = manifest && manifest.fallbackWardOffsets && typeof manifest.fallbackWardOffsets === "object"
        ? { ...manifest.fallbackWardOffsets }
        : {};
      const manager = {
        datumState: "pending",
        geoidOffsetMode: "pending",
        warning: "",
        grid: null,
        fallbackWardOffsets,
        constantOffsetM: 39.0,
      };
      const grid = manifest && manifest.grid && typeof manifest.grid === "object"
        ? manifest.grid
        : null;
      const hasGrid =
        !!grid &&
        Number.isFinite(grid.width) &&
        Number.isFinite(grid.height) &&
        grid.width >= 2 &&
        grid.height >= 2 &&
        Array.isArray(grid.values) &&
        grid.values.length >= grid.width * grid.height &&
        grid.bounds &&
        Number.isFinite(grid.bounds.west) &&
        Number.isFinite(grid.bounds.south) &&
        Number.isFinite(grid.bounds.east) &&
        Number.isFinite(grid.bounds.north);

      if (hasGrid) {
        manager.grid = {
          width: Math.trunc(grid.width),
          height: Math.trunc(grid.height),
          bounds: {
            west: Number(grid.bounds.west),
            south: Number(grid.bounds.south),
            east: Number(grid.bounds.east),
            north: Number(grid.bounds.north),
          },
          values: grid.values.map((value) => (Number.isFinite(value) ? Number(value) : Number.NaN)),
        };
        manager.datumState = "ready";
        manager.geoidOffsetMode = "grid";
      } else if (Object.keys(fallbackWardOffsets).length > 0) {
        manager.datumState = "fallback";
        manager.geoidOffsetMode = "ward_table";
        manager.warning = "Geoid grid missing; using ward-level fallback offsets.";
      } else {
        manager.datumState = "fallback";
        manager.geoidOffsetMode = "constant";
        manager.warning = "Geoid grid and ward offsets missing; using constant fallback.";
      }

      state.geoidManager = manager;
      if (state.tilesManager && state.tilesManager.groundCalibration) {
        state.tilesManager.groundCalibration.datumState = manager.datumState;
      }
      if (manager.warning) {
        debugLog("terrain:geoid_warning", {
          datumState: manager.datumState,
          mode: manager.geoidOffsetMode,
          warning: manager.warning,
        });
      } else {
        debugLog("terrain:geoid_ready", {
          datumState: manager.datumState,
          mode: manager.geoidOffsetMode,
        });
      }
      return manager;
    }

    function sampleGeoidOffsetM(lng, lat, wardId) {
      if (!Number.isFinite(lng) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
        return 0;
      }
      const geoid = buildGeoidManager();
      if (!geoid) {
        return 0;
      }
      const grid = geoid.grid;
      if (grid && grid.bounds && isWithinBounds(lng, lat, grid.bounds)) {
        const width = grid.width;
        const height = grid.height;
        const spanLng = Math.max(1e-9, grid.bounds.east - grid.bounds.west);
        const spanLat = Math.max(1e-9, grid.bounds.north - grid.bounds.south);
        const gx = clamp((lng - grid.bounds.west) / spanLng, 0, 1) * (width - 1);
        const gy = clamp((lat - grid.bounds.south) / spanLat, 0, 1) * (height - 1);
        const x0 = Math.floor(gx);
        const y0 = Math.floor(gy);
        const x1 = Math.min(width - 1, x0 + 1);
        const y1 = Math.min(height - 1, y0 + 1);
        const tx = gx - x0;
        const ty = gy - y0;
        const read = (ix, iy) => {
          const value = grid.values[iy * width + ix];
          return Number.isFinite(value) ? value : Number.NaN;
        };
        const g00 = read(x0, y0);
        const g10 = read(x1, y0);
        const g01 = read(x0, y1);
        const g11 = read(x1, y1);
        const fallback =
          Number.isFinite(g00) ? g00 :
          Number.isFinite(g10) ? g10 :
          Number.isFinite(g01) ? g01 :
          Number.isFinite(g11) ? g11 :
          Number.NaN;
        if (Number.isFinite(fallback)) {
          const a = Number.isFinite(g00) ? g00 : fallback;
          const b = Number.isFinite(g10) ? g10 : a;
          const c = Number.isFinite(g01) ? g01 : a;
          const d = Number.isFinite(g11) ? g11 : b;
          const g0 = a + (b - a) * tx;
          const g1 = c + (d - c) * tx;
          return g0 + (g1 - g0) * ty;
        }
      }
      const hintWardId = wardId || getWardCodeAtLonLat(lng, lat);
      if (hintWardId && geoid.fallbackWardOffsets && Number.isFinite(geoid.fallbackWardOffsets[hintWardId])) {
        return Number(geoid.fallbackWardOffsets[hintWardId]);
      }
      return Number.isFinite(geoid.constantOffsetM) ? geoid.constantOffsetM : 0;
    }

    function getOrCreateWardSyncState(wardId) {
      const manager = state.tilesManager;
      if (!manager.syncByWard) {
        manager.syncByWard = new Map();
      }
      let sync = manager.syncByWard.get(wardId);
      if (!sync) {
        sync = {
          samples: [],
          biasM: 0,
          biasApplied: false,
          lastAttemptMs: 0,
          state: "pending",
          sampleMethods: { vertex: 0, bbox: 0 },
          residualStats: null,
          convergedAtMs: 0,
        };
        manager.syncByWard.set(wardId, sync);
      }
      return sync;
    }

    function extractLowBaseSampleFromVertices(modelScene) {
      if (!modelScene || typeof modelScene.traverse !== "function") {
        return null;
      }
      const temp = new THREE.Vector3();
      const world = new THREE.Vector3();
      const candidates = [];
      const maxCandidates = 1400;

      try {
        modelScene.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }

      modelScene.traverse((obj) => {
        if (!obj || !obj.isMesh || !obj.geometry || !obj.geometry.getAttribute) {
          return;
        }
        const position = obj.geometry.getAttribute("position");
        if (!position || !Number.isFinite(position.count) || position.count <= 0) {
          return;
        }
        const stride = Math.max(1, Math.floor(position.count / 220));
        for (let i = 0; i < position.count; i += stride) {
          if (candidates.length >= maxCandidates) {
            break;
          }
          temp.fromBufferAttribute(position, i);
          world.copy(temp).applyMatrix4(obj.matrixWorld);
          const llh = ecefToLonLat(world);
          if (!llh || !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) || !Number.isFinite(llh.lat) || !Number.isFinite(llh.altitudeM)) {
            continue;
          }
          candidates.push({
            lng: llh.lng,
            lat: llh.lat,
            alt: llh.altitudeM,
          });
        }
      });

      if (candidates.length < 24) {
        return null;
      }
      candidates.sort((a, b) => a.alt - b.alt);
      const lowCount = Math.max(12, Math.min(120, Math.floor(candidates.length * 0.14)));
      const low = candidates.slice(0, lowCount);
      const altitudes = low.map((item) => item.alt).filter((value) => Number.isFinite(value));
      if (altitudes.length <= 0) {
        return null;
      }
      const lngs = low.map((item) => item.lng).filter((value) => Number.isFinite(value));
      const lats = low.map((item) => item.lat).filter((value) => Number.isFinite(value));
      if (lngs.length <= 0 || lats.length <= 0) {
        return null;
      }
      return {
        lng: median(lngs),
        lat: median(lats),
        buildingAltM: median(altitudes),
        method: "vertex",
      };
    }

    function extractLowBaseSampleFromBoundingBox(modelScene) {
      if (!modelScene) {
        return null;
      }
      let box = null;
      try {
        box = new THREE.Box3().setFromObject(modelScene);
      } catch (_error) {
        return null;
      }
      if (!box || box.isEmpty()) {
        return null;
      }
      const corners = [
        new THREE.Vector3(box.min.x, box.min.y, box.min.z),
        new THREE.Vector3(box.min.x, box.min.y, box.max.z),
        new THREE.Vector3(box.min.x, box.max.y, box.min.z),
        new THREE.Vector3(box.min.x, box.max.y, box.max.z),
        new THREE.Vector3(box.max.x, box.min.y, box.min.z),
        new THREE.Vector3(box.max.x, box.min.y, box.max.z),
        new THREE.Vector3(box.max.x, box.max.y, box.min.z),
        new THREE.Vector3(box.max.x, box.max.y, box.max.z),
      ];
      const samples = [];
      for (const corner of corners) {
        const llh = ecefToLonLat(corner);
        if (!llh || !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) || !Number.isFinite(llh.lat) || !Number.isFinite(llh.altitudeM)) {
          continue;
        }
        samples.push({
          lng: llh.lng,
          lat: llh.lat,
          alt: llh.altitudeM,
        });
      }
      if (samples.length < 4) {
        return null;
      }
      samples.sort((a, b) => a.alt - b.alt);
      const low = samples.slice(0, Math.max(4, Math.floor(samples.length * 0.5)));
      return {
        lng: median(low.map((item) => item.lng)),
        lat: median(low.map((item) => item.lat)),
        buildingAltM: median(low.map((item) => item.alt)),
        method: "bbox",
      };
    }

    function captureWardSample(entry, modelScene) {
      if (!entry || !modelScene) {
        return;
      }
      const sync = entry.sync;
      if (!sync) {
        return;
      }
      const limit = state.tilesManager.terrainSync.sampleLimitPerWard;
      if (sync.samples.length >= limit) {
        return;
      }
      const sampled =
        extractLowBaseSampleFromVertices(modelScene) ||
        extractLowBaseSampleFromBoundingBox(modelScene);
      if (!sampled) {
        return;
      }
      if (!Number.isFinite(sampled.lng) || !Number.isFinite(sampled.lat) || !Number.isFinite(sampled.buildingAltM)) {
        return;
      }
      sync.samples.push({
        lng: sampled.lng,
        lat: sampled.lat,
        buildingAltM: sampled.buildingAltM,
      });
      const method = sampled.method === "bbox" ? "bbox" : "vertex";
      sync.sampleMethods[method] = (sync.sampleMethods[method] || 0) + 1;
    }

    function applyWardVerticalBias(entry, biasM) {
      if (!entry || !entry.renderer || !entry.renderer.group || !Number.isFinite(biasM)) {
        return false;
      }
      const center = getWardCenter(entry.ward);
      const up = lonLatToECEF(center.lng, center.lat, 0).normalize();
      entry.renderer.group.position.copy(up.multiplyScalar(biasM));
      entry.renderer.group.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      entry.biasM = biasM;
      return true;
    }

    function getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(_lng, _lat) {
      if (!state.terrainManager || !state.terrainManager.tiles || state.terrainManager.tiles.size === 0) {
        return Number.NaN;
      }
      let best = null;
      for (const tile of state.terrainManager.tiles.values()) {
        if (!tile || !tile.bounds || !tile.heights || !tile.width || !tile.height) {
          continue;
        }
        if (!isWithinBounds(_lng, _lat, tile.bounds)) {
          continue;
        }
        if (!best || tile.z > best.z) {
          best = tile;
        }
      }
      if (!best) {
        return Number.NaN;
      }
      const u = clamp((_lng - best.bounds.west) / Math.max(1e-12, best.bounds.east - best.bounds.west), 0, 1);
      const v = clamp((best.bounds.north - _lat) / Math.max(1e-12, best.bounds.north - best.bounds.south), 0, 1);
      const x = u * (best.width - 1);
      const y = v * (best.height - 1);
      const x0 = Math.floor(x);
      const y0 = Math.floor(y);
      const x1 = Math.min(best.width - 1, x0 + 1);
      const y1 = Math.min(best.height - 1, y0 + 1);
      const fx = x - x0;
      const fy = y - y0;
      const idx = (ix, iy) => iy * best.width + ix;
      const h00 = best.heights[idx(x0, y0)];
      const h10 = best.heights[idx(x1, y0)];
      const h01 = best.heights[idx(x0, y1)];
      const h11 = best.heights[idx(x1, y1)];
      if (![h00, h10, h01, h11].some((value) => Number.isFinite(value))) {
        return Number.NaN;
      }
      const a = Number.isFinite(h00) ? h00 : (Number.isFinite(h10) ? h10 : h01);
      const b = Number.isFinite(h10) ? h10 : a;
      const c = Number.isFinite(h01) ? h01 : a;
      const d = Number.isFinite(h11) ? h11 : b;
      const h0 = a + (b - a) * fx;
      const h1 = c + (d - c) * fx;
      const orthometricHeightM = h0 + (h1 - h0) * fy;
      const wardId = best && best.wardId ? best.wardId : "";
      const geoidOffsetM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(_lng, _lat, wardId);
      return orthometricHeightM + geoidOffsetM;
    }

    function updateGroundCalibrationAggregate() {
      const manager = state.tilesManager;
      if (!manager || !manager.syncByWard || !manager.groundCalibration) {
        return;
      }
      const geoid = buildGeoidManager();
      if (geoid && geoid.datumState) {
        manager.groundCalibration.datumState = geoid.datumState;
      }
      const residuals = [];
      let converged = 0;
      let insufficient = 0;
      for (const sync of manager.syncByWard.values()) {
        if (!sync) {
          continue;
        }
        if (sync.state === "converged" && sync.residualStats) {
          converged += 1;
        } else if (sync.state === "insufficient_samples") {
          insufficient += 1;
        }
        if (Array.isArray(sync.lastResidualAbs)) {
          for (const value of sync.lastResidualAbs) {
            if (Number.isFinite(value)) {
              residuals.push(value);
            }
          }
        }
      }
      if (residuals.length > 0) {
        residuals.sort((a, b) => a - b);
        manager.groundCalibration.gapStats = {
          medianAbsM: median(residuals),
          p95AbsM: quantile(residuals, 0.95),
          maxAbsM: residuals[residuals.length - 1],
          sampleCount: residuals.length,
        };
      } else {
        manager.groundCalibration.gapStats = {
          medianAbsM: Number.NaN,
          p95AbsM: Number.NaN,
          maxAbsM: Number.NaN,
          sampleCount: 0,
        };
      }

      const totalWards = Array.isArray(manager.wardManifest) ? manager.wardManifest.length : 0;
      if (converged > 0) {
        manager.groundCalibration.residualBiasState = "converged";
      } else if (insufficient >= Math.max(1, Math.floor(totalWards * 0.3))) {
        manager.groundCalibration.residualBiasState = "insufficient_samples";
      } else {
        manager.groundCalibration.residualBiasState = "pending";
      }
    }

    function attemptWardTerrainSync(entry) {
      if (!entry || !entry.sync || entry.sync.state === "converged") {
        return;
      }
      if (!state.terrainManager || !state.terrainManager.ready) {
        return;
      }
      const geoid = buildGeoidManager();
      if (!geoid || (geoid.datumState !== "ready" && geoid.datumState !== "fallback")) {
        return;
      }
      const now = Date.now();
      const minRetryIntervalMs = Number(state.tilesManager.terrainSync.minRetryIntervalMs) || 1200;
      if (entry.sync.lastAttemptMs && now - entry.sync.lastAttemptMs < minRetryIntervalMs) {
        return;
      }
      entry.sync.lastAttemptMs = now;
      if (!Array.isArray(entry.sync.samples) || entry.sync.samples.length < state.tilesManager.terrainSync.minSamplesForBias) {
        if (entry.sync.samples && entry.sync.samples.length >= Math.max(4, Math.floor(state.tilesManager.terrainSync.minSamplesForBias * 0.5))) {
          entry.sync.state = "pending";
        } else {
          entry.sync.state = "insufficient_samples";
        }
        updateGroundCalibrationAggregate();
        return;
      }
      const deltas = [];
      for (const sample of entry.sync.samples) {
        const terrainH = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(sample.lng, sample.lat);
        if (!Number.isFinite(terrainH) || !Number.isFinite(sample.buildingAltM)) {
          continue;
        }
        const delta = terrainH - sample.buildingAltM;
        if (Math.abs(delta) <= state.tilesManager.terrainSync.maxAbsDeltaM) {
          deltas.push(delta);
        }
      }
      if (deltas.length < state.tilesManager.terrainSync.minSamplesForBias) {
        entry.sync.state = "insufficient_samples";
        updateGroundCalibrationAggregate();
        return;
      }
      deltas.sort((a, b) => a - b);
      const trimRatio = clamp(
        Number.isFinite(state.tilesManager.terrainSync.trimRatio)
          ? state.tilesManager.terrainSync.trimRatio
          : 0.12,
        0,
        0.35
      );
      const trimCount = Math.floor(deltas.length * trimRatio);
      const trimSafe = trimCount > 0 && deltas.length > (trimCount * 2 + 2)
        ? trimCount
        : 0;
      const trimmed = trimSafe > 0 ? deltas.slice(trimSafe, deltas.length - trimSafe) : deltas.slice();
      const wardBias = median(trimmed);
      if (!Number.isFinite(wardBias)) {
        entry.sync.state = "insufficient_samples";
        updateGroundCalibrationAggregate();
        return;
      }
      if (Math.abs(wardBias) > state.tilesManager.terrainSync.maxBiasMagnitudeM) {
        entry.sync.state = "insufficient_samples";
        debugLog("terrain:ward_bias_rejected", {
          wardCode: entry.wardId,
          wardName: entry.wardName,
          biasM: Number(wardBias.toFixed(2)),
          limitM: Number(state.tilesManager.terrainSync.maxBiasMagnitudeM),
        });
        updateGroundCalibrationAggregate();
        return;
      }
      if (applyWardVerticalBias(entry, wardBias)) {
        entry.sync.biasM = wardBias;
        entry.sync.biasApplied = true;
        entry.sync.state = "converged";
        entry.sync.convergedAtMs = now;
        const residualAbs = trimmed
          .map((delta) => Math.abs(delta - wardBias))
          .filter((value) => Number.isFinite(value));
        entry.sync.lastResidualAbs = residualAbs;
        entry.sync.residualStats = residualAbs.length > 0
          ? {
              medianAbsM: median(residualAbs),
              p95AbsM: quantile(residualAbs, 0.95),
              maxAbsM: Math.max(...residualAbs),
              sampleCount: residualAbs.length,
            }
          : null;
        updateGroundCalibrationAggregate();
        debugLog("terrain:ward_bias_applied", {
          wardCode: entry.wardId,
          wardName: entry.wardName,
          biasM: Number(wardBias.toFixed(2)),
          sampleCount: trimmed.length,
          residualMedianAbsM:
            entry.sync.residualStats && Number.isFinite(entry.sync.residualStats.medianAbsM)
              ? Number(entry.sync.residualStats.medianAbsM.toFixed(3))
              : null,
          residualP95AbsM:
            entry.sync.residualStats && Number.isFinite(entry.sync.residualStats.p95AbsM)
              ? Number(entry.sync.residualStats.p95AbsM.toFixed(3))
              : null,
        });
      }
    }

    function disposeWardEntry(entry, reason) {
      if (!entry) {
        return;
      }
      try {
        if (entry.renderer && entry.renderer.group && entry.renderer.group.parent) {
          entry.renderer.group.parent.remove(entry.renderer.group);
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      try {
        if (entry.renderer && typeof entry.renderer.dispose === "function") {
          entry.renderer.dispose();
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      debugLog("tiles:ward_disposed", {
        wardCode: entry.wardId,
        tier: entry.tier,
        reason: reason || "dispose",
      });
    }

    function clearTokyoTilesManager() {
      const manager = state.tilesManager;
      if (!manager || !manager.wards) {
        return;
      }
      for (const entry of manager.wards.values()) {
        disposeWardEntry(entry, "manager_reset");
      }
      manager.wards.clear();
      manager.activeWardIds = new Set();
      manager.loadingWardIds = new Set();
      manager.desiredWardIds = new Set();
      manager.tierDistribution = { A: 0, B: 0, C: 0 };
      manager.statsAggregate = {};
      if (manager.syncByWard) {
        manager.syncByWard.clear();
      }
      if (manager.groundCalibration) {
        manager.groundCalibration.residualBiasState = "pending";
        manager.groundCalibration.gapStats = {
          medianAbsM: Number.NaN,
          p95AbsM: Number.NaN,
          maxAbsM: Number.NaN,
          sampleCount: 0,
        };
      }
    }

    async function createWardRenderer(ward, desiredTier) {
      const tilesMod = await loadTilesModule();
      const TilesRendererClass =
        tilesMod.TilesRenderer ||
        (tilesMod.default && tilesMod.default.TilesRenderer) ||
        tilesMod.default;
      if (!TilesRendererClass) {
        throw new Error("TilesRenderer class missing.");
      }
      const pluginsMod = await loadTilesPluginsModule();
      const GLTFExtensionsPluginClass =
        pluginsMod &&
        (pluginsMod.GLTFExtensionsPlugin ||
          (pluginsMod.default && pluginsMod.default.GLTFExtensionsPlugin));
      if (!GLTFExtensionsPluginClass) {
        throw new Error("GLTFExtensionsPlugin missing; CESIUM_RTC support is required.");
      }
      const candidateUrls = getTierUrlCandidates(ward, desiredTier);
      const failures = [];
      for (const url of candidateUrls) {
        const preflight = await preflightTilesetUrl(url);
        if (!preflight.ok) {
          failures.push(url + ":" + String(preflight.reason || "preflight_fail"));
          continue;
        }
        try {
          const tiles = new TilesRendererClass(url);
          tiles.setCamera(state.camera);
          tiles.setResolutionFromRenderer(state.camera, state.renderer);
          tiles.registerPlugin(new GLTFExtensionsPluginClass({
            rtc: true,
            metadata: false,
          }));
          const tier = desiredTier || "A";
          tiles.errorTarget = tierErrorTarget(tier);
          tiles.maxDepth = tier === "C" ? 22 : (tier === "B" ? 20 : 18);
          if ("displayActiveTiles" in tiles) {
            tiles.displayActiveTiles = true;
          }
          if ("loadSiblings" in tiles) {
            tiles.loadSiblings = true;
          }
          if ("autoDisableRendererCulling" in tiles) {
            tiles.autoDisableRendererCulling = false;
          }
          if (tiles.lruCache) {
            if (Number.isFinite(tiles.lruCache.maxBytesSize)) {
              tiles.lruCache.maxBytesSize = tierCacheBytes(tier);
            }
            if (Number.isFinite(tiles.lruCache.maxSize)) {
              tiles.lruCache.maxSize = tier === "C" ? 2200 : (tier === "B" ? 1600 : 1200);
            }
          }
          state.scene.add(tiles.group);
          return {
            renderer: tiles,
            url,
            tier,
          };
        } catch (error) {
          failures.push(url + ":" + (error && error.message ? error.message : String(error)));
        }
      }
      throw new Error("Ward tileset load failed (" + ward.wardCode + "): " + failures.join(" | "));
    }

    async function ensureWardRenderer(ward, desiredTier, nowMs) {
      const manager = state.tilesManager;
      const wardId = ward.wardCode || ward.slug || ward.wardName || "ward";
      let entry = manager.wards.get(wardId) || null;
      if (entry && entry.tier === desiredTier && entry.renderer) {
        entry.lastWantedMs = nowMs;
        return entry;
      }
      if (entry && entry.renderer && entry.tier !== desiredTier) {
        const desiredCandidates = getTierUrlCandidates(ward, desiredTier);
        if (entry.url && desiredCandidates.includes(entry.url)) {
          const prevTier = entry.tier;
          entry.tier = desiredTier;
          entry.lastTierChangeMs = nowMs;
          entry.lastWantedMs = nowMs;
          debugLog("tiles:ward_tier_relabel", {
            wardCode: wardId,
            fromTier: prevTier,
            toTier: desiredTier,
            url: entry.url,
          });
          return entry;
        }
        const lastTierChangeMs = Number.isFinite(entry.lastTierChangeMs) ? entry.lastTierChangeMs : 0;
        const isPromotion = tierOrder(desiredTier) > tierOrder(entry.tier);
        const cooldownMs = isPromotion
          ? Math.max(2000, Math.floor((manager.tierSwitchCooldownMs || 7000) * 0.5))
          : (manager.tierSwitchCooldownMs || 7000);
        if (nowMs - lastTierChangeMs < cooldownMs) {
          entry.lastWantedMs = nowMs;
          return entry;
        }
      }
      if (manager.loadingWardIds.has(wardId)) {
        return entry;
      }
      manager.loadingWardIds.add(wardId);
      try {
        const next = await createWardRenderer(ward, desiredTier);
        manager.rtcPluginReady = true;
        const sync = getOrCreateWardSyncState(wardId);
        const nextEntry = {
          wardId,
          wardName: ward.wardName || wardId,
          ward,
          tier: next.tier,
          url: next.url,
          renderer: next.renderer,
          stats: {},
          knownTiles: 0,
          loadedModels: 0,
          failedModels: 0,
          seenModelIds: new Set(),
          lastWantedMs: nowMs,
          lastUsedMs: nowMs,
          sync,
          biasM: sync.biasApplied ? sync.biasM : 0,
          lastTierChangeMs: nowMs,
        };
        if (sync.biasApplied && Number.isFinite(sync.biasM)) {
          applyWardVerticalBias(nextEntry, sync.biasM);
        }
        if (entry && entry.renderer) {
          disposeWardEntry(entry, "tier_switch");
        }
        const registerEvent = (eventName, handler) => {
          try {
            nextEntry.renderer.addEventListener(eventName, handler);
          } catch (_error) {
            // no-op
          }
        };
        registerEvent("load-tile-set", (event) => {
          const root = extractTilesRoot(nextEntry.renderer, event);
          const count = countTilesInTree(root);
          if (count > 0) {
            nextEntry.knownTiles = Math.max(nextEntry.knownTiles, count);
          }
        });
        const onModelLoaded = (event) => {
          const modelScene =
            (event && (event.scene || event.model || event.modelScene || event.content || event.group)) ||
            null;
          if (!modelScene) {
            return;
          }
          applyCesiumRtcOffset(modelScene);
          prepareLoadedModelScene(modelScene);
          const key = modelScene.uuid ? String(modelScene.uuid) : "m_" + String(nextEntry.loadedModels + 1);
          if (nextEntry.seenModelIds.has(key)) {
            return;
          }
          nextEntry.seenModelIds.add(key);
          nextEntry.loadedModels += 1;
          captureWardSample(nextEntry, modelScene);
        };
        registerEvent("load-model", onModelLoaded);
        registerEvent("loadModel", onModelLoaded);
        const onLoadError = () => {
          nextEntry.failedModels += 1;
        };
        registerEvent("load-error", onLoadError);
        registerEvent("loadError", onLoadError);
        registerEvent("error", onLoadError);
        nextEntry.renderer.onLoadModel = (sceneModel) => {
          if (!sceneModel) {
            return;
          }
          applyCesiumRtcOffset(sceneModel);
          prepareLoadedModelScene(sceneModel);
          const key = sceneModel.uuid ? String(sceneModel.uuid) : "cb_" + String(nextEntry.loadedModels + 1);
          if (nextEntry.seenModelIds.has(key)) {
            return;
          }
          nextEntry.seenModelIds.add(key);
          nextEntry.loadedModels += 1;
          captureWardSample(nextEntry, sceneModel);
        };
        manager.wards.set(wardId, nextEntry);
        debugLog("tiles:ward_loaded", {
          wardCode: wardId,
          wardName: nextEntry.wardName,
          tier: nextEntry.tier,
          url: nextEntry.url,
        });
        return nextEntry;
      } catch (error) {
        const message = error && error.message ? error.message : String(error);
        manager.warnings.push("ward " + wardId + ": " + message);
        setStatus("Ward tileset unavailable: " + wardId + " (" + message + ")", "error");
        debugLog("tiles:ward_load_failed", {
          wardCode: wardId,
          tier: desiredTier,
          message,
        });
      } finally {
        manager.loadingWardIds.delete(wardId);
      }
      return null;
    }

    function computeTilesManagerStats() {
      const manager = state.tilesManager;
      const out = {
        inFrustum: 0,
        used: 0,
        active: 0,
        visible: 0,
        downloading: 0,
        parsing: 0,
        failed: 0,
        cached: 0,
      };
      for (const entry of manager.wards.values()) {
        if (!entry || !entry.renderer || !entry.renderer.stats) {
          continue;
        }
        const stats = entry.renderer.stats;
        for (const key of Object.keys(out)) {
          if (Number.isFinite(stats[key])) {
            out[key] += stats[key];
          }
        }
      }
      manager.statsAggregate = out;
      return out;
    }

    function shouldActivateWard(cameraLLH, ward, wardCenter, distanceM) {
      if (!cameraLLH || !wardCenter) {
        return false;
      }
      if (ward && ward.bounds && isWithinBounds(cameraLLH.lng, cameraLLH.lat, ward.bounds)) {
        return true;
      }
      if (!isWithinBounds(cameraLLH.lng, cameraLLH.lat, TOKYO23 && TOKYO23.bounds ? TOKYO23.bounds : null)) {
        return distanceM <= 20000;
      }
      return distanceM <= 26000;
    }

    function scheduleTokyoWardActivation(nowMs) {
      const manager = state.tilesManager;
      if (!manager || !manager.enabled || !state.camera) {
        return;
      }
      if (nowMs - manager.lastActivationTickMs < (manager.activationIntervalMs || 850)) {
        return;
      }
      manager.lastActivationTickMs = nowMs;
      const cameraLLH = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
      if (!cameraLLH || !Number.isFinite(cameraLLH.lng) || !Number.isFinite(cameraLLH.lat)) {
        return;
      }
      const altitudeM = Number.isFinite(cameraLLH.altitudeM) ? cameraLLH.altitudeM : 1200;
      const ranked = [];
      for (const ward of manager.wardManifest) {
        const wardId = ward && ward.wardCode ? ward.wardCode : "";
        const existing = wardId ? manager.wards.get(wardId) : null;
        const center = getWardCenter(ward);
        const distanceM = haversineDistanceM(cameraLLH.lng, cameraLLH.lat, center.lng, center.lat);
        if (!shouldActivateWard(cameraLLH, ward, center, distanceM)) {
          continue;
        }
        const stickyBonusM = existing && existing.renderer ? 900 : 0;
        ranked.push({
          ward,
          center,
          distanceM,
          sortDistanceM: Math.max(0, distanceM - stickyBonusM),
          tier: classifyWardTier(
            distanceM,
            altitudeM,
            existing && existing.tier ? existing.tier : "A",
            manager.tierPolicy
          ),
        });
      }
      ranked.sort((a, b) => a.sortDistanceM - b.sortDistanceM);
      const selected = ranked.slice(0, manager.maxActiveWards);
      const desiredIds = new Set(selected.map((item) => item.ward.wardCode));
      manager.desiredWardIds = desiredIds;
      manager.tierDistribution = { A: 0, B: 0, C: 0 };
      for (const item of selected) {
        manager.tierDistribution[item.tier] += 1;
        ensureWardRenderer(item.ward, item.tier, nowMs).catch((error) => {
          debugLog("tiles:ward_async_error", {
            wardCode: item.ward && item.ward.wardCode ? item.ward.wardCode : "unknown",
            message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
          });
        });
      }
      for (const [wardId, entry] of manager.wards.entries()) {
        if (desiredIds.has(wardId)) {
          entry.lastWantedMs = nowMs;
          continue;
        }
        if (nowMs - (entry.lastWantedMs || 0) >= manager.hysteresisMs) {
          disposeWardEntry(entry, "outside_hysteresis");
          manager.wards.delete(wardId);
        }
      }
    }

    function updateTokyoTilesManager(nowMs) {
      const manager = state.tilesManager;
      if (!manager || !manager.enabled) {
        return;
      }
      scheduleTokyoWardActivation(nowMs);
      manager.activeWardIds = new Set();
      for (const [wardId, entry] of manager.wards.entries()) {
        if (!entry || !entry.renderer) {
          continue;
        }
        manager.activeWardIds.add(wardId);
        entry.lastUsedMs = nowMs;
        entry.renderer.errorTarget = tierErrorTarget(entry.tier);
        entry.renderer.setCamera(state.camera);
        entry.renderer.setResolutionFromRenderer(state.camera, state.renderer);
        entry.renderer.update();
        attemptWardTerrainSync(entry);
      }
      computeTilesManagerStats();
    }

    function lonLatToSlippy(lon, lat, zoom) {
      const z2 = Math.pow(2, zoom);
      const x = Math.floor((lon + 180) / 360 * z2);
      const latR = toRad(lat);
      const y = Math.floor(
        (1 - Math.log(Math.tan(latR) + 1 / Math.cos(latR)) / Math.PI) * 0.5 * z2
      );
      return { x, y };
    }

    function slippyBounds(x, y, zoom) {
      const z2 = Math.pow(2, zoom);
      const west = x / z2 * 360 - 180;
      const east = (x + 1) / z2 * 360 - 180;
      const n = Math.PI - 2 * Math.PI * y / z2;
      const s = Math.PI - 2 * Math.PI * (y + 1) / z2;
      const north = toDeg(Math.atan(Math.sinh(n)));
      const south = toDeg(Math.atan(Math.sinh(s)));
      return { west, south, east, north };
    }

    function chooseTerrainZoom(altitudeM, currentZoom) {
      const range = TERRAIN_CONFIG.zoomRange || { min: 11, max: 14 };
      const minZoom = clamp(range.min, range.min, range.max);
      const maxZoom = clamp(range.max, minZoom, 24);
      if (maxZoom <= minZoom) {
        return maxZoom;
      }
      const alt = Number.isFinite(altitudeM) ? altitudeM : 1200;
      let target = maxZoom;
      if (alt > 2400) {
        target = minZoom;
      } else if (alt > 1200) {
        target = clamp(minZoom + 1, minZoom, maxZoom);
      } else if (alt > 550) {
        target = clamp(maxZoom - 1, minZoom, maxZoom);
      } else {
        target = maxZoom;
      }

      if (!Number.isFinite(currentZoom)) {
        return target;
      }
      if (currentZoom === maxZoom) {
        return alt <= 850 ? maxZoom : clamp(maxZoom - 1, minZoom, maxZoom);
      }
      if (currentZoom === maxZoom - 1) {
        if (alt < 500) {
          return maxZoom;
        }
        if (alt <= 2200) {
          return maxZoom - 1;
        }
        return clamp(maxZoom - 2, minZoom, maxZoom);
      }
      if (currentZoom === minZoom) {
        return alt < 2200 ? clamp(minZoom + 1, minZoom, maxZoom) : minZoom;
      }
      if (currentZoom > minZoom && currentZoom < maxZoom - 1) {
        if (alt < 1000) {
          return clamp(currentZoom + 1, minZoom, maxZoom);
        }
        if (alt > 3200) {
          return clamp(currentZoom - 1, minZoom, maxZoom);
        }
        return currentZoom;
      }
      return target;
    }

    function buildTerrainManager() {
      if (state.terrainManager) {
        return state.terrainManager;
      }
      const geoid = buildGeoidManager();
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.name = "terrainGroup";
      state.scene.add(group);
      state.terrainManager = {
        group,
        tiles: new Map(),
        pending: new Set(),
        desired: new Set(),
        lastTickMs: 0,
        currentZoom: null,
        lastZoomChangeMs: 0,
        zoomSwitchHoldMs: 6000,
        evictionHoldMs: 12000,
        loaded: 0,
        failed: 0,
        ready: false,
        warning: "",
        datumState: geoid ? geoid.datumState : "pending",
        geoidOffsetMode: geoid ? geoid.geoidOffsetMode : "pending",
      };
      if (state.tilesManager && state.tilesManager.groundCalibration) {
        state.tilesManager.groundCalibration.datumState = state.terrainManager.datumState;
      }
      return state.terrainManager;
    }

    async function readImageDataFromBlob(blob) {
      if (!blob) {
        throw new Error("missing_blob");
      }
      if (typeof createImageBitmap === "function") {
        const bitmap = await createImageBitmap(blob);
        const canvas = document.createElement("canvas");
        canvas.width = bitmap.width;
        canvas.height = bitmap.height;
        const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d", { willReadFrequently: true });
        if (!ctx) {
          throw new Error("canvas_context_unavailable");
        }
        ctx.drawImage(bitmap, 0, 0);
        const imageData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
        bitmap.close();
        return imageData;
      }
      const image = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        const img = new Image();
        img.crossOrigin = "anonymous";
        img.onload = () => {
          URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
          resolve(img);
        };
        img.onerror = (error) => {
          URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
          reject(error || new Error("image_decode_failed"));
        };
        img.src = url;
      });
      const canvas = document.createElement("canvas");
      canvas.width = image.width;
      canvas.height = image.height;
      const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d", { willReadFrequently: true });
      if (!ctx) {
        throw new Error("canvas_context_unavailable");
      }
      ctx.drawImage(image, 0, 0);
      return ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
    }

    function decodeGsiDem(imageData) {
      const width = imageData.width;
      const height = imageData.height;
      const data = imageData.data;
      const heights = new Float32Array(width * height);
      let finiteCount = 0;
      for (let i = 0; i < width * height; i += 1) {
        const r = data[i * 4];
        const g = data[i * 4 + 1];
        const b = data[i * 4 + 2];
        const v = r * 65536 + g * 256 + b;
        let h = Number.NaN;
        if (v !== 8388608) {
          if (v < 8388608) {
            h = v * 0.01;
          } else {
            h = (v - 16777216) * 0.01;
          }
        }
        heights[i] = Number.isFinite(h) ? h : Number.NaN;
        if (Number.isFinite(heights[i])) {
          finiteCount += 1;
        }
      }
      return {
        width,
        height,
        heights,
        finiteCount,
      };
    }

    function sampleTerrainGridHeight(decoded, u, v) {
      if (!decoded || !decoded.heights || !decoded.width || !decoded.height) {
        return 0;
      }
      const x = clamp(u, 0, 1) * (decoded.width - 1);
      const y = clamp(v, 0, 1) * (decoded.height - 1);
      const x0 = Math.floor(x);
      const y0 = Math.floor(y);
      const x1 = Math.min(decoded.width - 1, x0 + 1);
      const y1 = Math.min(decoded.height - 1, y0 + 1);
      const fx = x - x0;
      const fy = y - y0;
      const idx = (ix, iy) => iy * decoded.width + ix;
      const h00 = decoded.heights[idx(x0, y0)];
      const h10 = decoded.heights[idx(x1, y0)];
      const h01 = decoded.heights[idx(x0, y1)];
      const h11 = decoded.heights[idx(x1, y1)];
      if (![h00, h10, h01, h11].some((val) => Number.isFinite(val))) {
        return 0;
      }
      const a = Number.isFinite(h00) ? h00 : 0;
      const b = Number.isFinite(h10) ? h10 : a;
      const c = Number.isFinite(h01) ? h01 : a;
      const d = Number.isFinite(h11) ? h11 : b;
      const h0 = a + (b - a) * fx;
      const h1 = c + (d - c) * fx;
      return h0 + (h1 - h0) * fy;
    }

    function appendTerrainSkirts(geometry, positions, indices, centerECEF, gridSize) {
      const lowerByM = Number.isFinite(Number(TERRAIN_CONFIG && TERRAIN_CONFIG.skirtDepthM))
        ? Math.max(8, Number(TERRAIN_CONFIG.skirtDepthM))
        : 42;
      const borderIndices = [];
      for (let x = 0; x < gridSize; x += 1) {
        borderIndices.push(x);
      }
      for (let y = 1; y < gridSize - 1; y += 1) {
        borderIndices.push(y * gridSize + (gridSize - 1));
      }
      for (let x = gridSize - 1; x >= 0; x -= 1) {
        borderIndices.push((gridSize - 1) * gridSize + x);
      }
      for (let y = gridSize - 2; y >= 1; y -= 1) {
        borderIndices.push(y * gridSize);
      }
      const skirtOffsetStart = positions.length / 3;
      for (const idx of borderIndices) {
        const vx = positions[idx * 3];
        const vy = positions[idx * 3 + 1];
        const vz = positions[idx * 3 + 2];
        const world = new THREE.Vector3(vx + centerECEF.x, vy + centerECEF.y, vz + centerECEF.z);
        const radial = world.clone().normalize().multiplyScalar(lowerByM);
        const lowered = world.sub(radial);
        positions.push(lowered.x - centerECEF.x, lowered.y - centerECEF.y, lowered.z - centerECEF.z);
      }
      const count = borderIndices.length;
      for (let i = 0; i < count; i += 1) {
        const iNext = (i + 1) % count;
        const topA = borderIndices[i];
        const topB = borderIndices[iNext];
        const botA = skirtOffsetStart + i;
        const botB = skirtOffsetStart + iNext;
        indices.push(topA, topB, botA);
        indices.push(topB, botB, botA);
      }
      geometry.setAttribute("position", new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(positions, 3));
      geometry.setIndex(indices);
    }

    function applyTerrainRadialNormals(geometry, centerECEF) {
      if (!geometry || !centerECEF) {
        return;
      }
      const positionAttr = geometry.getAttribute("position");
      if (!positionAttr || !Number.isFinite(positionAttr.count) || positionAttr.count <= 0) {
        return;
      }
      const normals = new Float32Array(positionAttr.count * 3);
      for (let i = 0; i < positionAttr.count; i += 1) {
        const lx = Number(positionAttr.getX(i)) || 0;
        const ly = Number(positionAttr.getY(i)) || 0;
        const lz = Number(positionAttr.getZ(i)) || 0;
        const wx = lx + centerECEF.x;
        const wy = ly + centerECEF.y;
        const wz = lz + centerECEF.z;
        const len = Math.sqrt(wx * wx + wy * wy + wz * wz) || 1;
        normals[i * 3] = wx / len;
        normals[i * 3 + 1] = wy / len;
        normals[i * 3 + 2] = wz / len;
      }
      geometry.setAttribute("normal", new THREE.BufferAttribute(normals, 3));
    }

    function buildTerrainMeshFromDecoded(tile, decoded) {
      const zoom = tile.z;
      const nearRes = Number(TERRAIN_CONFIG.gridResolutionNear) || 65;
      const farRes = Number(TERRAIN_CONFIG.gridResolutionFar) || 33;
      const segments = zoom >= ((TERRAIN_CONFIG.zoomRange && TERRAIN_CONFIG.zoomRange.max) || 14) ? nearRes - 1 : farRes - 1;
      const gridSize = segments + 1;
      const bounds = tile.bounds;
      const centerLon = (bounds.west + bounds.east) * 0.5;
      const centerLat = (bounds.south + bounds.north) * 0.5;
      const centerECEF = lonLatToECEF(centerLon, centerLat, 0);
      const positions = [];
      const indices = [];
      for (let gy = 0; gy < gridSize; gy += 1) {
        const v = gy / segments;
        const lat = bounds.north + (bounds.south - bounds.north) * v;
        for (let gx = 0; gx < gridSize; gx += 1) {
          const u = gx / segments;
          const lon = bounds.west + (bounds.east - bounds.west) * u;
          const orthometricHeightM = sampleTerrainGridHeight(decoded, u, v);
          const geoidOffsetM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
          const heightM = orthometricHeightM + geoidOffsetM;
          const ecef = lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM);
          positions.push(
            ecef.x - centerECEF.x,
            ecef.y - centerECEF.y,
            ecef.z - centerECEF.z
          );
        }
      }
      for (let gy = 0; gy < segments; gy += 1) {
        for (let gx = 0; gx < segments; gx += 1) {
          const i0 = gy * gridSize + gx;
          const i1 = i0 + 1;
          const i2 = i0 + gridSize;
          const i3 = i2 + 1;
          indices.push(i0, i2, i1);
          indices.push(i1, i2, i3);
        }
      }
      const geometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
      appendTerrainSkirts(geometry, positions, indices, centerECEF, gridSize);
      applyTerrainRadialNormals(geometry, centerECEF);
      const material = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
        color: 0xdbe2ea,
        roughness: 1,
        metalness: 0,
        polygonOffset: true,
        polygonOffsetFactor: 2,
        polygonOffsetUnits: 2,
      });
      material.depthTest = true;
      material.depthWrite = true;
      const mesh = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, material);
      mesh.position.copy(centerECEF);
      mesh.frustumCulled = true;
      mesh.renderOrder = 2;
      return {
        mesh,
        centerECEF,
      };
    }

    function buildTerrainFlatFallbackMesh(tile) {
      const decoded = {
        width: 2,
        height: 2,
        heights: [0, 0, 0, 0],
        finiteCount: 4,
      };
      return buildTerrainMeshFromDecoded(tile, decoded);
    }

    async function loadTerrainTile(zoom, x, y) {
      const manager = buildTerrainManager();
      const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      if (manager.pending.has(key) || manager.tiles.has(key)) {
        return;
      }
      manager.pending.add(key);
      const priorities = Array.isArray(TERRAIN_CONFIG.sourcePriority)
        ? TERRAIN_CONFIG.sourcePriority
        : ["dem5a_png", "dem5b_png", "dem_png"];
      try {
        const bounds = slippyBounds(x, y, zoom);
        const failures = [];
        for (const source of priorities) {
          const url =
            "https://cyberjapandata.gsi.go.jp/xyz/" +
            String(source) +
            "/" +
            String(zoom) +
            "/" +
            String(x) +
            "/" +
            String(y) +
            ".png";
          try {
            const response = await fetch(url, {
              method: "GET",
              mode: "cors",
              credentials: "omit",
              cache: "force-cache",
            });
            if (!response || !response.ok) {
              failures.push(source + ":" + String(response ? response.status : 0));
              continue;
            }
            const blob = await response.blob();
            const imageData = await readImageDataFromBlob(blob);
            const decoded = decodeGsiDem(imageData);
            if (!decoded || decoded.finiteCount <= 0) {
              failures.push(source + ":empty");
              continue;
            }
            const built = buildTerrainMeshFromDecoded({ z: zoom, x, y, bounds }, decoded);
            const centerLng = (bounds.west + bounds.east) * 0.5;
            const centerLat = (bounds.south + bounds.north) * 0.5;
            const tile = {
              key,
              z: zoom,
              x,
              y,
              bounds,
              wardId: getWardCodeAtLonLat(centerLng, centerLat),
              source,
              width: decoded.width,
              height: decoded.height,
              heights: decoded.heights,
              mesh: built.mesh,
              lastWantedMs: Date.now(),
            };
            manager.group.add(tile.mesh);
            manager.tiles.set(key, tile);
            manager.loaded += 1;
            manager.ready = true;
            debugLog("terrain:tile_loaded", {
              key,
              source,
              finiteCount: decoded.finiteCount,
            });
            return;
          } catch (error) {
            failures.push(source + ":" + (error && error.message ? error.message : String(error)));
          }
        }
        if (!(TERRAIN_CONFIG && TERRAIN_CONFIG.fallbackFlatTileOnFailure === false)) {
          try {
            const builtFallback = buildTerrainFlatFallbackMesh({ z: zoom, x, y, bounds });
            const centerLng = (bounds.west + bounds.east) * 0.5;
            const centerLat = (bounds.south + bounds.north) * 0.5;
            const tile = {
              key,
              z: zoom,
              x,
              y,
              bounds,
              wardId: getWardCodeAtLonLat(centerLng, centerLat),
              source: "fallback_flat",
              width: 2,
              height: 2,
              heights: [0, 0, 0, 0],
              mesh: builtFallback.mesh,
              lastWantedMs: Date.now(),
            };
            manager.group.add(tile.mesh);
            manager.tiles.set(key, tile);
            manager.loaded += 1;
            manager.ready = true;
            manager.warning = "Terrain DEM fallback active.";
            debugLog("terrain:tile_loaded", {
              key,
              source: "fallback_flat",
              finiteCount: 4,
              failures,
            });
            return;
          } catch (fallbackError) {
            failures.push("fallback_flat:" + (fallbackError && fallbackError.message ? fallbackError.message : String(fallbackError)));
          }
        }
        manager.failed += 1;
        manager.warning = "Terrain tile failed: " + key;
        debugLog("terrain:tile_failed", {
          key,
          failures,
        });
      } finally {
        manager.pending.delete(key);
      }
    }

    function evictTerrainTile(tile, reason) {
      const manager = state.terrainManager;
      if (!manager || !tile) {
        return;
      }
      try {
        if (tile.mesh && tile.mesh.parent) {
          tile.mesh.parent.remove(tile.mesh);
        }
        if (tile.mesh && tile.mesh.geometry) {
          tile.mesh.geometry.dispose();
        }
        if (tile.mesh && tile.mesh.material && typeof tile.mesh.material.dispose === "function") {
          tile.mesh.material.dispose();
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      manager.tiles.delete(tile.key);
      debugLog("terrain:tile_evicted", {
        key: tile.key,
        reason: reason || "evict",
      });
    }

    function clearTerrainManager() {
      const manager = state.terrainManager;
      if (!manager) {
        return;
      }
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        evictTerrainTile(tile, "terrain_reset");
      }
      manager.tiles.clear();
      manager.pending.clear();
      manager.desired.clear();
      manager.currentZoom = null;
      manager.lastZoomChangeMs = 0;
      manager.loaded = 0;
      manager.failed = 0;
      manager.ready = false;
      manager.warning = "";
      const geoid = buildGeoidManager();
      manager.datumState = geoid ? geoid.datumState : "pending";
      manager.geoidOffsetMode = geoid ? geoid.geoidOffsetMode : "pending";
    }

    function scheduleTerrainTiles(nowMs) {
      const manager = buildTerrainManager();
      const geoid = buildGeoidManager();
      if (geoid) {
        manager.datumState = geoid.datumState;
        manager.geoidOffsetMode = geoid.geoidOffsetMode;
      }
      if (!state.camera) {
        return;
      }
      if (nowMs - manager.lastTickMs < 550) {
        return;
      }
      manager.lastTickMs = nowMs;
      const llh = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
      if (!llh || !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) || !Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) {
        return;
      }
      if (!isWithinBounds(llh.lng, llh.lat, TOKYO23 && TOKYO23.bounds ? TOKYO23.bounds : null)) {
        return;
      }
      const suggestedZoom = chooseTerrainZoom(
        Number.isFinite(llh.altitudeM) ? llh.altitudeM : 1200,
        manager.currentZoom
      );
      if (!Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom)) {
        manager.currentZoom = suggestedZoom;
        manager.lastZoomChangeMs = nowMs;
      } else if (suggestedZoom !== manager.currentZoom) {
        const holdMs = suggestedZoom > manager.currentZoom
          ? Math.max(2500, Math.floor((manager.zoomSwitchHoldMs || 6000) * 0.5))
          : (manager.zoomSwitchHoldMs || 6000);
        if (nowMs - manager.lastZoomChangeMs >= holdMs) {
          manager.currentZoom = suggestedZoom;
          manager.lastZoomChangeMs = nowMs;
          debugLog("terrain:zoom_change", {
            zoom: manager.currentZoom,
            altitudeM: Number.isFinite(llh.altitudeM) ? Number(llh.altitudeM.toFixed(1)) : null,
          });
        }
      }
      const zoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : suggestedZoom;
      const center = lonLatToSlippy(llh.lng, llh.lat, zoom);
      const radiusNear = Number.isFinite(Number(TERRAIN_CONFIG && TERRAIN_CONFIG.tileRadiusNear))
        ? Math.max(1, Math.trunc(Number(TERRAIN_CONFIG.tileRadiusNear)))
        : 2;
      const radiusFar = Number.isFinite(Number(TERRAIN_CONFIG && TERRAIN_CONFIG.tileRadiusFar))
        ? Math.max(radiusNear, Math.trunc(Number(TERRAIN_CONFIG.tileRadiusFar)))
        : Math.max(3, radiusNear);
      const radiusFarAltitudeM = Number.isFinite(Number(TERRAIN_CONFIG && TERRAIN_CONFIG.tileRadiusFarAltitudeM))
        ? Math.max(200, Number(TERRAIN_CONFIG.tileRadiusFarAltitudeM))
        : 700;
      const cameraAltitudeM = Number.isFinite(llh.altitudeM) ? Number(llh.altitudeM) : 0;
      const radius = cameraAltitudeM >= radiusFarAltitudeM ? radiusFar : radiusNear;
      const desired = new Set();
      const maxIndex = Math.pow(2, zoom) - 1;
      for (let dy = -radius; dy <= radius; dy += 1) {
        for (let dx = -radius; dx <= radius; dx += 1) {
          const tx = clamp(center.x + dx, 0, maxIndex);
          const ty = clamp(center.y + dy, 0, maxIndex);
          const tileBounds = slippyBounds(tx, ty, zoom);
          if (!transportTileRelevantToActiveWards(tileBounds, llh)) {
            continue;
          }
          const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(tx) + "/" + String(ty);
          desired.add(key);
          if (!manager.tiles.has(key)) {
            loadTerrainTile(zoom, tx, ty).catch((error) => {
              debugLog("terrain:tile_async_error", {
                key,
                message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
              });
            });
          } else {
            const tile = manager.tiles.get(key);
            tile.lastWantedMs = nowMs;
          }
        }
      }
      manager.desired = desired;
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        if (desired.has(tile.key)) {
          continue;
        }
        if (nowMs - (tile.lastWantedMs || 0) > (manager.evictionHoldMs || 12000)) {
          evictTerrainTile(tile, "outside_desired");
        }
      }
    }

    function chooseTransportZoom(altitudeM, currentZoom) {
      const cfg = TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.tileZoomRange
        ? TRANSPORT_CONFIG.tileZoomRange
        : { min: 12, max: 14 };
      const minZoom = clamp(Number(cfg.min) || 12, 10, 16);
      const maxZoom = clamp(Number(cfg.max) || 14, minZoom, 18);
      const alt = Number.isFinite(altitudeM) ? altitudeM : 1200;
      let target = maxZoom;
      if (alt > 2600) {
        target = minZoom;
      } else if (alt > 1300) {
        target = clamp(minZoom + 1, minZoom, maxZoom);
      } else if (alt > 500) {
        target = clamp(maxZoom - 1, minZoom, maxZoom);
      } else {
        target = maxZoom;
      }
      if (!Number.isFinite(currentZoom)) {
        return target;
      }
      if (currentZoom === target) {
        return currentZoom;
      }
      if (target > currentZoom) {
        return alt < 700 ? target : currentZoom;
      }
      return alt > 1600 ? target : currentZoom;
    }

    function getTileIndexZoomLevels(tileIndex) {
      if (!tileIndex || typeof tileIndex !== "object") {
        return [];
      }
      if (tileIndexZoomCache.has(tileIndex)) {
        const cached = tileIndexZoomCache.get(tileIndex);
        return Array.isArray(cached) ? cached : [];
      }
      const levels = [];
      const seen = new Set();
      const keys = Object.keys(tileIndex);
      for (const key of keys) {
        if (typeof key !== "string") {
          continue;
        }
        const parts = key.split("/");
        if (parts.length < 3) {
          continue;
        }
        const zoom = Number(parts[0]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(zoom)) {
          continue;
        }
        const z = Math.round(zoom);
        if (seen.has(z)) {
          continue;
        }
        seen.add(z);
        levels.push(z);
      }
      levels.sort((a, b) => a - b);
      tileIndexZoomCache.set(tileIndex, levels);
      return levels;
    }

    function constrainZoomToAvailableLevels(targetZoom, zoomLevels) {
      if (!Array.isArray(zoomLevels) || zoomLevels.length <= 0 || !Number.isFinite(targetZoom)) {
        return targetZoom;
      }
      const target = Math.round(targetZoom);
      if (zoomLevels.includes(target)) {
        return target;
      }
      let nearest = zoomLevels[0];
      let nearestDelta = Math.abs(nearest - target);
      for (let i = 1; i < zoomLevels.length; i += 1) {
        const candidate = zoomLevels[i];
        const delta = Math.abs(candidate - target);
        if (delta < nearestDelta) {
          nearest = candidate;
          nearestDelta = delta;
        }
      }
      return nearest;
    }

    function chooseTransportSimplifyProfile(altitudeM, driveMode) {
      const cfg =
        TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.simplifyLod && typeof TRANSPORT_CONFIG.simplifyLod === "object"
          ? TRANSPORT_CONFIG.simplifyLod
          : {};
      if (driveMode) {
        return { key: "off", toleranceM: 0 };
      }
      const mediumAltitudeM = Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.mediumAltitudeM)) ? Number(cfg.mediumAltitudeM) : 900;
      const highAltitudeM = Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.highAltitudeM)) ? Number(cfg.highAltitudeM) : 1800;
      const mediumToleranceM = Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.mediumToleranceM)) ? Number(cfg.mediumToleranceM) : 0.8;
      const highToleranceM = Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.highToleranceM)) ? Number(cfg.highToleranceM) : 1.6;
      const alt = Number.isFinite(altitudeM) ? altitudeM : 0;
      if (alt >= highAltitudeM) {
        return { key: "high", toleranceM: highToleranceM };
      }
      if (alt >= mediumAltitudeM) {
        return { key: "medium", toleranceM: mediumToleranceM };
      }
      return { key: "off", toleranceM: 0 };
    }

    function inferTransportClass(tags) {
      const safeTags = tags && typeof tags === "object" ? tags : {};
      const highway = safeTags.highway ? String(safeTags.highway).toLowerCase() : "";
      const footway = safeTags.footway ? String(safeTags.footway).toLowerCase() : "";
      if (highway === "steps") {
        return "steps";
      }
      if (highway === "footway" && footway === "crossing") {
        return "crosswalk";
      }
      if (highway === "pedestrian") {
        return "pedestrian";
      }
      if (highway === "footway" || highway === "path" || highway === "cycleway") {
        return "sidewalk";
      }
      return "road";
    }

    function inferTransportWidthM(featureClass, tags, widthHint) {
      if (Number.isFinite(widthHint) && widthHint > 0.2) {
        return Number(widthHint);
      }
      const safeTags = tags && typeof tags === "object" ? tags : {};
      const highway = safeTags.highway ? String(safeTags.highway).toLowerCase() : "";
      if (featureClass === "sidewalk") {
        return 2.0;
      }
      if (featureClass === "crosswalk") {
        return 2.6;
      }
      if (featureClass === "steps") {
        return 1.8;
      }
      if (featureClass === "pedestrian") {
        return 4.2;
      }
      if (highway === "motorway" || highway === "trunk") {
        return 14;
      }
      if (highway === "primary") {
        return 10;
      }
      if (highway === "secondary") {
        return 8;
      }
      if (highway === "tertiary") {
        return 7;
      }
      if (highway === "residential" || highway === "unclassified") {
        return 6;
      }
      if (highway === "service" || highway === "living_street") {
        return 4.8;
      }
      return 5.5;
    }

    function getTransportOffsetM(featureClass) {
      const offsets = TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.meshOffsets
        ? TRANSPORT_CONFIG.meshOffsets
        : {};
      const hardFloors = {
        road: 0.32,
        sidewalk: 0.42,
        crosswalk: 0.54,
        steps: 0.38,
        pedestrian: 0.36,
      };
      if (featureClass === "sidewalk") {
        const value = Number.isFinite(offsets.sidewalk) ? Number(offsets.sidewalk) : 0.42;
        return Math.max(value, hardFloors.sidewalk);
      }
      if (featureClass === "crosswalk") {
        const value = Number.isFinite(offsets.crosswalk) ? Number(offsets.crosswalk) : 0.54;
        return Math.max(value, hardFloors.crosswalk);
      }
      if (featureClass === "steps") {
        const value = Number.isFinite(offsets.steps) ? Number(offsets.steps) : 0.38;
        return Math.max(value, hardFloors.steps);
      }
      if (featureClass === "pedestrian") {
        const value = Number.isFinite(offsets.pedestrian) ? Number(offsets.pedestrian) : 0.36;
        return Math.max(value, hardFloors.pedestrian);
      }
      const value = Number.isFinite(offsets.road) ? Number(offsets.road) : 0.32;
      return Math.max(value, hardFloors.road);
    }

    function parseTransportNumericTag(value) {
      if (Number.isFinite(value)) {
        return Number(value);
      }
      if (typeof value !== "string") {
        return NaN;
      }
      const match = value.match(/-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?/);
      if (!match) {
        return NaN;
      }
      const parsed = Number(match[0]);
