      return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : NaN;
    }

    function normalizeTagToken(value) {
      if (typeof value === "string") {
        return value.trim().toLowerCase();
      }
      if (Number.isFinite(value)) {
        return String(value);
      }
      return "";
    }

    function isTruthyTagToken(value) {
      const token = normalizeTagToken(value);
      if (!token) {
        return false;
      }
      return token !== "no" && token !== "none" && token !== "false" && token !== "0";
    }

    function isUndergroundFeature(attrs, options) {
      const safeAttrs = attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {};
      const safeOptions = options && typeof options === "object" ? options : {};
      const zMode = safeOptions.zMode ? normalizeTagToken(safeOptions.zMode) : "";
      if (zMode === "tunnel" || zMode === "underground" || zMode === "below_ground") {
        return true;
      }

      if (isTruthyTagToken(safeAttrs.tunnel)) {
        return true;
      }

      const locationTag = normalizeTagToken(safeAttrs.location);
      if (
        locationTag &&
        (locationTag.includes("underground") ||
          locationTag.includes("subterranean") ||
          locationTag.includes("below_ground") ||
          locationTag.includes("basement") ||
          locationTag.includes("underpass") ||
          locationTag.includes("tunnel"))
      ) {
        return true;
      }

      const layer = parseTransportNumericTag(safeAttrs.layer);
      if (Number.isFinite(layer) && layer < 0) {
        return true;
      }
      const level = parseTransportNumericTag(safeAttrs.level);
      if (Number.isFinite(level) && level < 0) {
        return true;
      }
      const minLevel = parseTransportNumericTag(safeAttrs.min_level);
      if (Number.isFinite(minLevel) && minLevel < 0) {
        return true;
      }

      if (safeOptions.includeSubway) {
        const route = normalizeTagToken(safeAttrs.route);
        const railway = normalizeTagToken(safeAttrs.railway);
        const station = normalizeTagToken(safeAttrs.station);
        if (route === "subway" || railway === "subway" || station === "subway") {
          return true;
        }
      }

      return false;
    }

    function isShallowCoveredTransport(attrs, zMode) {
      const safeAttrs = attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {};
      const tunnelTag = normalizeTagToken(safeAttrs.tunnel);
      const locationTag = normalizeTagToken(safeAttrs.location);
      const zModeTag = normalizeTagToken(zMode);
      if (
        tunnelTag.includes("building_passage") ||
        tunnelTag.includes("covered") ||
        tunnelTag.includes("canopy")
      ) {
        return true;
      }
      if (
        locationTag.includes("underpass") ||
        locationTag.includes("covered")
      ) {
        return true;
      }
      return (
        zModeTag === "underpass" ||
        zModeTag === "covered" ||
        zModeTag === "building_passage"
      );
    }

    function isTransportBridgeLike(attrs, zMode) {
      const safeAttrs = attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {};
      const zModeTag = normalizeTagToken(zMode);
      const bridgeTag = normalizeTagToken(safeAttrs.bridge);
      if (bridgeTag && bridgeTag !== "no") {
        return true;
      }
      return (
        zModeTag === "bridge" ||
        zModeTag === "overpass" ||
        zModeTag === "elevated" ||
        zModeTag === "viaduct"
      );
    }

    function getTransportStackDescriptor(featureClass, attrs, zMode) {
      const safeAttrs = attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {};
      const cls = normalizeTagToken(featureClass) || "road";
      const layer = parseTransportLayerTag(safeAttrs);
      const underground = isUndergroundFeature(safeAttrs, { zMode });
      const shallowCovered = isShallowCoveredTransport(safeAttrs, zMode);
      const bridgeLike = isTransportBridgeLike(safeAttrs, zMode);
      let stack = "surface";
      if (underground) {
        stack = shallowCovered ? "covered" : "underground";
      } else if (bridgeLike || layer > 0) {
        stack = "elevated";
      } else if (layer < 0) {
        stack = "subgrade";
      }
      return {
        cls,
        layer,
        stack,
        underground,
        shallowCovered,
        bridgeLike,
      };
    }

    function buildTransportStackKey(featureClass, attrs, zMode) {
      const info = getTransportStackDescriptor(featureClass, attrs, zMode);
      return info.cls + ":" + info.stack + ":" + String(info.layer);
    }

    function isRoadEligibleForLaneJunctions(attrs, zMode) {
      const info = getTransportStackDescriptor("road", attrs, zMode);
      return info.stack === "surface" && info.layer === 0;
    }

    function shouldSkipTransportFeatureByDepth(featureClass, attrs, options) {
      const cls = normalizeTagToken(featureClass);
      const safeAttrs = attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {};
      const safeOptions = options && typeof options === "object" ? options : {};
      const zMode = safeOptions.zMode || "";
      const info = getTransportStackDescriptor(cls, safeAttrs, zMode);
      if (!info.underground) {
        return false;
      }
      if (cls === "road") {
        return false;
      }
      if (cls === "sidewalk" || cls === "crosswalk" || cls === "pedestrian" || cls === "steps") {
        if (info.shallowCovered) {
          return false;
        }
        if (info.layer >= -1) {
          return false;
        }
      }
      return true;
    }

    function parseTransportLayerTag(attrs) {
      const safeAttrs = attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {};
      const layer = parseTransportNumericTag(safeAttrs.layer);
      if (Number.isFinite(layer)) {
        return clamp(Math.round(layer), -5, 6);
      }
      const level = parseTransportNumericTag(safeAttrs.level);
      if (Number.isFinite(level)) {
        return clamp(Math.round(level), -5, 6);
      }
      return 0;
    }

    function parseTransportIncline(attrs) {
      const safeAttrs = attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {};
      const raw = safeAttrs.incline ? String(safeAttrs.incline).trim().toLowerCase() : "";
      if (!raw || raw === "no" || raw === "none") {
        return { direction: 0, slopeAbs: null };
      }
      if (raw.includes("up")) {
        return { direction: 1, slopeAbs: null };
      }
      if (raw.includes("down")) {
        return { direction: -1, slopeAbs: null };
      }
      const percentMatch = raw.match(/(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%/);
      if (percentMatch) {
        const percent = Number(percentMatch[1]);
        if (Number.isFinite(percent) && percent !== 0) {
          return { direction: percent < 0 ? -1 : 1, slopeAbs: Math.abs(percent) / 100 };
        }
      }
      const degreeMatch = raw.match(/(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(deg|°)/);
      if (degreeMatch) {
        const degrees = Number(degreeMatch[1]);
        if (Number.isFinite(degrees) && degrees !== 0) {
          const slope = Math.tan(Math.abs(degrees) * Math.PI / 180);
          return { direction: degrees < 0 ? -1 : 1, slopeAbs: Number.isFinite(slope) ? slope : null };
        }
      }
      const numericMatch = raw.match(/-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?/);
      if (numericMatch) {
        const numeric = Number(numericMatch[0]);
        if (Number.isFinite(numeric) && numeric !== 0) {
          return { direction: numeric < 0 ? -1 : 1, slopeAbs: Math.abs(numeric) / 100 };
        }
      }
      return { direction: 1, slopeAbs: null };
    }

    function getTransportElevationConfig() {
      const cfg =
        TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.elevation && typeof TRANSPORT_CONFIG.elevation === "object"
          ? TRANSPORT_CONFIG.elevation
          : {};
      return {
        layerHeightM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.layerHeightM)) ? Number(cfg.layerHeightM) : 4.6,
        bridgeClearanceM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.bridgeClearanceM)) ? Number(cfg.bridgeClearanceM) : 5.2,
        tunnelDepthM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.tunnelDepthM)) ? Number(cfg.tunnelDepthM) : 4.2,
        coveredDepthM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.coveredDepthM)) ? Number(cfg.coveredDepthM) : 0.9,
        embankmentLiftM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.embankmentLiftM)) ? Number(cfg.embankmentLiftM) : 1.2,
        stepsDefaultRiseM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.stepsDefaultRiseM)) ? Number(cfg.stepsDefaultRiseM) : 2.2,
        maxRoadBridgeOffsetM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxRoadBridgeOffsetM))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.maxRoadBridgeOffsetM), 0.8, 4.2)
          : 2.4,
        maxRoadTunnelDepthM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxRoadTunnelDepthM))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.maxRoadTunnelDepthM), 1.0, 5.0)
          : 2.8,
        maxAbsOffsetM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxAbsOffsetM)) ? Math.max(3, Number(cfg.maxAbsOffsetM)) : 26,
      };
    }

    function inferTransportElevationProfileM(featureClass, attrs, zMode, totalLengthM) {
      const safeAttrs = attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {};
      const cfg = getTransportElevationConfig();
      const layer = parseTransportLayerTag(safeAttrs);
      const bridgeTag = safeAttrs.bridge ? String(safeAttrs.bridge).toLowerCase() : "";
      const tunnelTag = safeAttrs.tunnel ? String(safeAttrs.tunnel).toLowerCase() : "";
      const locationTag = safeAttrs.location ? String(safeAttrs.location).toLowerCase() : "";
      const embankmentTag = safeAttrs.embankment ? String(safeAttrs.embankment).toLowerCase() : "";
      const zModeNorm = zMode ? String(zMode).toLowerCase() : "";

      let baseM = layer * cfg.layerHeightM;
      const isRoad = String(featureClass || "").toLowerCase() === "road";
      const bridgeLike =
        (bridgeTag && bridgeTag !== "no") ||
        zModeNorm === "bridge" ||
        zModeNorm === "overpass" ||
        zModeNorm === "elevated" ||
        zModeNorm === "viaduct";
      if (bridgeLike) {
        baseM = Math.max(baseM, cfg.bridgeClearanceM);
      }

      const tunnelLike =
        (tunnelTag && tunnelTag !== "no") ||
        locationTag === "underground" ||
        zModeNorm === "tunnel" ||
        zModeNorm === "underground" ||
        zModeNorm === "below_ground";
      if (tunnelLike) {
        const shallowCovered =
          isShallowCoveredTransport(safeAttrs, zModeNorm);
        const targetDepthM = shallowCovered
          ? Math.max(0.35, Number(cfg.coveredDepthM) || 0.9)
          : Math.max(0.7, Number(cfg.tunnelDepthM) || 4.2);
        if (isRoad) {
          if (shallowCovered) {
            baseM = -Math.max(0.45, targetDepthM);
          } else {
            const layerDepth = Math.max(0, -layer) * 0.55;
            const depth = clamp(
              Math.max(targetDepthM * 0.34, 1.0 + layerDepth),
              1.0,
              Number(cfg.maxRoadTunnelDepthM) || 2.8
            );
            baseM = -depth;
          }
        } else if (shallowCovered) {
          baseM = -targetDepthM;
        } else {
          baseM = Math.min(baseM, -targetDepthM);
        }
      }

      if (isRoad && (bridgeLike || layer > 0)) {
        const bridgeLift = clamp(
          (bridgeLike ? 1.05 : 0.6) + Math.max(0, layer) * 0.55,
          0.45,
          Number(cfg.maxRoadBridgeOffsetM) || 2.4
        );
        baseM = bridgeLift;
      }

      if (embankmentTag && embankmentTag !== "no") {
        baseM = Math.max(baseM, cfg.embankmentLiftM);
      }

      let startM = baseM;
      let endM = baseM;
      if (featureClass === "steps") {
        const incline = parseTransportIncline(safeAttrs);
        let riseM = cfg.stepsDefaultRiseM;
        if (
          Number.isFinite(incline.slopeAbs) &&
          incline.slopeAbs > 0 &&
          Number.isFinite(totalLengthM) &&
          totalLengthM > 0.5
        ) {
          riseM = Math.max(riseM, totalLengthM * incline.slopeAbs);
        }
        riseM = clamp(riseM, 0.8, cfg.maxAbsOffsetM);
        const topM = Math.max(baseM, riseM);
        if (incline.direction < 0) {
          startM = topM;
          endM = baseM;
        } else {
          startM = baseM;
          endM = topM;
        }
      }

      return {
        startM: clamp(startM, -cfg.maxAbsOffsetM, cfg.maxAbsOffsetM),
        endM: clamp(endM, -cfg.maxAbsOffsetM, cfg.maxAbsOffsetM),
      };
    }

    function normalizeTransportFeature(rawFeature, sourceLabel) {
      if (!rawFeature || typeof rawFeature !== "object") {
        return null;
      }
      if (rawFeature.geometry && rawFeature.geometry.type) {
        const properties = rawFeature.properties && typeof rawFeature.properties === "object"
          ? rawFeature.properties
          : {};
        const clsRaw = properties.featureClass ? String(properties.featureClass).toLowerCase() : "";
        const featureClass =
          clsRaw === "road" || clsRaw === "sidewalk" || clsRaw === "crosswalk" || clsRaw === "steps" || clsRaw === "pedestrian"
            ? clsRaw
            : inferTransportClass(properties.tags || properties);
        const source = properties.source ? String(properties.source).toLowerCase() : sourceLabel;
        const widthM = inferTransportWidthM(featureClass, properties.tags || properties, Number(properties.width_m));
        const zMode = properties.z_mode ? String(properties.z_mode) : "drape";
        const attrs = properties.attrs && typeof properties.attrs === "object"
          ? properties.attrs
          : (properties.tags && typeof properties.tags === "object" ? properties.tags : {});
        if (shouldSkipTransportFeatureByDepth(featureClass, attrs, { zMode })) {
          return null;
        }
        if (rawFeature.geometry.type === "LineString" && Array.isArray(rawFeature.geometry.coordinates)) {
          return {
            featureClass,
            source,
            widthM,
            zMode,
            coordinates: rawFeature.geometry.coordinates,
            priority: Number.isFinite(properties.priority) ? Number(properties.priority) : 0,
            attrs,
            wayId: Number.isFinite(Number(properties.way_id))
              ? Number(properties.way_id)
              : (Number.isFinite(Number(properties.wayId)) ? Number(properties.wayId) : null),
          };
        }
        if (rawFeature.geometry.type === "MultiLineString" && Array.isArray(rawFeature.geometry.coordinates)) {
          const out = [];
          for (const line of rawFeature.geometry.coordinates) {
            if (Array.isArray(line) && line.length >= 2) {
              out.push({
                featureClass,
                source,
                widthM,
                zMode,
                coordinates: line,
                priority: Number.isFinite(properties.priority) ? Number(properties.priority) : 0,
                attrs,
                wayId: Number.isFinite(Number(properties.way_id))
                  ? Number(properties.way_id)
                  : (Number.isFinite(Number(properties.wayId)) ? Number(properties.wayId) : null),
              });
            }
          }
          return out.length > 0 ? out : null;
        }
        return null;
      }
      const tags = rawFeature.tags && typeof rawFeature.tags === "object" ? rawFeature.tags : {};
      const featureClass = inferTransportClass(tags);
      const widthM = inferTransportWidthM(featureClass, tags, Number(rawFeature.width_m));
      const coords = Array.isArray(rawFeature.coordinates) ? rawFeature.coordinates : [];
      if (coords.length < 2) {
        return null;
      }
      if (shouldSkipTransportFeatureByDepth(featureClass, tags, { zMode: "drape" })) {
        return null;
      }
      return {
        featureClass,
        source: sourceLabel,
        widthM,
        zMode: "drape",
        coordinates: coords,
        priority: 0,
        attrs: tags,
        wayId: Number.isFinite(Number(rawFeature.wayId))
          ? Number(rawFeature.wayId)
          : (Number.isFinite(Number(rawFeature.id)) ? Number(rawFeature.id) : null),
      };
    }

    function flattenNormalizedFeatures(normalized) {
      if (!normalized) {
        return [];
      }
      if (Array.isArray(normalized)) {
        return normalized.filter(Boolean);
      }
      return [normalized];
    }

    function buildTransportLinearOverlapKey(coords, precisionScale) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length < 2) {
        return "";
      }
      const scale = Number.isFinite(precisionScale) ? Math.max(1, Number(precisionScale)) : 1e5;
      const lastIndex = coords.length - 1;
      const pickIndices = [
        0,
        Math.floor(lastIndex * 0.25),
        Math.floor(lastIndex * 0.5),
        Math.floor(lastIndex * 0.75),
        lastIndex,
      ];
      const tokens = [];
      for (const idx of pickIndices) {
        const coord = coords[idx];
        if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) {
          return "";
        }
        const lon = Number(coord[0]);
        const lat = Number(coord[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
          return "";
        }
        tokens.push(String(Math.round(lon * scale)) + ":" + String(Math.round(lat * scale)));
      }
      const forward = tokens.join("|");
      const reverse = tokens.slice().reverse().join("|");
      return forward <= reverse ? forward : reverse;
    }

    function buildWalkwayOverlapKey(feature, coords) {
      const safeFeature = feature && typeof feature === "object" ? feature : {};
      const attrs = safeFeature.attrs && typeof safeFeature.attrs === "object" ? safeFeature.attrs : {};
      const zMode = safeFeature.zMode ? String(safeFeature.zMode) : "drape";
      const stackInfo = getTransportStackDescriptor("sidewalk", attrs, zMode);
      const stackKey = (stackInfo && stackInfo.stack ? stackInfo.stack : "surface") + ":" + String(
        stackInfo && Number.isFinite(stackInfo.layer) ? stackInfo.layer : 0
      );
      const geomKey = buildTransportLinearOverlapKey(coords, 1e5);
      if (!geomKey) {
        return "";
      }
      return stackKey + "|" + geomKey;
    }

    function buildTransportFeatureMergeKey(feature) {
      if (!feature || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) || feature.coordinates.length < 2) {
        return "";
      }
      const coords = feature.coordinates;
      const first = coords[0];
      const last = coords[coords.length - 1];
      if (!Array.isArray(first) || !Array.isArray(last) || first.length < 2 || last.length < 2) {
        return "";
      }
      const round = (value, scale) => Math.round((Number(value) || 0) * scale);
      const a = round(first[0], 1e5) + ":" + round(first[1], 1e5);
      const b = round(last[0], 1e5) + ":" + round(last[1], 1e5);
      const qIndex = Math.floor((coords.length - 1) * 0.25);
      const mIndex = Math.floor((coords.length - 1) * 0.5);
      const tIndex = Math.floor((coords.length - 1) * 0.75);
      const q = Array.isArray(coords[qIndex]) && coords[qIndex].length >= 2
        ? round(coords[qIndex][0], 1e5) + ":" + round(coords[qIndex][1], 1e5)
        : a;
      const m = Array.isArray(coords[mIndex]) && coords[mIndex].length >= 2
        ? round(coords[mIndex][0], 1e5) + ":" + round(coords[mIndex][1], 1e5)
        : a;
      const t = Array.isArray(coords[tIndex]) && coords[tIndex].length >= 2
        ? round(coords[tIndex][0], 1e5) + ":" + round(coords[tIndex][1], 1e5)
        : b;
      const c = coords.length;
      const classKey = String(feature.featureClass || "road").toLowerCase();
      const attrs = feature.attrs && typeof feature.attrs === "object" ? feature.attrs : {};
      const stackKey = buildTransportStackKey(classKey, attrs, feature.zMode);
      const orderA = a <= b ? a : b;
      const orderB = a <= b ? b : a;
      const qOrdered = a <= b ? q : t;
      const tOrdered = a <= b ? t : q;
      return classKey + "|" + stackKey + "|" + orderA + "|" + orderB + "|" + qOrdered + "|" + m + "|" + tOrdered + "|" + c;
    }

    function getSimplifiedTransportCoordinates(tileKey, feature, profileKey, toleranceM) {
      if (!feature || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) || feature.coordinates.length < 2) {
        return [];
      }
      const tolerance = Number.isFinite(toleranceM) ? Math.max(0, toleranceM) : 0;
      const keyProfile = String(profileKey || "off");
      if (tolerance <= 0 || keyProfile === "off") {
        return feature.coordinates;
      }
      const featureKey = buildTransportFeatureMergeKey(feature) ||
        String(feature.wayId || "w") + ":" + String(feature.coordinates.length);
      const cacheKey = String(tileKey || "tile") + "|" + keyProfile + "|" + featureKey;
      const cached = transportSimplifiedCoordinateCache.get(cacheKey);
      if (Array.isArray(cached) && cached.length >= 2) {
        return cached;
      }
      const simplified = simplifyLineDouglasPeucker(feature.coordinates, tolerance);
      const out = Array.isArray(simplified) && simplified.length >= 2 ? simplified : feature.coordinates;
      transportSimplifiedCoordinateCache.set(cacheKey, out);
      return out;
    }

    function mergeTransportFeatureSets(primaryFeatures, secondaryFeatures) {
      const out = [];
      const seen = new Set();
      const append = (feature, sourceFallback) => {
        if (!feature || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) || feature.coordinates.length < 2) {
          return;
        }
        const normalized = {
          ...feature,
          source:
            feature.source === "plateau" || feature.source === "osm"
              ? feature.source
              : sourceFallback,
        };
        const key = buildTransportFeatureMergeKey(normalized);
        if (key && seen.has(key)) {
          return;
        }
        if (key) {
          seen.add(key);
        }
        out.push(normalized);
      };

      for (const feature of Array.isArray(primaryFeatures) ? primaryFeatures : []) {
        append(feature, "plateau");
      }
      for (const feature of Array.isArray(secondaryFeatures) ? secondaryFeatures : []) {
        append(feature, "osm");
      }
      return out;
    }

    function createSidewalkTransportMaterial() {
      return new THREE.ShaderMaterial({
        transparent: true,
        depthTest: true,
        depthWrite: true,
        polygonOffset: true,
        polygonOffsetFactor: -4,
        polygonOffsetUnits: -4,
        uniforms: {
          uCenterColor: { value: new THREE.Color(0xf2f4f7) },
          uEdgeColor: { value: new THREE.Color(0xffffff) },
          uEdgeBlend: { value: 0.16 },
          uOpacity: { value: 0.98 },
        },
        vertexShader: [
          "attribute float side;",
          "varying float vSide;",
          "void main() {",
          "  vSide = side;",
          "  gl_Position = projectionMatrix * modelViewMatrix * vec4(position, 1.0);",
          "}",
        ].join("\\n"),
        fragmentShader: [
          "uniform vec3 uCenterColor;",
          "uniform vec3 uEdgeColor;",
          "uniform float uEdgeBlend;",
          "uniform float uOpacity;",
          "varying float vSide;",
          "void main() {",
          "  float edge = smoothstep(1.0 - uEdgeBlend, 1.0, abs(vSide));",
          "  vec3 color = mix(uCenterColor, uEdgeColor, edge);",
          "  gl_FragColor = vec4(color, uOpacity);",
          "}",
        ].join("\\n"),
      });
    }

    function createCrosswalkTransportMaterial() {
      return new THREE.ShaderMaterial({
        transparent: true,
        depthTest: true,
        depthWrite: false,
        polygonOffset: true,
        polygonOffsetFactor: -20,
        polygonOffsetUnits: -20,
        uniforms: {
          uStripeColor: { value: new THREE.Color(0xffd45a) },
          uStripeLength: { value: 0.52 },
          uGapLength: { value: 0.5 },
          uStripeFeather: { value: 0.08 },
          uEdgeFeather: { value: 0.12 },
          uOpacity: { value: 0.98 },
        },
        vertexShader: [
          "attribute float lineDistance;",
          "attribute float side;",
          "varying float vLineDistance;",
          "varying float vSide;",
          "void main() {",
          "  vLineDistance = lineDistance;",
          "  vSide = side;",
          "  gl_Position = projectionMatrix * modelViewMatrix * vec4(position, 1.0);",
          "}",
        ].join("\\n"),
        fragmentShader: [
          "uniform vec3 uStripeColor;",
          "uniform float uStripeLength;",
          "uniform float uGapLength;",
          "uniform float uStripeFeather;",
          "uniform float uEdgeFeather;",
          "uniform float uOpacity;",
          "varying float vLineDistance;",
          "varying float vSide;",
          "void main() {",
          "  float cycle = max(0.05, uStripeLength + uGapLength);",
          "  float phase = mod(vLineDistance + 0.12, cycle);",
          "  float stripe = 1.0 - smoothstep(uStripeLength - uStripeFeather, uStripeLength + uStripeFeather, phase);",
          "  float edgeMask = 1.0 - smoothstep(1.0 - uEdgeFeather, 1.0, abs(vSide));",
          "  float alpha = uOpacity * edgeMask * stripe;",
          "  if (alpha <= 0.001) discard;",
          "  gl_FragColor = vec4(uStripeColor, alpha);",
          "}",
        ].join("\\n"),
      });
    }

    function buildTransportManager() {
      if (state.transportManager) {
        return state.transportManager;
      }
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.name = "transportGroup";
      state.scene.add(group);
      const manager = {
        group,
        tiles: new Map(),
        pending: new Set(),
        desired: new Set(),
        failureBackoffByKey: new Map(),
        failureReasonByKey: new Map(),
        lastTickMs: 0,
        currentZoom: null,
        loaded: 0,
        failed: 0,
        ready: false,
        warning: "",
        maxActiveTiles: Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG.maxActiveTiles) || 24,
        hysteresisMs: Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG.hysteresisMs) || 9000,
        requestIntervalMs: Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG.requestIntervalMs) || 700,
        simplifyProfileKey: "off",
        simplifyToleranceM: 0,
        lastCameraAltitudeM: 0,
        renderModeRequested:
          String(
            (TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.rendererMode)
              ? TRANSPORT_CONFIG.rendererMode
              : "lane_mesh"
          ).toLowerCase(),
        renderModeActive: "ribbon",
        renderModeReason: "init",
        laneMeshQuality: "off",
        renderBuildMode: "ribbon",
        renderBuildModeSwitchMs: 0,
        renderBuildGeneration: 0,
        sourceMix: { plateau: 0, osm: 0 },
        featureCounts: { road: 0, sidewalk: 0, crosswalk: 0, steps: 0, pedestrian: 0, total: 0 },
        materials: {
          road: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xd53a3a,
            emissive: 0x170202,
            roughness: 0.92,
            metalness: 0.02,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -4,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -4,
          }),
          road_lane_mesh: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xd53a3a,
            emissive: 0x1b0202,
            roughness: 0.9,
            metalness: 0.03,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -4,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -4,
          }),
          sidewalk: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xf4f6f9,
            roughness: 0.97,
            metalness: 0.01,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -4,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -4,
          }),
          crosswalk: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xffd45a,
            roughness: 0.93,
            metalness: 0.01,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -20,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -20,
          }),
          steps: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xc6a46e,
            roughness: 0.98,
            metalness: 0.01,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -4,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -4,
          }),
          pedestrian: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xa88fe6,
            roughness: 0.97,
            metalness: 0.01,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -4,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -4,
          }),
          junction_surface: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0x9e1b1b,
            emissive: 0x140101,
            roughness: 0.92,
            metalness: 0.02,
            transparent: true,
            opacity: 0.96,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -4.3,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -4.3,
          }),
          turn_channel: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xe65a5a,
            emissive: 0x1a0303,
            roughness: 0.9,
            metalness: 0.02,
            transparent: true,
            opacity: 0.95,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -4.1,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -4.1,
          }),
          sidewalk_stylized: createSidewalkTransportMaterial(),
          crosswalk_stylized: createCrosswalkTransportMaterial(),
        },
      };
      for (const material of Object.values(manager.materials)) {
        if (!material) {
          continue;
        }
        if (material === manager.materials.crosswalk_stylized || material === manager.materials.crosswalk) {
          material.depthTest = true;
          material.depthWrite = false;
          continue;
        }
        material.depthTest = true;
        material.depthWrite = true;
      }
      state.transportManager = manager;
      return manager;
    }

    async function fetchTransportFeaturesFromManifestTile(zoom, x, y) {
      const manifest = TRANSPORT_MANIFEST && typeof TRANSPORT_MANIFEST === "object"
        ? TRANSPORT_MANIFEST
        : {};
      const urls = [];
      const basePath = manifest.basePath ? String(manifest.basePath) : "";
      const tileKey = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      const flatName = "transport_z" + String(zoom) + "_x" + String(x) + "_y" + String(y) + ".json";
      if (manifest.tileIndex && typeof manifest.tileIndex === "object") {
        const indexed = manifest.tileIndex[tileKey];
        if (typeof indexed === "string" && indexed.length > 0) {
          const lowerIndexed = indexed.toLowerCase();
          if (lowerIndexed.startsWith("http://") || lowerIndexed.startsWith("https://")) {
            urls.push(indexed);
          } else {
            urls.push(basePath ? joinAssetPath(basePath, indexed) : indexed);
          }
        }
      }
      if (manifest.plateauTiles && manifest.plateauTiles.urlTemplate) {
        urls.push(
          String(manifest.plateauTiles.urlTemplate)
            .replace("{z}", String(zoom))
            .replace("{x}", String(x))
            .replace("{y}", String(y))
        );
      }
      if (basePath) {
        urls.push(
          joinAssetPath(basePath, String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json")
        );
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, flatName));
        urls.push(
          joinAssetPath(basePath, "transport_osm_tiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json")
        );
        urls.push(
          joinAssetPath(basePath, "transport_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json")
        );
      }
      urls.push("./patch_assets/" + flatName);
      urls.push("patch_assets/" + flatName);
      urls.push("./" + flatName);
      urls.push(flatName);
      urls.push("./patch_assets/transport_osm_tiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("patch_assets/transport_osm_tiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("./transport_osm_tiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("transport_osm_tiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("./patch_assets/transport_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("patch_assets/transport_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("./transport_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("transport_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      const uniqueUrls = Array.from(new Set(urls.filter((url) => typeof url === "string" && url.length > 0)));
      if (uniqueUrls.length === 0) {
        return [];
      }
      for (const url of uniqueUrls) {
        try {
          const payload = await tryFetchJsonCandidate(url, 7000, isFeatureCollectionPayload);
          if (!payload || !Array.isArray(payload.features)) {
            continue;
          }
          const features = [];
          for (const feature of payload.features) {
            features.push(...flattenNormalizedFeatures(normalizeTransportFeature(feature, "plateau")));
          }
          if (features.length > 0) {
            return features;
          }
        } catch (_error) {
          // Continue to next URL candidate.
        }
      }
      return [];
    }

    function isRuntimeOverpassFallbackEnabled() {
      const config = TRANSPORT_CONFIG && typeof TRANSPORT_CONFIG === "object"
        ? TRANSPORT_CONFIG
        : {};
      if (typeof config.runtimeOverpassFallback === "boolean") {
        return config.runtimeOverpassFallback;
      }
      if (typeof config.allowRuntimeOverpassFallback === "boolean") {
        return config.allowRuntimeOverpassFallback;
      }
      if (
        TRANSPORT_MANIFEST &&
        TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.osmFallback &&
        typeof TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.osmFallback === "object" &&
        typeof TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.osmFallback.enabled === "boolean"
      ) {
        return !!TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.osmFallback.enabled;
      }
      return true;
    }

    async function fetchTransportFeaturesFromOverpass(bounds, zoom) {
      const manifest = TRANSPORT_MANIFEST && typeof TRANSPORT_MANIFEST === "object"
        ? TRANSPORT_MANIFEST
        : {};
      const fallback = manifest.osmFallback && typeof manifest.osmFallback === "object"
        ? manifest.osmFallback
        : {};
      if (!fallback.enabled || !isRuntimeOverpassFallbackEnabled()) {
        return [];
      }
      const maxZoom = Number.isFinite(fallback.maxZoom) ? Number(fallback.maxZoom) : 14;
      if (zoom > maxZoom) {
        return [];
      }
      const endpointList = Array.isArray(fallback.endpoints)
        ? fallback.endpoints.map((item) => String(item || "").trim()).filter(Boolean)
        : [];
      if (endpointList.length === 0) {
        endpointList.push(
          fallback.endpoint
            ? String(fallback.endpoint)
            : "https://overpass-api.de/api/interpreter"
        );
      }
      const timeoutSec = Number.isFinite(fallback.timeoutSec) ? Math.max(10, Number(fallback.timeoutSec)) : 24;
      const maxRetries = Number.isFinite(fallback.maxRetries) ? clamp(Number(fallback.maxRetries), 0, 7) : 3;
      const retryBaseMs = Number.isFinite(fallback.retryBaseMs) ? Math.max(300, Number(fallback.retryBaseMs)) : 1300;
      const retryJitterMs = Number.isFinite(fallback.retryJitterMs) ? Math.max(0, Number(fallback.retryJitterMs)) : 420;
      const maxWaysConfigured = Number.isFinite(Number(fallback.maxWays))
        ? Number(fallback.maxWays)
        : (
          Number.isFinite(Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.overpassMaxWays))
            ? Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG.overpassMaxWays)
            : 5200
        );
      const hardMinimumWays = Number.isFinite(Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.overpassHardMinWays))
        ? Math.max(3200, Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG.overpassHardMinWays))
        : 6200;
      const configuredFloor = Number.isFinite(Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.overpassMaxWays))
        ? Math.max(hardMinimumWays, Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG.overpassMaxWays))
        : hardMinimumWays;
      const maxWays = clampInt(
        Math.max(maxWaysConfigured, configuredFloor, hardMinimumWays),
        configuredFloor,
        hardMinimumWays,
        24000
      );
      // Disabled intentionally: synthesized sidewalks from road tags duplicate
      // explicit sidewalk geometries and create stacked overlaps.
      const synthesizeRoadSidewalkFromTag = false;
      const bbox = [
        Number(bounds.south).toFixed(6),
        Number(bounds.west).toFixed(6),
        Number(bounds.north).toFixed(6),
        Number(bounds.east).toFixed(6),
      ].join(",");
      const query = '[out:json][timeout:' + String(timeoutSec) + '];(way["highway"](' + String(bbox) + '););out geom qt;';
      let payload = null;
      let lastError = null;
      for (let attempt = 0; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt += 1) {
        const endpoint = endpointList[attempt % endpointList.length];
        try {
          const response = await fetch(endpoint, {
            method: "POST",
            mode: "cors",
            credentials: "omit",
            headers: {
              "content-type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=UTF-8",
            },
            body: "data=" + encodeURIComponent(query),
          });
          if (!response || !response.ok) {
            const status = response ? Number(response.status) || 0 : 0;
            const error = new Error("overpass_http_" + String(status));
            error.status = status;
            error.retryAfterMs = parseRetryAfterMs(response && response.headers ? response.headers.get("retry-after") : null);
            throw error;
          }
          payload = await parseJsonResponseWithContext(response, "overpass_payload");
          break;
        } catch (error) {
          lastError = error;
          const status = Number(error && error.status);
          const retryable = !Number.isFinite(status) || status === 0 || status === 408 || status === 429 || status >= 500;
          if ((error && error.message ? String(error.message) : "").includes("non_json")) {
            debugLog("transport:overpass_non_json", {
              status: Number.isFinite(status) ? status : "unknown",
              endpoint,
              snippet: error && error.snippet ? String(error.snippet).slice(0, 120) : "",
            });
          }
          if (!retryable || attempt >= maxRetries) {
            break;
          }
          const retryAfterMs = Number(error && error.retryAfterMs) || 0;
          const backoffMs = retryAfterMs > 0
            ? retryAfterMs + Math.floor(Math.random() * 320)
            : Math.floor(retryBaseMs * Math.pow(2, Math.min(attempt, 5)) + Math.random() * retryJitterMs);
          debugLog("transport:overpass_retry", {
            status: Number.isFinite(status) ? status : "network",
            attempt: attempt + 1,
            waitMs: backoffMs,
            endpoint,
          });
          await sleepMs(backoffMs);
        }
      }
      if (!payload) {
        throw lastError || new Error("overpass_empty_response");
      }
      const elements = payload && Array.isArray(payload.elements) ? payload.elements : [];
      const features = [];
      const candidates = [];
      const highwayRoadScore = {
        motorway: 36,
        trunk: 34,
        primary: 31,
        secondary: 27,
        tertiary: 23,
        residential: 19,
        unclassified: 18,
        service: 15,
        living_street: 14,
      };
      const classBaseScore = {
        road: 200,
        crosswalk: 120,
        sidewalk: 70,
        pedestrian: 60,
        steps: 56,
      };
      const classCaps = {
        road: Math.max(420, Math.round(maxWays * 0.72)),
        sidewalk: Math.max(140, Math.round(maxWays * 0.15)),
        crosswalk: Math.max(90, Math.round(maxWays * 0.07)),
        steps: Math.max(64, Math.round(maxWays * 0.04)),
        pedestrian: Math.max(42, Math.round(maxWays * 0.03)),
      };
      let hadOverflow = false;
      for (const element of elements) {
        if (!element || element.type !== "way" || !Array.isArray(element.geometry) || element.geometry.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        const tags = element.tags && typeof element.tags === "object" ? element.tags : {};
        const coords = element.geometry
          .map((pt) => {
            if (!pt) {
              return null;
            }
            const lon = Number(pt.lon);
            const lat = Number(pt.lat);
            if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
              return null;
            }
            return [lon, lat];
          })
          .filter(Boolean);
        if (coords.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        const cls = inferTransportClass(tags);
        if (shouldSkipTransportFeatureByDepth(cls, tags, { zMode: "drape" })) {
          continue;
        }
        const widthM = inferTransportWidthM(cls, tags, Number(tags.width));
        const highway = normalizeTagToken(tags.highway);
        const layer = parseTransportLayerTag(tags);
        const isBridge = isTransportBridgeLike(tags, "drape");
        const isCovered = isShallowCoveredTransport(tags, "drape");
        const isTunnelLike = isUndergroundFeature(tags, { zMode: "drape" });
        const candidate = {
          featureClass: cls,
          source: "osm",
          widthM,
          zMode: "drape",
          coordinates: coords,
          priority: 0,
          attrs: tags,
          wayId: Number.isFinite(Number(element.id)) ? Number(element.id) : null,
        };
        let score = Number(classBaseScore[cls]) || 40;
        if (cls === "road") {
          score += Number(highwayRoadScore[highway]) || 12;
        } else if (cls === "sidewalk" && (highway === "path" || highway === "cycleway")) {
          score -= 22;
        } else if (cls === "steps") {
          score -= 8;
        }
        if (isBridge || isTunnelLike || isCovered || layer !== 0) {
          score += 24;
        }
        score += clamp(Math.round(coords.length * 0.12), 0, 14);
        candidate.priority = score;
        candidates.push(candidate);
        const sidewalkTag = tags.sidewalk ? String(tags.sidewalk).toLowerCase() : "";
        if (
          synthesizeRoadSidewalkFromTag &&
          cls === "road" &&
          (sidewalkTag === "both" || sidewalkTag === "left" || sidewalkTag === "right" || sidewalkTag === "yes")
        ) {
          features.push({
            featureClass: "sidewalk",
            source: "osm",
            widthM: 1.8,
            zMode: "drape",
            coordinates: coords,
            priority: 1,
            attrs: tags,
            wayId: Number.isFinite(Number(element.id)) ? Number(element.id) : null,
          });
        }
      }
      const truncated = candidates.length > maxWays;
      if (!truncated) {
        return candidates;
      }
      const sorted = candidates.slice().sort((a, b) => {
        const pa = Number(a && a.priority) || 0;
        const pb = Number(b && b.priority) || 0;
        if (pb !== pa) return pb - pa;
        const aw = Number(a && a.widthM) || 0;
        const bw = Number(b && b.widthM) || 0;
        if (bw !== aw) return bw - aw;
        const al = Array.isArray(a && a.coordinates) ? a.coordinates.length : 0;
        const bl = Array.isArray(b && b.coordinates) ? b.coordinates.length : 0;
        return bl - al;
      });
      const keptCounts = { road: 0, sidewalk: 0, crosswalk: 0, steps: 0, pedestrian: 0 };
      const deferred = [];
      for (const candidate of sorted) {
        if (features.length >= maxWays) {
          break;
        }
        const cls = String(candidate && candidate.featureClass ? candidate.featureClass : "road");
        const cap = Number.isFinite(classCaps[cls]) ? classCaps[cls] : Math.max(20, Math.round(maxWays * 0.08));
        if ((keptCounts[cls] || 0) >= cap) {
          deferred.push(candidate);
          hadOverflow = true;
          continue;
        }
        features.push(candidate);
        keptCounts[cls] = (keptCounts[cls] || 0) + 1;
      }
      if (features.length < maxWays && deferred.length > 0) {
        const softCaps = {
          road: Math.round(classCaps.road * 1.45),
          sidewalk: Math.round(classCaps.sidewalk * 1.25),
          crosswalk: Math.round(classCaps.crosswalk * 1.25),
          steps: Math.round(classCaps.steps * 1.25),
          pedestrian: Math.round(classCaps.pedestrian * 1.35),
        };
        for (const candidate of deferred) {
          if (features.length >= maxWays) {
            break;
          }
          const cls = String(candidate && candidate.featureClass ? candidate.featureClass : "road");
          const cap = Number.isFinite(softCaps[cls]) ? softCaps[cls] : maxWays;
          if ((keptCounts[cls] || 0) >= cap) {
            continue;
          }
          features.push(candidate);
          keptCounts[cls] = (keptCounts[cls] || 0) + 1;
        }
      }
      if (truncated || hadOverflow) {
        debugLog("transport:overpass_truncated", {
          maxWays,
          elementCount: elements.length,
          candidateCount: candidates.length,
          keptCount: features.length,
          keptCounts,
          bbox,
        });
      }
      return features;
    }

    async function fetchTransportFeaturesForTile(zoom, x, y, bounds) {
      const cacheKey = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      const cached = transportTileFeatureCache.get(cacheKey);
      if (cached && cached.expiresAt > Date.now()) {
        return {
          features: Array.isArray(cached.features) ? cached.features : [],
          source: cached.source || "none",
          sourceBreakdown:
            cached && cached.sourceBreakdown && typeof cached.sourceBreakdown === "object"
              ? cached.sourceBreakdown
              : { plateau: 0, osm: 0 },
          failures: [],
        };
      }
      const sourcePriority = Array.isArray(TRANSPORT_CONFIG.sourcePriority)
        ? TRANSPORT_CONFIG.sourcePriority
        : ["plateau", "osm"];
      const mergeSources = TRANSPORT_CONFIG.mergeSources !== false;
      const failures = [];
      const uniqueSources = Array.from(new Set(sourcePriority.map((value) => String(value || "").toLowerCase())));
      const sourceFeatures = { plateau: [], osm: [] };
      for (const source of uniqueSources) {
        if (source !== "plateau" && source !== "osm") {
          continue;
        }
        try {
          if (source === "plateau") {
            const features = await fetchTransportFeaturesFromManifestTile(zoom, x, y);
            if (features.length > 0) {
              sourceFeatures.plateau = features;
              if (!mergeSources) {
                const sourceBreakdown = { plateau: features.length, osm: 0 };
                transportTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, {
                  features,
                  source: "plateau",
                  sourceBreakdown,
                  expiresAt: Date.now() + 8 * 60 * 1000,
                });
                return { features, source: "plateau", sourceBreakdown };
              }
            } else {
              failures.push("plateau:no_data");
            }
            continue;
          }
          if (source === "osm") {
            if (!isRuntimeOverpassFallbackEnabled()) {
              failures.push("osm:runtime_fallback_disabled");
              continue;
            }
            const features = await fetchTransportFeaturesFromOverpass(bounds, zoom);
            if (features.length > 0) {
              sourceFeatures.osm = features;
              if (!mergeSources) {
                const sourceBreakdown = { plateau: 0, osm: features.length };
                transportTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, {
                  features,
                  source: "osm",
                  sourceBreakdown,
                  expiresAt: Date.now() + 5 * 60 * 1000,
                });
                return { features, source: "osm", sourceBreakdown };
              }
            } else {
              failures.push("osm:no_data");
            }
          }
        } catch (error) {
          failures.push(
            String(source) + ":" + (error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error))
          );
        }
      }

      if (mergeSources) {
        const merged = mergeTransportFeatureSets(sourceFeatures.plateau, sourceFeatures.osm);
        const sourceBreakdown = {
          plateau: Array.isArray(sourceFeatures.plateau) ? sourceFeatures.plateau.length : 0,
          osm: Array.isArray(sourceFeatures.osm) ? sourceFeatures.osm.length : 0,
        };
        const source =
          sourceBreakdown.plateau > 0 && sourceBreakdown.osm > 0
            ? "mixed"
            : sourceBreakdown.plateau > 0
              ? "plateau"
              : sourceBreakdown.osm > 0
                ? "osm"
                : "none";
        if (merged.length > 0) {
          transportTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, {
            features: merged,
            source,
            sourceBreakdown,
            expiresAt: Date.now() + 5 * 60 * 1000,
          });
          return { features: merged, source, sourceBreakdown };
        }
      }
      transportTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, {
        features: [],
        source: "none",
        sourceBreakdown: { plateau: 0, osm: 0 },
        expiresAt: Date.now() + 5 * 60 * 1000,
      });
      return { features: [], source: "none", failures };
    }

    function getTransportLaneMeshConfig() {
      const cfg = TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.laneMesh && typeof TRANSPORT_CONFIG.laneMesh === "object"
        ? TRANSPORT_CONFIG.laneMesh
        : {};
      return {
        lowAltitudeM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.lowAltitudeM)) ? Number(cfg.lowAltitudeM) : 520,
        mediumAltitudeM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.mediumAltitudeM)) ? Number(cfg.mediumAltitudeM) : 1100,
        highAltitudeM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.highAltitudeM)) ? Number(cfg.highAltitudeM) : 1900,
        maxLanesHigh: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxLanesHigh)) ? Math.max(1, Number(cfg.maxLanesHigh)) : 5,
        maxLanesMedium: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxLanesMedium)) ? Math.max(1, Number(cfg.maxLanesMedium)) : 3,
        maxLanesLow: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxLanesLow)) ? Math.max(1, Number(cfg.maxLanesLow)) : 2,
        maxTransitionM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxTransitionM)) ? Math.max(4, Number(cfg.maxTransitionM)) : 22,
        minTransitionM: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.minTransitionM)) ? Math.max(1.5, Number(cfg.minTransitionM)) : 4,
        turnAngleThresholdDeg: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.turnAngleThresholdDeg))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.turnAngleThresholdDeg), 1, 40)
          : 7,
        curveSubdivisionsHigh: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.curveSubdivisionsHigh))
          ? Math.max(3, Math.round(Number(cfg.curveSubdivisionsHigh)))
          : 16,
        curveSubdivisionsMedium: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.curveSubdivisionsMedium))
          ? Math.max(3, Math.round(Number(cfg.curveSubdivisionsMedium)))
          : 10,
        curveSubdivisionsLow: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.curveSubdivisionsLow))
          ? Math.max(2, Math.round(Number(cfg.curveSubdivisionsLow)))
          : 6,
        laneInsetFactor: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.laneInsetFactor))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.laneInsetFactor), 0.65, 1.0)
          : 0.9,
        junctionSidesHigh: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.junctionSidesHigh))
          ? Math.max(6, Math.round(Number(cfg.junctionSidesHigh)))
          : 14,
        junctionSidesMedium: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.junctionSidesMedium))
          ? Math.max(6, Math.round(Number(cfg.junctionSidesMedium)))
          : 10,
        junctionSidesLow: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.junctionSidesLow))
          ? Math.max(5, Math.round(Number(cfg.junctionSidesLow)))
          : 8,
        junctionHeadingDedupeDeg: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.junctionHeadingDedupeDeg))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.junctionHeadingDedupeDeg), 4, 32)
          : 12,
        maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionHigh: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionHigh))
          ? Math.max(4, Math.round(Number(cfg.maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionHigh)))
          : 18,
        maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionMedium: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionMedium))
          ? Math.max(4, Math.round(Number(cfg.maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionMedium)))
          : 14,
        maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionLow: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionLow))
          ? Math.max(4, Math.round(Number(cfg.maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionLow)))
          : 10,
        maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionHigh: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionHigh))
          ? Math.max(3, Math.round(Number(cfg.maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionHigh)))
          : 8,
        maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionMedium: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionMedium))
          ? Math.max(3, Math.round(Number(cfg.maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionMedium)))
          : 7,
        maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionLow: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionLow))
          ? Math.max(3, Math.round(Number(cfg.maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionLow)))
          : 6,
        maxJunctionRadiusMHigh: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxJunctionRadiusMHigh))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.maxJunctionRadiusMHigh), 3, 20)
          : 9.2,
        maxJunctionRadiusMMedium: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxJunctionRadiusMMedium))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.maxJunctionRadiusMMedium), 3, 20)
          : 8,
        maxJunctionRadiusMLow: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxJunctionRadiusMLow))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.maxJunctionRadiusMLow), 2.5, 20)
          : 6.8,
        junctionRadiusScale: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.junctionRadiusScale))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.junctionRadiusScale), 0.2, 1.2)
          : 0.62,
        turnChannelRadiusScale: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.turnChannelRadiusScale))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.turnChannelRadiusScale), 0.2, 1.1)
          : 0.68,
        maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionHigh: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionHigh))
          ? Math.max(1, Math.round(Number(cfg.maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionHigh)))
          : 14,
        maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionMedium: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionMedium))
          ? Math.max(1, Math.round(Number(cfg.maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionMedium)))
          : 8,
        maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionLow: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionLow))
          ? Math.max(1, Math.round(Number(cfg.maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionLow)))
          : 4,
        minTurnChannelAngleDeg: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.minTurnChannelAngleDeg))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.minTurnChannelAngleDeg), 8, 80)
          : 28,
        maxTurnChannelAngleDeg: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxTurnChannelAngleDeg))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.maxTurnChannelAngleDeg), 90, 178)
          : 164,
        maxAdjacentTurnGapDeg: Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.maxAdjacentTurnGapDeg))
          ? clamp(Number(cfg.maxAdjacentTurnGapDeg), 60, 178)
          : 132,
        // Off by default: junction overlays can generate unstable slabs at complex grade-separated nodes.
        enableJunctionOverlays: cfg.enableJunctionOverlays === true,
      };
    }

    function resolveTransportRoadRenderState(manager) {
      const modeRaw = manager && manager.renderModeRequested
        ? String(manager.renderModeRequested).toLowerCase()
        : String((TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.rendererMode) || "lane_mesh").toLowerCase();
      const laneCfg = getTransportLaneMeshConfig();
      const budgetMs = Number.isFinite(Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.frameBudgetMs))
        ? Math.max(8, Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG.frameBudgetMs))
        : 16.7;
      const frameMs = Number.isFinite(state.frameTimeAvgMs) ? Number(state.frameTimeAvgMs) : budgetMs;
      const allowFallback = TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.rendererFallback !== false;
      if (modeRaw !== "lane_mesh") {
        return { mode: "ribbon", quality: "off", reason: "config_ribbon", laneCfg };
      }
      if (allowFallback && !state.driveMode && frameMs > budgetMs * 1.8) {
        return { mode: "ribbon", quality: "off", reason: "frame_over_budget", laneCfg };
      }
      const altitudeM = Number.isFinite(manager && manager.lastCameraAltitudeM)
        ? Number(manager.lastCameraAltitudeM)
        : 0;
      let quality = "high";
      if (altitudeM >= laneCfg.highAltitudeM || frameMs > budgetMs * 1.18) {
        quality = "low";
      } else if (altitudeM >= laneCfg.mediumAltitudeM || frameMs > budgetMs * 1.06) {
        quality = "medium";
      }
      return { mode: "lane_mesh", quality, reason: "lane_mesh_active", laneCfg };
    }

    function transportDistance2D(a, b) {
      if (!a || !b) return 0;
      const dx = Number(b.x) - Number(a.x);
      const dy = Number(b.y) - Number(a.y);
      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
    }

    function transportNormalizeVec2(vx, vy) {
      const len = Math.sqrt(vx * vx + vy * vy);
      if (!Number.isFinite(len) || len <= 1e-8) {
        return null;
      }
      return { x: vx / len, y: vy / len };
    }

    function transportSignedAngleRad(a, b) {
      if (!a || !b) return 0;
      const cross = a.x * b.y - a.y * b.x;
      const dot = a.x * b.x + a.y * b.y;
      return Math.atan2(cross, dot);
    }

    function transportNormalizeAngleRad(value) {
      const twoPi = Math.PI * 2;
      if (!Number.isFinite(value)) {
        return 0;
      }
      let out = value % twoPi;
      if (out < 0) {
        out += twoPi;
      }
      return out;
    }

    function transportAbsoluteAngleDiffRad(a, b) {
      const twoPi = Math.PI * 2;
      let diff = Math.abs(transportNormalizeAngleRad(a) - transportNormalizeAngleRad(b));
      if (diff > Math.PI) {
        diff = twoPi - diff;
      }
      return diff;
    }

    function dedupeJunctionEndpointEntries(entries, angleToleranceDeg, maxEntries) {
      if (!Array.isArray(entries) || entries.length <= 0) {
        return [];
      }
      const toleranceRad = toRad(Number.isFinite(Number(angleToleranceDeg)) ? Number(angleToleranceDeg) : 12);
      const keepLimit = Number.isFinite(Number(maxEntries)) ? Math.max(1, Math.round(Number(maxEntries))) : 9999;
      const ranked = [];
      for (const entry of entries) {
        if (!entry) continue;
        const dir = transportNormalizeVec2(Number(entry.dirX), Number(entry.dirY));
        if (!dir) continue;
        const angleRad = transportNormalizeAngleRad(Math.atan2(dir.y, dir.x));
        ranked.push({
          ...entry,
          dirX: dir.x,
          dirY: dir.y,
          angleRad,
          widthM: Number.isFinite(Number(entry.widthM)) ? Number(entry.widthM) : 5.5,
          laneWidthM: Number.isFinite(Number(entry.laneWidthM)) ? Number(entry.laneWidthM) : 3.2,
          laneCount: Number.isFinite(Number(entry.laneCount)) ? Number(entry.laneCount) : 1,
        });
      }
      ranked.sort((a, b) => {
        const aw = Number(a.widthM) || 0;
        const bw = Number(b.widthM) || 0;
        if (bw !== aw) return bw - aw;
        const al = Number(a.laneCount) || 0;
        const bl = Number(b.laneCount) || 0;
        return bl - al;
      });
      const out = [];
      for (const entry of ranked) {
        let duplicate = false;
        for (const existing of out) {
          const diff = transportAbsoluteAngleDiffRad(entry.angleRad, existing.angleRad);
          if (diff <= toleranceRad) {
            duplicate = true;
            break;
          }
          if (
            entry.featureKey &&
            existing.featureKey &&
            entry.featureKey === existing.featureKey &&
            diff <= toleranceRad * 1.2
          ) {
            duplicate = true;
            break;
          }
        }
        if (!duplicate) {
          out.push(entry);
          if (out.length >= keepLimit) {
            break;
          }
        }
      }
      out.sort((a, b) => a.angleRad - b.angleRad);
      return out;
    }

    function transportToPlanarPoint(lon, lat, refLon, refLat) {
      const metersPerDegLon = 111320 * Math.cos(toRad(refLat));
      const metersPerDegLat = 110540;
      return {
        x: (Number(lon) - Number(refLon)) * metersPerDegLon,
        y: (Number(lat) - Number(refLat)) * metersPerDegLat,
      };
    }

    function transportFromPlanarPoint(x, y, refLon, refLat) {
      const metersPerDegLon = 111320 * Math.cos(toRad(refLat));
      const metersPerDegLat = 110540;
      return {
        lon: Number(refLon) + (metersPerDegLon !== 0 ? Number(x) / metersPerDegLon : 0),
        lat: Number(refLat) + (metersPerDegLat !== 0 ? Number(y) / metersPerDegLat : 0),
      };
    }

    function sampleClothoidLikeConnector2D(start, end, dirIn, dirOut, sampleCount, handleLenM) {
      const out = [];
      if (!start || !end || !dirIn || !dirOut) {
        return out;
      }
      const chord = transportDistance2D(start, end);
      if (!Number.isFinite(chord) || chord < 0.2) {
        return out;
      }
      const samples = Math.max(1, Math.round(Number(sampleCount) || 1));
      const handle = clamp(
        Number.isFinite(handleLenM) ? Number(handleLenM) : chord * 0.44,
        chord * 0.12,
        chord * 0.68
      );
      const c1 = {
        x: start.x + dirIn.x * handle,
        y: start.y + dirIn.y * handle,
      };
      const c2 = {
        x: end.x - dirOut.x * handle,
        y: end.y - dirOut.y * handle,
      };
      for (let i = 1; i <= samples; i += 1) {
        const t = i / (samples + 1);
        const u = 1 - t;
        const x =
          u * u * u * start.x +
          3 * u * u * t * c1.x +
          3 * u * t * t * c2.x +
          t * t * t * end.x;
        const y =
          u * u * u * start.y +
          3 * u * u * t * c1.y +
          3 * u * t * t * c2.y +
          t * t * t * end.y;
        out.push({ x, y });
      }
      return out;
    }

    function smoothTransportRoadCoordinates(coords, qualityKey, laneCfg) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length < 3) {
        return Array.isArray(coords) ? coords : [];
      }
      let refLon = 0;
      let refLat = 0;
      const points = [];
      for (const coord of coords) {
        if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) continue;
        const lon = Number(coord[0]);
        const lat = Number(coord[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) continue;
        refLon += lon;
        refLat += lat;
        points.push([lon, lat]);
      }
      if (points.length < 3) {
        return points;
      }
      refLon /= points.length;
      refLat /= points.length;
      const planar = points.map((coord) => transportToPlanarPoint(coord[0], coord[1], refLon, refLat));
      const thresholdRad = toRad(Number(laneCfg.turnAngleThresholdDeg) || 7);
      const baseSubdivisions =
        qualityKey === "low"
          ? laneCfg.curveSubdivisionsLow
          : (qualityKey === "medium" ? laneCfg.curveSubdivisionsMedium : laneCfg.curveSubdivisionsHigh);
      const maxTransitionM = Number(laneCfg.maxTransitionM) || 22;
      const minTransitionM = Number(laneCfg.minTransitionM) || 4;
      const out = [planar[0]];
      for (let i = 1; i < planar.length - 1; i += 1) {
        const prev = planar[i - 1];
        const cur = planar[i];
        const next = planar[i + 1];
        const inVec = transportNormalizeVec2(cur.x - prev.x, cur.y - prev.y);
        const outVec = transportNormalizeVec2(next.x - cur.x, next.y - cur.y);
        const lenIn = transportDistance2D(prev, cur);
        const lenOut = transportDistance2D(cur, next);
        if (!inVec || !outVec || lenIn < 0.15 || lenOut < 0.15) {
          out.push(cur);
          continue;
        }
        const turnAbs = Math.abs(transportSignedAngleRad(inVec, outVec));
        if (!Number.isFinite(turnAbs) || turnAbs < thresholdRad) {
          out.push(cur);
          continue;
        }
        let transitionM = Math.min(lenIn, lenOut, maxTransitionM);
        const turnRatio = clamp(turnAbs / Math.PI, 0, 1);
        transitionM = clamp(
          transitionM * (0.24 + 0.5 * turnRatio),
          Math.min(minTransitionM, Math.min(lenIn, lenOut) * 0.45),
          maxTransitionM
        );
        if (!Number.isFinite(transitionM) || transitionM < 0.2) {
          out.push(cur);
          continue;
        }
        const start = {
          x: cur.x - inVec.x * transitionM,
          y: cur.y - inVec.y * transitionM,
        };
        const end = {
          x: cur.x + outVec.x * transitionM,
          y: cur.y + outVec.y * transitionM,
        };
        const prevOut = out[out.length - 1];
        if (!prevOut || transportDistance2D(prevOut, start) > 0.12) {
          out.push(start);
        }
        const sampleCount = clamp(
          Math.round(baseSubdivisions * (0.45 + turnRatio * 1.25)),
          2,
          24
        );
        const curve = sampleClothoidLikeConnector2D(
          start,
          end,
          inVec,
          outVec,
          sampleCount,
          transitionM * 0.82
        );
        out.push(...curve);
        out.push(end);
      }
      out.push(planar[planar.length - 1]);
      const simplified = [];
      for (const p of out) {
        if (!p || !Number.isFinite(p.x) || !Number.isFinite(p.y)) continue;
        if (simplified.length > 0 && transportDistance2D(simplified[simplified.length - 1], p) < 0.06) {
          continue;
        }
        simplified.push(p);
      }
      return simplified.map((p) => {
        const ll = transportFromPlanarPoint(p.x, p.y, refLon, refLat);
        return [ll.lon, ll.lat];
      });
    }

    function offsetPolylineCoordinatesMeters(coords, offsetM) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length < 2 || !Number.isFinite(offsetM) || Math.abs(offsetM) < 0.01) {
        return Array.isArray(coords) ? coords : [];
      }
      let refLon = 0;
      let refLat = 0;
      const points = [];
      for (const coord of coords) {
        if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) continue;
        const lon = Number(coord[0]);
        const lat = Number(coord[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) continue;
        refLon += lon;
        refLat += lat;
        points.push([lon, lat]);
      }
      if (points.length < 2) {
        return points;
      }
      refLon /= points.length;
      refLat /= points.length;
      const planar = points.map((coord) => transportToPlanarPoint(coord[0], coord[1], refLon, refLat));
      const normals = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < planar.length - 1; i += 1) {
        const a = planar[i];
        const b = planar[i + 1];
        const dir = transportNormalizeVec2(b.x - a.x, b.y - a.y);
        if (!dir) {
          normals.push({ x: 0, y: 0 });
          continue;
        }
        normals.push({ x: -dir.y, y: dir.x });
      }
      const outPlanar = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < planar.length; i += 1) {
        const base = planar[i];
        let nx = 0;
        let ny = 0;
        let miterScale = 1;
        if (i === 0) {
          nx = normals[0] ? normals[0].x : 0;
          ny = normals[0] ? normals[0].y : 0;
        } else if (i === planar.length - 1) {
          nx = normals[normals.length - 1] ? normals[normals.length - 1].x : 0;
          ny = normals[normals.length - 1] ? normals[normals.length - 1].y : 0;
        } else {
          const nA = normals[i - 1] || { x: 0, y: 0 };
          const nB = normals[i] || { x: 0, y: 0 };
          const m = transportNormalizeVec2(nA.x + nB.x, nA.y + nB.y);
          if (m) {
            nx = m.x;
            ny = m.y;
            const denom = nx * nB.x + ny * nB.y;
            if (Math.abs(denom) > 1e-5) {
              miterScale = clamp(1 / denom, -3.2, 3.2);
            }
          } else {
            nx = nB.x;
            ny = nB.y;
          }
        }
        outPlanar.push({
          x: base.x + nx * offsetM * miterScale,
          y: base.y + ny * offsetM * miterScale,
        });
      }
      const out = [];
      for (const p of outPlanar) {
        const ll = transportFromPlanarPoint(p.x, p.y, refLon, refLat);
        out.push([ll.lon, ll.lat]);
      }
      return out;
    }

    function inferTransportLaneCount(attrs, widthM) {
      const safe = attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {};
      const laneRaw = safe.lanes != null ? Number(safe.lanes) : Number.NaN;
      if (Number.isFinite(laneRaw) && laneRaw > 0) {
        return clamp(Math.round(laneRaw), 1, 8);
      }
      const turnLanes =
        safe["turn:lanes"] ||
        safe["turn:lanes:forward"] ||
        safe["turn:lanes:backward"] ||
        "";
      if (typeof turnLanes === "string" && turnLanes.trim().length > 0) {
        const inferred = String(turnLanes).split("|").filter(Boolean).length;
        if (inferred > 0) {
          return clamp(inferred, 1, 8);
        }
      }
      const width = Number.isFinite(Number(widthM)) ? Number(widthM) : 5.5;
      return clamp(Math.round(width / 3.35), 1, 8);
    }

    function buildRoadEndpointEntriesForJunctions(coords, widthM, laneWidthM, laneCount, feature) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length < 2) {
        return [];
      }
      const entries = [];
      const quantize = (value, scale) => Math.round(Number(value) * scale);
      const attrs = feature && feature.attrs && typeof feature.attrs === "object" ? feature.attrs : {};
      const stackKey = buildTransportStackKey("road", attrs, feature && feature.zMode);
      const candidateFeatureKey =
        (feature && (feature.id || feature.osmId || feature.gmlId || feature.featureId)) ||
        attrs.id ||
        attrs["@id"] ||
        attrs["gml:id"] ||
        attrs.gml_id ||
        attrs.osm_id ||
        attrs["osm:id"] ||
        "";
      const fallbackFeatureKey =
        Array.isArray(coords[0]) &&
        Array.isArray(coords[coords.length - 1]) &&
        coords[0].length >= 2 &&
        coords[coords.length - 1].length >= 2
          ? String(quantize(coords[0][0], 1e5)) +
            ":" +
            String(quantize(coords[0][1], 1e5)) +
            "->" +
            String(quantize(coords[coords.length - 1][0], 1e5)) +
            ":" +
            String(quantize(coords[coords.length - 1][1], 1e5))
          : "";
      const featureKey = String(candidateFeatureKey || fallbackFeatureKey || "").slice(0, 120);
      const buildEndpoint = (pivot, neighbor, endpointRole) => {
        if (!Array.isArray(pivot) || !Array.isArray(neighbor) || pivot.length < 2 || neighbor.length < 2) {
          return null;
        }
        const lon = Number(pivot[0]);
        const lat = Number(pivot[1]);
        const nLon = Number(neighbor[0]);
        const nLat = Number(neighbor[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat) || !Number.isFinite(nLon) || !Number.isFinite(nLat)) {
          return null;
        }
        const nLocal = transportToPlanarPoint(nLon, nLat, lon, lat);
        const vec = transportNormalizeVec2(nLocal.x, nLocal.y);
        if (!vec) return null;
        return {
          key: String(quantize(lon, 1e5)) + ":" + String(quantize(lat, 1e5)) + "|" + stackKey,
          lon,
          lat,
          dirX: vec.x,
          dirY: vec.y,
          widthM: Number.isFinite(widthM) ? widthM : 5.5,
          laneWidthM: Number.isFinite(laneWidthM) ? laneWidthM : 3.2,
          laneCount: Number.isFinite(laneCount) ? laneCount : 1,
          featureKey,
          stackKey,
          endpointRole: endpointRole || "",
        };
      };
      const start = buildEndpoint(coords[0], coords[1], "start");
      const end = buildEndpoint(coords[coords.length - 1], coords[coords.length - 2], "end");
      if (start) entries.push(start);
      if (end) entries.push(end);
      return entries;
    }

    function appendDrapedPolygon(builder, coordinates, className, centerECEF, offsetOverrideM) {
      if (!builder || !Array.isArray(builder.positions) || !Array.isArray(builder.indices)) {
        return 0;
      }
      if (!Array.isArray(coordinates) || coordinates.length < 3) {
        return 0;
      }
      const scopeBounds = getActiveWardBounds();
      const ring = coordinates.slice();
      if (ring.length > 3) {
        const first = ring[0];
        const last = ring[ring.length - 1];
        if (
          Array.isArray(first) &&
          Array.isArray(last) &&
          first.length >= 2 &&
          last.length >= 2 &&
          Number(first[0]) === Number(last[0]) &&
          Number(first[1]) === Number(last[1])
        ) {
          ring.pop();
        }
      }
      if (ring.length < 3) {
        return 0;
      }
      const offsetM = Number.isFinite(offsetOverrideM) ? Number(offsetOverrideM) : getTransportOffsetM(className);
      const startVertex = builder.positions.length / 3;
      for (const coord of ring) {
        if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) continue;
        const lon = Number(coord[0]);
        const lat = Number(coord[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) continue;
        if (!isWithinAnyBounds(lon, lat, scopeBounds)) continue;
        let heightM = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lon, lat);
        if (!Number.isFinite(heightM)) {
          heightM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
        }
        const point = lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM + offsetM);
        builder.positions.push(
          point.x - centerECEF.x,
          point.y - centerECEF.y,
          point.z - centerECEF.z
        );
      }
      const vertexCount = builder.positions.length / 3 - startVertex;
      if (vertexCount < 3) {
        return 0;
      }
      for (let i = 1; i < vertexCount - 1; i += 1) {
        builder.indices.push(startVertex, startVertex + i, startVertex + i + 1);
      }
      return 1;
    }

    function appendLaneBasedRoadFeature(builder, feature, coordinates, centerECEF, qualityKey, laneCfg) {
      const attrs = feature && feature.attrs && typeof feature.attrs === "object" ? feature.attrs : {};
      const sourceCoords = Array.isArray(coordinates) ? coordinates : [];
      if (sourceCoords.length < 2) {
        return { appended: 0, endpointEntries: [] };
      }
      const smoothedCoords = smoothTransportRoadCoordinates(sourceCoords, qualityKey, laneCfg);
      const totalWidthM = inferTransportWidthM("road", null, feature && feature.widthM);
      const rawLaneCount = inferTransportLaneCount(attrs, totalWidthM);
      const laneCap =
        qualityKey === "low"
          ? laneCfg.maxLanesLow
          : (qualityKey === "medium" ? laneCfg.maxLanesMedium : laneCfg.maxLanesHigh);
      const laneCount = clamp(rawLaneCount, 1, laneCap);
      const laneWidthM = clamp(totalWidthM / Math.max(1, laneCount), 2.4, 4.6);
      const laneRenderWidthM = laneWidthM * laneCfg.laneInsetFactor;
      let appendedAny = 0;
      if (laneCount <= 1) {
        appendedAny = appendDrapedRibbon(
          builder,
          smoothedCoords,
          totalWidthM,
          "road",
          centerECEF,
          feature,
          getTransportOffsetM("road")
        );
      } else {
        for (let laneIndex = 0; laneIndex < laneCount; laneIndex += 1) {
          const signedIndex = laneIndex - (laneCount - 1) * 0.5;
          const offsetM = signedIndex * laneWidthM;
          const offsetCoords = offsetPolylineCoordinatesMeters(smoothedCoords, offsetM);
          if (!Array.isArray(offsetCoords) || offsetCoords.length < 2) {
            continue;
          }
          const appended = appendDrapedRibbon(
            builder,
            offsetCoords,
            laneRenderWidthM,
            "road",
            centerECEF,
            feature,
            getTransportOffsetM("road") + 0.012
          );
          if (appended > 0) {
            appendedAny += 1;
          }
        }
      }
      const endpointEntries = isRoadEligibleForLaneJunctions(attrs, feature && feature.zMode)
        ? buildRoadEndpointEntriesForJunctions(
          smoothedCoords,
          totalWidthM,
          laneWidthM,
          laneCount,
          feature
        )
        : [];
      return {
        appended: appendedAny > 0 ? 1 : 0,
        endpointEntries,
      };
    }

    function buildLaneMeshRoadJunctions(junctionBuilder, turnBuilder, endpointEntries, centerECEF, qualityKey, laneCfg) {
      if (!Array.isArray(endpointEntries) || endpointEntries.length < 3) {
        return { junctionCount: 0, turnCount: 0 };
      }
      const groups = new Map();
      for (const entry of endpointEntries) {
        if (!entry || !entry.key) continue;
        if (!groups.has(entry.key)) {
          groups.set(entry.key, []);
        }
        groups.get(entry.key).push(entry);
      }
      const minTurnAngleRad = toRad(Number(laneCfg.minTurnChannelAngleDeg) || 28);
      const maxTurnAngleRad = toRad(Number(laneCfg.maxTurnChannelAngleDeg) || 164);
      const maxAdjacentTurnGapRad = toRad(Number(laneCfg.maxAdjacentTurnGapDeg) || 132);
      const turnLimit =
        qualityKey === "low"
          ? laneCfg.maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionLow
          : (qualityKey === "medium" ? laneCfg.maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionMedium : laneCfg.maxTurnChannelsPerJunctionHigh);
      const junctionSides =
        qualityKey === "low"
          ? laneCfg.junctionSidesLow
          : (qualityKey === "medium" ? laneCfg.junctionSidesMedium : laneCfg.junctionSidesHigh);
      const maxRawEndpoints =
        qualityKey === "low"
          ? laneCfg.maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionLow
          : (qualityKey === "medium" ? laneCfg.maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionMedium : laneCfg.maxRawEndpointsPerJunctionHigh);
      const maxUniqueEndpoints =
        qualityKey === "low"
          ? laneCfg.maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionLow
          : (qualityKey === "medium" ? laneCfg.maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionMedium : laneCfg.maxUniqueEndpointsPerJunctionHigh);
      const maxJunctionRadiusM =
        qualityKey === "low"
          ? laneCfg.maxJunctionRadiusMLow
          : (qualityKey === "medium" ? laneCfg.maxJunctionRadiusMMedium : laneCfg.maxJunctionRadiusMHigh);
      const curveSubdivisions =
        qualityKey === "low"
          ? laneCfg.curveSubdivisionsLow
          : (qualityKey === "medium" ? laneCfg.curveSubdivisionsMedium : laneCfg.curveSubdivisionsHigh);
      let junctionCount = 0;
      let turnCount = 0;
      for (const rawGroup of groups.values()) {
        if (!Array.isArray(rawGroup) || rawGroup.length < 3) {
          continue;
        }
        if (rawGroup.length > Math.max(4, Number(maxRawEndpoints) || 16)) {
          continue;
        }
        let group = dedupeJunctionEndpointEntries(
          rawGroup,
          laneCfg.junctionHeadingDedupeDeg,
          Math.max(3, (Number(maxUniqueEndpoints) || 7) + 3)
        );
        if (!Array.isArray(group) || group.length < 3) {
          continue;
        }
        if (group.length > Math.max(3, Number(maxUniqueEndpoints) || 7)) {
          group = group
            .slice()
            .sort((a, b) => {
              const aw = Number(a.widthM) || 0;
              const bw = Number(b.widthM) || 0;
              if (bw !== aw) return bw - aw;
              return (Number(b.laneCount) || 0) - (Number(a.laneCount) || 0);
            })
            .slice(0, Math.max(3, Number(maxUniqueEndpoints) || 7))
            .sort((a, b) => Number(a.angleRad) - Number(b.angleRad));
        }
        if (group.length < 3) {
          continue;
        }
        let lon = 0;
        let lat = 0;
        let avgHalfWidth = 0;
        for (const item of group) {
          lon += Number(item.lon) || 0;
          lat += Number(item.lat) || 0;
          avgHalfWidth += (Number(item.widthM) || 5.5) * 0.5;
        }
        lon /= group.length;
        lat /= group.length;
        avgHalfWidth /= group.length;
        let radiusM = clamp(
