          avgHalfWidth * laneCfg.junctionRadiusScale + 1.3,
          2.2,
          Number.isFinite(Number(maxJunctionRadiusM)) ? Number(maxJunctionRadiusM) : 9
        );
        if (group.length >= 7) {
          radiusM *= 0.84;
        }
        const renderSides = clamp(
          Math.max(Number(junctionSides) || 8, Math.round(group.length * 2)),
          6,
          24
        );
        const ring = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < renderSides; i += 1) {
          const angle = (Math.PI * 2 * i) / renderSides;
          const local = transportFromPlanarPoint(
            Math.cos(angle) * radiusM,
            Math.sin(angle) * radiusM,
            lon,
            lat
          );
          ring.push([local.lon, local.lat]);
        }
        if (ring.length > 0) {
          ring.push([ring[0][0], ring[0][1]]);
        }
        const appendedJunction = appendDrapedPolygon(
          junctionBuilder,
          ring,
          "road",
          centerECEF,
          getTransportOffsetM("road") + 0.018
        );
        if (appendedJunction > 0) {
          junctionCount += 1;
        }
        const anchorRadiusM = radiusM * laneCfg.turnChannelRadiusScale;
        let channelBuilt = 0;
        for (let i = 0; i < group.length; i += 1) {
          if (channelBuilt >= turnLimit) break;
          const a = group[i];
          const b = group[(i + 1) % group.length];
          if (!a || !b) {
            continue;
          }
          if (a.featureKey && b.featureKey && a.featureKey === b.featureKey) {
            continue;
          }
          const dirA = transportNormalizeVec2(a.dirX, a.dirY);
          const dirB = transportNormalizeVec2(b.dirX, b.dirY);
          if (!dirA || !dirB) continue;
          const gapRad = transportNormalizeAngleRad((Number(b.angleRad) || 0) - (Number(a.angleRad) || 0));
          const turnAbs = Math.abs(transportSignedAngleRad(dirA, dirB));
          if (
            !Number.isFinite(gapRad) ||
            gapRad < minTurnAngleRad ||
            gapRad > maxAdjacentTurnGapRad ||
            !Number.isFinite(turnAbs) ||
            turnAbs < minTurnAngleRad ||
            turnAbs > maxTurnAngleRad
          ) {
            continue;
          }
          const start = transportFromPlanarPoint(
            dirA.x * anchorRadiusM,
            dirA.y * anchorRadiusM,
            lon,
            lat
          );
          const end = transportFromPlanarPoint(
            dirB.x * anchorRadiusM,
            dirB.y * anchorRadiusM,
            lon,
            lat
          );
          const startPt = { x: dirA.x * anchorRadiusM, y: dirA.y * anchorRadiusM };
          const endPt = { x: dirB.x * anchorRadiusM, y: dirB.y * anchorRadiusM };
          const channelCurve = sampleClothoidLikeConnector2D(
            startPt,
            endPt,
            dirA,
            dirB,
            clamp(Math.round(curveSubdivisions * (0.32 + gapRad / Math.PI)), 2, 18),
            anchorRadiusM * 0.76
          );
          const coords = [[start.lon, start.lat]];
          for (const p of channelCurve) {
            const ll = transportFromPlanarPoint(p.x, p.y, lon, lat);
            coords.push([ll.lon, ll.lat]);
          }
          coords.push([end.lon, end.lat]);
          const channelWidthM = clamp(
            ((Number(a.laneWidthM) || 3.2) + (Number(b.laneWidthM) || 3.2)) * 0.5 * 0.82,
            2.0,
            3.8
          );
          const appendedTurn = appendDrapedRibbon(
            turnBuilder,
            coords,
            channelWidthM,
            "road",
            centerECEF,
            { attrs: { junction: true }, zMode: "drape" },
            getTransportOffsetM("road") + 0.028
          );
          if (appendedTurn > 0) {
            channelBuilt += 1;
            turnCount += 1;
          }
        }
      }
      return { junctionCount, turnCount };
    }

    function appendDrapedRibbon(builder, coordinates, widthM, className, centerECEF, featureMeta, offsetOverrideM) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coordinates) || coordinates.length < 2) {
        return 0;
      }
      const scopeBounds = getActiveWardBounds();
      const halfWidth = Math.max(0.15, Number(widthM) * 0.5);
      const offsetM = Number.isFinite(offsetOverrideM) ? Number(offsetOverrideM) : getTransportOffsetM(className);
      const attrs =
        featureMeta && featureMeta.attrs && typeof featureMeta.attrs === "object"
          ? featureMeta.attrs
          : {};
      const zMode = featureMeta && typeof featureMeta.zMode === "string" ? featureMeta.zMode : "drape";
      const worldPoint = new THREE.Vector3();
      const maxGapM = Number.isFinite(Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.maxSegmentGapM))
        ? clamp(Number(TRANSPORT_CONFIG.maxSegmentGapM), 20, 240)
        : 80;
      const segments = [];
      let currentSegment = [];
      const flushSegment = () => {
        if (currentSegment.length >= 2) {
          segments.push(currentSegment);
        }
        currentSegment = [];
      };
      for (const coord of coordinates) {
        if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) {
          flushSegment();
          continue;
        }
        const lon = Number(coord[0]);
        const lat = Number(coord[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat) || !isWithinAnyBounds(lon, lat, scopeBounds)) {
          flushSegment();
          continue;
        }
        let heightM = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lon, lat);
        if (!Number.isFinite(heightM)) {
          heightM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
        }
        worldPoint.copy(lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM + offsetM));
        const nextPoint = worldPoint.clone();
        const lastPoint = currentSegment.length > 0 ? currentSegment[currentSegment.length - 1] : null;
        if (lastPoint) {
          const jumpM = nextPoint.distanceTo(lastPoint);
          if (!Number.isFinite(jumpM) || jumpM > maxGapM) {
            flushSegment();
          } else if (jumpM < 0.08) {
            continue;
          }
        }
        currentSegment.push(nextPoint);
      }
      flushSegment();
      if (segments.length <= 0) {
        return 0;
      }
      const tangent = new THREE.Vector3();
      const up = new THREE.Vector3();
      const right = new THREE.Vector3();
      let appendedAny = 0;
      for (const points of segments) {
        if (!Array.isArray(points) || points.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        let totalLengthM = 0;
        for (let i = 1; i < points.length; i += 1) {
          totalLengthM += points[i].distanceTo(points[i - 1]);
        }
        const elevationProfile = inferTransportElevationProfileM(className, attrs, zMode, totalLengthM);
        const elevatedPoints = [];
        let profileDistanceM = 0;
        for (let i = 0; i < points.length; i += 1) {
          if (i > 0) {
            profileDistanceM += points[i].distanceTo(points[i - 1]);
          }
          const t = totalLengthM > 1e-4 ? clamp(profileDistanceM / totalLengthM, 0, 1) : 0;
          const extraM = elevationProfile.startM + (elevationProfile.endM - elevationProfile.startM) * t;
          if (Math.abs(extraM) <= 1e-4) {
            elevatedPoints.push(points[i]);
            continue;
          }
          const upAtPoint = points[i].clone().normalize();
          elevatedPoints.push(points[i].clone().addScaledVector(upAtPoint, extraM));
        }
        const startVertex = builder.positions.length / 3;
        const startPositionLen = builder.positions.length;
        const startLineLen = Array.isArray(builder.lineDistance) ? builder.lineDistance.length : 0;
        const startSideLen = Array.isArray(builder.side) ? builder.side.length : 0;
        let runningDistanceM = 0;
        for (let i = 0; i < elevatedPoints.length; i += 1) {
          const point = elevatedPoints[i];
          if (i > 0) {
            runningDistanceM += elevatedPoints[i].distanceTo(elevatedPoints[i - 1]);
          }
          const prev = elevatedPoints[Math.max(0, i - 1)];
          const next = elevatedPoints[Math.min(elevatedPoints.length - 1, i + 1)];
          tangent.copy(next).sub(prev);
          up.copy(point).normalize();
          tangent.addScaledVector(up, -tangent.dot(up));
          if (tangent.lengthSq() < 1e-10) {
            continue;
          }
          tangent.normalize();
          right.crossVectors(tangent, up);
          if (right.lengthSq() < 1e-10) {
            continue;
          }
          right.normalize();
          const leftPoint = point.clone().addScaledVector(right, halfWidth);
          const rightPoint = point.clone().addScaledVector(right, -halfWidth);
          builder.positions.push(
            leftPoint.x - centerECEF.x,
            leftPoint.y - centerECEF.y,
            leftPoint.z - centerECEF.z,
            rightPoint.x - centerECEF.x,
            rightPoint.y - centerECEF.y,
            rightPoint.z - centerECEF.z
          );
          if (Array.isArray(builder.lineDistance)) {
            builder.lineDistance.push(runningDistanceM, runningDistanceM);
          }
          if (Array.isArray(builder.side)) {
            builder.side.push(1, -1);
          }
        }
        const vertexPairs = Math.floor((builder.positions.length / 3 - startVertex) / 2);
        if (vertexPairs < 2) {
          builder.positions.length = startPositionLen;
          if (Array.isArray(builder.lineDistance)) {
            builder.lineDistance.length = startLineLen;
          }
          if (Array.isArray(builder.side)) {
            builder.side.length = startSideLen;
          }
          continue;
        }
        for (let i = 0; i < vertexPairs - 1; i += 1) {
          const a = startVertex + i * 2;
          const b = a + 1;
          const c = a + 2;
          const d = a + 3;
          builder.indices.push(a, c, b);
          builder.indices.push(b, c, d);
        }
        appendedAny = 1;
      }
      return appendedAny;
    }

    function createTransportGeometry(build) {
      if (!build || !Array.isArray(build.positions) || !Array.isArray(build.indices)) {
        return null;
      }
      if (build.positions.length < 6 || build.indices.length < 3) {
        return null;
      }
      const geometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
      geometry.setAttribute("position", new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(build.positions, 3));
      geometry.setIndex(build.indices);
      const vertexCount = build.positions.length / 3;
      if (Array.isArray(build.lineDistance) && build.lineDistance.length === vertexCount) {
        geometry.setAttribute("lineDistance", new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(build.lineDistance, 1));
      }
      if (Array.isArray(build.side) && build.side.length === vertexCount) {
        geometry.setAttribute("side", new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(build.side, 1));
      }
      geometry.computeVertexNormals();
      return geometry;
    }

    function buildTransportTileGroup(tile, features, sourceLabel) {
      const manager = buildTransportManager();
      const renderState = resolveTransportRoadRenderState(manager);
      manager.renderModeActive = renderState.mode;
      manager.renderModeReason = renderState.reason;
      manager.laneMeshQuality = renderState.quality;
      const bounds = tile.bounds;
      const centerECEF = lonLatToECEF(
        (bounds.west + bounds.east) * 0.5,
        (bounds.south + bounds.north) * 0.5,
        0
      );
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.position.copy(centerECEF);
      group.name = "transportTile:" + tile.key;
      const builders = {
        road: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        sidewalk: { positions: [], indices: [], lineDistance: [], side: [] },
        crosswalk: { positions: [], indices: [], lineDistance: [], side: [] },
        steps: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        pedestrian: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        junction_surface: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        turn_channel: { positions: [], indices: [] },
      };
      const counts = { road: 0, sidewalk: 0, crosswalk: 0, steps: 0, pedestrian: 0, total: 0 };
      const sourceCounts = { plateau: 0, osm: 0 };
      const endpointEntries = [];
      const sidewalkOverlapKeys = new Set();
      for (const feature of features) {
        if (!feature || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) || feature.coordinates.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        const cls = String(feature.featureClass || "").toLowerCase();
        if (cls !== "sidewalk") {
          continue;
        }
        const coords = getSimplifiedTransportCoordinates(
          tile && tile.key ? tile.key : "",
          feature,
          manager.simplifyProfileKey,
          manager.simplifyToleranceM
        );
        const overlapKey = buildWalkwayOverlapKey(feature, coords);
        if (overlapKey) {
          sidewalkOverlapKeys.add(overlapKey);
        }
      }
      const seenWalkwayOverlapKeys = new Set();
      for (const feature of features) {
        if (!feature || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) || feature.coordinates.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        const cls = builders[feature.featureClass] ? feature.featureClass : "road";
        let coords = feature.coordinates;
        if (cls === "road" || cls === "sidewalk") {
          coords = getSimplifiedTransportCoordinates(
            tile && tile.key ? tile.key : "",
            feature,
            manager.simplifyProfileKey,
            manager.simplifyToleranceM
          );
        }
        if (cls === "sidewalk" || cls === "pedestrian") {
          const overlapKey = buildWalkwayOverlapKey(feature, coords);
          if (overlapKey) {
            if (cls === "pedestrian" && sidewalkOverlapKeys.has(overlapKey)) {
              continue;
            }
            if (seenWalkwayOverlapKeys.has(overlapKey)) {
              continue;
            }
            seenWalkwayOverlapKeys.add(overlapKey);
          }
        }
        let appended = 0;
        if (cls === "road" && renderState.mode === "lane_mesh") {
          const laneBuilt = appendLaneBasedRoadFeature(
            builders.road,
            feature,
            coords,
            centerECEF,
            renderState.quality,
            renderState.laneCfg
          );
          appended = laneBuilt && Number(laneBuilt.appended) > 0 ? Number(laneBuilt.appended) : 0;
          if (laneBuilt && Array.isArray(laneBuilt.endpointEntries) && laneBuilt.endpointEntries.length > 0) {
            endpointEntries.push(...laneBuilt.endpointEntries);
          }
        } else {
          appended = appendDrapedRibbon(
            builders[cls],
            coords,
            inferTransportWidthM(cls, null, feature.widthM),
            cls,
            centerECEF,
            feature
          );
        }
        if (appended > 0) {
          counts[cls] += appended;
          counts.total += appended;
          const source = feature.source === "plateau" ? "plateau" : "osm";
          sourceCounts[source] += appended;
        }
      }
      const enableJunctionOverlays = !(
        renderState &&
        renderState.laneCfg &&
        renderState.laneCfg.enableJunctionOverlays === false
      );
      if (renderState.mode === "lane_mesh" && enableJunctionOverlays && endpointEntries.length >= 3) {
        const extras = buildLaneMeshRoadJunctions(
          builders.junction_surface,
          builders.turn_channel,
          endpointEntries,
          centerECEF,
          renderState.quality,
          renderState.laneCfg
        );
        const junctionCount = Number(extras && extras.junctionCount) || 0;
        const turnCount = Number(extras && extras.turnCount) || 0;
        if (junctionCount > 0 || turnCount > 0) {
          counts.road += junctionCount + turnCount;
          counts.total += junctionCount + turnCount;
        }
      }
      for (const cls of Object.keys(builders)) {
        const geometry = createTransportGeometry(builders[cls]);
        if (!geometry) {
          continue;
        }
        const material =
          (cls === "road" && renderState.mode === "lane_mesh" && manager.materials.road_lane_mesh) ||
          (cls === "junction_surface" && manager.materials.junction_surface) ||
          (cls === "turn_channel" && manager.materials.turn_channel) ||
          (cls === "sidewalk" && manager.materials.sidewalk_stylized) ||
          (cls === "crosswalk" && manager.materials.crosswalk_stylized) ||
          manager.materials[cls] ||
          manager.materials.road;
        const mesh = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, material);
        mesh.frustumCulled = true;
        let renderOrder = 40;
        if (cls === "crosswalk") {
          renderOrder = 64;
        } else if (cls === "sidewalk" || cls === "turn_channel") {
          renderOrder = 41;
        }
        mesh.renderOrder = renderOrder;
        group.add(mesh);
      }
      return {
        group,
        counts,
        sourceCounts,
      };
    }

    function addTransportStats(target, delta, sign) {
      if (!target || !delta) {
        return;
      }
      const mul = sign < 0 ? -1 : 1;
      const keys = ["road", "sidewalk", "crosswalk", "steps", "pedestrian", "total"];
      for (const key of keys) {
        const base = Number.isFinite(target[key]) ? target[key] : 0;
        const add = Number.isFinite(delta[key]) ? delta[key] : 0;
        target[key] = Math.max(0, base + add * mul);
      }
    }

    function disposeTransportGroupGeometry(group) {
      if (!group || typeof group.traverse !== "function") {
        return;
      }
      try {
        group.traverse((obj) => {
          if (!obj || !obj.isMesh) {
            return;
          }
          if (obj.geometry && typeof obj.geometry.dispose === "function") {
            obj.geometry.dispose();
          }
        });
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
    }

    async function loadTransportTile(zoom, x, y) {
      const manager = buildTransportManager();
      if (!(manager.failureBackoffByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureBackoffByKey = new Map();
      }
      if (!(manager.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureReasonByKey = new Map();
      }
      const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      if (manager.pending.has(key) || manager.tiles.has(key)) {
        return;
      }
      const buildModeAtStart = String(manager.renderBuildMode || "ribbon");
      const buildGenerationAtStart = Number(manager.renderBuildGeneration) || 0;
      const backoffUntil = Number(manager.failureBackoffByKey.get(key)) || 0;
      if (backoffUntil > Date.now()) {
        return;
      }
      manager.pending.add(key);
      const bounds = slippyBounds(x, y, zoom);
      try {
        const tileIndex =
          TRANSPORT_MANIFEST && TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.tileIndex && typeof TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.tileIndex === "object"
            ? TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.tileIndex
            : null;
        const strictTileIndex =
          (TRANSPORT_CONFIG && TRANSPORT_CONFIG.strictTileIndex === true) ||
          (TRANSPORT_MANIFEST && TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.strictTileIndex === true);
        if (strictTileIndex && tileIndex && Object.keys(tileIndex).length > 0 && !tileIndex[key]) {
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 60 * 1000);
          manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, "not_indexed");
          return;
        }
        const result = await fetchTransportFeaturesForTile(zoom, x, y, bounds);
        const features = Array.isArray(result.features) ? result.features : [];
        if (features.length <= 0) {
          manager.failed += 1;
          manager.warning = "Transport tile failed: " + key;
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 15000);
          manager.failureReasonByKey.set(
            key,
            Array.isArray(result.failures) && result.failures.length > 0
              ? String(result.failures[0])
              : "no_data"
          );
          debugLog("transport:tile_failed", {
            key,
            failures: result.failures || ["no_data"],
          });
          return;
        }
        const built = buildTransportTileGroup({ key, z: zoom, x, y, bounds }, features, result.source || "none");
        if (!built || !built.group || built.counts.total <= 0) {
          return;
        }
        const buildModeNow = String(manager.renderBuildMode || "ribbon");
        const buildGenerationNow = Number(manager.renderBuildGeneration) || 0;
        if (
          buildGenerationNow !== buildGenerationAtStart ||
          buildModeNow !== buildModeAtStart ||
          !manager.desired.has(key) ||
          manager.tiles.has(key)
        ) {
          disposeTransportGroupGeometry(built.group);
          debugLog("transport:tile_discarded_stale", {
            key,
            requestedMode: buildModeAtStart,
            activeMode: buildModeNow,
            requestedGeneration: buildGenerationAtStart,
            activeGeneration: buildGenerationNow,
            desired: manager.desired.has(key),
            alreadyLoaded: manager.tiles.has(key),
          });
          return;
        }
        manager.group.add(built.group);
        const tile = {
          key,
          z: zoom,
          x,
          y,
          bounds,
          group: built.group,
          counts: built.counts,
          sourceCounts: built.sourceCounts,
          features,
          lastWantedMs: Date.now(),
          renderBuildMode: buildModeAtStart,
          renderBuildGeneration: buildGenerationAtStart,
        };
        manager.tiles.set(key, tile);
        manager.loaded += 1;
        manager.ready = true;
        manager.failureBackoffByKey.delete(key);
        manager.failureReasonByKey.delete(key);
        manager.sourceMix.plateau += Number(tile.sourceCounts.plateau) || 0;
        manager.sourceMix.osm += Number(tile.sourceCounts.osm) || 0;
        addTransportStats(manager.featureCounts, tile.counts, 1);
        debugLog("transport:tile_loaded", {
          key,
          source: result.source || "mixed",
          sourceBreakdown:
            result && result.sourceBreakdown && typeof result.sourceBreakdown === "object"
              ? result.sourceBreakdown
              : null,
          featureCount: tile.counts.total,
          counts: tile.counts,
          renderMode: manager.renderModeActive || "ribbon",
          renderQuality: manager.laneMeshQuality || "off",
          renderReason: manager.renderModeReason || "n/a",
        });
      } finally {
        manager.pending.delete(key);
      }
    }

    function evictTransportTile(tile, reason) {
      const manager = state.transportManager;
      if (!manager || !tile) {
        return;
      }
      try {
        if (tile.group && tile.group.parent) {
          tile.group.parent.remove(tile.group);
        }
        if (tile.group) {
          tile.group.traverse((obj) => {
            if (!obj || !obj.isMesh) {
              return;
            }
            if (obj.geometry && typeof obj.geometry.dispose === "function") {
              obj.geometry.dispose();
            }
          });
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      manager.tiles.delete(tile.key);
      manager.sourceMix.plateau = Math.max(0, (manager.sourceMix.plateau || 0) - (Number(tile.sourceCounts && tile.sourceCounts.plateau) || 0));
      manager.sourceMix.osm = Math.max(0, (manager.sourceMix.osm || 0) - (Number(tile.sourceCounts && tile.sourceCounts.osm) || 0));
      addTransportStats(manager.featureCounts, tile.counts, -1);
      debugLog("transport:tile_evicted", {
        key: tile.key,
        reason: reason || "evict",
      });
    }

    function clearTransportManager() {
      const manager = state.transportManager;
      if (!manager) {
        return;
      }
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        evictTransportTile(tile, "transport_reset");
      }
      manager.tiles.clear();
      manager.pending.clear();
      manager.desired.clear();
      manager.currentZoom = null;
      manager.loaded = 0;
      manager.failed = 0;
      manager.ready = false;
      manager.warning = "";
      manager.failureBackoffByKey.clear();
      manager.failureReasonByKey.clear();
      manager.sourceMix = { plateau: 0, osm: 0 };
      manager.featureCounts = { road: 0, sidewalk: 0, crosswalk: 0, steps: 0, pedestrian: 0, total: 0 };
      manager.renderModeActive = "ribbon";
      manager.renderModeReason = "reset";
      manager.laneMeshQuality = "off";
      manager.renderBuildMode = "ribbon";
      manager.renderBuildModeSwitchMs = 0;
      manager.renderBuildGeneration = 0;
      manager.lastCameraAltitudeM = 0;
      transportTileFeatureCache.clear();
      transportSimplifiedCoordinateCache.clear();
    }

    function inferTransitFeatureClassFromTags(tags, geometryType) {
      const safe = tags && typeof tags === "object" ? tags : {};
      const route = safe.route ? String(safe.route).toLowerCase() : "";
      const railway = safe.railway ? String(safe.railway).toLowerCase() : "";
      const publicTransport = safe.public_transport ? String(safe.public_transport).toLowerCase() : "";
      const highway = safe.highway ? String(safe.highway).toLowerCase() : "";
      if (geometryType === "LineString") {
        if (railway && railway !== "station" && railway !== "halt" && railway !== "tram_stop") {
          return "rail_line";
        }
        if (route === "train" || route === "subway" || route === "light_rail" || route === "monorail" || route === "tram") {
          return "rail_line";
        }
        if (route === "bus" || route === "trolleybus") {
          return "bus_route";
        }
        return "rail_line";
      }
      if (railway === "station" || railway === "halt" || railway === "tram_stop" || publicTransport === "station") {
        return "rail_station";
      }
      if (highway === "bus_stop" || route === "bus" || publicTransport === "platform" || publicTransport === "stop_position") {
        return "bus_stop";
      }
      return "rail_station";
    }

    function normalizeTransitFeature(rawFeature, sourceLabel) {
      if (!rawFeature || typeof rawFeature !== "object") {
        return null;
      }
      if (rawFeature.geometry && rawFeature.geometry.type) {
        const geometry = rawFeature.geometry;
        const properties = rawFeature.properties && typeof rawFeature.properties === "object"
          ? rawFeature.properties
          : {};
        const attrs = properties.attrs && typeof properties.attrs === "object"
          ? properties.attrs
          : (properties.tags && typeof properties.tags === "object" ? properties.tags : properties);
        const source = properties.source ? String(properties.source).toLowerCase() : sourceLabel;
        const priority = Number.isFinite(Number(properties.priority)) ? Number(properties.priority) : 0;
        const id = properties.id ? String(properties.id) : "";
        const explicitClass = properties.featureClass ? String(properties.featureClass).toLowerCase() : "";
        const zMode = properties.z_mode ? String(properties.z_mode) : (properties.zMode ? String(properties.zMode) : "");
        if (isUndergroundFeature(attrs, { zMode, includeSubway: true })) {
          return null;
        }
        const widthM = Number.isFinite(Number(properties.width_m))
          ? Number(properties.width_m)
          : (Number.isFinite(Number(properties.widthM)) ? Number(properties.widthM) : Number.NaN);
        if (geometry.type === "Point" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates) && geometry.coordinates.length >= 2) {
          const lon = Number(geometry.coordinates[0]);
          const lat = Number(geometry.coordinates[1]);
          if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) return null;
          const featureClass = explicitClass || inferTransitFeatureClassFromTags(attrs, "Point");
          return {
            id,
            source,
            featureClass: featureClass === "bus_stop" ? "bus_stop" : "rail_station",
            priority,
            attrs,
            widthM,
            geometryType: "Point",
            coordinates: [lon, lat],
          };
        }
        if (geometry.type === "MultiPoint" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates)) {
          const out = [];
          for (const coord of geometry.coordinates) {
            if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) {
              continue;
            }
            const lon = Number(coord[0]);
            const lat = Number(coord[1]);
            if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
              continue;
            }
            const featureClass = explicitClass || inferTransitFeatureClassFromTags(attrs, "Point");
            out.push({
              id,
              source,
              featureClass: featureClass === "bus_stop" ? "bus_stop" : "rail_station",
              priority,
              attrs,
              widthM,
              geometryType: "Point",
              coordinates: [lon, lat],
            });
          }
          return out.length > 0 ? out : null;
        }
        if (geometry.type === "LineString" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates) && geometry.coordinates.length >= 2) {
          const coords = geometry.coordinates
            .map((coord) => {
              if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) return null;
              const lon = Number(coord[0]);
              const lat = Number(coord[1]);
              return Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat) ? [lon, lat] : null;
            })
            .filter(Boolean);
          if (coords.length < 2) return null;
          const featureClass = explicitClass || inferTransitFeatureClassFromTags(attrs, "LineString");
          return {
            id,
            source,
            featureClass: featureClass === "bus_route" ? "bus_route" : "rail_line",
            priority,
            attrs,
            widthM,
            geometryType: "LineString",
            coordinates: coords,
          };
        }
        if (geometry.type === "MultiLineString" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates)) {
          const out = [];
          for (const line of geometry.coordinates) {
            const coords = Array.isArray(line)
              ? line
                .map((coord) => {
                  if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) return null;
                  const lon = Number(coord[0]);
                  const lat = Number(coord[1]);
                  return Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat) ? [lon, lat] : null;
                })
                .filter(Boolean)
              : [];
            if (coords.length < 2) continue;
            const featureClass = explicitClass || inferTransitFeatureClassFromTags(attrs, "LineString");
            out.push({
              id,
              source,
              featureClass: featureClass === "bus_route" ? "bus_route" : "rail_line",
              priority,
              attrs,
              widthM,
              geometryType: "LineString",
              coordinates: coords,
            });
          }
          return out.length > 0 ? out : null;
        }
      }
      return null;
    }

    function flattenNormalizedTransitFeatures(value) {
      if (!value) return [];
      if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.filter(Boolean);
      return [value];
    }

    function buildTransitFeatureMergeKey(feature) {
      if (!feature || !feature.geometryType) {
        return "";
      }
      const cls = String(feature.featureClass || "");
      if (feature.geometryType === "Point" && Array.isArray(feature.coordinates)) {
        const lon = Math.round((Number(feature.coordinates[0]) || 0) * 1e6);
        const lat = Math.round((Number(feature.coordinates[1]) || 0) * 1e6);
        return cls + "|" + String(lon) + ":" + String(lat);
      }
      if (feature.geometryType === "LineString" && Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) && feature.coordinates.length >= 2) {
        const first = feature.coordinates[0];
        const last = feature.coordinates[feature.coordinates.length - 1];
        if (!Array.isArray(first) || !Array.isArray(last)) return "";
        const a = Math.round((Number(first[0]) || 0) * 1e6) + ":" + Math.round((Number(first[1]) || 0) * 1e6);
        const b = Math.round((Number(last[0]) || 0) * 1e6) + ":" + Math.round((Number(last[1]) || 0) * 1e6);
        const width = Math.round((Number(feature.widthM) || 0) * 10);
        const orderA = a <= b ? a : b;
        const orderB = a <= b ? b : a;
        return cls + "|" + String(width) + "|" + orderA + "|" + orderB + "|" + String(feature.coordinates.length);
      }
      return "";
    }

    function synthesizeTransitLayerFallbackFromTransport(transportFeatures, bounds) {
      const features = [];
      const lineSeen = new Set();
      const pointSeen = new Set();
      const scopeBounds = bounds && typeof bounds === "object" ? [bounds] : getActiveWardBounds();
      const maxLines = 180;
      const maxPoints = 120;
      let ordinal = 0;
      for (const feature of Array.isArray(transportFeatures) ? transportFeatures : []) {
        if (features.length >= maxLines + maxPoints) {
          break;
        }
        if (!feature || String(feature.featureClass || "").toLowerCase() !== "road" || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates)) {
          continue;
        }
        const coords = feature.coordinates
          .map((coord) => {
            if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) return null;
            const lon = Number(coord[0]);
            const lat = Number(coord[1]);
            if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) return null;
            if (!isWithinAnyBounds(lon, lat, scopeBounds)) return null;
            return [lon, lat];
          })
          .filter(Boolean);
        if (coords.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        ordinal += 1;
        const asRail = ordinal % 9 === 0;
        if (lineSeen.size < maxLines) {
          const lineFeature = {
            id: "fallback_line_" + String(ordinal),
            source: "transport_fallback",
            featureClass: asRail ? "rail_line" : "bus_route",
            priority: 8,
            attrs: feature.attrs && typeof feature.attrs === "object" ? feature.attrs : {},
            widthM: asRail ? 2.2 : 1.2,
            geometryType: "LineString",
            coordinates: coords,
          };
          const lineKey = buildTransitFeatureMergeKey(lineFeature);
          if (!lineKey || !lineSeen.has(lineKey)) {
            if (lineKey) {
              lineSeen.add(lineKey);
            }
            features.push(lineFeature);
          }
        }
        if (pointSeen.size >= maxPoints) {
          continue;
        }
        const pointIndex = Math.min(coords.length - 1, Math.max(0, Math.floor(coords.length * (asRail ? 0.5 : 0.35))));
        const point = coords[pointIndex];
        if (!Array.isArray(point) || point.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        const lon = Number(point[0]);
        const lat = Number(point[1]);
        const pointClass = asRail ? "rail_station" : "bus_stop";
        const pointKey = pointClass + "|" + Math.round(lon * 1e5) + ":" + Math.round(lat * 1e5);
        if (pointSeen.has(pointKey)) {
          continue;
        }
        pointSeen.add(pointKey);
        features.push({
          id: "fallback_point_" + String(ordinal),
          source: "transport_fallback",
          featureClass: pointClass,
          priority: 9,
          attrs: {},
          widthM: Number.NaN,
          geometryType: "Point",
          coordinates: [lon, lat],
        });
      }
      return features;
    }

    function buildTransitLayerManager() {
      if (state.transitLayerManager) {
        return state.transitLayerManager;
      }
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.name = "transitLayerGroup";
      const linesGroup = new THREE.Group();
      linesGroup.name = "transitLinesGroup";
      const pointsGroup = new THREE.Group();
      pointsGroup.name = "transitPointsGroup";
      group.add(linesGroup);
      group.add(pointsGroup);
      state.scene.add(group);
      const manager = {
        group,
        linesGroup,
        pointsGroup,
        tiles: new Map(),
        pending: new Set(),
        desired: new Set(),
        failureBackoffByKey: new Map(),
        failureReasonByKey: new Map(),
        assetTemplateByClass: new Map(),
        lastTickMs: 0,
        currentZoom: null,
        loaded: 0,
        failed: 0,
        ready: false,
        warning: "",
        requestIntervalMs: Number(TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.requestIntervalMs) || 900,
        maxActiveTiles: Number(TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.maxActiveTiles) || 28,
        hysteresisMs: Number(TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.hysteresisMs) || 9000,
        featureCounts: {
          rail_line: 0,
          bus_route: 0,
          rail_station: 0,
          bus_stop: 0,
          total: 0,
        },
        materials: {
          rail_line: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xff8f2a,
            emissive: 0x442000,
            emissiveIntensity: 0.22,
            roughness: 0.9,
            metalness: 0.02,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -4,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -4,
          }),
          bus_route: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xff8f2a,
            emissive: 0x442000,
            emissiveIntensity: 0.22,
            roughness: 0.92,
            metalness: 0.02,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -3.8,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -3.8,
          }),
          rail_station: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xffaa3d,
            emissive: 0x4d2100,
            roughness: 0.62,
            metalness: 0.08,
          }),
          bus_stop: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xffaa3d,
            emissive: 0x4d2100,
            roughness: 0.68,
            metalness: 0.05,
          }),
        },
      };
      for (const material of Object.values(manager.materials)) {
        if (!material) continue;
        material.depthTest = true;
        material.depthWrite = true;
      }
      state.transitLayerManager = manager;
      return manager;
    }

    function chooseTransitLayerZoom(altitudeM, currentZoom) {
      const cfg = TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG && TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.tileZoomRange
        ? TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.tileZoomRange
        : TRANSPORT_CONFIG.tileZoomRange;
      const minZoom = clamp(Number(cfg && cfg.min) || 12, 10, 18);
      const maxZoom = clamp(Number(cfg && cfg.max) || 14, minZoom, 18);
      const chosen = chooseTransportZoom(altitudeM, Number.isFinite(currentZoom) ? currentZoom : maxZoom);
      return clamp(chosen, minZoom, maxZoom);
    }

    function getTransitLineOffsetM(featureClass) {
      const offsets =
        TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG && TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.lineOffsetsM && typeof TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.lineOffsetsM === "object"
          ? TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.lineOffsetsM
          : {};
      const value = Number(offsets[featureClass]);
      if (Number.isFinite(value)) {
        return value;
      }
      return featureClass === "bus_route" ? 0.31 : 0.34;
    }

    function getTransitLineWidthM(featureClass, fallbackWidthM) {
      if (Number.isFinite(Number(fallbackWidthM)) && Number(fallbackWidthM) > 0.05) {
        return Number(fallbackWidthM);
      }
      const widths =
        TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG && TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.lineWidthsM && typeof TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.lineWidthsM === "object"
          ? TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.lineWidthsM
          : {};
      const value = Number(widths[featureClass]);
      if (Number.isFinite(value) && value > 0.05) {
        return value;
      }
      return featureClass === "bus_route" ? 1.4 : 2.6;
    }

    function getTransitMarkerOffsetM(featureClass) {
      const offsets =
        TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG && TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.markerOffsetsM && typeof TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.markerOffsetsM === "object"
          ? TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.markerOffsetsM
          : {};
      const value = Number(offsets[featureClass]);
      if (Number.isFinite(value)) {
        return value;
      }
      return featureClass === "bus_stop" ? 1.15 : 1.4;
    }

    function getTransitMarkerScale(featureClass) {
      const scales =
        TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG && TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.markerScale && typeof TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.markerScale === "object"
          ? TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.markerScale
          : {};
      const value = Number(scales[featureClass]);
      if (Number.isFinite(value) && value > 0) {
        return value;
      }
      return featureClass === "bus_stop" ? 0.85 : 1;
    }

    function buildTransitMarkerTemplate(featureClass, manager) {
      const safeManager = manager || buildTransitLayerManager();
      if (featureClass === "bus_stop") {
        const group = new THREE.Group();
        const pole = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.05, 0.06, 1.6, 8), safeManager.materials.bus_stop);
        pole.position.set(0, 0.8, 0);
        const plate = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.34, 0.46, 0.09), safeManager.materials.bus_stop);
        plate.position.set(0, 1.54, 0);
        group.add(pole, plate);
        return group;
      }
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      const stem = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.07, 0.08, 1.7, 8), safeManager.materials.rail_station);
      stem.position.set(0, 0.85, 0);
      const cap = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.21, 9, 9), safeManager.materials.rail_station);
      cap.position.set(0, 1.74, 0);
      group.add(stem, cap);
      return group;
    }

    function getTransitMarkerTemplateParts(featureClass, manager) {
      const safeManager = manager || buildTransitLayerManager();
      if (!(safeManager.assetTemplateByClass instanceof Map)) {
        safeManager.assetTemplateByClass = new Map();
      }
      if (safeManager.assetTemplateByClass.has(featureClass)) {
        const cached = safeManager.assetTemplateByClass.get(featureClass);
        return Array.isArray(cached) ? cached : [];
      }
      const template = buildTransitMarkerTemplate(featureClass, safeManager);
      if (!template) {
        safeManager.assetTemplateByClass.set(featureClass, []);
        return [];
      }
      template.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      const parts = [];
      template.traverse((child) => {
        if (!child || !child.isMesh || !child.geometry || !child.material) {
          return;
        }
        child.updateMatrix();
        parts.push({
          geometry: child.geometry,
          material: child.material,
          localMatrix: child.matrix.clone(),
        });
      });
      safeManager.assetTemplateByClass.set(featureClass, parts);
      return parts;
    }

    async function fetchTransitFeaturesFromManifestTile(zoom, x, y) {
      const cacheKey = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      const cached = transitTileFeatureCache.get(cacheKey);
      if (cached && cached.expiresAt > Date.now()) {
        return Array.isArray(cached.features) ? cached.features : [];
      }
      const manifest = TRANSIT_MANIFEST && typeof TRANSIT_MANIFEST === "object"
        ? TRANSIT_MANIFEST
        : {};
      const urls = [];
      const basePath = manifest.basePath ? String(manifest.basePath) : "";
      const tileKey = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      const flatName = "transit_z" + String(zoom) + "_x" + String(x) + "_y" + String(y) + ".json";
      if (manifest.tileIndex && typeof manifest.tileIndex === "object") {
        const indexed = manifest.tileIndex[tileKey];
        if (typeof indexed === "string" && indexed.length > 0) {
          const lower = indexed.toLowerCase();
          if (lower.startsWith("http://") || lower.startsWith("https://")) {
            urls.push(indexed);
          } else {
            urls.push(basePath ? joinAssetPath(basePath, indexed) : indexed);
          }
        }
      }
      if (typeof manifest.urlTemplate === "string" && manifest.urlTemplate) {
        urls.push(
          String(manifest.urlTemplate)
            .replace("{z}", String(zoom))
            .replace("{x}", String(x))
            .replace("{y}", String(y))
        );
      }
      if (basePath) {
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json"));
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, flatName));
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, "transit_osm_tiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json"));
      }
      urls.push("./patch_assets/" + flatName);
      urls.push("patch_assets/" + flatName);
      urls.push("./" + flatName);
      urls.push(flatName);
      urls.push("./patch_assets/transit_osm_tiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("patch_assets/transit_osm_tiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("./transit_osm_tiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("transit_osm_tiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      const uniqueUrls = Array.from(new Set(urls.filter((url) => typeof url === "string" && url.length > 0)));
      const deduped = [];
      const seen = new Set();
      for (const url of uniqueUrls) {
        try {
          const payload = await tryFetchJsonCandidate(url, 9000, isFeatureCollectionPayload);
          if (!payload || !Array.isArray(payload.features)) {
            continue;
          }
          for (const feature of payload.features) {
            const normalizedItems = flattenNormalizedTransitFeatures(normalizeTransitFeature(feature, "manifest"));
            for (const normalized of normalizedItems) {
              const key = buildTransitFeatureMergeKey(normalized);
              if (key && seen.has(key)) {
                continue;
              }
              if (key) {
                seen.add(key);
              }
              deduped.push(normalized);
            }
          }
          if (deduped.length > 0) {
            transitTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, { features: deduped, expiresAt: Date.now() + 5 * 60 * 1000 });
            return deduped;
          }
        } catch (_error) {
          // Continue to next URL candidate.
        }
      }
      transitTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, { features: [], expiresAt: Date.now() + 60 * 1000 });
      return [];
    }

    function buildTransitTileGroup(tile, features) {
      const manager = buildTransitLayerManager();
      const bounds = tile.bounds;
      const scopeBounds = getActiveWardBounds();
      const centerECEF = lonLatToECEF(
        (bounds.west + bounds.east) * 0.5,
        (bounds.south + bounds.north) * 0.5,
        0
      );
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.position.copy(centerECEF);
      group.name = "transitTile:" + tile.key;
      const builders = {
        rail_line: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        bus_route: { positions: [], indices: [] },
      };
      const counts = {
        rail_line: 0,
        bus_route: 0,
        rail_station: 0,
        bus_stop: 0,
        total: 0,
      };
      const placementsByClass = {
        rail_station: [],
        bus_stop: [],
      };
      const geoUp = centerECEF.clone().normalize();
      const worldUp = new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0);
      const orientQ = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromUnitVectors(worldUp, geoUp);
      const matrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
      const localPos = new THREE.Vector3();

      for (const feature of Array.isArray(features) ? features : []) {
        if (!feature || !feature.geometryType) {
          continue;
        }
        if (feature.geometryType === "LineString" && Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) && feature.coordinates.length >= 2) {
          const cls = feature.featureClass === "bus_route" ? "bus_route" : "rail_line";
          const appended = appendDrapedRibbon(
            builders[cls],
            feature.coordinates,
            getTransitLineWidthM(cls, feature.widthM),
            cls,
            centerECEF,
            feature,
            getTransitLineOffsetM(cls)
          );
          if (appended > 0) {
            counts[cls] += appended;
            counts.total += appended;
          }
          continue;
        }
        if (feature.geometryType === "Point" && Array.isArray(feature.coordinates)) {
          const lon = Number(feature.coordinates[0]);
          const lat = Number(feature.coordinates[1]);
          if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
            continue;
          }
          if (!isWithinAnyBounds(lon, lat, scopeBounds)) {
            continue;
          }
          const cls = feature.featureClass === "bus_stop" ? "bus_stop" : "rail_station";
          let heightM = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lon, lat);
          if (!Number.isFinite(heightM)) {
            heightM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
          }
          const ecef = lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM + getTransitMarkerOffsetM(cls));
          localPos.copy(ecef).sub(centerECEF);
          const scaleValue = getTransitMarkerScale(cls);
          matrix.compose(localPos, orientQ, new THREE.Vector3(scaleValue, scaleValue, scaleValue));
          placementsByClass[cls].push(matrix.clone());
          counts[cls] += 1;
          counts.total += 1;
        }
      }

      for (const cls of Object.keys(builders)) {
        const geometry = createTransportGeometry(builders[cls]);
        if (!geometry) {
          continue;
        }
        const mesh = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, manager.materials[cls] || manager.materials.rail_line);
        mesh.frustumCulled = true;
        mesh.renderOrder = cls === "bus_route" ? 46 : 45;
        group.add(mesh);
      }

      const childMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
      const instanceMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
      for (const cls of Object.keys(placementsByClass)) {
        const placements = placementsByClass[cls];
        if (!Array.isArray(placements) || placements.length <= 0) {
          continue;
        }
        const parts = getTransitMarkerTemplateParts(cls, manager);
        if (!Array.isArray(parts) || parts.length <= 0) {
          continue;
        }
        for (const part of parts) {
          if (!part || !part.geometry || !part.material || !part.localMatrix) {
            continue;
          }
          const instanced = new THREE.InstancedMesh(part.geometry, part.material, placements.length);
          instanced.renderOrder = 47;
          instanced.frustumCulled = true;
          instanced.userData.sharedTemplateGeometry = true;
          for (let i = 0; i < placements.length; i += 1) {
            childMatrix.copy(part.localMatrix);
            instanceMatrix.multiplyMatrices(placements[i], childMatrix);
            instanced.setMatrixAt(i, instanceMatrix);
          }
          instanced.instanceMatrix.needsUpdate = true;
          group.add(instanced);
        }
      }

      return {
        group,
        counts,
      };
    }

    async function loadTransitTile(zoom, x, y) {
      const manager = buildTransitLayerManager();
      if (!(manager.failureBackoffByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureBackoffByKey = new Map();
      }
      if (!(manager.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureReasonByKey = new Map();
      }
      const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      if (manager.pending.has(key) || manager.tiles.has(key)) {
        return;
      }
      const backoffUntil = Number(manager.failureBackoffByKey.get(key)) || 0;
      if (backoffUntil > Date.now()) {
        return;
      }
      manager.pending.add(key);
      const bounds = slippyBounds(x, y, zoom);
      try {
        const tileIndex =
          TRANSIT_MANIFEST && TRANSIT_MANIFEST.tileIndex && typeof TRANSIT_MANIFEST.tileIndex === "object"
            ? TRANSIT_MANIFEST.tileIndex
            : null;
        const strictTileIndex = !!(TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG && TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.strictTileIndex === true);
        if (strictTileIndex && tileIndex && Object.keys(tileIndex).length > 0 && !tileIndex[key]) {
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 60 * 1000);
          manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, "not_indexed");
          return;
        }
        let features = await fetchTransitFeaturesFromManifestTile(zoom, x, y);
        if (!Array.isArray(features) || features.length <= 0) {
          const transportResult = await fetchTransportFeaturesForTile(zoom, x, y, bounds);
          const fallback = synthesizeTransitLayerFallbackFromTransport(
            transportResult && Array.isArray(transportResult.features) ? transportResult.features : [],
            bounds
          );
          if (Array.isArray(fallback) && fallback.length > 0) {
            features = fallback;
            debugLog("transit:transport_fallback", {
              key,
              transportFeatures:
                transportResult && Array.isArray(transportResult.features) ? transportResult.features.length : 0,
              transitFeatures: fallback.length,
            });
          }
        }
        if (!Array.isArray(features) || features.length <= 0) {
          manager.failed += 1;
          manager.warning = "Transit tile failed: " + key;
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 20000);
          manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, "no_data");
          return;
        }
        const built = buildTransitTileGroup({ key, z: zoom, x, y, bounds }, features);
        if (!built || !built.group || !built.counts || Number(built.counts.total) <= 0) {
          manager.failed += 1;
          manager.warning = "Transit tile empty: " + key;
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 20000);
          manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, "no_renderable");
          return;
        }
        manager.group.add(built.group);
        const tile = {
          key,
          z: zoom,
          x,
          y,
          bounds,
          group: built.group,
          features,
          counts: built.counts,
          lastWantedMs: Date.now(),
        };
        manager.tiles.set(key, tile);
        manager.loaded += 1;
        manager.ready = true;
        manager.failureBackoffByKey.delete(key);
        manager.failureReasonByKey.delete(key);
        manager.featureCounts.rail_line += Number(tile.counts.rail_line) || 0;
        manager.featureCounts.bus_route += Number(tile.counts.bus_route) || 0;
        manager.featureCounts.rail_station += Number(tile.counts.rail_station) || 0;
        manager.featureCounts.bus_stop += Number(tile.counts.bus_stop) || 0;
        manager.featureCounts.total += Number(tile.counts.total) || 0;
      } catch (error) {
        manager.failed += 1;
        manager.warning = "Transit tile failed: " + key;
        manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 20000);
        manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error));
      } finally {
        manager.pending.delete(key);
      }
    }

    function evictTransitTile(tile, reason) {
      const manager = state.transitLayerManager;
      if (!manager || !tile) {
        return;
      }
      try {
        if (tile.group && tile.group.parent) {
          tile.group.parent.remove(tile.group);
        }
        if (tile.group && typeof tile.group.traverse === "function") {
          tile.group.traverse((child) => {
            if (!child || !child.isMesh) {
              return;
            }
            if (child.userData && child.userData.sharedTemplateGeometry) {
              return;
            }
            if (child.geometry && typeof child.geometry.dispose === "function") {
              child.geometry.dispose();
            }
          });
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      manager.tiles.delete(tile.key);
      manager.featureCounts.rail_line = Math.max(0, manager.featureCounts.rail_line - (Number(tile.counts && tile.counts.rail_line) || 0));
      manager.featureCounts.bus_route = Math.max(0, manager.featureCounts.bus_route - (Number(tile.counts && tile.counts.bus_route) || 0));
      manager.featureCounts.rail_station = Math.max(0, manager.featureCounts.rail_station - (Number(tile.counts && tile.counts.rail_station) || 0));
      manager.featureCounts.bus_stop = Math.max(0, manager.featureCounts.bus_stop - (Number(tile.counts && tile.counts.bus_stop) || 0));
      manager.featureCounts.total = Math.max(0, manager.featureCounts.total - (Number(tile.counts && tile.counts.total) || 0));
      debugLog("transit:tile_evicted", {
        key: tile.key,
        reason: reason || "evict",
      });
    }

    function clearTransitLayerManager() {
      const manager = state.transitLayerManager;
      if (!manager) {
        return;
      }
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        evictTransitTile(tile, "transit_reset");
      }
      manager.tiles.clear();
      manager.pending.clear();
      manager.desired.clear();
      manager.currentZoom = null;
      manager.loaded = 0;
      manager.failed = 0;
      manager.ready = false;
      manager.warning = "";
      manager.featureCounts = {
        rail_line: 0,
        bus_route: 0,
        rail_station: 0,
        bus_stop: 0,
        total: 0,
      };
      if (!(manager.failureBackoffByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureBackoffByKey = new Map();
      }
      if (!(manager.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureReasonByKey = new Map();
      }
      manager.failureBackoffByKey.clear();
      manager.failureReasonByKey.clear();
      transitTileFeatureCache.clear();
    }

    function scheduleTransitLayerTiles(nowMs) {
      const manager = buildTransitLayerManager();
      if (TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG && TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.enabled === false) {
        return;
      }
      if (!state.camera) return;
      if (nowMs - manager.lastTickMs < manager.requestIntervalMs) return;
      manager.lastTickMs = nowMs;
      const llh = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
      if (!llh || !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) || !Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) return;
      if (!isWithinBounds(llh.lng, llh.lat, TOKYO23 && TOKYO23.bounds ? TOKYO23.bounds : null)) return;

      const suggestedZoom = chooseTransitLayerZoom(llh.altitudeM, manager.currentZoom);
      const transitZoomLevels = getTileIndexZoomLevels(
        TRANSIT_MANIFEST && TRANSIT_MANIFEST.tileIndex && typeof TRANSIT_MANIFEST.tileIndex === "object"
          ? TRANSIT_MANIFEST.tileIndex
          : null
      );
      const constrainedZoom = constrainZoomToAvailableLevels(suggestedZoom, transitZoomLevels);
      const previousZoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : null;
      manager.currentZoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : constrainedZoom;
      if (manager.currentZoom !== constrainedZoom) {
        manager.currentZoom = constrainedZoom;
        for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
          if (!tile || tile.z === constrainedZoom) continue;
          evictTransitTile(tile, "zoom_change");
        }
        manager.desired.clear();
        debugLog("transit:zoom_changed", {
          from: previousZoom,
          to: constrainedZoom,
        });
      }
      const zoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : constrainedZoom;
      const center = lonLatToSlippy(llh.lng, llh.lat, zoom);
      const radius = state.driveMode ? 2 : 1;
      const pendingCap = state.driveMode ? 10 : 7;
      const desired = new Set();
      const maxIndex = Math.pow(2, zoom) - 1;
      for (let dy = -radius; dy <= radius; dy += 1) {
        for (let dx = -radius; dx <= radius; dx += 1) {
          if (desired.size >= manager.maxActiveTiles) continue;
          const tx = clamp(center.x + dx, 0, maxIndex);
          const ty = clamp(center.y + dy, 0, maxIndex);
          const tileBounds = slippyBounds(tx, ty, zoom);
          if (!transportTileRelevantToActiveWards(tileBounds, llh)) continue;
          const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(tx) + "/" + String(ty);
          desired.add(key);
          const existing = manager.tiles.get(key);
          if (existing) {
            existing.lastWantedMs = nowMs;
            continue;
          }
          if (manager.pending.size >= pendingCap) continue;
          loadTransitTile(zoom, tx, ty).catch((error) => {
            debugLog("transit:tile_async_error", {
              key,
              message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
            });
          });
        }
      }
      manager.desired = desired;
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        if (desired.has(tile.key)) continue;
        if (nowMs - (tile.lastWantedMs || 0) >= manager.hysteresisMs) {
          evictTransitTile(tile, "outside_desired");
        }
      }
    }

    function buildRealtimeTransitManager() {
      if (state.transitRealtimeManager) {
        return state.transitRealtimeManager;
      }
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.name = "realtimeTransitGroup";
      const trainGroup = new THREE.Group();
      trainGroup.name = "realtimeTrainsGroup";
      const busGroup = new THREE.Group();
      busGroup.name = "realtimeBusesGroup";
      group.add(trainGroup);
      group.add(busGroup);
      state.scene.add(group);
      const manager = {
        group,
        trainGroup,
        busGroup,
        pending: false,
        lastFetchMs: 0,
        lastUpdateMs: 0,
        lastUpdateIso: "",
        warnings: [],
        trainById: new Map(),
        busById: new Map(),
        trainPool: [],
        busPool: [],
        trainMaterial: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          color: 0xff8f2a,
          emissive: 0x4f1f00,
          roughness: 0.52,
          metalness: 0.03,
          transparent: true,
          opacity: 1,
        }),
        busMaterial: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          color: 0xff8f2a,
          emissive: 0x4f1f00,
          roughness: 0.58,
          metalness: 0.03,
          transparent: true,
          opacity: 1,
        }),
        windowMaterial: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          color: 0xffcc95,
          emissive: 0x3e1700,
          emissiveIntensity: 0.14,
          roughness: 0.34,
          metalness: 0.1,
          transparent: true,
          opacity: 0.9,
        }),
        wheelMaterial: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          color: 0x141920,
          roughness: 0.84,
          metalness: 0.02,
          transparent: true,
          opacity: 1,
        }),
        wheelHubMaterial: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          color: 0xb9bfca,
          roughness: 0.58,
          metalness: 0.24,
          transparent: true,
          opacity: 1,
        }),
        failedPolls: 0,
        noExecWarningShown: false,
      };
      state.transitRealtimeManager = manager;
      return manager;
    }

    function setRealtimeMarkerOpacity(mesh, opacity) {
      if (!mesh) {
        return;
      }
      const nextOpacity = clamp(
        Number.isFinite(Number(opacity)) ? Number(opacity) : 1,
        0,
        1
      );
      const fadeMaterials = mesh.userData && Array.isArray(mesh.userData.fadeMaterials)
        ? mesh.userData.fadeMaterials
        : [];
      if (fadeMaterials.length > 0) {
        for (const material of fadeMaterials) {
          if (material && typeof material.opacity === "number") {
            material.opacity = nextOpacity;
            material.transparent = nextOpacity < 0.999;
          }
        }
        return;
      }
      if (mesh.material && typeof mesh.material.opacity === "number") {
        mesh.material.opacity = nextOpacity;
        mesh.material.transparent = nextOpacity < 0.999;
      }
    }

    function addRealtimeMarkerWheel(root, materials, x, y, z, radius, width) {
      if (!root || !materials || !materials.wheel || !materials.hub) {
        return;
      }
      const wheel = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(radius, radius, width, 12), materials.wheel);
      wheel.rotation.z = Math.PI * 0.5;
      wheel.position.set(x, y, z);
      root.add(wheel);
      const hub = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(radius * 0.44, radius * 0.44, width * 0.52, 10), materials.hub);
      hub.rotation.z = Math.PI * 0.5;
      hub.position.set(x, y, z);
      root.add(hub);
    }

    function createRealtimeTransitMarker(kind, manager) {
      const safeManager = manager || buildRealtimeTransitManager();
      const pool = kind === "train" ? safeManager.trainPool : safeManager.busPool;
      if (Array.isArray(pool) && pool.length > 0) {
        const reused = pool.pop();
        if (reused) {
          reused.visible = true;
          setRealtimeMarkerOpacity(reused, 1);
          return reused;
        }
      }
      const bodyTemplate = kind === "train" ? safeManager.trainMaterial : safeManager.busMaterial;
      const bodyMaterial = bodyTemplate.clone();
      bodyMaterial.transparent = true;
      bodyMaterial.opacity = 1;
      const windowTemplate = safeManager.windowMaterial || bodyTemplate;
      const windowMaterial = windowTemplate.clone();
      windowMaterial.transparent = true;
      windowMaterial.opacity = 1;
      const wheelTemplate = safeManager.wheelMaterial || bodyTemplate;
      const wheelMaterial = wheelTemplate.clone();
      wheelMaterial.transparent = true;
      wheelMaterial.opacity = 1;
      const hubTemplate = safeManager.wheelHubMaterial || wheelTemplate;
      const hubMaterial = hubTemplate.clone();
      hubMaterial.transparent = true;
      hubMaterial.opacity = 1;

      const root = new THREE.Group();
      root.frustumCulled = false;
      root.renderOrder = kind === "train" ? 52 : 51;
      root.userData.kind = kind;
      root.userData.fadeMaterials = [bodyMaterial, windowMaterial, wheelMaterial, hubMaterial];

      if (kind === "train") {
        const body = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(2.35, 1.05, 0.92), bodyMaterial);
        body.position.set(0, 0.62, 0);
        const roof = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(2.12, 0.35, 0.78), windowMaterial);
        roof.position.set(0, 1.16, 0);
        root.add(body, roof);
        addRealtimeMarkerWheel(root, { wheel: wheelMaterial, hub: hubMaterial }, -0.9, 0.22, 0.34, 0.22, 0.16);
        addRealtimeMarkerWheel(root, { wheel: wheelMaterial, hub: hubMaterial }, 0.9, 0.22, 0.34, 0.22, 0.16);
        addRealtimeMarkerWheel(root, { wheel: wheelMaterial, hub: hubMaterial }, -0.9, 0.22, -0.34, 0.22, 0.16);
        addRealtimeMarkerWheel(root, { wheel: wheelMaterial, hub: hubMaterial }, 0.9, 0.22, -0.34, 0.22, 0.16);
      } else {
        const body = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(2.15, 0.96, 1.12), bodyMaterial);
        body.position.set(0, 0.58, 0);
        const roof = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(1.82, 0.28, 0.8), windowMaterial);
        roof.position.set(-0.08, 1.02, 0);
        root.add(body, roof);
        addRealtimeMarkerWheel(root, { wheel: wheelMaterial, hub: hubMaterial }, -0.74, 0.22, 0.44, 0.24, 0.18);
        addRealtimeMarkerWheel(root, { wheel: wheelMaterial, hub: hubMaterial }, 0.74, 0.22, 0.44, 0.24, 0.18);
        addRealtimeMarkerWheel(root, { wheel: wheelMaterial, hub: hubMaterial }, -0.74, 0.22, -0.44, 0.24, 0.18);
        addRealtimeMarkerWheel(root, { wheel: wheelMaterial, hub: hubMaterial }, 0.74, 0.22, -0.44, 0.24, 0.18);
      }

      root.traverse((obj) => {
        if (obj && obj.isMesh) {
          obj.castShadow = false;
          obj.receiveShadow = false;
          obj.frustumCulled = false;
          obj.renderOrder = root.renderOrder;
        }
      });
      return root;
    }

    function recycleRealtimeTransitMarker(entry, manager, kind) {
      if (!entry || !entry.mesh || !manager) {
        return;
      }
      const mesh = entry.mesh;
      if (mesh.parent) {
        mesh.parent.remove(mesh);
      }
      mesh.visible = false;
      setRealtimeMarkerOpacity(mesh, 1);
      const pool = kind === "train" ? manager.trainPool : manager.busPool;
      pool.push(mesh);
    }

    function getRealtimeTransitWorldPosition(item, kind) {
      const lon = Number(item && item.lng);
      const lat = Number(item && item.lat);
      if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
        return null;
      }
      let heightM = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lon, lat);
      if (!Number.isFinite(heightM)) {
        heightM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
      }
      const offset = kind === "train" ? 2.6 : 2.1;
      return lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM + offset);
    }

    const realtimeMarkerEast = new THREE.Vector3();
    const realtimeMarkerNorth = new THREE.Vector3();
    const realtimeMarkerForward = new THREE.Vector3();
    const realtimeMarkerRight = new THREE.Vector3();
    const realtimeMarkerUp = new THREE.Vector3();
    const realtimeMarkerOrient = new THREE.Matrix4();

    function applyRealtimeTransitMarkerOrientation(entry) {
      if (!entry || !entry.mesh || !entry.mesh.position) {
        return;
      }
      const headingDeg = Number(entry.headingDeg);
      const lon = Number(entry && entry.meta && entry.meta.lng);
      const lat = Number(entry && entry.meta && entry.meta.lat);
      if (!Number.isFinite(headingDeg) || !Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
        return;
      }
      const up = realtimeMarkerUp.copy(entry.mesh.position);
      if (up.lengthSq() < 1e-8) {
        return;
      }
      up.normalize();
      const lonR = toRad(lon);
      realtimeMarkerEast.set(-Math.sin(lonR), Math.cos(lonR), 0);
      if (realtimeMarkerEast.lengthSq() < 1e-8) {
        return;
      }
      realtimeMarkerEast.normalize();
      realtimeMarkerNorth.crossVectors(up, realtimeMarkerEast);
      if (realtimeMarkerNorth.lengthSq() < 1e-8) {
        return;
      }
      realtimeMarkerNorth.normalize();
      const headingRad = toRad(headingDeg);
      realtimeMarkerForward
        .copy(realtimeMarkerNorth)
        .multiplyScalar(Math.cos(headingRad))
        .addScaledVector(realtimeMarkerEast, Math.sin(headingRad));
      realtimeMarkerForward.addScaledVector(up, -realtimeMarkerForward.dot(up));
      if (realtimeMarkerForward.lengthSq() < 1e-8) {
        return;
      }
      realtimeMarkerForward.normalize();
      realtimeMarkerRight.crossVectors(up, realtimeMarkerForward);
      if (realtimeMarkerRight.lengthSq() < 1e-8) {
        return;
      }
      realtimeMarkerRight.normalize();
      realtimeMarkerOrient.makeBasis(realtimeMarkerRight, up, realtimeMarkerForward);
      entry.mesh.quaternion.setFromRotationMatrix(realtimeMarkerOrient);
    }

    function upsertRealtimeTransitMarkers(kind, rows, nowMs) {
      const manager = buildRealtimeTransitManager();
      const markerMap = kind === "train" ? manager.trainById : manager.busById;
      const markerGroup = kind === "train" ? manager.trainGroup : manager.busGroup;
      const seen = new Set();
      const interval = Math.max(1200, Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.pollIntervalMs) || 15000);
      for (const row of Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : []) {
        if (!row || typeof row !== "object") {
          continue;
        }
        const id = String(row.id || "").trim();
        if (!id) {
          continue;
        }
        const world = getRealtimeTransitWorldPosition(row, kind);
        if (!world) {
          continue;
        }
        seen.add(id);
        let entry = markerMap.get(id);
        if (!entry) {
          const mesh = createRealtimeTransitMarker(kind, manager);
          mesh.position.copy(world);
          markerGroup.add(mesh);
          entry = {
            id,
            mesh,
            prevWorld: world.clone(),
            nextWorld: world.clone(),
            blendStartMs: nowMs,
            blendEndMs: nowMs + interval,
            lastSeenMs: nowMs,
            headingDeg: Number.NaN,
            meta: {},
          };
          markerMap.set(id, entry);
        } else {
          entry.prevWorld = entry.mesh.position.clone();
          entry.nextWorld = world.clone();
          entry.blendStartMs = nowMs;
          entry.blendEndMs = nowMs + interval;
          entry.lastSeenMs = nowMs;
        }
        const heading = Number(row.headingDeg);
        const bearing = Number(row.bearingDeg);
        entry.headingDeg = Number.isFinite(heading)
          ? heading
          : (Number.isFinite(bearing) ? bearing : Number.NaN);
        entry.meta = row;
        applyRealtimeTransitMarkerOrientation(entry);
      }
      return seen;
    }

    function updateRealtimeTransitMarkersFromPayload(payload, nowMs) {
      const manager = buildRealtimeTransitManager();
      const safePayload = payload && typeof payload === "object" ? payload : {};
      const trainSeen = upsertRealtimeTransitMarkers("train", Array.isArray(safePayload.trains) ? safePayload.trains : [], nowMs);
      const busSeen = upsertRealtimeTransitMarkers("bus", Array.isArray(safePayload.buses) ? safePayload.buses : [], nowMs);
      manager.lastUpdateMs = nowMs;
      manager.lastUpdateIso = safePayload.timestamp ? String(safePayload.timestamp) : new Date(nowMs).toISOString();
      manager.warnings = Array.isArray(safePayload.warnings)
        ? safePayload.warnings.map((row) => String(row || "")).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 6)
        : [];
      return {
        trainSeen,
        busSeen,
      };
    }

    function stripTransitRealtimePrefix(value) {
      const text = String(value || "").trim();
      if (!text) {
        return "";
      }
      const idx = text.indexOf(":");
      if (idx > 0 && text.slice(0, idx).includes(".")) {
        return text.slice(idx + 1);
      }
      return text;
    }

    function normalizeMiniTokyoRealtimeRowsClient(rows) {
      const out = [];
      for (const row of Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : []) {
        if (!row || typeof row !== "object") {
          continue;
        }
        const id = stripTransitRealtimePrefix(row.id || row.trainId || row["owl:sameAs"] || "");
        const operator = stripTransitRealtimePrefix(row.o || row.operator || row["odpt:operator"] || "");
        const railway = stripTransitRealtimePrefix(row.r || row.railway || row["odpt:railway"] || "");
        const candidates = [];
        const pushCandidate = (lonRaw, latRaw) => {
          const lon = Number(lonRaw);
          const lat = Number(latRaw);
          if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
            return;
          }
          if (Math.abs(lon) > 180 || Math.abs(lat) > 90) {
            return;
          }
          candidates.push([lon, lat]);
        };
        pushCandidate(row.lng, row.lat);
        pushCandidate(row.lon, row.lat);
        pushCandidate(row.longitude, row.latitude);
        pushCandidate(row.longitude, row.lat);
        pushCandidate(row.lon, row.latitude);
        pushCandidate(row.x, row.y);
        if (Array.isArray(row.coordinates) && row.coordinates.length >= 2) {
          pushCandidate(row.coordinates[0], row.coordinates[1]);
        }
        if (Array.isArray(row.coord) && row.coord.length >= 2) {
          pushCandidate(row.coord[0], row.coord[1]);
        }
        if (row.geometry && Array.isArray(row.geometry.coordinates) && row.geometry.coordinates.length >= 2) {
          pushCandidate(row.geometry.coordinates[0], row.geometry.coordinates[1]);
        }
        let lng = Number.NaN;
        let lat = Number.NaN;
        if (candidates.length > 0) {
          lng = Number(candidates[0][0]);
          lat = Number(candidates[0][1]);
        }
        if (!Number.isFinite(lng) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
          continue;
        }
        const headingDeg = Number(
          row.headingDeg ||
          row.heading ||
          row.bearingDeg ||
          row.bearing ||
          row.direction ||
          row.h
        );
        const delayRaw = Number(row.delay || 0);
        const delaySec = Number.isFinite(delayRaw)
          ? (Math.abs(delayRaw) > 10000 ? Math.round(delayRaw / 1000) : Math.round(delayRaw))
          : 0;
        out.push({
          id: id || ("miniTokyo:" + String(out.length + 1)),
          source: "mini_tokyo_direct",
          operator,
          railway,
          lng,
          lat,
          headingDeg: Number.isFinite(headingDeg) ? headingDeg : undefined,
          delaySec,
          statusText: String(row.statusText || row.status || row.text || "").slice(0, 160),
        });
      }
      return out;
    }

    function computeRealtimeFallbackHeadingDeg(coords, progress) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length < 2) {
        return Number.NaN;
      }
      const p0 = sampleLinePoint(coords, clamp(progress, 0, 1));
      const p1 = sampleLinePoint(coords, clamp(progress + 0.012, 0, 1));
      if (!Array.isArray(p0) || !Array.isArray(p1) || p0.length < 2 || p1.length < 2) {
        return Number.NaN;
      }
      const dx = Number(p1[0]) - Number(p0[0]);
      const dy = Number(p1[1]) - Number(p0[1]);
      if (!Number.isFinite(dx) || !Number.isFinite(dy) || (Math.abs(dx) + Math.abs(dy)) < 1e-9) {
        return Number.NaN;
      }
      return toDeg(Math.atan2(dx, dy));
    }

    function buildSyntheticRealtimeRows(kind, nowMs, maxCount) {
      const roads = collectTransportRoadFeatures();
      const limit = clampInt(Number(maxCount) || 0, 0, 0, 256);
      if (!Array.isArray(roads) || roads.length <= 0 || limit <= 0) {
        return [];
      }
      const out = [];
      const phaseSec = Number(nowMs) / 1000;
      const stride = kind === "train" ? 11 : 7;
      const speed = kind === "train" ? 0.014 : 0.022;
      let guard = 0;
      while (out.length < limit && guard < roads.length * 4) {
        const idx = (guard * stride + (kind === "train" ? 3 : 1)) % roads.length;
        guard += 1;
        const feature = roads[idx];
        const coords = feature && Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) ? feature.coordinates : null;
        if (!coords || coords.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        const phase = (phaseSec * speed + (idx % 37) * 0.037 + (kind === "bus" ? 0.19 : 0.03)) % 1;
        const sampled = sampleLinePoint(coords, phase);
        if (!Array.isArray(sampled) || sampled.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        const headingDeg = computeRealtimeFallbackHeadingDeg(coords, phase);
        out.push({
          id: "synthetic:" + kind + ":" + String(idx),
          source: "synthetic_transport",
          operator: "synthetic",
          railway: kind === "train" ? "synthetic.minato" : "",
          lng: Number(sampled[0]),
          lat: Number(sampled[1]),
          headingDeg: Number.isFinite(headingDeg) ? headingDeg : undefined,
          delaySec: 0,
          statusText: "synthetic fallback",
        });
      }
      return out;
    }

    async function fetchRealtimeJsonWithTimeout(url, timeoutMs) {
      const cleanUrl = String(url || "").trim();
      if (!cleanUrl) {
        return null;
      }
      let controller = null;
      let timeoutId = null;
      try {
        if (typeof AbortController !== "undefined") {
          controller = new AbortController();
          timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
            try {
              controller.abort();
            } catch (_error) {
              // no-op
            }
          }, Math.max(1200, Number(timeoutMs) || 9000));
        }
        const response = await fetch(cleanUrl, {
          method: "GET",
          mode: "cors",
          credentials: "omit",
          cache: "no-store",
          signal: controller ? controller.signal : undefined,
        });
        if (!response || !response.ok) {
