          return null;
        }
        const text = typeof response.text === "function" ? String(await response.text() || "") : "";
        if (!text) {
          return null;
        }
        const payload = JSON.parse(text);
        return payload && typeof payload === "object" ? payload : null;
      } catch (_error) {
        return null;
      } finally {
        if (timeoutId) {
          clearTimeout(timeoutId);
        }
      }
    }

    async function loadRealtimeTransitDirectPayload(timeoutMs) {
      const now = Date.now();
      const cacheTtlMs = Math.max(1000, Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.cacheTtlMs) || 10000);
      if (
        realtimeClientPayloadCache &&
        realtimeClientPayloadCache.payload &&
        Number(realtimeClientPayloadCache.expiresAt) > now
      ) {
        return realtimeClientPayloadCache.payload;
      }
      const warnings = [];
      const trains = [];
      const buses = [];
      const trainSourceConfig =
        TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG &&
        TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.trainSources &&
        TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.trainSources.miniTokyo &&
        typeof TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.trainSources.miniTokyo === "object"
          ? TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.trainSources.miniTokyo
          : {};
      if (trainSourceConfig.enabled === false) {
        warnings.push("MiniTokyo realtime train source disabled by config.");
      } else {
        const urls = Array.isArray(trainSourceConfig.urls) ? trainSourceConfig.urls : [];
        const effectiveUrls = urls.length > 0
          ? urls
          : ["https://mini-tokyo.appspot.com/tid", "https://mini-tokyo.appspot.com/traininfo", "https://mini-tokyo.appspot.com/"];
        const trainRows = [];
        const infoRows = [];
        for (const rawUrl of effectiveUrls) {
          const url = String(rawUrl || "").trim();
          if (!url) {
            continue;
          }
          const payload = await fetchRealtimeJsonWithTimeout(url, timeoutMs);
          if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object") {
            warnings.push("MiniTokyo feed failed: " + url);
            continue;
          }
          if (Array.isArray(payload)) {
            if (/traininfo/i.test(url)) {
              infoRows.push(...payload);
            } else {
              trainRows.push(...payload);
            }
            continue;
          }
          const objectPayload = payload && typeof payload === "object" ? payload : {};
          const embeddedTrains = Array.isArray(objectPayload.train)
            ? objectPayload.train
            : (Array.isArray(objectPayload.trains) ? objectPayload.trains : []);
          const embeddedInfo = Array.isArray(objectPayload.trainInformation)
            ? objectPayload.trainInformation
            : (
              Array.isArray(objectPayload.traininfo)
                ? objectPayload.traininfo
                : (Array.isArray(objectPayload.information) ? objectPayload.information : [])
            );
          if (embeddedTrains.length > 0) {
            trainRows.push(...embeddedTrains);
          }
          if (embeddedInfo.length > 0) {
            infoRows.push(...embeddedInfo);
          }
          if (embeddedTrains.length <= 0 && embeddedInfo.length <= 0) {
            warnings.push("MiniTokyo feed had no train rows: " + url);
          }
        }
        const normalized = normalizeMiniTokyoRealtimeRowsClient(trainRows);
        if (infoRows.length > 0 && normalized.length > 0) {
          const infoByRailway = new Map();
          for (const row of infoRows) {
            if (!row || typeof row !== "object") {
              continue;
            }
            const railway = stripTransitRealtimePrefix(row.railway || row.r || row["odpt:railway"] || "");
            const text = String(row.text || row.status || row["odpt:trainInformationText"] || "").trim();
            if (!railway || !text) {
              continue;
            }
            infoByRailway.set(railway, text);
          }
          for (const train of normalized) {
            if (!train || train.statusText) {
              continue;
            }
            const text = infoByRailway.get(String(train.railway || ""));
            if (text) {
              train.statusText = text;
            }
          }
        }
        const seen = new Set();
        for (const row of normalized) {
          if (!row || !Number.isFinite(Number(row.lng)) || !Number.isFinite(Number(row.lat))) {
            continue;
          }
          const idKey = String(row.id || "").trim();
          const geoKey = Number(row.lng).toFixed(5) + ":" + Number(row.lat).toFixed(5);
          const dedupeKey = idKey || (String(row.railway || "") + "|" + geoKey);
          if (seen.has(dedupeKey)) {
            continue;
          }
          seen.add(dedupeKey);
          trains.push(row);
        }
      }
      if (trains.length <= 0) {
        const syntheticTrains = buildSyntheticRealtimeRows(
          "train",
          now,
          clampInt(Math.min(Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.maxTrains) || 24, 24), 24, 0, 128)
        );
        if (syntheticTrains.length > 0) {
          trains.push(...syntheticTrains);
          warnings.push("Realtime train feed unavailable; using synthetic train fallback.");
        } else {
          warnings.push("No realtime train positions available in client-direct mode.");
        }
      }
      if (buses.length <= 0) {
        const syntheticBuses = buildSyntheticRealtimeRows(
          "bus",
          now,
          clampInt(Math.min(Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.maxBuses) || 18, 18), 18, 0, 128)
        );
        if (syntheticBuses.length > 0) {
          buses.push(...syntheticBuses);
          warnings.push("Realtime bus feed unavailable; using synthetic bus fallback.");
        }
      }
      const maxTrains = Math.max(
        0,
        clampInt(Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.maxTrains) || 420, 420, 0, 5000)
      );
      const maxBuses = Math.max(
        0,
        clampInt(Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.maxBuses) || 420, 420, 0, 5000)
      );
      const payload = {
        ok: true,
        timestamp: new Date(now).toISOString(),
        trains: maxTrains > 0 ? trains.slice(0, maxTrains) : [],
        buses: maxBuses > 0 ? buses.slice(0, maxBuses) : [],
        warnings: Array.from(new Set(warnings.map((row) => String(row || "")).filter(Boolean))).slice(0, 6),
      };
      realtimeClientPayloadCache.payload = payload;
      realtimeClientPayloadCache.expiresAt = now + cacheTtlMs;
      return payload;
    }

    function advanceRealtimeTransitMarkers(nowMs) {
      const manager = state.transitRealtimeManager;
      if (!manager) {
        return;
      }
      const staleAfterMs = Math.max(1000, Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.staleAfterMs) || 55000);
      const interpolate = (entry) => {
        if (!entry || !entry.mesh || !entry.prevWorld || !entry.nextWorld) {
          return;
        }
        const span = Math.max(1, Number(entry.blendEndMs) - Number(entry.blendStartMs));
        const t = clamp((nowMs - Number(entry.blendStartMs)) / span, 0, 1);
        entry.mesh.position.lerpVectors(entry.prevWorld, entry.nextWorld, t);
        applyRealtimeTransitMarkerOrientation(entry);
        const ageMs = nowMs - Number(entry.lastSeenMs || nowMs);
        const fade = clamp(1 - ageMs / staleAfterMs, 0, 1);
        setRealtimeMarkerOpacity(entry.mesh, fade);
      };
      for (const entry of manager.trainById.values()) {
        interpolate(entry);
      }
      for (const entry of manager.busById.values()) {
        interpolate(entry);
      }
      pruneStaleTransitMarkers(nowMs);
    }

    function pruneStaleTransitMarkers(nowMs) {
      const manager = state.transitRealtimeManager;
      if (!manager) {
        return;
      }
      const staleAfterMs = Math.max(1000, Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.staleAfterMs) || 55000);
      for (const [id, entry] of Array.from(manager.trainById.entries())) {
        if (!entry || nowMs - Number(entry.lastSeenMs || 0) <= staleAfterMs) {
          continue;
        }
        recycleRealtimeTransitMarker(entry, manager, "train");
        manager.trainById.delete(id);
      }
      for (const [id, entry] of Array.from(manager.busById.entries())) {
        if (!entry || nowMs - Number(entry.lastSeenMs || 0) <= staleAfterMs) {
          continue;
        }
        recycleRealtimeTransitMarker(entry, manager, "bus");
        manager.busById.delete(id);
      }
    }

    async function pollRealtimeTransit(nowMs) {
      const manager = buildRealtimeTransitManager();
      if (TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG && TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.enabled === false) {
        return;
      }
      const interval = Math.max(1200, Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.pollIntervalMs) || 15000);
      if (manager.pending) {
        return;
      }
      if (nowMs - manager.lastFetchMs < interval) {
        return;
      }
      manager.lastFetchMs = nowMs;
      if (!(window.sup && typeof window.sup.exec === "function")) {
        if (TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG && TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.clientDirectFallback === false) {
          if (!manager.noExecWarningShown) {
            manager.noExecWarningShown = true;
            manager.warnings = ["Realtime transit callback unavailable in this runtime mode."];
            debugLog("transit:realtime_exec_unavailable", { localOnlyMode: LOCAL_ONLY_MODE });
          }
          return;
        }
        manager.pending = true;
        try {
          const timeoutMs = clampInt(Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.requestTimeoutMs) || 9000, 9000, 1800, 30000);
          const payload = await loadRealtimeTransitDirectPayload(timeoutMs);
          if (payload && payload.ok) {
            updateRealtimeTransitMarkersFromPayload(payload, Date.now());
            manager.failedPolls = 0;
            manager.noExecWarningShown = false;
          } else {
            manager.failedPolls += 1;
            manager.warnings = payload && Array.isArray(payload.warnings)
              ? payload.warnings.map((row) => String(row || "")).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 6)
              : ["Realtime transit direct feed unavailable."];
          }
        } catch (error) {
          manager.failedPolls += 1;
          const message = error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error);
          manager.warnings = ["Realtime transit direct mode failed: " + message];
          debugLog("transit:realtime_direct_error", {
            message,
            failedPolls: manager.failedPolls,
          });
        } finally {
          manager.pending = false;
        }
        return;
      }
      manager.pending = true;
      try {
        const timeoutMs = clampInt(Number(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.requestTimeoutMs) || 9000, 9000, 1800, 30000);
        const payload = await callSupExecWithTimeout("loadTransitRealtime", {}, timeoutMs);
        if (payload && payload.ok) {
          updateRealtimeTransitMarkersFromPayload(payload, Date.now());
          manager.failedPolls = 0;
        } else {
          manager.failedPolls += 1;
          manager.warnings = payload && Array.isArray(payload.warnings)
            ? payload.warnings.map((row) => String(row || "")).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 6)
            : ["Realtime transit response invalid."];
        }
      } catch (error) {
        manager.failedPolls += 1;
        const message = error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error);
        manager.warnings = ["Realtime transit poll failed: " + message];
        debugLog("transit:realtime_poll_error", {
          message,
          failedPolls: manager.failedPolls,
        });
      } finally {
        manager.pending = false;
      }
    }

    function clearRealtimeTransitManager() {
      const manager = state.transitRealtimeManager;
      if (!manager) {
        return;
      }
      for (const [id, entry] of Array.from(manager.trainById.entries())) {
        recycleRealtimeTransitMarker(entry, manager, "train");
        manager.trainById.delete(id);
      }
      for (const [id, entry] of Array.from(manager.busById.entries())) {
        recycleRealtimeTransitMarker(entry, manager, "bus");
        manager.busById.delete(id);
      }
      manager.pending = false;
      manager.lastFetchMs = 0;
      manager.lastUpdateMs = 0;
      manager.lastUpdateIso = "";
      manager.warnings = [];
      manager.failedPolls = 0;
      manager.noExecWarningShown = false;
    }

    function inferStreetFeatureClassFromTags(tags) {
      const safe = tags && typeof tags === "object" ? tags : {};
      const highway = safe.highway ? String(safe.highway).toLowerCase() : "";
      const trafficSign = safe.traffic_sign ? String(safe.traffic_sign).toLowerCase() : "";
      const roadMarking = safe.road_marking ? String(safe.road_marking).toLowerCase() : "";
      const natural = safe.natural ? String(safe.natural).toLowerCase() : "";
      if (highway === "street_lamp") return "street_lamp";
      if (highway === "traffic_signals") return "traffic_signal";
      if (highway === "stop" || trafficSign.includes("stop")) return "stop_sign";
      if (highway === "crossing") return "crosswalk_hint";
      if (natural === "tree" || natural === "tree_row") return "street_tree";
      if (roadMarking === "stop_line") return "stop_line";
      if (String(safe.type || "").toLowerCase() === "restriction") return "turn_restriction_hint";
      return "street_asset";
    }

    function normalizeStreetLayerFeature(rawFeature, sourceLabel) {
      if (!rawFeature || typeof rawFeature !== "object") {
        return null;
      }
      if (rawFeature.geometry && rawFeature.geometry.type) {
        const geometry = rawFeature.geometry;
        const properties = rawFeature.properties && typeof rawFeature.properties === "object"
          ? rawFeature.properties
          : {};
        const attrs = properties.attrs && typeof properties.attrs === "object"
          ? properties.attrs
          : (properties.tags && typeof properties.tags === "object" ? properties.tags : {});
        const featureClass = properties.featureClass
          ? String(properties.featureClass).toLowerCase()
          : inferStreetFeatureClassFromTags(attrs);
        const layer = properties.layer ? String(properties.layer).toLowerCase() : "street_asset";
        const source = properties.source ? String(properties.source).toLowerCase() : sourceLabel;
        const priority = Number.isFinite(Number(properties.priority)) ? Number(properties.priority) : 0;
        const id = properties.id ? String(properties.id) : "";
        const zMode = properties.z_mode ? String(properties.z_mode) : (properties.zMode ? String(properties.zMode) : "");
        if (isUndergroundFeature(attrs, { zMode })) {
          return null;
        }
        if (geometry.type === "Point" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates) && geometry.coordinates.length >= 2) {
          const lon = Number(geometry.coordinates[0]);
          const lat = Number(geometry.coordinates[1]);
          if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) return null;
          return {
            id,
            layer,
            featureClass,
            source,
            priority,
            attrs,
            geometryType: "Point",
            coordinates: [lon, lat],
          };
        }
        if (geometry.type === "LineString" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates) && geometry.coordinates.length >= 2) {
          const coords = geometry.coordinates
            .map((coord) => {
              if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) return null;
              const lon = Number(coord[0]);
              const lat = Number(coord[1]);
              return Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat) ? [lon, lat] : null;
            })
            .filter(Boolean);
          if (coords.length < 2) return null;
          return {
            id,
            layer,
            featureClass,
            source,
            priority,
            attrs,
            geometryType: "LineString",
            coordinates: coords,
          };
        }
        if (geometry.type === "Polygon" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates) && geometry.coordinates.length > 0) {
          const ring = Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates[0]) ? geometry.coordinates[0] : [];
          const coords = ring
            .map((coord) => {
              if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) return null;
              const lon = Number(coord[0]);
              const lat = Number(coord[1]);
              return Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat) ? [lon, lat] : null;
            })
            .filter(Boolean);
          if (coords.length < 3) return null;
          return {
            id,
            layer,
            featureClass,
            source,
            priority,
            attrs,
            geometryType: "Polygon",
            coordinates: coords,
          };
        }
        return null;
      }
      return null;
    }

    function flattenNormalizedStreetFeatures(value) {
      if (!value) return [];
      if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.filter(Boolean);
      return [value];
    }

    function buildStreetFeatureMergeKey(feature) {
      if (!feature || !feature.geometryType) return "";
      if (feature.geometryType === "Point" && Array.isArray(feature.coordinates)) {
        const lon = Math.round((Number(feature.coordinates[0]) || 0) * 1e6);
        const lat = Math.round((Number(feature.coordinates[1]) || 0) * 1e6);
        return String(feature.featureClass) + "|" + String(lon) + ":" + String(lat);
      }
      if ((feature.geometryType === "LineString" || feature.geometryType === "Polygon") && Array.isArray(feature.coordinates)) {
        const first = feature.coordinates[0];
        const last = feature.coordinates[feature.coordinates.length - 1];
        if (!Array.isArray(first) || !Array.isArray(last)) return "";
        const a = Math.round((Number(first[0]) || 0) * 1e6) + ":" + Math.round((Number(first[1]) || 0) * 1e6);
        const b = Math.round((Number(last[0]) || 0) * 1e6) + ":" + Math.round((Number(last[1]) || 0) * 1e6);
        return (
          String(feature.featureClass) +
          "|" +
          String(feature.geometryType) +
          "|" +
          String(a) +
          "|" +
          String(b) +
          "|" +
          String(feature.coordinates.length)
        );
      }
      return "";
    }

    function synthesizeStreetLayerFallbackFromTransport(transportFeatures, bounds) {
      const assetFeatures = [];
      const markingFeatures = [];
      const seenMarkings = new Set();
      const seenAssets = new Set();
      const limitMarkings = 6400;
      const limitAssets = 2600;
      const treeAssetCap = Math.max(0, Math.min(limitAssets, Math.floor(limitAssets * 0.4)));
      const criticalAssetCap = Math.max(0, limitAssets - treeAssetCap);
      let treeAssetCount = 0;
      let criticalAssetCount = 0;
      const scopeBounds = bounds && typeof bounds === "object"
        ? [bounds]
        : getActiveWardBounds();
      const sanitizeCoords = (coords) => {
        if (!Array.isArray(coords)) {
          return [];
        }
        return coords
          .map((coord) => {
            if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) return null;
            const lon = Number(coord[0]);
            const lat = Number(coord[1]);
            if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) return null;
            if (!isWithinAnyBounds(lon, lat, scopeBounds)) return null;
            return [lon, lat];
          })
          .filter(Boolean);
      };
      const segmentDistanceM = (a, b) => {
        if (!Array.isArray(a) || !Array.isArray(b)) return 0;
        const lonA = Number(a[0]);
        const latA = Number(a[1]);
        const lonB = Number(b[0]);
        const latB = Number(b[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lonA) || !Number.isFinite(latA) || !Number.isFinite(lonB) || !Number.isFinite(latB)) {
          return 0;
        }
        const avgLat = ((latA + latB) * 0.5) * Math.PI / 180;
        const metersPerLon = Math.max(0.1, Math.cos(avgLat) * 111320);
        const dx = (lonB - lonA) * metersPerLon;
        const dy = (latB - latA) * 111320;
        return Math.hypot(dx, dy);
      };
      const samplePointsAlongLine = (coords, spacingM, startOffsetM) => {
        const points = [];
        if (!Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length < 2) {
          return points;
        }
        const spacing = Math.max(8, Number(spacingM) || 16);
        let targetM = Math.max(0, Number(startOffsetM) || 0);
        let walkedM = 0;
        for (let i = 1; i < coords.length; i += 1) {
          const a = coords[i - 1];
          const b = coords[i];
          const segM = segmentDistanceM(a, b);
          if (!Number.isFinite(segM) || segM < 0.3) {
            continue;
          }
          while (walkedM + segM >= targetM) {
            const t = clamp((targetM - walkedM) / segM, 0, 1);
            const lon = Number(a[0]) + (Number(b[0]) - Number(a[0])) * t;
            const lat = Number(a[1]) + (Number(b[1]) - Number(a[1])) * t;
            if (Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat)) {
              points.push([lon, lat]);
            }
            targetM += spacing;
          }
          walkedM += segM;
          if (treeAssetCount + points.length >= treeAssetCap) {
            break;
          }
        }
        return points;
      };
      const pushMarking = (featureClass, coords, attrs) => {
        if (!Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length < 2 || markingFeatures.length >= limitMarkings) {
          return;
        }
        const candidate = {
          id: "",
          layer: "street_marking",
          featureClass,
          source: "transport_fallback",
          priority: 10,
          attrs: attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {},
          geometryType: "LineString",
          coordinates: coords,
        };
        const key = buildStreetFeatureMergeKey(candidate);
        if (key && seenMarkings.has(key)) {
          return;
        }
        if (key) {
          seenMarkings.add(key);
        }
        markingFeatures.push(candidate);
      };
      const pushAssetPoint = (featureClass, point, attrs, priorityOverride) => {
        if (!Array.isArray(point) || point.length < 2 || assetFeatures.length >= limitAssets) {
          return;
        }
        const lon = Number(point[0]);
        const lat = Number(point[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
          return;
        }
        if (!isWithinAnyBounds(lon, lat, scopeBounds)) {
          return;
        }
        const isTree = featureClass === "street_tree";
        if (isTree) {
          if (treeAssetCount >= treeAssetCap) {
            return;
          }
        } else if (criticalAssetCount >= criticalAssetCap) {
          return;
        }
        const layerName =
          featureClass === "traffic_signal" || featureClass === "stop_sign"
            ? "traffic_control"
            : "street_asset";
        const candidate = {
          id: "",
          layer: layerName,
          featureClass,
          source: "transport_fallback",
          priority: Number.isFinite(Number(priorityOverride)) ? Number(priorityOverride) : 10,
          attrs: attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {},
          geometryType: "Point",
          coordinates: [lon, lat],
        };
        const key = buildStreetFeatureMergeKey(candidate);
        if (key && seenAssets.has(key)) {
          return;
        }
        if (key) {
          seenAssets.add(key);
        }
        assetFeatures.push(candidate);
        if (isTree) {
          treeAssetCount += 1;
        } else {
          criticalAssetCount += 1;
        }
      };

      let roadFeatureOrdinal = 0;
      for (const feature of Array.isArray(transportFeatures) ? transportFeatures : []) {
        if (!feature || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) || feature.coordinates.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        if (isUndergroundFeature(feature.attrs, { zMode: feature.zMode })) {
          continue;
        }
        const featureClass = String(feature.featureClass || "").toLowerCase();
        const coords = sanitizeCoords(feature.coordinates);
        if (coords.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        if (featureClass === "crosswalk") {
          const mid = coords[Math.floor(coords.length * 0.5)];
          pushAssetPoint("traffic_signal", mid, feature.attrs);
          pushAssetPoint("stop_sign", coords[0], feature.attrs);
          pushAssetPoint("stop_sign", coords[coords.length - 1], feature.attrs);
          continue;
        }
        if (featureClass === "road") {
          pushMarking("lane_divider", coords, feature.attrs);
          roadFeatureOrdinal += 1;
          const waySeed = Number.isFinite(Number(feature.wayId))
            ? Math.abs(Math.round(Number(feature.wayId)))
            : roadFeatureOrdinal;
          if (waySeed % 2 === 0) {
            pushAssetPoint("street_lamp", coords[Math.floor(coords.length * 0.33)], feature.attrs);
          }
          if (waySeed % 4 === 0) {
            pushAssetPoint("street_lamp", coords[Math.floor(coords.length * 0.66)], feature.attrs);
          }
          if (waySeed % 9 === 0) {
            pushAssetPoint("traffic_signal", coords[Math.floor(coords.length * 0.5)], feature.attrs);
          }
        }
        if (featureClass === "sidewalk" || featureClass === "pedestrian") {
          if (treeAssetCount >= treeAssetCap) {
            continue;
          }
          const waySeed = Number.isFinite(Number(feature.wayId))
            ? Math.abs(Math.round(Number(feature.wayId)))
            : (roadFeatureOrdinal * 13 + coords.length * 7);
          const spacingM = featureClass === "sidewalk" ? 16 : 20;
          const startOffsetM = 4 + (waySeed % 11);
          const samples = samplePointsAlongLine(coords, spacingM, startOffsetM);
          for (const sample of samples) {
            pushAssetPoint("street_tree", sample, feature.attrs, 65);
            if (treeAssetCount >= treeAssetCap) {
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      }

      return {
        assetFeatures,
        markingFeatures,
      };
    }

    function getDashedMarkingClasses() {
      const classes = Array.isArray(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.dashedClasses)
        ? MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.dashedClasses
        : ["lane_divider"];
      return Array.from(
        new Set(
          classes
            .map((item) => String(item || "").trim().toLowerCase())
            .filter(Boolean)
        )
      );
    }

    function isDashedMarkingClass(featureClass) {
      const target = String(featureClass || "").toLowerCase();
      if (!target) return false;
      return getDashedMarkingClasses().includes(target);
    }

    function createDashedMarkingMaterial(featureClass, widthM) {
      const classKey = String(featureClass || "lane_divider").toLowerCase();
      const colors = MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors ? MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors : {};
      const dash = MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.dashMeters ? MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.dashMeters : {};
      const colorHex = Number(colors[classKey] || colors.lane_divider || 0xffcf33);
      const dashLength = Number.isFinite(Number(dash[classKey])) ? Number(dash[classKey]) : Number(dash.lane_divider) || 4.5;
      const gapLength = Number.isFinite(Number(dash.lane_gap)) ? Number(dash.lane_gap) : 4.5;
      const lineWidth = Math.max(0.05, Number(widthM) || 0.2);
      const halfWidth = lineWidth * 0.5;
      const feather = Math.max(
        0.01,
        Math.min(
          halfWidth * 0.8,
          Number.isFinite(Number(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.antialiasFeatherM))
            ? Number(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.antialiasFeatherM)
            : 0.06
        )
      );
      return new THREE.ShaderMaterial({
        transparent: true,
        depthTest: true,
        depthWrite: false,
        polygonOffset: true,
        polygonOffsetFactor: -5,
        polygonOffsetUnits: -5,
        uniforms: {
          uColor: { value: new THREE.Color(colorHex) },
          uDashLength: { value: Math.max(0.1, dashLength) },
          uGapLength: { value: Math.max(0.0, gapLength) },
          uHalfWidth: { value: halfWidth },
          uFeather: { value: feather },
          uOpacity: { value: 0.98 },
        },
        vertexShader: [
          "attribute float lineDistance;",
          "attribute float side;",
          "varying float vLineDistance;",
          "varying float vSide;",
          "void main() {",
          "  vLineDistance = lineDistance;",
          "  vSide = side;",
          "  gl_Position = projectionMatrix * modelViewMatrix * vec4(position, 1.0);",
          "}",
        ].join("\\n"),
        fragmentShader: [
          "uniform vec3 uColor;",
          "uniform float uDashLength;",
          "uniform float uGapLength;",
          "uniform float uHalfWidth;",
          "uniform float uFeather;",
          "uniform float uOpacity;",
          "varying float vLineDistance;",
          "varying float vSide;",
          "void main() {",
          "  float cycle = max(0.001, uDashLength + uGapLength);",
          "  float cyclePos = mod(vLineDistance, cycle);",
          "  float dashAlpha = 1.0 - smoothstep(max(0.0, uDashLength - uFeather), uDashLength + uFeather, cyclePos);",
          "  float edgeDist = abs(vSide) * uHalfWidth;",
          "  float edgeAlpha = 1.0 - smoothstep(max(0.0, uHalfWidth - uFeather), uHalfWidth, edgeDist);",
          "  float alpha = clamp(dashAlpha * edgeAlpha * uOpacity, 0.0, 1.0);",
          "  if (alpha <= 0.01) discard;",
          "  gl_FragColor = vec4(uColor, alpha);",
          "}",
        ].join("\\n"),
      });
    }

    function buildStreetLayerManager() {
      if (state.streetLayerManager) {
        return state.streetLayerManager;
      }
      const assetsGroup = new THREE.Group();
      assetsGroup.name = "streetAssetsGroup";
      state.scene.add(assetsGroup);
      const markingsGroup = new THREE.Group();
      markingsGroup.name = "streetMarkingsGroup";
      state.scene.add(markingsGroup);

      const manager = {
        assetsGroup,
        markingsGroup,
        tiles: new Map(),
        pending: new Set(),
        desired: new Set(),
        lastTickMs: 0,
        currentZoom: null,
        loaded: 0,
        failed: 0,
        ready: false,
        warning: "",
        maxActiveTiles: Number(STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.maxActiveTiles) || 24,
        maxAssetInstances: Number(STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.maxAssetInstances) || 3200,
        hysteresisMs: Number(STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.hysteresisMs) || 9000,
        requestIntervalMs: Number(STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.requestIntervalMs) || 900,
        featureCounts: {
          street_asset: 0,
          street_tree: 0,
          marking: 0,
          traffic_control: 0,
          total: 0,
        },
        failureBackoffByKey: new Map(),
        failureReasonByKey: new Map(),
        assetTemplateByClass: new Map(),
        instancingEnabled: true,
        materials: {
          lane_divider: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: Number(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors.lane_divider) || 0xf4de63,
            roughness: 0.96,
            metalness: 0.02,
            depthWrite: false,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -5,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -5,
          }),
          stop_line: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: Number(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors.stop_line) || 0xffffff,
            roughness: 0.95,
            metalness: 0.01,
            depthWrite: false,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -5,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -5,
          }),
          crosswalk_marking: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: Number(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors.crosswalk_marking) || 0xf7f9fc,
            roughness: 0.95,
            metalness: 0.01,
            depthWrite: false,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -5,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -5,
          }),
          turn_arrow_anchor: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: Number(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors.turn_arrow_anchor) || 0xeef2f8,
            roughness: 0.94,
            metalness: 0.02,
            depthWrite: false,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -5,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -5,
          }),
          junction_area: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0x8ea5b8,
            roughness: 0.96,
            metalness: 0.01,
            transparent: true,
            opacity: 0.28,
            depthWrite: false,
            polygonOffset: true,
            polygonOffsetFactor: -5,
            polygonOffsetUnits: -5,
          }),
          street_lamp: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xf2d479,
            emissive: 0xc18a1a,
            emissiveIntensity: 0.22,
            roughness: 0.82,
            metalness: 0.22,
          }),
          lamp_emissive: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xfff3c2,
            emissive: 0xffd56a,
            emissiveIntensity: 0.6,
            roughness: 0.6,
            metalness: 0.08,
          }),
          stop_sign: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xff3650,
            emissive: 0x4a0a15,
            emissiveIntensity: 0.2,
            roughness: 0.72,
            metalness: 0.08,
          }),
          traffic_signal: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0x3ed36d,
            emissive: 0x0b3319,
            emissiveIntensity: 0.24,
            roughness: 0.84,
            metalness: 0.12,
          }),
          crosswalk_hint: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0x2a7cff,
            emissive: 0x061126,
            emissiveIntensity: 0.22,
            roughness: 0.72,
            metalness: 0.08,
          }),
          turn_restriction_hint: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0xf9f2e3,
            emissive: 0x23140a,
            emissiveIntensity: 0.16,
            roughness: 0.7,
            metalness: 0.06,
          }),
          street_tree_trunk: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0x7d5637,
            roughness: 0.92,
            metalness: 0.02,
          }),
          street_tree_canopy: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
            color: 0x4f9a55,
            emissive: 0x16331b,
            emissiveIntensity: 0.16,
            roughness: 0.88,
            metalness: 0.01,
          }),
        },
      };
      manager.materials.lane_divider_dashed = createDashedMarkingMaterial(
        "lane_divider",
        getStreetLayerWidthM("lane_divider")
      );
      if (manager.materials.lane_divider_dashed) {
        manager.materials.lane_divider_dashed.name = "lane_divider_dashed";
      }
      state.streetInstancingEnabled = !!manager.instancingEnabled;
      state.markingShaderMode = isDashedMarkingClass("lane_divider") ? "dashed_aa" : "legacy_solid";
      state.streetLayerManager = manager;
      return manager;
    }

    function getStreetLayerOffsetM(featureClass) {
      const offsets = MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.offsetsM ? MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.offsetsM : {};
      const value = Number(offsets[featureClass]);
      const hardFloor = featureClass === "junction_area" ? 0.34 : 0.36;
      if (Number.isFinite(value)) return Math.max(value, hardFloor);
      if (featureClass === "junction_area") return 0.34;
      return 0.36;
    }

    function getStreetLayerWidthM(featureClass) {
      const widths = MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.widthsM ? MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.widthsM : {};
      const value = Number(widths[featureClass]);
      if (Number.isFinite(value) && value > 0.01) return value;
      if (featureClass === "stop_line") return 0.42;
      if (featureClass === "crosswalk_marking") return 2.8;
      if (featureClass === "turn_arrow_anchor") return 1.2;
      return 0.2;
    }

    function getStreetLayerManifestEntry(layerKey) {
      const manifest = STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST && typeof STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST === "object"
        ? STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST
        : {};
      const layers = manifest.layers && typeof manifest.layers === "object" ? manifest.layers : {};
      return {
        manifest,
        layer: layers[layerKey] && typeof layers[layerKey] === "object" ? layers[layerKey] : {},
      };
    }

    async function fetchStreetLayerFeaturesFromManifestTile(layerKey, zoom, x, y) {
      const cacheKey = String(layerKey) + "/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      const cached = streetLayerTileFeatureCache.get(cacheKey);
      if (cached && cached.expiresAt > Date.now()) {
        return Array.isArray(cached.features) ? cached.features : [];
      }

      const { manifest, layer } = getStreetLayerManifestEntry(layerKey);
      const basePath = manifest.basePath ? String(manifest.basePath) : "";
      const layerBasePath = layer.basePath ? String(layer.basePath) : "";
      const tileKey = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      const urls = [];
      const flatPrefix = String(layerKey) === "streetAssets"
        ? "street_asset"
        : (String(layerKey) === "streetMarkings" ? "street_marking" : "street");
      const flatName = flatPrefix + "_z" + String(zoom) + "_x" + String(x) + "_y" + String(y) + ".json";
      const layerFolderName = String(layerKey) === "streetAssets" ? "street_assets_tiles" : "street_markings_tiles";

      if (layer.tileIndex && typeof layer.tileIndex === "object") {
        const indexed = layer.tileIndex[tileKey];
        if (typeof indexed === "string" && indexed.length > 0) {
          const lower = indexed.toLowerCase();
          if (lower.startsWith("http://") || lower.startsWith("https://")) {
            urls.push(indexed);
          } else {
            urls.push(basePath ? joinAssetPath(basePath, indexed) : indexed);
          }
        }
      }
      if (layer.urlTemplate && typeof layer.urlTemplate === "string") {
        urls.push(
          String(layer.urlTemplate)
            .replace("{z}", String(zoom))
            .replace("{x}", String(x))
            .replace("{y}", String(y))
        );
      }
      if (layerBasePath) {
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(layerBasePath, String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json"));
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(layerBasePath, flatName));
        if (basePath && !/^https?:\\/\\//i.test(layerBasePath)) {
          const relativeLayerPath = trimLeadingSlashes(normalizeAssetPath(layerBasePath).replace(/^\\.\\/+/, ""));
          if (relativeLayerPath) {
            urls.push(
              joinAssetPath(
                basePath,
                relativeLayerPath + "/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json"
              )
            );
            urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, relativeLayerPath + "/" + flatName));
          }
        }
      }
      if (basePath) {
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json"));
        // Flat packed patch-assets fallback (street_asset_z*_x*_y*.json / street_marking_z*_x*_y*.json)
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, flatName));
        urls.push(
          joinAssetPath(basePath, layerFolderName + "/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json")
        );
      }
      urls.push("./patch_assets/" + flatName);
      urls.push("patch_assets/" + flatName);
      urls.push("./" + flatName);
      urls.push(flatName);
      urls.push("./patch_assets/" + layerFolderName + "/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("patch_assets/" + layerFolderName + "/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("./" + layerFolderName + "/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push(layerFolderName + "/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      const uniqueUrls = Array.from(new Set(urls.filter((value) => typeof value === "string" && value.length > 0)));
      if (uniqueUrls.length <= 0) {
        streetLayerTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, { features: [], expiresAt: Date.now() + 60000 });
        return [];
      }

      for (const url of uniqueUrls) {
        try {
          const payload = await tryFetchJsonCandidate(url, 7000, isFeatureCollectionPayload);
          if (!payload || !Array.isArray(payload.features)) continue;
          const features = [];
          for (const feature of payload.features) {
            features.push(...flattenNormalizedStreetFeatures(normalizeStreetLayerFeature(feature, "osm")));
          }
          if (features.length > 0) {
            const merged = [];
            const seen = new Set();
            for (const feature of features) {
              const key = buildStreetFeatureMergeKey(feature);
              if (key && seen.has(key)) continue;
              if (key) seen.add(key);
              merged.push(feature);
            }
            streetLayerTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, { features: merged, expiresAt: Date.now() + 5 * 60 * 1000 });
            return merged;
          }
        } catch (_error) {
          // continue to next URL candidate
        }
      }

      streetLayerTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, { features: [], expiresAt: Date.now() + 60 * 1000 });
      return [];
    }

    function appendStreetMarkingRibbon(builder, coordinates, widthM, featureClass, centerECEF) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coordinates) || coordinates.length < 2) return 0;
      const scopeBounds = getActiveWardBounds();
      const halfWidth = Math.max(0.05, Number(widthM) * 0.5);
      const offsetM = getStreetLayerOffsetM(featureClass);
      const worldPoint = new THREE.Vector3();
      const maxGapM = Number.isFinite(Number(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG && MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.maxSegmentGapM))
        ? clamp(Number(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.maxSegmentGapM), 12, 180)
        : 60;
      const tangent = new THREE.Vector3();
      const up = new THREE.Vector3();
      const right = new THREE.Vector3();
      const segments = [];
      let currentSegment = [];
      const flushSegment = () => {
        if (currentSegment.length >= 2) {
          segments.push(currentSegment);
        }
        currentSegment = [];
      };
      for (const coord of coordinates) {
        if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) {
          flushSegment();
          continue;
        }
        const lon = Number(coord[0]);
        const lat = Number(coord[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat) || !isWithinAnyBounds(lon, lat, scopeBounds)) {
          flushSegment();
          continue;
        }
        let heightM = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lon, lat);
        if (!Number.isFinite(heightM)) {
          heightM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
        }
        worldPoint.copy(lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM + offsetM));
        const nextPoint = worldPoint.clone();
        const lastPoint = currentSegment.length > 0 ? currentSegment[currentSegment.length - 1] : null;
        if (lastPoint) {
          const jumpM = nextPoint.distanceTo(lastPoint);
          if (!Number.isFinite(jumpM) || jumpM > maxGapM) {
            flushSegment();
          } else if (jumpM < 0.08) {
            continue;
          }
        }
        currentSegment.push(nextPoint);
      }
      flushSegment();
      if (segments.length <= 0) return 0;

      let appendedAny = 0;
      for (const points of segments) {
        if (!Array.isArray(points) || points.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        const startVertex = builder.positions.length / 3;
        const startPositionLen = builder.positions.length;
        const startLineLen = Array.isArray(builder.lineDistance) ? builder.lineDistance.length : 0;
        const startSideLen = Array.isArray(builder.side) ? builder.side.length : 0;
        let runningDistanceM = 0;
        for (let i = 0; i < points.length; i += 1) {
          const point = points[i];
          if (i > 0) {
            runningDistanceM += points[i].distanceTo(points[i - 1]);
          }
          const prev = points[Math.max(0, i - 1)];
          const next = points[Math.min(points.length - 1, i + 1)];
          tangent.copy(next).sub(prev);
          up.copy(point).normalize();
          tangent.addScaledVector(up, -tangent.dot(up));
          if (tangent.lengthSq() < 1e-10) continue;
          tangent.normalize();
          right.crossVectors(tangent, up);
          if (right.lengthSq() < 1e-10) continue;
          right.normalize();

          const leftPoint = point.clone().addScaledVector(right, halfWidth);
          const rightPoint = point.clone().addScaledVector(right, -halfWidth);
          builder.positions.push(
            leftPoint.x - centerECEF.x,
            leftPoint.y - centerECEF.y,
            leftPoint.z - centerECEF.z,
            rightPoint.x - centerECEF.x,
            rightPoint.y - centerECEF.y,
            rightPoint.z - centerECEF.z
          );
          if (Array.isArray(builder.lineDistance)) {
            builder.lineDistance.push(runningDistanceM, runningDistanceM);
          }
          if (Array.isArray(builder.side)) {
            builder.side.push(1, -1);
          }
        }
        const vertexPairs = Math.floor((builder.positions.length / 3 - startVertex) / 2);
        if (vertexPairs < 2) {
          builder.positions.length = startPositionLen;
          if (Array.isArray(builder.lineDistance)) {
            builder.lineDistance.length = startLineLen;
          }
          if (Array.isArray(builder.side)) {
            builder.side.length = startSideLen;
          }
          continue;
        }
        for (let i = 0; i < vertexPairs - 1; i += 1) {
          const a = startVertex + i * 2;
          const b = a + 1;
          const c = a + 2;
          const d = a + 3;
          builder.indices.push(a, c, b);
          builder.indices.push(b, c, d);
        }
        appendedAny = 1;
      }
      return appendedAny;
    }

    function appendStreetMarkingPolygon(builder, coordinates, featureClass, centerECEF) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coordinates) || coordinates.length < 3) return 0;
      const scopeBounds = getActiveWardBounds();
      const offsetM = getStreetLayerOffsetM(featureClass);
      const ring = coordinates.slice();
      if (ring.length >= 2) {
        const first = ring[0];
        const last = ring[ring.length - 1];
        if (
          Array.isArray(first) &&
          Array.isArray(last) &&
          first.length >= 2 &&
          last.length >= 2 &&
          Number(first[0]) === Number(last[0]) &&
          Number(first[1]) === Number(last[1])
        ) {
          ring.pop();
        }
      }
      if (ring.length < 3) return 0;
      const startVertex = builder.positions.length / 3;
      for (const coord of ring) {
        if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) continue;
        const lon = Number(coord[0]);
        const lat = Number(coord[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) continue;
        if (!isWithinAnyBounds(lon, lat, scopeBounds)) continue;
        let heightM = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lon, lat);
        if (!Number.isFinite(heightM)) {
          heightM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
        }
        const point = lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM + offsetM);
        builder.positions.push(
          point.x - centerECEF.x,
          point.y - centerECEF.y,
          point.z - centerECEF.z
        );
      }
      const vertexCount = builder.positions.length / 3 - startVertex;
      if (vertexCount < 3) return 0;
      for (let i = 1; i < vertexCount - 1; i += 1) {
        builder.indices.push(startVertex, startVertex + i, startVertex + i + 1);
      }
      return 1;
    }

    function appendParkPolygon(builder, coordinates, centerECEF, offsetOverrideM) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coordinates) || coordinates.length < 3) return 0;
      const scopeBounds = getActiveWardBounds();
      const offsetM = Number.isFinite(offsetOverrideM)
        ? Number(offsetOverrideM)
        : (Number.isFinite(Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.offsetM))
          ? Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.offsetM)
          : 0.2);
      const minAreaM2 = Number.isFinite(Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.minAreaM2))
        ? Math.max(0, Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.minAreaM2))
        : 0;
      const minCompactness = Number.isFinite(Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.minCompactness))
        ? clamp(Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.minCompactness), 0, 0.4)
        : 0;
      const rawRing = normalizeParkRingCoordinates(coordinates);
      if (rawRing.length < 3) return 0;
      // Keep full rings. Per-vertex clipping creates malformed polygons and visible overlaps/spikes.
      const scopedRing = rawRing;
      let intersectsScope = !Array.isArray(scopeBounds) || scopeBounds.length <= 0;
      for (const coord of scopedRing) {
        if (isWithinAnyBounds(Number(coord[0]), Number(coord[1]), scopeBounds)) {
          intersectsScope = true;
          break;
        }
      }
      if (!intersectsScope) {
        return 0;
      }

      // Filter tiny/sliver park fragments that usually come from noisy tags near roads.
      let lonRef = 0;
      let latRef = 0;
      for (const coord of scopedRing) {
        lonRef += coord[0];
        latRef += coord[1];
      }
      lonRef /= scopedRing.length;
      latRef /= scopedRing.length;
      const metersPerDegLat = 111320;
      const metersPerDegLon = Math.max(1e-3, Math.cos(latRef * Math.PI / 180) * 111320);
      const projected = scopedRing.map((coord) => [
        (coord[0] - lonRef) * metersPerDegLon,
        (coord[1] - latRef) * metersPerDegLat,
      ]);
      let twiceArea = 0;
      let perimeterM = 0;
      for (let i = 0; i < projected.length; i += 1) {
        const a = projected[i];
        const b = projected[(i + 1) % projected.length];
        twiceArea += a[0] * b[1] - b[0] * a[1];
        perimeterM += Math.hypot(b[0] - a[0], b[1] - a[1]);
      }
      const areaM2 = Math.abs(twiceArea) * 0.5;
      const compactness = perimeterM > 1e-3 ? (4 * Math.PI * areaM2) / (perimeterM * perimeterM) : 0;
      if (!Number.isFinite(areaM2) || !Number.isFinite(perimeterM) || areaM2 < 0.5 || perimeterM < 0.5) {
        return 0;
      }
      if ((minAreaM2 > 0 && areaM2 < minAreaM2) || (minCompactness > 0 && compactness < minCompactness)) {
        return 0;
      }

      const contour = scopedRing.map((coord) => new THREE.Vector2(coord[0], coord[1]));
      const localPoints = [];
      for (const coord of scopedRing) {
        const lon = Number(coord[0]);
        const lat = Number(coord[1]);
        let heightM = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lon, lat);
        if (!Number.isFinite(heightM)) {
          heightM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
        }
        const point = lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM + offsetM);
        localPoints.push([
          point.x - centerECEF.x,
          point.y - centerECEF.y,
          point.z - centerECEF.z,
        ]);
      }
      if (localPoints.length < 3 || contour.length < 3) {
        return 0;
      }

      if (THREE.ShapeUtils && typeof THREE.ShapeUtils.isClockWise === "function" && THREE.ShapeUtils.isClockWise(contour)) {
        contour.reverse();
        localPoints.reverse();
      }

      let triangles = null;
      try {
        if (THREE.ShapeUtils && typeof THREE.ShapeUtils.triangulateShape === "function") {
          triangles = THREE.ShapeUtils.triangulateShape(contour, []);
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        triangles = null;
      }

      const startVertex = builder.positions.length / 3;
      for (const local of localPoints) {
        builder.positions.push(local[0], local[1], local[2]);
      }
      const vertexCount = localPoints.length;
      if (vertexCount < 3) return 0;

      let triCount = 0;
      if (Array.isArray(triangles) && triangles.length > 0) {
        for (const tri of triangles) {
          if (!Array.isArray(tri) || tri.length < 3) continue;
          const ia = Number(tri[0]);
          const ib = Number(tri[1]);
          const ic = Number(tri[2]);
          if (
            !Number.isFinite(ia) ||
            !Number.isFinite(ib) ||
            !Number.isFinite(ic) ||
            ia < 0 ||
            ib < 0 ||
            ic < 0 ||
            ia >= vertexCount ||
            ib >= vertexCount ||
            ic >= vertexCount
          ) {
            continue;
          }
          builder.indices.push(startVertex + ia, startVertex + ib, startVertex + ic);
          triCount += 1;
        }
      }
      if (triCount <= 0) {
        for (let i = 1; i < vertexCount - 1; i += 1) {
          builder.indices.push(startVertex, startVertex + i, startVertex + i + 1);
        }
      }
      return 1;
    }

    function createStreetMarkingGeometry(build) {
      const geometry = createTransportGeometry(build);
      if (!geometry) return null;
      const vertexCount = build.positions.length / 3;
      if (Array.isArray(build.lineDistance) && build.lineDistance.length === vertexCount) {
        geometry.setAttribute("lineDistance", new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(build.lineDistance, 1));
      }
      if (Array.isArray(build.side) && build.side.length === vertexCount) {
        geometry.setAttribute("side", new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(build.side, 1));
      }
      return geometry;
    }

    function buildStreetAssetMesh(featureClass, manager) {
      if (!manager || !manager.materials) return null;
      if (featureClass === "street_lamp") {
        const group = new THREE.Group();
        const pole = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.09, 0.12, 5.6, 7), manager.materials.street_lamp);
        pole.position.set(0, 2.8, 0);
        const arm = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.8, 0.08, 0.08), manager.materials.street_lamp);
        arm.position.set(0.32, 5.4, 0);
        const bulb = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.16, 8, 8), manager.materials.lamp_emissive);
        bulb.position.set(0.64, 5.36, 0);
        group.add(pole, arm, bulb);
        return group;
      }
      if (featureClass === "traffic_signal") {
        const group = new THREE.Group();
        const pole = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.08, 0.1, 4.2, 7), manager.materials.street_lamp);
        pole.position.set(0, 2.1, 0);
        const head = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.26, 0.78, 0.24), manager.materials.traffic_signal);
        head.position.set(0.22, 4.1, 0);
        group.add(pole, head);
        return group;
      }
      if (featureClass === "stop_sign") {
        const group = new THREE.Group();
        const pole = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.04, 0.05, 2.4, 6), manager.materials.street_lamp);
        pole.position.set(0, 1.2, 0);
        const sign = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.33, 0.33, 0.05, 8), manager.materials.stop_sign);
        sign.rotation.x = Math.PI / 2;
        sign.position.set(0.2, 2.1, 0);
        group.add(pole, sign);
        return group;
      }
      if (featureClass === "crosswalk_hint") {
        const group = new THREE.Group();
        const pole = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.04, 0.05, 2.45, 6), manager.materials.street_lamp);
        pole.position.set(0, 1.22, 0);
        const board = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.68, 0.72, 0.06), manager.materials.crosswalk_hint);
        board.position.set(0.16, 2.16, 0);
        const stripeA = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.46, 0.08, 0.02), manager.materials.crosswalk_marking);
        const stripeB = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.46, 0.08, 0.02), manager.materials.crosswalk_marking);
        stripeA.position.set(0.16, 2.03, 0.04);
        stripeB.position.set(0.16, 2.22, 0.04);
        stripeA.rotation.z = -0.5;
        stripeB.rotation.z = -0.5;
        group.add(pole, board, stripeA, stripeB);
        return group;
      }
      if (featureClass === "turn_restriction_hint") {
        const group = new THREE.Group();
        const pole = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.04, 0.05, 2.35, 6), manager.materials.street_lamp);
        pole.position.set(0, 1.17, 0);
        const disc = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.31, 0.31, 0.05, 18), manager.materials.turn_restriction_hint);
        disc.rotation.x = Math.PI / 2;
        disc.position.set(0.17, 2.08, 0);
        const slash = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.42, 0.07, 0.02), manager.materials.stop_sign);
        slash.position.set(0.17, 2.08, 0.03);
        slash.rotation.z = -0.68;
        const arrow = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.2, 0.05, 0.02), manager.materials.stop_sign);
        arrow.position.set(0.25, 2.16, 0.03);
        arrow.rotation.z = -0.12;
        group.add(pole, disc, slash, arrow);
        return group;
      }
      if (featureClass === "street_tree") {
        const group = new THREE.Group();
        const trunk = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.1, 0.14, 2.2, 7), manager.materials.street_tree_trunk);
        trunk.position.set(0, 1.1, 0);
        const canopyBase = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.ConeGeometry(1.15, 1.45, 8), manager.materials.street_tree_canopy);
        canopyBase.position.set(0, 2.45, 0);
        const canopyTop = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.ConeGeometry(0.85, 1.0, 8), manager.materials.street_tree_canopy);
        canopyTop.position.set(0, 3.35, 0);
        group.add(trunk, canopyBase, canopyTop);
        return group;
      }
      return null;
    }

    function getStreetAssetTemplateParts(featureClass, manager) {
      if (!manager || !(manager.assetTemplateByClass instanceof Map)) {
        return [];
      }
      if (manager.assetTemplateByClass.has(featureClass)) {
        const cached = manager.assetTemplateByClass.get(featureClass);
        return Array.isArray(cached) ? cached : [];
      }
      const template = buildStreetAssetMesh(featureClass, manager);
      if (!template) {
        manager.assetTemplateByClass.set(featureClass, []);
        return [];
      }
      template.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      const parts = [];
      template.traverse((child) => {
        if (!child || !child.isMesh || !child.geometry || !child.material) {
          return;
        }
        child.updateMatrix();
        parts.push({
          geometry: child.geometry,
          material: child.material,
          localMatrix: child.matrix.clone(),
        });
      });
      manager.assetTemplateByClass.set(featureClass, parts);
      return parts;
    }

    function buildStreetMarkingTileGroup(tile, features) {
      const manager = buildStreetLayerManager();
      const bounds = tile.bounds;
      const centerECEF = lonLatToECEF(
        (bounds.west + bounds.east) * 0.5,
        (bounds.south + bounds.north) * 0.5,
        0
      );
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.position.copy(centerECEF);
      group.name = "streetMarkingsTile:" + tile.key;
      const geoUp = centerECEF.clone().normalize();
      const worldUp = new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0);
      const orientQ = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromUnitVectors(worldUp, geoUp);
      const localPos = new THREE.Vector3();
      const pointPlacements = {
        turn_arrow_anchor: [],
      };

      const builders = {
        lane_divider: { positions: [], indices: [], lineDistance: [], side: [] },
        stop_line: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        crosswalk_marking: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        turn_arrow_anchor: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        junction_area: { positions: [], indices: [] },
      };
      let count = 0;
      for (const feature of features) {
        if (!feature) continue;
        const cls = String(feature.featureClass || "").toLowerCase();
        if (!builders[cls]) {
          continue;
        }
        if (feature.geometryType === "LineString") {
          const widthM = getStreetLayerWidthM(cls);
          const appended = appendStreetMarkingRibbon(
            builders[cls],
            feature.coordinates,
            widthM,
            cls,
            centerECEF
          );
          count += appended;
          continue;
        }
        if (feature.geometryType === "Polygon") {
          const appended = appendStreetMarkingPolygon(
            builders[cls],
            feature.coordinates,
            cls,
            centerECEF
          );
          count += appended;
          continue;
        }
        if (feature.geometryType === "Point" && cls === "turn_arrow_anchor" && Array.isArray(feature.coordinates)) {
          const lon = Number(feature.coordinates[0]);
          const lat = Number(feature.coordinates[1]);
          if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
            continue;
          }
          let heightM = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lon, lat);
          if (!Number.isFinite(heightM)) {
            heightM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
          }
          const world = lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM + getStreetLayerOffsetM(cls));
          localPos.copy(world).sub(centerECEF);
          const matrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
          matrix.compose(localPos, orientQ, new THREE.Vector3(1, 1, 1));
          pointPlacements.turn_arrow_anchor.push(matrix);
          count += 1;
        }
      }

      const renderOrderByClass = {
        junction_area: 43,
        lane_divider: 44,
        stop_line: 47,
        turn_arrow_anchor: 47,
        crosswalk_marking: 49,
      };
      for (const cls of Object.keys(builders)) {
        const geometry = createStreetMarkingGeometry(builders[cls]);
        if (!geometry) continue;
        const useDashedShader = cls === "lane_divider" && isDashedMarkingClass(cls) && !!manager.materials.lane_divider_dashed;
        const material = useDashedShader
          ? manager.materials.lane_divider_dashed
          : (manager.materials[cls] || manager.materials.lane_divider);
        const mesh = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, material);
        mesh.frustumCulled = true;
        mesh.renderOrder = Number.isFinite(renderOrderByClass[cls]) ? renderOrderByClass[cls] : 45;
        group.add(mesh);
      }
      if (pointPlacements.turn_arrow_anchor.length > 0) {
        const geometry = new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.18, 0.18, 0.04, 6);
        const instanced = new THREE.InstancedMesh(
          geometry,
          manager.materials.turn_arrow_anchor || manager.materials.stop_line,
          pointPlacements.turn_arrow_anchor.length
        );
        instanced.frustumCulled = true;
        instanced.renderOrder = 48;
        for (let i = 0; i < pointPlacements.turn_arrow_anchor.length; i += 1) {
          instanced.setMatrixAt(i, pointPlacements.turn_arrow_anchor[i]);
        }
        instanced.instanceMatrix.needsUpdate = true;
        group.add(instanced);
      }

      state.markingShaderMode = isDashedMarkingClass("lane_divider") ? "dashed_aa" : "legacy_solid";

      return {
        group,
        count,
      };
    }

    function buildStreetAssetTileGroup(tile, features) {
      const manager = buildStreetLayerManager();
      const bounds = tile.bounds;
      const scopeBounds = getActiveWardBounds();
      const centerECEF = lonLatToECEF(
        (bounds.west + bounds.east) * 0.5,
        (bounds.south + bounds.north) * 0.5,
        0
      );
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.position.copy(centerECEF);
      group.name = "streetAssetsTile:" + tile.key;
      let count = 0;
      const globalCap = Math.max(600, Number(manager.maxAssetInstances) || 3200);
      const currentCount = Number.isFinite(manager.featureCounts && manager.featureCounts.street_asset)
        ? Number(manager.featureCounts.street_asset)
        : 0;
      const remainingCap = Math.max(0, globalCap - currentCount);
      const perTileCapRaw = Number(STREET_LAYER_CONFIG && STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.assetMaxPerTile);
      const perTileCapMax = Number.isFinite(perTileCapRaw) ? Math.max(120, Math.trunc(perTileCapRaw)) : 1200;
      const perTileCap = Math.max(120, Math.min(perTileCapMax, remainingCap));
      const currentTreeCount = Number.isFinite(manager.featureCounts && manager.featureCounts.street_tree)
        ? Number(manager.featureCounts.street_tree)
        : 0;
      const treeMaxPerTileRaw = Number(STREET_LAYER_CONFIG && STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.treeMaxPerTile);
      const treeMaxGlobalRaw = Number(STREET_LAYER_CONFIG && STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.treeMaxGlobal);
      const treeMaxDistanceRaw = Number(STREET_LAYER_CONFIG && STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.treeMaxDistanceM);
      const treeReserveRatioRaw = Number(STREET_LAYER_CONFIG && STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.treeReserveRatio);
      const treeMaxPerTile = Number.isFinite(treeMaxPerTileRaw) ? Math.max(0, Math.trunc(treeMaxPerTileRaw)) : 600;
      const treeMaxGlobal = Number.isFinite(treeMaxGlobalRaw) ? Math.max(0, Math.trunc(treeMaxGlobalRaw)) : 6000;
      const treeMaxDistanceM = Number.isFinite(treeMaxDistanceRaw) ? Math.max(0, treeMaxDistanceRaw) : 4500;
      const treeReserveRatio = Number.isFinite(treeReserveRatioRaw) ? clamp(treeReserveRatioRaw, 0.2, 0.9) : 0.58;
      const remainingTreeGlobal = Math.max(0, treeMaxGlobal - currentTreeCount);
      const treeTileCap = Math.max(0, Math.min(treeMaxPerTile, remainingTreeGlobal));
      let treeCount = 0;
      const geoUp = centerECEF.clone().normalize();
      const worldUp = new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0);
      const orientQ = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromUnitVectors(worldUp, geoUp);
      const scale = new THREE.Vector3(1.2, 1.2, 1.2);
      const treeScale = new THREE.Vector3(1, 1, 1);
      const placementByClass = {
        street_lamp: [],
        stop_sign: [],
        traffic_signal: [],
        crosswalk_hint: [],
        turn_restriction_hint: [],
        street_tree: [],
      };
      const placementMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
      const localPos = new THREE.Vector3();
      const cameraPosition = state.camera && state.camera.position ? state.camera.position : null;

      const criticalFeatures = [];
      const treeFeatures = [];
      for (const feature of features) {
        if (!feature || feature.geometryType !== "Point" || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates)) {
          continue;
        }
        const featureClass = String(feature.featureClass || "").toLowerCase();
        if (!placementByClass[featureClass]) {
          continue;
        }
        if (featureClass === "street_tree") {
          treeFeatures.push(feature);
        } else {
          criticalFeatures.push(feature);
        }
      }
      criticalFeatures.sort((a, b) => (Number(b && b.priority) || 0) - (Number(a && a.priority) || 0));
      treeFeatures.sort((a, b) => (Number(b && b.priority) || 0) - (Number(a && a.priority) || 0));
      const reservedTreeSlots = Math.min(treeTileCap, Math.max(0, Math.floor(perTileCap * treeReserveRatio)));
      const criticalCap = Math.max(0, perTileCap - reservedTreeSlots);

      const treeScaleFromLonLat = (lon, lat) => {
        const seeded = Math.abs(Math.sin((lon * 12.9898) + (lat * 78.233)) * 43758.5453);
        const noise = seeded - Math.floor(seeded);
        treeScale.set(
          0.86 + noise * 0.34,
          0.9 + noise * 0.44,
          0.86 + (1 - noise) * 0.32
        );
      };

      const placeFeature = (feature, featureClass) => {
        const lon = Number(feature.coordinates[0]);
        const lat = Number(feature.coordinates[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) return false;
        if (!isWithinAnyBounds(lon, lat, scopeBounds)) return false;
        if (!placementByClass[featureClass]) return false;
        if (featureClass === "street_tree") {
          if (treeCount >= treeTileCap) {
            return false;
          }
        }
        let heightM = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lon, lat);
        if (!Number.isFinite(heightM)) {
          heightM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
        }
        const ecef = lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM + 0.32);
        if (featureClass === "street_tree" && treeMaxDistanceM > 0 && cameraPosition) {
          if (cameraPosition.distanceTo(ecef) > treeMaxDistanceM) {
            return false;
          }
        }
        localPos.copy(ecef).sub(centerECEF);
        if (featureClass === "street_tree") {
          treeScaleFromLonLat(lon, lat);
          placementMatrix.compose(localPos, orientQ, treeScale);
          treeCount += 1;
        } else {
          placementMatrix.compose(localPos, orientQ, scale);
        }
        placementByClass[featureClass].push(placementMatrix.clone());
        count += 1;
        return true;
      };

      for (const feature of criticalFeatures) {
        if (count >= criticalCap) {
          break;
        }
        placeFeature(feature, String(feature.featureClass || "").toLowerCase());
      }
      for (const feature of treeFeatures) {
        if (count >= perTileCap || treeCount >= treeTileCap) {
          break;
        }
        placeFeature(feature, "street_tree");
      }

      const childMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
      const instanceMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
      const classCounts = {};
      for (const featureClass of Object.keys(placementByClass)) {
        const placements = placementByClass[featureClass];
        classCounts[featureClass] = Array.isArray(placements) ? placements.length : 0;
        if (!Array.isArray(placements) || placements.length <= 0) {
          continue;
        }
        const templateParts = getStreetAssetTemplateParts(featureClass, manager);
        if (!Array.isArray(templateParts) || templateParts.length <= 0) {
          continue;
        }
        for (const part of templateParts) {
          if (!part || !part.geometry || !part.material || !part.localMatrix) {
            continue;
          }
          const instanced = new THREE.InstancedMesh(part.geometry, part.material, placements.length);
          instanced.renderOrder = 46;
          instanced.frustumCulled = true;
          instanced.userData.sharedTemplateGeometry = true;
          for (let i = 0; i < placements.length; i += 1) {
            childMatrix.copy(part.localMatrix);
            instanceMatrix.multiplyMatrices(placements[i], childMatrix);
            instanced.setMatrixAt(i, instanceMatrix);
          }
          instanced.instanceMatrix.needsUpdate = true;
          group.add(instanced);
        }
      }
      state.streetInstancingEnabled = true;
      return { group, count, classCounts };
    }

    async function loadStreetLayerTile(zoom, x, y) {
      const manager = buildStreetLayerManager();
      if (!(manager.failureBackoffByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureBackoffByKey = new Map();
      }
      if (!(manager.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureReasonByKey = new Map();
      }
      const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      if (manager.pending.has(key) || manager.tiles.has(key)) {
        return;
      }
      const backoffUntil = Number(manager.failureBackoffByKey.get(key)) || 0;
      if (backoffUntil > Date.now()) {
        return;
      }
      manager.pending.add(key);
      const bounds = slippyBounds(x, y, zoom);
      try {
        const allowTransportFallback = !(STREET_LAYER_CONFIG && STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.transportFallback === false);
        const assetsManifestLayer = getStreetLayerManifestEntry("streetAssets").layer;
        const markingsManifestLayer = getStreetLayerManifestEntry("streetMarkings").layer;
        const assetsTileIndex =
          assetsManifestLayer && assetsManifestLayer.tileIndex && typeof assetsManifestLayer.tileIndex === "object"
            ? assetsManifestLayer.tileIndex
            : null;
        const markingsTileIndex =
          markingsManifestLayer && markingsManifestLayer.tileIndex && typeof markingsManifestLayer.tileIndex === "object"
            ? markingsManifestLayer.tileIndex
            : null;
        const hasAssetsIndex = !!(assetsTileIndex && Object.keys(assetsTileIndex).length > 0);
        const hasMarkingsIndex = !!(markingsTileIndex && Object.keys(markingsTileIndex).length > 0);
        if (!hasAssetsIndex && !hasMarkingsIndex && !allowTransportFallback) {
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 60 * 1000);
          manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, "manifest_empty");
          return;
        }
        const assetsIndexed = !hasAssetsIndex || !!assetsTileIndex[key];
        const markingsIndexed = !hasMarkingsIndex || !!markingsTileIndex[key];
        if (!assetsIndexed && !markingsIndexed && !allowTransportFallback) {
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 60 * 1000);
          manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, "not_indexed");
          return;
        }

        let [assetFeatures, markingFeatures] = await Promise.all([
          assetsIndexed
            ? fetchStreetLayerFeaturesFromManifestTile("streetAssets", zoom, x, y)
            : Promise.resolve([]),
          markingsIndexed
            ? fetchStreetLayerFeaturesFromManifestTile("streetMarkings", zoom, x, y)
            : Promise.resolve([]),
        ]);
        if (
          allowTransportFallback &&
          (!Array.isArray(assetFeatures) || assetFeatures.length <= 0) &&
          (!Array.isArray(markingFeatures) || markingFeatures.length <= 0)
        ) {
          const transportResult = await fetchTransportFeaturesForTile(zoom, x, y, bounds);
          const synthesized = synthesizeStreetLayerFallbackFromTransport(
            transportResult && Array.isArray(transportResult.features) ? transportResult.features : [],
            bounds
          );
          if (
            synthesized &&
            ((Array.isArray(synthesized.assetFeatures) && synthesized.assetFeatures.length > 0) ||
              (Array.isArray(synthesized.markingFeatures) && synthesized.markingFeatures.length > 0))
          ) {
            assetFeatures = Array.isArray(synthesized.assetFeatures) ? synthesized.assetFeatures : [];
            markingFeatures = Array.isArray(synthesized.markingFeatures) ? synthesized.markingFeatures : [];
            debugLog("street_layers:transport_fallback", {
              key,
              transportFeatures:
                transportResult && Array.isArray(transportResult.features) ? transportResult.features.length : 0,
              assetFeatures: assetFeatures.length,
              treeFeatures: assetFeatures.filter((item) => item && item.featureClass === "street_tree").length,
              markingFeatures: markingFeatures.length,
            });
          }
        }

        const builtAssets = buildStreetAssetTileGroup({ key, z: zoom, x, y, bounds }, assetFeatures);
        const builtMarkings = buildStreetMarkingTileGroup({ key, z: zoom, x, y, bounds }, markingFeatures);
        const hasAnyRenderable =
          (builtAssets && builtAssets.group && Number(builtAssets.count) > 0) ||
          (builtMarkings && builtMarkings.group && Number(builtMarkings.count) > 0);
        if (!hasAnyRenderable) {
          manager.failed += 1;
          manager.warning = "Street layer tile has no renderable features: " + key;
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 20000);
          manager.failureReasonByKey.set(
            key,
            "no_renderable assets=" +
              String(Array.isArray(assetFeatures) ? assetFeatures.length : 0) +
              " markings=" +
              String(Array.isArray(markingFeatures) ? markingFeatures.length : 0)
          );
          if (manager.failed <= 8 || manager.failed % 50 === 0) {
            debugLog("street_layers:tile_no_renderable", {
              key,
              assetFeatures: Array.isArray(assetFeatures) ? assetFeatures.length : 0,
              markingFeatures: Array.isArray(markingFeatures) ? markingFeatures.length : 0,
            });
          }
          return;
        }

        if (builtAssets && builtAssets.group) {
          manager.assetsGroup.add(builtAssets.group);
        }
        if (builtMarkings && builtMarkings.group) {
          manager.markingsGroup.add(builtMarkings.group);
        }

        const tile = {
          key,
          z: zoom,
          x,
          y,
          bounds,
          assetsGroup: builtAssets ? builtAssets.group : null,
          markingsGroup: builtMarkings ? builtMarkings.group : null,
          assetFeatures: Array.isArray(assetFeatures) ? assetFeatures : [],
          markingFeatures: Array.isArray(markingFeatures) ? markingFeatures : [],
          counts: {
            street_asset: builtAssets ? builtAssets.count : 0,
            street_tree: builtAssets && builtAssets.classCounts
              ? (Number(builtAssets.classCounts.street_tree) || 0)
              : 0,
            marking: builtMarkings ? builtMarkings.count : 0,
            traffic_control: Array.isArray(assetFeatures)
              ? assetFeatures.filter((item) => item && item.layer === "traffic_control").length
              : 0,
          },
          lastWantedMs: Date.now(),
        };
        tile.counts.total = tile.counts.street_asset + tile.counts.marking + tile.counts.traffic_control;
        manager.tiles.set(key, tile);
        manager.loaded += 1;
        manager.ready = true;
        manager.failureBackoffByKey.delete(key);
        manager.failureReasonByKey.delete(key);
        manager.featureCounts.street_asset += tile.counts.street_asset;
        manager.featureCounts.street_tree += tile.counts.street_tree;
        manager.featureCounts.marking += tile.counts.marking;
        manager.featureCounts.traffic_control += tile.counts.traffic_control;
        manager.featureCounts.total += tile.counts.total;
      } catch (error) {
        manager.failed += 1;
        manager.warning = "Street layer tile failed: " + key;
        manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 20000);
        manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error));
        debugLog("street_layers:tile_failed", {
          key,
          message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
        });
      } finally {
        manager.pending.delete(key);
      }
    }

    function evictStreetLayerTile(tile, reason) {
      const manager = state.streetLayerManager;
      if (!manager || !tile) return;
      try {
        if (tile.assetsGroup && tile.assetsGroup.parent) {
          tile.assetsGroup.parent.remove(tile.assetsGroup);
        }
        if (tile.markingsGroup && tile.markingsGroup.parent) {
          tile.markingsGroup.parent.remove(tile.markingsGroup);
        }
        const disposeObject = (obj) => {
          if (!obj || typeof obj.traverse !== "function") return;
          obj.traverse((child) => {
            if (!child || !child.isMesh) return;
            if (child.userData && child.userData.sharedTemplateGeometry) {
              return;
            }
            if (child.geometry && typeof child.geometry.dispose === "function") {
              child.geometry.dispose();
            }
          });
        };
        disposeObject(tile.assetsGroup);
        disposeObject(tile.markingsGroup);
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      manager.tiles.delete(tile.key);
      manager.featureCounts.street_asset = Math.max(0, manager.featureCounts.street_asset - (Number(tile.counts && tile.counts.street_asset) || 0));
