      manager.featureCounts.street_tree = Math.max(0, manager.featureCounts.street_tree - (Number(tile.counts && tile.counts.street_tree) || 0));
      manager.featureCounts.marking = Math.max(0, manager.featureCounts.marking - (Number(tile.counts && tile.counts.marking) || 0));
      manager.featureCounts.traffic_control = Math.max(0, manager.featureCounts.traffic_control - (Number(tile.counts && tile.counts.traffic_control) || 0));
      manager.featureCounts.total = Math.max(0, manager.featureCounts.total - (Number(tile.counts && tile.counts.total) || 0));
      debugLog("street_layers:tile_evicted", {
        key: tile.key,
        reason: reason || "evict",
      });
    }

    function clearStreetLayerManager() {
      const manager = state.streetLayerManager;
      if (!manager) return;
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        evictStreetLayerTile(tile, "street_layers_reset");
      }
      manager.tiles.clear();
      manager.pending.clear();
      manager.desired.clear();
      manager.currentZoom = null;
      manager.loaded = 0;
      manager.failed = 0;
      manager.ready = false;
      manager.warning = "";
      manager.featureCounts = {
        street_asset: 0,
        street_tree: 0,
        marking: 0,
        traffic_control: 0,
        total: 0,
      };
      if (!(manager.failureBackoffByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureBackoffByKey = new Map();
      }
      if (!(manager.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureReasonByKey = new Map();
      }
      manager.failureBackoffByKey.clear();
      manager.failureReasonByKey.clear();
      streetLayerTileFeatureCache.clear();
      state.streetInstancingEnabled = !!manager.instancingEnabled;
    }

    function chooseStreetLayerZoom(altitudeM, currentZoom) {
      const cfg = STREET_LAYER_CONFIG && STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.tileZoomRange
        ? STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.tileZoomRange
        : TRANSPORT_CONFIG.tileZoomRange;
      return chooseTransportZoom(altitudeM, Number.isFinite(currentZoom) ? currentZoom : Number(cfg && cfg.max));
    }

    function scheduleStreetLayerTiles(nowMs) {
      const manager = buildStreetLayerManager();
      if (STREET_LAYER_CONFIG && STREET_LAYER_CONFIG.enabled === false) {
        return;
      }
      if (!state.camera) return;
      if (nowMs - manager.lastTickMs < manager.requestIntervalMs) return;
      manager.lastTickMs = nowMs;

      const llh = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
      if (!llh || !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) || !Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) return;
      if (!isWithinBounds(llh.lng, llh.lat, TOKYO23 && TOKYO23.bounds ? TOKYO23.bounds : null)) return;

      const suggestedZoom = chooseStreetLayerZoom(llh.altitudeM, manager.currentZoom);
      const assetsIndex =
        STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST &&
        STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers &&
        STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers.streetAssets &&
        STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers.streetAssets.tileIndex &&
        typeof STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers.streetAssets.tileIndex === "object"
          ? STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers.streetAssets.tileIndex
          : null;
      const markingsIndex =
        STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST &&
        STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers &&
        STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers.streetMarkings &&
        STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers.streetMarkings.tileIndex &&
        typeof STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers.streetMarkings.tileIndex === "object"
          ? STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers.streetMarkings.tileIndex
          : null;
      const availableZooms = Array.from(
        new Set([
          ...getTileIndexZoomLevels(assetsIndex),
          ...getTileIndexZoomLevels(markingsIndex),
        ])
      ).sort((a, b) => a - b);
      const constrainedZoom = constrainZoomToAvailableLevels(suggestedZoom, availableZooms);
      const previousZoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : null;
      manager.currentZoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : constrainedZoom;
      if (manager.currentZoom !== constrainedZoom) {
        manager.currentZoom = constrainedZoom;
        for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
          if (!tile || tile.z === constrainedZoom) continue;
          evictStreetLayerTile(tile, "zoom_change");
        }
        manager.desired.clear();
        debugLog("street_layers:zoom_changed", {
          from: previousZoom,
          to: constrainedZoom,
        });
      }
      const zoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : constrainedZoom;
      const center = lonLatToSlippy(llh.lng, llh.lat, zoom);
      const radius = state.driveMode ? 2 : 1;
      const pendingCap = state.driveMode ? 10 : 6;
      const desired = new Set();
      const maxIndex = Math.pow(2, zoom) - 1;
      for (let dy = -radius; dy <= radius; dy += 1) {
        for (let dx = -radius; dx <= radius; dx += 1) {
          if (desired.size >= manager.maxActiveTiles) continue;
          const tx = clamp(center.x + dx, 0, maxIndex);
          const ty = clamp(center.y + dy, 0, maxIndex);
          const tileBounds = slippyBounds(tx, ty, zoom);
          if (!transportTileRelevantToActiveWards(tileBounds, llh)) continue;
          const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(tx) + "/" + String(ty);
          desired.add(key);
          const existing = manager.tiles.get(key);
          if (existing) {
            existing.lastWantedMs = nowMs;
            continue;
          }
          if (manager.pending.size >= pendingCap) continue;
          loadStreetLayerTile(zoom, tx, ty).catch((error) => {
            debugLog("street_layers:tile_async_error", {
              key,
              message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
            });
          });
        }
      }
      manager.desired = desired;
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        if (desired.has(tile.key)) continue;
        if (nowMs - (tile.lastWantedMs || 0) >= manager.hysteresisMs) {
          evictStreetLayerTile(tile, "outside_desired");
        }
      }
    }

    function normalizeParkLayerFeature(rawFeature, sourceLabel) {
      if (!rawFeature || typeof rawFeature !== "object" || !rawFeature.geometry) return null;
      const properties = rawFeature.properties && typeof rawFeature.properties === "object"
        ? rawFeature.properties
        : {};
      const source = properties.source ? String(properties.source).toLowerCase() : sourceLabel;
      const featureClass = properties.featureClass ? String(properties.featureClass).toLowerCase() : "park";
      const attrs = properties.attrs && typeof properties.attrs === "object" ? properties.attrs : properties;
      const id = properties.id ? String(properties.id) : "";
      const geometry = rawFeature.geometry;
      if (geometry.type === "Polygon" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates) && geometry.coordinates.length > 0) {
        const outer = Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates[0]) ? geometry.coordinates[0] : [];
        const coords = outer
          .map((coord) => {
            if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) return null;
            const lon = Number(coord[0]);
            const lat = Number(coord[1]);
            return Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat) ? [lon, lat] : null;
          })
          .filter(Boolean);
        if (coords.length < 3) return null;
        return {
          id,
          source,
          featureClass,
          attrs,
          geometryType: "Polygon",
          coordinates: coords,
        };
      }
      if (geometry.type === "MultiPolygon" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates)) {
        const out = [];
        for (const poly of geometry.coordinates) {
          const outer = Array.isArray(poly) && Array.isArray(poly[0]) ? poly[0] : [];
          const coords = outer
            .map((coord) => {
              if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) return null;
              const lon = Number(coord[0]);
              const lat = Number(coord[1]);
              return Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat) ? [lon, lat] : null;
            })
            .filter(Boolean);
          if (coords.length < 3) continue;
          out.push({
            id,
            source,
            featureClass,
            attrs,
            geometryType: "Polygon",
            coordinates: coords,
          });
        }
        return out.length > 0 ? out : null;
      }
      return null;
    }

    function flattenNormalizedParkFeatures(value) {
      if (!value) return [];
      if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.filter(Boolean);
      return [value];
    }

    function normalizeParkRingCoordinates(coords) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length < 3) {
        return [];
      }
      const ring = [];
      for (const coord of coords) {
        if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        const lon = Number(coord[0]);
        const lat = Number(coord[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
          continue;
        }
        if (ring.length > 0) {
          const prev = ring[ring.length - 1];
          if (Math.abs(prev[0] - lon) < 1e-9 && Math.abs(prev[1] - lat) < 1e-9) {
            continue;
          }
        }
        ring.push([lon, lat]);
      }
      if (ring.length >= 2) {
        const first = ring[0];
        const last = ring[ring.length - 1];
        if (Math.abs(first[0] - last[0]) < 1e-9 && Math.abs(first[1] - last[1]) < 1e-9) {
          ring.pop();
        }
      }
      return ring.length >= 3 ? ring : [];
    }

    function buildCanonicalParkRingKey(coords) {
      const ring = normalizeParkRingCoordinates(coords);
      if (ring.length < 3) {
        return "";
      }
      const rounded = ring.map((coord) => [
        Math.round(Number(coord[0]) * 1e6),
        Math.round(Number(coord[1]) * 1e6),
      ]);
      const n = rounded.length;
      let best = null;
      const makeSeq = (start, dir) => {
        const out = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < n; i += 1) {
          const idx = (start + dir * i + n * 64) % n;
          const pt = rounded[idx];
          out.push(String(pt[0]) + ":" + String(pt[1]));
        }
        return out.join("|");
      };
      for (let i = 0; i < n; i += 1) {
        const forward = makeSeq(i, 1);
        if (best === null || forward < best) {
          best = forward;
        }
        const reverse = makeSeq(i, -1);
        if (best === null || reverse < best) {
          best = reverse;
        }
      }
      return best || "";
    }

    function computeParkRingCentroid(ring) {
      if (!Array.isArray(ring) || ring.length < 3) {
        return null;
      }
      let crossSum = 0;
      let cx = 0;
      let cy = 0;
      for (let i = 0; i < ring.length; i += 1) {
        const a = ring[i];
        const b = ring[(i + 1) % ring.length];
        const x1 = Number(a[0]);
        const y1 = Number(a[1]);
        const x2 = Number(b[0]);
        const y2 = Number(b[1]);
        const cross = x1 * y2 - x2 * y1;
        crossSum += cross;
        cx += (x1 + x2) * cross;
        cy += (y1 + y2) * cross;
      }
      if (Math.abs(crossSum) > 1e-12) {
        const inv = 1 / (3 * crossSum);
        const lon = cx * inv;
        const lat = cy * inv;
        if (Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat)) {
          return [lon, lat];
        }
      }
      let lon = 0;
      let lat = 0;
      for (const coord of ring) {
        lon += Number(coord[0]);
        lat += Number(coord[1]);
      }
      lon /= ring.length;
      lat /= ring.length;
      return Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat) ? [lon, lat] : null;
    }

    function getParkFeatureOwnerTileKey(feature, zoom) {
      if (!feature || feature.geometryType !== "Polygon" || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) || !Number.isFinite(zoom)) {
        return "";
      }
      const ring = normalizeParkRingCoordinates(feature.coordinates);
      if (ring.length < 3) {
        return "";
      }
      const centroid = computeParkRingCentroid(ring);
      if (!Array.isArray(centroid) || centroid.length < 2) {
        return "";
      }
      const slippy = lonLatToSlippy(Number(centroid[0]), Number(centroid[1]), zoom);
      const maxIndex = Math.pow(2, zoom) - 1;
      const tx = clamp(Math.floor(Number(slippy.x)), 0, maxIndex);
      const ty = clamp(Math.floor(Number(slippy.y)), 0, maxIndex);
      return String(zoom) + "/" + String(tx) + "/" + String(ty);
    }

    function buildParkFeatureMergeKey(feature) {
      if (!feature || feature.geometryType !== "Polygon" || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates)) return "";
      const ringKey = buildCanonicalParkRingKey(feature.coordinates);
      if (!ringKey) return "";
      return (
        String(feature.featureClass || "park") + "|" +
        ringKey
      );
    }

    function computeParkRingBounds(ring) {
      if (!Array.isArray(ring) || ring.length < 3) {
        return null;
      }
      let west = Infinity;
      let south = Infinity;
      let east = -Infinity;
      let north = -Infinity;
      for (const coord of ring) {
        if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) continue;
        const lon = Number(coord[0]);
        const lat = Number(coord[1]);
        if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) continue;
        if (lon < west) west = lon;
        if (lat < south) south = lat;
        if (lon > east) east = lon;
        if (lat > north) north = lat;
      }
      if (!Number.isFinite(west) || !Number.isFinite(south) || !Number.isFinite(east) || !Number.isFinite(north)) {
        return null;
      }
      return { west, south, east, north };
    }

    function pointInParkRing(lon, lat, ring) {
      if (!Array.isArray(ring) || ring.length < 3 || !Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) {
        return false;
      }
      let inside = false;
      for (let i = 0, j = ring.length - 1; i < ring.length; j = i, i += 1) {
        const a = ring[i];
        const b = ring[j];
        if (!Array.isArray(a) || !Array.isArray(b) || a.length < 2 || b.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        const xi = Number(a[0]);
        const yi = Number(a[1]);
        const xj = Number(b[0]);
        const yj = Number(b[1]);
        const intersects = ((yi > lat) !== (yj > lat)) &&
          (lon < ((xj - xi) * (lat - yi)) / Math.max(1e-12, (yj - yi)) + xi);
        if (intersects) inside = !inside;
      }
      return inside;
    }

    function pointToSegmentDistanceMeters(px, py, ax, ay, bx, by) {
      const abx = bx - ax;
      const aby = by - ay;
      const apx = px - ax;
      const apy = py - ay;
      const denom = abx * abx + aby * aby;
      let t = denom > 1e-9 ? ((apx * abx + apy * aby) / denom) : 0;
      t = clamp(t, 0, 1);
      const cx = ax + abx * t;
      const cy = ay + aby * t;
      return Math.hypot(px - cx, py - cy);
    }

    function minParkEdgeDistanceMeters(lon, lat, ring, metersPerDegLon, metersPerDegLat) {
      if (!Array.isArray(ring) || ring.length < 2) {
        return Infinity;
      }
      let minDistance = Infinity;
      for (let i = 0; i < ring.length; i += 1) {
        const a = ring[i];
        const b = ring[(i + 1) % ring.length];
        if (!Array.isArray(a) || !Array.isArray(b) || a.length < 2 || b.length < 2) {
          continue;
        }
        const ax = (Number(a[0]) - lon) * metersPerDegLon;
        const ay = (Number(a[1]) - lat) * metersPerDegLat;
        const bx = (Number(b[0]) - lon) * metersPerDegLon;
        const by = (Number(b[1]) - lat) * metersPerDegLat;
        const dist = pointToSegmentDistanceMeters(0, 0, ax, ay, bx, by);
        if (dist < minDistance) {
          minDistance = dist;
        }
      }
      return minDistance;
    }

    function hashStringUInt32(value) {
      const text = String(value || "");
      let hash = 2166136261;
      for (let i = 0; i < text.length; i += 1) {
        hash ^= text.charCodeAt(i);
        hash = Math.imul(hash, 16777619);
      }
      return hash >>> 0;
    }

    function pseudoRandom(seed, index) {
      const value = Math.sin((Number(seed) + Number(index) * 374761.393) * 0.000001) * 43758.5453123;
      return value - Math.floor(value);
    }

    function buildParkTreePointsFromRing(ring, featureKey, options) {
      const normalized = normalizeParkRingCoordinates(ring);
      if (normalized.length < 3) {
        return [];
      }
      const bounds = computeParkRingBounds(normalized);
      if (!bounds) {
        return [];
      }

      let lonRef = 0;
      let latRef = 0;
      for (const coord of normalized) {
        lonRef += Number(coord[0]);
        latRef += Number(coord[1]);
      }
      lonRef /= normalized.length;
      latRef /= normalized.length;
      const metersPerDegLat = 111320;
      const metersPerDegLon = Math.max(1e-3, Math.cos(latRef * Math.PI / 180) * 111320);
      const spacingM = Math.max(3, Number(options && options.spacingM) || 12);
      const minAreaM2 = Math.max(0, Number(options && options.minAreaM2) || 120);
      const edgeInsetM = Math.max(0, Number(options && options.edgeInsetM) || 0);
      const jitterRatio = clamp(Number(options && options.jitterRatio) || 0, 0, 0.45);
      const maxCount = Math.max(0, Math.trunc(Number(options && options.maxCount) || 0));
      if (maxCount <= 0) {
        return [];
      }

      const projected = normalized.map((coord) => [
        (Number(coord[0]) - lonRef) * metersPerDegLon,
        (Number(coord[1]) - latRef) * metersPerDegLat,
      ]);
      let twiceArea = 0;
      for (let i = 0; i < projected.length; i += 1) {
        const a = projected[i];
        const b = projected[(i + 1) % projected.length];
        twiceArea += a[0] * b[1] - b[0] * a[1];
      }
      const areaM2 = Math.abs(twiceArea) * 0.5;
      if (!Number.isFinite(areaM2) || areaM2 < minAreaM2) {
        return [];
      }

      const stepLon = Math.max(1e-6, spacingM / metersPerDegLon);
      const stepLat = Math.max(1e-6, spacingM / metersPerDegLat);
      const seed = hashStringUInt32(featureKey || String(normalized.length));
      const offsetLon = pseudoRandom(seed, 1) * stepLon;
      const offsetLat = pseudoRandom(seed, 2) * stepLat;
      const jitterLon = stepLon * jitterRatio;
      const jitterLat = stepLat * jitterRatio;

      const out = [];
      let sampleIndex = 0;
      for (let lat = bounds.south + offsetLat; lat <= bounds.north; lat += stepLat) {
        if (out.length >= maxCount) break;
        for (let lon = bounds.west + offsetLon; lon <= bounds.east; lon += stepLon) {
          if (out.length >= maxCount) break;
          const jitteredLon = lon + (pseudoRandom(seed, sampleIndex * 2 + 3) - 0.5) * 2 * jitterLon;
          const jitteredLat = lat + (pseudoRandom(seed, sampleIndex * 2 + 4) - 0.5) * 2 * jitterLat;
          sampleIndex += 1;
          if (!pointInParkRing(jitteredLon, jitteredLat, normalized)) {
            continue;
          }
          if (edgeInsetM > 0) {
            const edgeDistance = minParkEdgeDistanceMeters(
              jitteredLon,
              jitteredLat,
              normalized,
              metersPerDegLon,
              metersPerDegLat
            );
            if (edgeDistance < edgeInsetM) {
              continue;
            }
          }
          out.push([jitteredLon, jitteredLat]);
        }
      }
      return out;
    }

    function isParkRuntimeOverpassFallbackEnabled() {
      if (PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && typeof PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.runtimeOverpassFallback === "boolean") {
        return PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.runtimeOverpassFallback;
      }
      return true;
    }

    function overpassCoordsToRing(geometryList) {
      if (!Array.isArray(geometryList) || geometryList.length < 4) {
        return null;
      }
      const coords = geometryList
        .map((pt) => {
          if (!pt) return null;
          const lon = Number(pt.lon);
          const lat = Number(pt.lat);
          return Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat) ? [lon, lat] : null;
        })
        .filter(Boolean);
      if (coords.length < 4) {
        return null;
      }
      const first = coords[0];
      const last = coords[coords.length - 1];
      if (
        !Array.isArray(first) ||
        !Array.isArray(last) ||
        first.length < 2 ||
        last.length < 2 ||
        Number(first[0]) !== Number(last[0]) ||
        Number(first[1]) !== Number(last[1])
      ) {
        return null;
      }
      return coords;
    }

    function buildParkFeatureFromOverpassWay(element) {
      const tags = element && element.tags && typeof element.tags === "object" ? element.tags : {};
      const ring = overpassCoordsToRing(element && element.geometry);
      if (!ring) {
        return null;
      }
      return {
        type: "Feature",
        geometry: {
          type: "Polygon",
          coordinates: [ring],
        },
        properties: {
          featureClass: "park",
          source: "osm",
          name: String(tags.name || ""),
          parkType: String(tags.leisure || tags.landuse || "park"),
          attrs: tags,
          tags,
        },
      };
    }

    function buildParkFeatureFromOverpassRelation(element) {
      const tags = element && element.tags && typeof element.tags === "object" ? element.tags : {};
      const members = Array.isArray(element && element.members) ? element.members : [];
      const outerRings = [];
      for (const member of members) {
        if (!member || member.type !== "way" || member.role !== "outer") {
          continue;
        }
        const ring = overpassCoordsToRing(member.geometry);
        if (!ring) {
          continue;
        }
        outerRings.push([ring]);
      }
      if (outerRings.length <= 0) {
        return null;
      }
      return {
        type: "Feature",
        geometry: {
          type: outerRings.length === 1 ? "Polygon" : "MultiPolygon",
          coordinates: outerRings.length === 1 ? outerRings[0] : outerRings,
        },
        properties: {
          featureClass: "park",
          source: "osm",
          name: String(tags.name || ""),
          parkType: String(tags.leisure || tags.landuse || "park"),
          attrs: tags,
          tags,
        },
      };
    }

    async function fetchParkFeaturesFromOverpass(bounds, zoom) {
      if (!bounds || !isParkRuntimeOverpassFallbackEnabled()) {
        return [];
      }
      const maxZoom = Number.isFinite(Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassMaxZoom))
        ? Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassMaxZoom)
        : 14;
      if (Number(zoom) > maxZoom) {
        return [];
      }
      const endpointList =
        Array.isArray(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassEndpoints)
          ? PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassEndpoints.map((value) => String(value || "").trim()).filter(Boolean)
          : [];
      if (endpointList.length <= 0) {
        endpointList.push(
          "https://overpass-api.de/api/interpreter",
          "https://overpass.kumi.systems/api/interpreter",
          "https://overpass.private.coffee/api/interpreter"
        );
      }
      const timeoutSec = Number.isFinite(Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassTimeoutSec))
        ? Math.max(10, Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassTimeoutSec))
        : 24;
      const maxRetries = Number.isFinite(Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassMaxRetries))
        ? clamp(Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassMaxRetries), 0, 6)
        : 2;
      const retryBaseMs = Number.isFinite(Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassRetryBaseMs))
        ? Math.max(300, Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassRetryBaseMs))
        : 1200;
      const retryJitterMs = Number.isFinite(Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassRetryJitterMs))
        ? Math.max(0, Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassRetryJitterMs))
        : 420;
      const bbox = [
        Number(bounds.south).toFixed(6),
        Number(bounds.west).toFixed(6),
        Number(bounds.north).toFixed(6),
        Number(bounds.east).toFixed(6),
      ].join(",");
      const query =
        '[out:json][timeout:' + String(timeoutSec) + '];(' +
        'way["leisure"~"^(park|garden|nature_reserve|recreation_ground)$"](' + bbox + ');' +
        'way["landuse"~"^(recreation_ground|village_green)$"](' + bbox + ');' +
        'relation["leisure"~"^(park|garden|nature_reserve|recreation_ground)$"](' + bbox + ');' +
        'relation["landuse"~"^(recreation_ground|village_green)$"](' + bbox + ');' +
        ');out geom qt;';

      let payload = null;
      let lastError = null;
      for (let attempt = 0; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt += 1) {
        const endpoint = endpointList[attempt % endpointList.length];
        try {
          const response = await fetch(endpoint, {
            method: "POST",
            mode: "cors",
            credentials: "omit",
            headers: {
              "content-type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=UTF-8",
            },
            body: "data=" + encodeURIComponent(query),
          });
          if (!response || !response.ok) {
            const status = response ? Number(response.status) || 0 : 0;
            const error = new Error("parks_overpass_http_" + String(status));
            error.status = status;
            error.retryAfterMs = parseRetryAfterMs(response && response.headers ? response.headers.get("retry-after") : null);
            throw error;
          }
          payload = await parseJsonResponseWithContext(response, "parks_overpass_payload");
          break;
        } catch (error) {
          lastError = error;
          const status = Number(error && error.status);
          const retryable = !Number.isFinite(status) || status === 0 || status === 408 || status === 429 || status >= 500;
          if ((error && error.message ? String(error.message) : "").includes("non_json")) {
            debugLog("parks:overpass_non_json", {
              status: Number.isFinite(status) ? status : "unknown",
              endpoint,
              snippet: error && error.snippet ? String(error.snippet).slice(0, 120) : "",
            });
          }
          if (!retryable || attempt >= maxRetries) {
            break;
          }
          const retryAfterMs = Number(error && error.retryAfterMs) || 0;
          const backoffMs = retryAfterMs > 0
            ? retryAfterMs + Math.floor(Math.random() * 280)
            : Math.floor(retryBaseMs * Math.pow(2, Math.min(attempt, 5)) + Math.random() * retryJitterMs);
          await sleepMs(backoffMs);
        }
      }
      if (!payload) {
        throw lastError || new Error("parks_overpass_empty_response");
      }
      const elements = payload && Array.isArray(payload.elements) ? payload.elements : [];
      const normalized = [];
      for (const element of elements) {
        if (!element || (element.type !== "way" && element.type !== "relation")) {
          continue;
        }
        const feature = element.type === "way"
          ? buildParkFeatureFromOverpassWay(element)
          : buildParkFeatureFromOverpassRelation(element);
        if (!feature) {
          continue;
        }
        normalized.push(...flattenNormalizedParkFeatures(normalizeParkLayerFeature(feature, "osm")));
      }
      if (normalized.length <= 0) {
        return [];
      }
      const deduped = [];
      const seen = new Set();
      for (const feature of normalized) {
        const key = buildParkFeatureMergeKey(feature);
        if (key && seen.has(key)) {
          continue;
        }
        if (key) {
          seen.add(key);
        }
        deduped.push(feature);
      }
      return deduped.slice(0, 640);
    }

    function buildParkLayerManager() {
      if (state.parkLayerManager) {
        if (!Number.isFinite(Number(state.parkLayerManager.treeCount))) {
          state.parkLayerManager.treeCount = 0;
        }
        return state.parkLayerManager;
      }
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.name = "parksLayerGroup";
      state.scene.add(group);
      const manager = {
        group,
        tiles: new Map(),
        pending: new Set(),
        desired: new Set(),
        failureBackoffByKey: new Map(),
        failureReasonByKey: new Map(),
        lastTickMs: 0,
        currentZoom: null,
        loaded: 0,
        failed: 0,
        ready: false,
        warning: "",
        maxActiveTiles: Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.maxActiveTiles) || 18,
        hysteresisMs: Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.hysteresisMs) || 10000,
        requestIntervalMs: Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.requestIntervalMs) || 1000,
        featureCount: 0,
        treeCount: 0,
        material: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          color: 0x6b9d79,
          roughness: 0.96,
          metalness: 0.01,
          transparent: false,
          opacity: 1,
          depthTest: true,
          depthWrite: false,
          polygonOffset: true,
          polygonOffsetFactor: -12,
          polygonOffsetUnits: -12,
        }),
      };
      state.parkLayerManager = manager;
      return manager;
    }

    async function fetchParkFeaturesFromManifestTile(zoom, x, y) {
      const cacheKey = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      const cached = parkLayerTileFeatureCache.get(cacheKey);
      if (cached && cached.expiresAt > Date.now()) {
        return Array.isArray(cached.features) ? cached.features : [];
      }
      const manifest = PARKS_MANIFEST && typeof PARKS_MANIFEST === "object"
        ? PARKS_MANIFEST
        : {};
      const basePath = manifest.basePath ? String(manifest.basePath) : "";
      const tileKey = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      const flatName = "park_z" + String(zoom) + "_x" + String(x) + "_y" + String(y) + ".json";
      const urls = [];
      if (manifest.tileIndex && typeof manifest.tileIndex === "object") {
        const indexed = manifest.tileIndex[tileKey];
        if (typeof indexed === "string" && indexed.length > 0) {
          const lower = indexed.toLowerCase();
          if (lower.startsWith("http://") || lower.startsWith("https://")) {
            urls.push(indexed);
          } else {
            urls.push(basePath ? joinAssetPath(basePath, indexed) : indexed);
          }
        }
      }
      if (typeof manifest.urlTemplate === "string" && manifest.urlTemplate) {
        urls.push(
          String(manifest.urlTemplate)
            .replace("{z}", String(zoom))
            .replace("{x}", String(x))
            .replace("{y}", String(y))
        );
      }
      if (basePath) {
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json"));
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, flatName));
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, "parks_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json"));
      }
      urls.push("./patch_assets/" + flatName);
      urls.push("patch_assets/" + flatName);
      urls.push("./" + flatName);
      urls.push(flatName);
      urls.push("./patch_assets/parks_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("patch_assets/parks_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("./parks_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("parks_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      const uniqueUrls = Array.from(new Set(urls.filter((item) => typeof item === "string" && item.length > 0)));
      for (const url of uniqueUrls) {
        try {
          const payload = await tryFetchJsonCandidate(url, 7000, isFeatureCollectionPayload);
          if (!payload || !Array.isArray(payload.features)) continue;
          const normalized = [];
          for (const feature of payload.features) {
            normalized.push(...flattenNormalizedParkFeatures(normalizeParkLayerFeature(feature, "osm")));
          }
          if (normalized.length > 0) {
            const merged = [];
            const seen = new Set();
            for (const feature of normalized) {
              const key = buildParkFeatureMergeKey(feature);
              if (key && seen.has(key)) continue;
              if (key) seen.add(key);
              merged.push(feature);
            }
            parkLayerTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, { features: merged, expiresAt: Date.now() + 5 * 60 * 1000 });
            return merged;
          }
        } catch (_error) {
          // continue
        }
      }
      parkLayerTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, { features: [], expiresAt: Date.now() + 60 * 1000 });
      return [];
    }

    function buildParkTileGroup(tile, features) {
      const manager = buildParkLayerManager();
      const streetManager = buildStreetLayerManager();
      const bounds = tile.bounds;
      const centerECEF = lonLatToECEF(
        (bounds.west + bounds.east) * 0.5,
        (bounds.south + bounds.north) * 0.5,
        0
      );
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.position.copy(centerECEF);
      group.name = "parkTile:" + tile.key;
      const builder = { positions: [], indices: [] };
      const seenFeatureKeys = new Set();
      let count = 0;
      const treeTemplateParts = getStreetAssetTemplateParts("street_tree", streetManager);
      const treeEnabled = !(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.treeEnabled === false) && treeTemplateParts.length > 0;
      const treeMaxPerTileRaw = Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.treeMaxPerTile);
      const treeMaxGlobalRaw = Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.treeMaxGlobal);
      const treeSpacingRaw = Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.treeSpacingM);
      const treeMinAreaRaw = Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.treeMinAreaM2);
      const treeEdgeInsetRaw = Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.treeEdgeInsetM);
      const treeJitterRaw = Number(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.treeJitterRatio);
      const treeMaxPerTile = Number.isFinite(treeMaxPerTileRaw) ? Math.max(0, Math.trunc(treeMaxPerTileRaw)) : 420;
      const treeMaxGlobal = Number.isFinite(treeMaxGlobalRaw) ? Math.max(0, Math.trunc(treeMaxGlobalRaw)) : 3000;
      const treeSpacingM = Number.isFinite(treeSpacingRaw) ? Math.max(3, treeSpacingRaw) : 12;
      const treeMinAreaM2 = Number.isFinite(treeMinAreaRaw) ? Math.max(0, treeMinAreaRaw) : 120;
      const treeEdgeInsetM = Number.isFinite(treeEdgeInsetRaw) ? Math.max(0, treeEdgeInsetRaw) : 1.8;
      const treeJitterRatio = Number.isFinite(treeJitterRaw) ? clamp(treeJitterRaw, 0, 0.45) : 0.28;
      const remainingTreeGlobal = Math.max(0, treeMaxGlobal - (Number(manager.treeCount) || 0));
      const treeTileCap = treeEnabled ? Math.max(0, Math.min(treeMaxPerTile, remainingTreeGlobal)) : 0;
      const treePlacements = [];
      const geoUp = centerECEF.clone().normalize();
      const worldUp = new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0);
      const orientQ = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromUnitVectors(worldUp, geoUp);
      const treeScale = new THREE.Vector3(1, 1, 1);
      const treeLocalPos = new THREE.Vector3();
      const treeMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
      for (const feature of features) {
        if (!feature || feature.geometryType !== "Polygon" || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates)) continue;
        const ownerTileKey = getParkFeatureOwnerTileKey(feature, tile.z);
        if (ownerTileKey && ownerTileKey !== tile.key) {
          continue;
        }
        const featureKey = buildParkFeatureMergeKey(feature);
        if (featureKey) {
          if (seenFeatureKeys.has(featureKey)) {
            continue;
          }
          seenFeatureKeys.add(featureKey);
        }
        const appended = appendParkPolygon(
          builder,
          feature.coordinates,
          centerECEF
        );
        count += appended;
        if (treePlacements.length >= treeTileCap) {
          continue;
        }
        const ring = normalizeParkRingCoordinates(feature.coordinates);
        if (ring.length < 3) {
          continue;
        }
        const treePoints = buildParkTreePointsFromRing(ring, featureKey || ownerTileKey || tile.key, {
          spacingM: treeSpacingM,
          minAreaM2: treeMinAreaM2,
          edgeInsetM: treeEdgeInsetM,
          jitterRatio: treeJitterRatio,
          maxCount: treeTileCap - treePlacements.length,
        });
        for (const point of treePoints) {
          if (!Array.isArray(point) || point.length < 2) continue;
          const lon = Number(point[0]);
          const lat = Number(point[1]);
          if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) continue;
          let heightM = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lon, lat);
          if (!Number.isFinite(heightM)) {
            heightM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
          }
          const world = lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM + 0.35);
          treeLocalPos.copy(world).sub(centerECEF);
          const seeded = Math.abs(Math.sin((lon * 19.231) + (lat * 67.873)) * 43758.5453);
          const noise = seeded - Math.floor(seeded);
          treeScale.set(
            0.8 + noise * 0.45,
            0.86 + noise * 0.62,
            0.8 + (1 - noise) * 0.42
          );
          treeMatrix.compose(treeLocalPos, orientQ, treeScale);
          treePlacements.push(treeMatrix.clone());
          if (treePlacements.length >= treeTileCap) {
            break;
          }
        }
      }
      const geometry = createTransportGeometry(builder);
      if (geometry) {
        const mesh = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, manager.material);
        mesh.frustumCulled = true;
        mesh.renderOrder = 39;
        group.add(mesh);
      }
      let treeCount = 0;
      if (treePlacements.length > 0 && treeTemplateParts.length > 0) {
        const childMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
        const instanceMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
        for (const part of treeTemplateParts) {
          if (!part || !part.geometry || !part.material || !part.localMatrix) {
            continue;
          }
          const instanced = new THREE.InstancedMesh(part.geometry, part.material, treePlacements.length);
          instanced.renderOrder = 41;
          instanced.frustumCulled = true;
          instanced.userData.sharedTemplateGeometry = true;
          for (let i = 0; i < treePlacements.length; i += 1) {
            childMatrix.copy(part.localMatrix);
            instanceMatrix.multiplyMatrices(treePlacements[i], childMatrix);
            instanced.setMatrixAt(i, instanceMatrix);
          }
          instanced.instanceMatrix.needsUpdate = true;
          group.add(instanced);
        }
        treeCount = treePlacements.length;
      }
      return { group, count, treeCount };
    }

    async function loadParkLayerTile(zoom, x, y) {
      const manager = buildParkLayerManager();
      if (!(manager.failureBackoffByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureBackoffByKey = new Map();
      }
      if (!(manager.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureReasonByKey = new Map();
      }
      const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      if (manager.pending.has(key) || manager.tiles.has(key)) {
        return;
      }
      const backoffUntil = Number(manager.failureBackoffByKey.get(key)) || 0;
      if (backoffUntil > Date.now()) {
        return;
      }
      manager.pending.add(key);
      const bounds = slippyBounds(x, y, zoom);
      try {
        let features = await fetchParkFeaturesFromManifestTile(zoom, x, y);
        if ((!Array.isArray(features) || features.length <= 0) && isParkRuntimeOverpassFallbackEnabled()) {
          try {
            const fallback = await fetchParkFeaturesFromOverpass(bounds, zoom);
            if (Array.isArray(fallback) && fallback.length > 0) {
              features = fallback;
            }
          } catch (fallbackError) {
            manager.failureReasonByKey.set(
              key,
              fallbackError && fallbackError.message
                ? String(fallbackError.message)
                : String(fallbackError)
            );
          }
        }
        if (!Array.isArray(features) || features.length <= 0) {
          manager.failed += 1;
          manager.warning = "Park tile failed: " + key;
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 25000);
          if (!manager.failureReasonByKey.has(key)) {
            manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, "no_data");
          }
          return;
        }
        const built = buildParkTileGroup({ key, z: zoom, x, y, bounds }, features);
        if (!built || !built.group || built.count <= 0) {
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 20000);
          manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, "no_renderable");
          return;
        }
        manager.group.add(built.group);
        manager.tiles.set(key, {
          key,
          z: zoom,
          x,
          y,
          bounds,
          group: built.group,
          count: built.count,
          treeCount: Number(built.treeCount) || 0,
          lastWantedMs: Date.now(),
        });
        manager.featureCount += built.count;
        manager.treeCount += Number(built.treeCount) || 0;
        manager.loaded += 1;
        manager.ready = true;
        manager.failureBackoffByKey.delete(key);
        manager.failureReasonByKey.delete(key);
      } catch (error) {
        manager.failed += 1;
        manager.warning = "Park tile failed: " + key;
        manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 25000);
        manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error));
        debugLog("parks:tile_failed", {
          key,
          message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
        });
      } finally {
        manager.pending.delete(key);
      }
    }

    function evictParkLayerTile(tile, reason) {
      const manager = state.parkLayerManager;
      if (!manager || !tile) return;
      try {
        if (tile.group && tile.group.parent) {
          tile.group.parent.remove(tile.group);
        }
        if (tile.group && typeof tile.group.traverse === "function") {
          tile.group.traverse((child) => {
            if (!child || !child.isMesh) return;
            if (child.geometry && typeof child.geometry.dispose === "function") {
              child.geometry.dispose();
            }
          });
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      manager.tiles.delete(tile.key);
      manager.featureCount = Math.max(0, manager.featureCount - (Number(tile.count) || 0));
      manager.treeCount = Math.max(0, manager.treeCount - (Number(tile.treeCount) || 0));
      debugLog("parks:tile_evicted", { key: tile.key, reason: reason || "evict" });
    }

    function clearParkLayerManager() {
      const manager = state.parkLayerManager;
      if (!manager) return;
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        evictParkLayerTile(tile, "parks_reset");
      }
      manager.tiles.clear();
      manager.pending.clear();
      manager.desired.clear();
      manager.currentZoom = null;
      manager.loaded = 0;
      manager.failed = 0;
      manager.ready = false;
      manager.warning = "";
      manager.featureCount = 0;
      manager.treeCount = 0;
      if (!(manager.failureBackoffByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureBackoffByKey = new Map();
      }
      if (!(manager.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureReasonByKey = new Map();
      }
      manager.failureBackoffByKey.clear();
      manager.failureReasonByKey.clear();
      parkLayerTileFeatureCache.clear();
    }

    function chooseParkLayerZoom(altitudeM, currentZoom) {
      const cfg = PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.tileZoomRange
        ? PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.tileZoomRange
        : TRANSPORT_CONFIG.tileZoomRange;
      return chooseTransportZoom(altitudeM, Number.isFinite(currentZoom) ? currentZoom : Number(cfg && cfg.max));
    }

    function scheduleParkLayerTiles(nowMs) {
      if (PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.enabled === false) {
        return;
      }
      const manager = buildParkLayerManager();
      if (!state.camera) return;
      if (nowMs - manager.lastTickMs < manager.requestIntervalMs) return;
      manager.lastTickMs = nowMs;
      const llh = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
      if (!llh || !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) || !Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) return;
      if (!isWithinBounds(llh.lng, llh.lat, TOKYO23 && TOKYO23.bounds ? TOKYO23.bounds : null)) return;
      const suggestedZoom = chooseParkLayerZoom(llh.altitudeM, manager.currentZoom);
      const availableZooms = getTileIndexZoomLevels(
        PARKS_MANIFEST && PARKS_MANIFEST.tileIndex && typeof PARKS_MANIFEST.tileIndex === "object"
          ? PARKS_MANIFEST.tileIndex
          : null
      );
      const constrainedZoom = constrainZoomToAvailableLevels(suggestedZoom, availableZooms);
      const previousZoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : null;
      manager.currentZoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : constrainedZoom;
      if (manager.currentZoom !== constrainedZoom) {
        manager.currentZoom = constrainedZoom;
        for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
          if (!tile || tile.z === constrainedZoom) continue;
          evictParkLayerTile(tile, "zoom_change");
        }
        manager.desired.clear();
        debugLog("parks:zoom_changed", {
          from: previousZoom,
          to: constrainedZoom,
        });
      }
      const zoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : constrainedZoom;
      const center = lonLatToSlippy(llh.lng, llh.lat, zoom);
      const radius = state.driveMode ? 1 : 1;
      const pendingCap = state.driveMode ? 6 : 4;
      const desired = new Set();
      const maxIndex = Math.pow(2, zoom) - 1;
      for (let dy = -radius; dy <= radius; dy += 1) {
        for (let dx = -radius; dx <= radius; dx += 1) {
          if (desired.size >= manager.maxActiveTiles) continue;
          const tx = clamp(center.x + dx, 0, maxIndex);
          const ty = clamp(center.y + dy, 0, maxIndex);
          const tileBounds = slippyBounds(tx, ty, zoom);
          if (!transportTileRelevantToActiveWards(tileBounds, llh)) continue;
          const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(tx) + "/" + String(ty);
          desired.add(key);
          const existing = manager.tiles.get(key);
          if (existing) {
            existing.lastWantedMs = nowMs;
            continue;
          }
          if (manager.pending.size >= pendingCap) continue;
          loadParkLayerTile(zoom, tx, ty).catch((error) => {
            debugLog("parks:tile_async_error", {
              key,
              message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
            });
          });
        }
      }
      manager.desired = desired;
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        if (desired.has(tile.key)) continue;
        if (nowMs - (tile.lastWantedMs || 0) >= manager.hysteresisMs) {
          evictParkLayerTile(tile, "outside_desired");
        }
      }
    }

    const WATER_LINE_CLASS_SET = new Set(["river", "canal", "stream"]);
    const WATER_AREA_CLASS_SET = new Set(["lake", "pond", "reservoir", "riverbank"]);
    const WATER_CLASS_LIST = ["river", "canal", "stream", "lake", "pond", "reservoir", "riverbank"];

    function isWaterClassArea(featureClass) {
      return WATER_AREA_CLASS_SET.has(String(featureClass || "").toLowerCase());
    }

    function normalizeWaterFeatureClass(featureClass, geometryType) {
      const cls = String(featureClass || "").toLowerCase();
      if (WATER_LINE_CLASS_SET.has(cls)) {
        if (geometryType === "Polygon" && cls === "river") {
          return "riverbank";
        }
        if (geometryType === "Polygon") {
          return "lake";
        }
        return cls;
      }
      if (WATER_AREA_CLASS_SET.has(cls)) {
        if (geometryType === "LineString" && cls === "riverbank") {
          return "river";
        }
        if (geometryType === "LineString" && cls === "reservoir") {
          return "canal";
        }
        if (geometryType === "LineString") {
          return "stream";
        }
        return cls;
      }
      return geometryType === "LineString" ? "river" : "lake";
    }

    function isExcludedOpenWaterTags(tags) {
      const safeTags = tags && typeof tags === "object" ? tags : {};
      const water = safeTags.water ? String(safeTags.water).toLowerCase() : "";
      const natural = safeTags.natural ? String(safeTags.natural).toLowerCase() : "";
      if (natural === "coastline") {
        return true;
      }
      if (water === "sea" || water === "ocean" || water === "bay") {
        return true;
      }
      return false;
    }

    function shouldTreatWaterFeatureAsArea(tags, geometryType) {
      if (geometryType !== "Polygon") {
        return false;
      }
      const safeTags = tags && typeof tags === "object" ? tags : {};
      const waterway = safeTags.waterway ? String(safeTags.waterway).toLowerCase() : "";
      const natural = safeTags.natural ? String(safeTags.natural).toLowerCase() : "";
      const water = safeTags.water ? String(safeTags.water).toLowerCase() : "";
      const landuse = safeTags.landuse ? String(safeTags.landuse).toLowerCase() : "";
      if (waterway === "riverbank") {
        return true;
      }
      if (natural === "water") {
        return true;
      }
      if (water.length > 0) {
        return true;
      }
      if (landuse === "reservoir" || landuse === "basin") {
        return true;
      }
      return false;
    }

    function inferWaterFeatureClass(tags, geometryType) {
      const safeTags = tags && typeof tags === "object" ? tags : {};
      if (isExcludedOpenWaterTags(safeTags)) {
        return "";
      }
      const waterway = safeTags.waterway ? String(safeTags.waterway).toLowerCase() : "";
      const natural = safeTags.natural ? String(safeTags.natural).toLowerCase() : "";
      const water = safeTags.water ? String(safeTags.water).toLowerCase() : "";
      const landuse = safeTags.landuse ? String(safeTags.landuse).toLowerCase() : "";
      if (geometryType === "LineString") {
        if (waterway === "river") return "river";
        if (waterway === "canal" || waterway === "ditch") return "canal";
        if (waterway === "stream" || waterway === "drain" || waterway === "brook") return "stream";
        if (waterway === "riverbank") return "river";
        if (water === "river") return "river";
        if (water === "canal") return "canal";
        if (water === "stream") return "stream";
        return "river";
      }
      if (waterway === "riverbank") return "riverbank";
      if (landuse === "reservoir" || landuse === "basin") return "reservoir";
      if (water === "pond") return "pond";
      if (water === "reservoir" || water === "basin") return "reservoir";
      if (water === "river" || water === "riverbank") return "riverbank";
      if (water === "canal") return "riverbank";
      if (water === "lake" || water === "lagoon" || water === "oxbow") return "lake";
      if (natural === "water") return "lake";
      return "lake";
    }

    function parseWaterNumericTag(value) {
      if (Number.isFinite(value)) {
        return Number(value);
      }
      if (typeof value !== "string") {
        return NaN;
      }
      const match = String(value).match(/-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?/);
      if (!match) {
        return NaN;
      }
      const parsed = Number(match[0]);
      return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : NaN;
    }

    function inferWaterWidthM(featureClass, tags, widthHint) {
      if (Number.isFinite(widthHint) && widthHint > 0.3) {
        return Number(widthHint);
      }
      const safeTags = tags && typeof tags === "object" ? tags : {};
      const explicitWidth = parseWaterNumericTag(safeTags.width);
      if (Number.isFinite(explicitWidth) && explicitWidth > 0.3) {
        return clamp(explicitWidth, 0.6, 90);
      }
      const estWidth = parseWaterNumericTag(safeTags.est_width);
      if (Number.isFinite(estWidth) && estWidth > 0.3) {
        return clamp(estWidth, 0.6, 90);
      }
      if (featureClass === "river") return 14;
      if (featureClass === "canal") return 9;
      if (featureClass === "stream") return 4;
      return 6;
    }

    function getWaterLineOffsetM(featureClass) {
      const base = Number.isFinite(Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.lineOffsetM))
        ? Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.lineOffsetM)
        : 0.1;
      const cls = String(featureClass || "").toLowerCase();
      if (cls === "stream") return base * 0.88;
      if (cls === "river") return base * 1.1;
      return base;
    }

    function getWaterAreaOffsetM() {
      return Number.isFinite(Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.areaOffsetM))
        ? Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.areaOffsetM)
        : 0.06;
    }

    function normalizeWaterLineCoordinates(rawCoords) {
      const coords = Array.isArray(rawCoords)
        ? rawCoords
            .map((coord) => {
              if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) return null;
              const lon = Number(coord[0]);
              const lat = Number(coord[1]);
              return Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat) ? [lon, lat] : null;
            })
            .filter(Boolean)
        : [];
      return coords.length >= 2 ? coords : null;
    }

    function normalizeWaterRingCoordinates(rawCoords) {
      const coords = Array.isArray(rawCoords)
        ? rawCoords
            .map((coord) => {
              if (!Array.isArray(coord) || coord.length < 2) return null;
              const lon = Number(coord[0]);
              const lat = Number(coord[1]);
              return Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat) ? [lon, lat] : null;
            })
            .filter(Boolean)
        : [];
      if (coords.length < 3) {
        return null;
      }
      return coords;
    }

    function normalizeWaterLayerFeature(rawFeature, sourceLabel) {
      if (!rawFeature || typeof rawFeature !== "object") {
        return null;
      }
      if (!rawFeature.geometry || !rawFeature.geometry.type) {
        return null;
      }
      const geometry = rawFeature.geometry;
      const properties = rawFeature.properties && typeof rawFeature.properties === "object"
        ? rawFeature.properties
        : {};
      const attrs = properties.attrs && typeof properties.attrs === "object"
        ? properties.attrs
        : (properties.tags && typeof properties.tags === "object" ? properties.tags : properties);
      const zMode = properties.z_mode ? String(properties.z_mode) : (properties.zMode ? String(properties.zMode) : "");
      if (isUndergroundFeature(attrs, { zMode })) {
        return null;
      }
      if (isExcludedOpenWaterTags(attrs)) {
        return null;
      }
      const source = properties.source ? String(properties.source).toLowerCase() : sourceLabel;
      const priority = Number.isFinite(Number(properties.priority)) ? Number(properties.priority) : 0;
      const id = properties.id ? String(properties.id) : "";
      const widthHint = Number.isFinite(Number(properties.width_m))
        ? Number(properties.width_m)
        : (Number.isFinite(Number(properties.widthM)) ? Number(properties.widthM) : NaN);
      const classHint = properties.featureClass ? String(properties.featureClass).toLowerCase() : "";

      if (geometry.type === "LineString") {
        const coords = normalizeWaterLineCoordinates(geometry.coordinates);
        if (!coords) return null;
        const featureClass = normalizeWaterFeatureClass(
          classHint || inferWaterFeatureClass(attrs, "LineString"),
          "LineString"
        );
        return {
          id,
          source,
          featureClass,
          attrs,
          priority,
          widthM: inferWaterWidthM(featureClass, attrs, widthHint),
          geometryType: "LineString",
          coordinates: coords,
        };
      }
      if (geometry.type === "MultiLineString" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates)) {
        const out = [];
        for (const line of geometry.coordinates) {
          const coords = normalizeWaterLineCoordinates(line);
          if (!coords) continue;
          const featureClass = normalizeWaterFeatureClass(
            classHint || inferWaterFeatureClass(attrs, "LineString"),
            "LineString"
          );
          out.push({
            id,
            source,
            featureClass,
            attrs,
            priority,
            widthM: inferWaterWidthM(featureClass, attrs, widthHint),
            geometryType: "LineString",
            coordinates: coords,
          });
        }
        return out.length > 0 ? out : null;
      }
      if (geometry.type === "Polygon" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates) && geometry.coordinates.length > 0) {
        const ring = normalizeWaterRingCoordinates(geometry.coordinates[0]);
        if (!ring) return null;
        if (!shouldTreatWaterFeatureAsArea(attrs, "Polygon")) {
          const featureClass = normalizeWaterFeatureClass(
            classHint || inferWaterFeatureClass(attrs, "LineString"),
            "LineString"
          );
          return {
            id,
            source,
            featureClass,
            attrs,
            priority,
            widthM: inferWaterWidthM(featureClass, attrs, widthHint),
            geometryType: "LineString",
            coordinates: ring,
          };
        }
        const featureClass = normalizeWaterFeatureClass(
          classHint || inferWaterFeatureClass(attrs, "Polygon"),
          "Polygon"
        );
        return {
          id,
          source,
          featureClass,
          attrs,
          priority,
          geometryType: "Polygon",
          coordinates: ring,
        };
      }
      if (geometry.type === "MultiPolygon" && Array.isArray(geometry.coordinates)) {
        const out = [];
        for (const poly of geometry.coordinates) {
          const ring = Array.isArray(poly) ? normalizeWaterRingCoordinates(poly[0]) : null;
          if (!ring) continue;
          if (!shouldTreatWaterFeatureAsArea(attrs, "Polygon")) {
            const featureClass = normalizeWaterFeatureClass(
              classHint || inferWaterFeatureClass(attrs, "LineString"),
              "LineString"
            );
            out.push({
              id,
              source,
              featureClass,
              attrs,
              priority,
              widthM: inferWaterWidthM(featureClass, attrs, widthHint),
              geometryType: "LineString",
              coordinates: ring,
            });
            continue;
          }
          const featureClass = normalizeWaterFeatureClass(
            classHint || inferWaterFeatureClass(attrs, "Polygon"),
            "Polygon"
          );
          out.push({
            id,
            source,
            featureClass,
            attrs,
            priority,
            geometryType: "Polygon",
            coordinates: ring,
          });
        }
        return out.length > 0 ? out : null;
      }
      return null;
    }

    function flattenNormalizedWaterFeatures(value) {
      if (!value) return [];
      if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.filter(Boolean);
      return [value];
    }

    function buildWaterFeatureMergeKey(feature) {
      if (!feature || !feature.geometryType || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) || feature.coordinates.length < 2) {
        return "";
      }
      const first = feature.coordinates[0];
      const last = feature.coordinates[feature.coordinates.length - 1];
      if (!Array.isArray(first) || !Array.isArray(last) || first.length < 2 || last.length < 2) {
        return "";
      }
      const round = (value, scale) => Math.round((Number(value) || 0) * scale);
      const a = round(first[0], 1e6) + ":" + round(first[1], 1e6);
      const b = round(last[0], 1e6) + ":" + round(last[1], 1e6);
      const orderA = a <= b ? a : b;
      const orderB = a <= b ? b : a;
      const geomKey = String(feature.geometryType);
      const cls = String(feature.featureClass || "").toLowerCase();
      const widthKey = feature.geometryType === "LineString" ? round(feature.widthM, 10) : 0;
      return cls + "|" + geomKey + "|" + orderA + "|" + orderB + "|" + String(feature.coordinates.length) + "|" + String(widthKey);
    }

    function mergeWaterFeatureSets(primaryFeatures, secondaryFeatures) {
      const out = [];
      const seen = new Set();
      const append = (feature, sourceFallback) => {
        if (!feature || !feature.geometryType || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) || feature.coordinates.length < 2) {
          return;
        }
        const normalized = {
          ...feature,
          source: feature.source ? String(feature.source).toLowerCase() : sourceFallback,
        };
        const key = buildWaterFeatureMergeKey(normalized);
        if (key && seen.has(key)) {
          return;
        }
        if (key) {
          seen.add(key);
        }
        out.push(normalized);
      };
      for (const feature of Array.isArray(primaryFeatures) ? primaryFeatures : []) {
        append(feature, "manifest");
      }
      for (const feature of Array.isArray(secondaryFeatures) ? secondaryFeatures : []) {
        append(feature, "osm");
      }
      return out;
    }

    function buildWaterLayerManager() {
      if (state.waterLayerManager) {
        return state.waterLayerManager;
      }
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.name = "waterLayerGroup";
      state.scene.add(group);
      const opacity = Number.isFinite(Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.opacity))
        ? clamp(Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.opacity), 0.15, 0.95)
        : 0.62;
      const createWaterMaterial = (colorHex, roughness, metalness) => new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
        color: colorHex,
        roughness,
        metalness,
        transparent: true,
        opacity,
        depthTest: true,
        depthWrite: false,
        polygonOffset: true,
        polygonOffsetFactor: -2,
        polygonOffsetUnits: -2,
      });
      const manager = {
        group,
        tiles: new Map(),
        pending: new Set(),
        desired: new Set(),
        failureBackoffByKey: new Map(),
        failureReasonByKey: new Map(),
        lastTickMs: 0,
        currentZoom: null,
        loaded: 0,
        failed: 0,
        ready: false,
        warning: "",
        maxActiveTiles: Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.maxActiveTiles) || 24,
        hysteresisMs: Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.hysteresisMs) || 10000,
        requestIntervalMs: Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.requestIntervalMs) || 950,
        featureCounts: {
          river: 0,
          canal: 0,
          stream: 0,
          lake: 0,
          pond: 0,
          reservoir: 0,
          riverbank: 0,
          total: 0,
        },
        materials: {
          river: createWaterMaterial(0x5e90af, 0.9, 0.02),
          canal: createWaterMaterial(0x6c9fbe, 0.89, 0.02),
          stream: createWaterMaterial(0x7caecd, 0.88, 0.02),
          lake: createWaterMaterial(0x4f7f9e, 0.94, 0.01),
          pond: createWaterMaterial(0x6289a3, 0.94, 0.01),
          reservoir: createWaterMaterial(0x4d7896, 0.95, 0.01),
          riverbank: createWaterMaterial(0x5b88a8, 0.93, 0.01),
        },
      };
      state.waterLayerManager = manager;
      return manager;
    }

    async function fetchWaterFeaturesFromManifestTile(zoom, x, y) {
      const cacheKey = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      const cached = waterLayerTileFeatureCache.get(cacheKey);
      if (cached && cached.expiresAt > Date.now()) {
        return Array.isArray(cached.features) ? cached.features : [];
      }
      const manifest = WATERWAYS_MANIFEST && typeof WATERWAYS_MANIFEST === "object"
        ? WATERWAYS_MANIFEST
        : {};
      const basePath = manifest.basePath ? String(manifest.basePath) : "";
      const tileKey = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      const flatName = "water_z" + String(zoom) + "_x" + String(x) + "_y" + String(y) + ".json";
      const urls = [];
      if (manifest.tileIndex && typeof manifest.tileIndex === "object") {
        const indexed = manifest.tileIndex[tileKey];
        if (typeof indexed === "string" && indexed.length > 0) {
          const lower = indexed.toLowerCase();
          if (lower.startsWith("http://") || lower.startsWith("https://")) {
            urls.push(indexed);
          } else {
            urls.push(basePath ? joinAssetPath(basePath, indexed) : indexed);
          }
        }
      }
      if (typeof manifest.urlTemplate === "string" && manifest.urlTemplate) {
        urls.push(
          String(manifest.urlTemplate)
            .replace("{z}", String(zoom))
            .replace("{x}", String(x))
            .replace("{y}", String(y))
        );
      }
      if (basePath) {
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json"));
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, flatName));
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, "waterways_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json"));
        urls.push(joinAssetPath(basePath, "waterways_osm_tiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json"));
      }
      urls.push("./patch_assets/" + flatName);
      urls.push("patch_assets/" + flatName);
      urls.push("./" + flatName);
      urls.push(flatName);
      urls.push("./patch_assets/waterways_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("patch_assets/waterways_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("./waterways_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      urls.push("waterways_pmtiles/" + String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y) + ".json");
      const uniqueUrls = Array.from(new Set(urls.filter((value) => typeof value === "string" && value.length > 0)));
      for (const url of uniqueUrls) {
        try {
          const payload = await tryFetchJsonCandidate(url, 7000, isFeatureCollectionPayload);
          if (!payload || !Array.isArray(payload.features)) continue;
          const normalized = [];
          for (const feature of payload.features) {
            normalized.push(...flattenNormalizedWaterFeatures(normalizeWaterLayerFeature(feature, "manifest")));
          }
          if (normalized.length > 0) {
            const deduped = mergeWaterFeatureSets(normalized, []);
            waterLayerTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, {
              features: deduped,
              expiresAt: Date.now() + 5 * 60 * 1000,
            });
            return deduped;
          }
        } catch (_error) {
          // continue
        }
      }
      waterLayerTileFeatureCache.set(cacheKey, { features: [], expiresAt: Date.now() + 60 * 1000 });
      return [];
    }

    function isWaterRuntimeOverpassFallbackEnabled() {
      if (WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && typeof WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.runtimeOverpassFallback === "boolean") {
        return WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.runtimeOverpassFallback;
      }
      return true;
    }

    function overpassCoordsToLine(geometryList) {
      if (!Array.isArray(geometryList) || geometryList.length < 2) {
        return null;
      }
      const coords = geometryList
        .map((pt) => {
          if (!pt) return null;
          const lon = Number(pt.lon);
          const lat = Number(pt.lat);
          return Number.isFinite(lon) && Number.isFinite(lat) ? [lon, lat] : null;
        })
        .filter(Boolean);
      return coords.length >= 2 ? coords : null;
    }

    function buildWaterFeatureFromOverpassWay(element) {
      const tags = element && element.tags && typeof element.tags === "object" ? element.tags : {};
      if (isExcludedOpenWaterTags(tags)) {
        return null;
      }
      const ring = overpassCoordsToRing(element && element.geometry);
      const treatAsArea = !!ring && shouldTreatWaterFeatureAsArea(tags, "Polygon");
      if (treatAsArea) {
        const cls = normalizeWaterFeatureClass(inferWaterFeatureClass(tags, "Polygon"), "Polygon");
        return {
          type: "Feature",
          geometry: {
            type: "Polygon",
            coordinates: [ring],
          },
          properties: {
            id: "osm:way:" + String(element && element.id ? element.id : ""),
            featureClass: cls,
            source: "osm",
            priority: 45,
            attrs: tags,
            tags,
          },
        };
      }
      const line = overpassCoordsToLine(element && element.geometry);
      if (!line) {
        return null;
      }
      const cls = normalizeWaterFeatureClass(inferWaterFeatureClass(tags, "LineString"), "LineString");
      return {
        type: "Feature",
        geometry: {
          type: "LineString",
          coordinates: line,
        },
        properties: {
          id: "osm:way:" + String(element && element.id ? element.id : ""),
          featureClass: cls,
          source: "osm",
          width_m: inferWaterWidthM(cls, tags, NaN),
          priority: 40,
          attrs: tags,
          tags,
        },
      };
    }

    function buildWaterFeatureFromOverpassRelation(element) {
      const tags = element && element.tags && typeof element.tags === "object" ? element.tags : {};
      if (isExcludedOpenWaterTags(tags)) {
        return null;
      }
      const members = Array.isArray(element && element.members) ? element.members : [];
      const outerRings = [];
      for (const member of members) {
        if (!member || member.type !== "way") {
          continue;
        }
        const role = String(member.role || "").toLowerCase();
        if (role && role !== "outer") {
          continue;
        }
        const ring = overpassCoordsToRing(member.geometry);
        if (!ring) {
          continue;
        }
        outerRings.push([ring]);
      }
      if (outerRings.length > 0 && shouldTreatWaterFeatureAsArea(tags, "Polygon")) {
        const cls = normalizeWaterFeatureClass(inferWaterFeatureClass(tags, "Polygon"), "Polygon");
        return {
          type: "Feature",
          geometry: {
            type: outerRings.length === 1 ? "Polygon" : "MultiPolygon",
            coordinates: outerRings.length === 1 ? outerRings[0] : outerRings,
          },
          properties: {
            id: "osm:relation:" + String(element && element.id ? element.id : ""),
            featureClass: cls,
            source: "osm",
            priority: 46,
            attrs: tags,
            tags,
          },
        };
      }
      const line = overpassCoordsToLine(element && element.geometry);
      if (!line) {
        return null;
      }
      const cls = normalizeWaterFeatureClass(inferWaterFeatureClass(tags, "LineString"), "LineString");
      return {
        type: "Feature",
        geometry: {
          type: "LineString",
          coordinates: line,
        },
        properties: {
          id: "osm:relation:" + String(element && element.id ? element.id : ""),
          featureClass: cls,
          source: "osm",
          width_m: inferWaterWidthM(cls, tags, NaN),
          priority: 42,
          attrs: tags,
          tags,
        },
      };
    }

    async function fetchWaterFeaturesFromOverpass(bounds, zoom) {
      if (!bounds || !isWaterRuntimeOverpassFallbackEnabled()) {
        return [];
      }
      const maxZoom = Number.isFinite(Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassMaxZoom))
        ? Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassMaxZoom)
        : 14;
      if (Number(zoom) > maxZoom) {
        return [];
      }
      const endpointList =
        Array.isArray(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassEndpoints)
          ? WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassEndpoints.map((value) => String(value || "").trim()).filter(Boolean)
          : [];
      if (endpointList.length <= 0) {
        endpointList.push(
          "https://overpass-api.de/api/interpreter",
          "https://overpass.kumi.systems/api/interpreter",
          "https://overpass.private.coffee/api/interpreter"
        );
      }
      const timeoutSec = Number.isFinite(Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassTimeoutSec))
        ? Math.max(10, Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassTimeoutSec))
        : 24;
      const maxRetries = Number.isFinite(Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassMaxRetries))
        ? clamp(Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassMaxRetries), 0, 6)
        : 2;
      const retryBaseMs = Number.isFinite(Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassRetryBaseMs))
        ? Math.max(300, Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassRetryBaseMs))
        : 1200;
      const retryJitterMs = Number.isFinite(Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassRetryJitterMs))
        ? Math.max(0, Number(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.overpassRetryJitterMs))
        : 420;
      const bbox = [
        Number(bounds.south).toFixed(6),
        Number(bounds.west).toFixed(6),
        Number(bounds.north).toFixed(6),
        Number(bounds.east).toFixed(6),
      ].join(",");
      const query =
        '[out:json][timeout:' + String(timeoutSec) + '];(' +
        'way["waterway"~"^(river|canal|stream|ditch|drain|brook|riverbank)$"](' + bbox + ');' +
        'way["natural"="water"](' + bbox + ');' +
        'way["water"](' + bbox + ');' +
        'way["landuse"~"^(reservoir|basin)$"](' + bbox + ');' +
        'relation["waterway"~"^(river|canal|stream|riverbank)$"](' + bbox + ');' +
        'relation["natural"="water"](' + bbox + ');' +
        'relation["water"](' + bbox + ');' +
        'relation["landuse"~"^(reservoir|basin)$"](' + bbox + ');' +
        ');out geom qt;';

      let payload = null;
      let lastError = null;
      for (let attempt = 0; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt += 1) {
        const endpoint = endpointList[attempt % endpointList.length];
        try {
          const response = await fetch(endpoint, {
            method: "POST",
            mode: "cors",
            credentials: "omit",
            headers: {
              "content-type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=UTF-8",
            },
            body: "data=" + encodeURIComponent(query),
          });
          if (!response || !response.ok) {
            const status = response ? Number(response.status) || 0 : 0;
            const error = new Error("water_overpass_http_" + String(status));
            error.status = status;
            error.retryAfterMs = parseRetryAfterMs(response && response.headers ? response.headers.get("retry-after") : null);
            throw error;
          }
          payload = await parseJsonResponseWithContext(response, "water_overpass_payload");
          break;
        } catch (error) {
          lastError = error;
          const status = Number(error && error.status);
          const retryable = !Number.isFinite(status) || status === 0 || status === 408 || status === 429 || status >= 500;
          if ((error && error.message ? String(error.message) : "").includes("non_json")) {
            debugLog("water:overpass_non_json", {
              status: Number.isFinite(status) ? status : "unknown",
              endpoint,
              snippet: error && error.snippet ? String(error.snippet).slice(0, 120) : "",
            });
          }
          if (!retryable || attempt >= maxRetries) {
            break;
          }
          const retryAfterMs = Number(error && error.retryAfterMs) || 0;
          const backoffMs = retryAfterMs > 0
            ? retryAfterMs + Math.floor(Math.random() * 280)
            : Math.floor(retryBaseMs * Math.pow(2, Math.min(attempt, 5)) + Math.random() * retryJitterMs);
          await sleepMs(backoffMs);
        }
      }
      if (!payload) {
        throw lastError || new Error("water_overpass_empty_response");
      }
      const elements = payload && Array.isArray(payload.elements) ? payload.elements : [];
      const normalized = [];
      for (const element of elements) {
        if (!element || (element.type !== "way" && element.type !== "relation")) {
          continue;
        }
        const feature = element.type === "way"
          ? buildWaterFeatureFromOverpassWay(element)
          : buildWaterFeatureFromOverpassRelation(element);
        if (!feature) {
          continue;
        }
        normalized.push(...flattenNormalizedWaterFeatures(normalizeWaterLayerFeature(feature, "osm")));
      }
      if (normalized.length <= 0) {
        return [];
      }
      const deduped = mergeWaterFeatureSets(normalized, []);
      return deduped.slice(0, 900);
    }

    function addWaterStats(target, delta, sign) {
      if (!target || !delta) {
        return;
      }
      const mul = sign < 0 ? -1 : 1;
      for (const key of WATER_CLASS_LIST.concat(["total"])) {
        const base = Number.isFinite(target[key]) ? target[key] : 0;
        const add = Number.isFinite(delta[key]) ? delta[key] : 0;
        target[key] = Math.max(0, base + add * mul);
      }
    }

    function buildWaterTileGroup(tile, features) {
      const manager = buildWaterLayerManager();
      const bounds = tile.bounds;
      const centerECEF = lonLatToECEF(
        (bounds.west + bounds.east) * 0.5,
        (bounds.south + bounds.north) * 0.5,
        0
      );
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.position.copy(centerECEF);
      group.name = "waterTile:" + tile.key;
      const builders = {
        river: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        canal: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        stream: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        lake: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        pond: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        reservoir: { positions: [], indices: [] },
        riverbank: { positions: [], indices: [] },
      };
      const counts = {
        river: 0,
        canal: 0,
        stream: 0,
        lake: 0,
        pond: 0,
        reservoir: 0,
        riverbank: 0,
        total: 0,
      };
      for (const feature of features) {
        if (!feature || !feature.geometryType || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates)) {
          continue;
        }
        if (feature.geometryType === "LineString") {
          const cls = WATER_LINE_CLASS_SET.has(String(feature.featureClass || "").toLowerCase())
            ? String(feature.featureClass).toLowerCase()
            : "river";
          const widthM = inferWaterWidthM(cls, feature.attrs, Number(feature.widthM));
          const appended = appendDrapedRibbon(
            builders[cls],
            feature.coordinates,
            widthM,
            cls,
            centerECEF,
            { attrs: {}, zMode: "drape" },
            getWaterLineOffsetM(cls)
          );
          if (appended > 0) {
            counts[cls] += appended;
            counts.total += appended;
          }
          continue;
        }
        if (feature.geometryType === "Polygon") {
          const cls = WATER_AREA_CLASS_SET.has(String(feature.featureClass || "").toLowerCase())
            ? String(feature.featureClass).toLowerCase()
            : "lake";
          const appended = appendParkPolygon(
            builders[cls],
            feature.coordinates,
            centerECEF,
            getWaterAreaOffsetM(cls)
          );
          if (appended > 0) {
            counts[cls] += appended;
            counts.total += appended;
          }
        }
      }

      for (const cls of Object.keys(builders)) {
