        const geometry = createTransportGeometry(builders[cls]);
        if (!geometry) {
          continue;
        }
        const material = manager.materials[cls] || manager.materials.river;
        const mesh = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, material);
        mesh.frustumCulled = true;
        mesh.renderOrder = isWaterClassArea(cls) ? 34 : 35;
        group.add(mesh);
      }
      return { group, counts };
    }

    async function loadWaterLayerTile(zoom, x, y) {
      const manager = buildWaterLayerManager();
      if (!(manager.failureBackoffByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureBackoffByKey = new Map();
      }
      if (!(manager.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureReasonByKey = new Map();
      }
      const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(x) + "/" + String(y);
      if (manager.pending.has(key) || manager.tiles.has(key)) {
        return;
      }
      const backoffUntil = Number(manager.failureBackoffByKey.get(key)) || 0;
      if (backoffUntil > Date.now()) {
        return;
      }
      manager.pending.add(key);
      const bounds = slippyBounds(x, y, zoom);
      try {
        const bundled = await fetchWaterFeaturesFromManifestTile(zoom, x, y);
        let features = Array.isArray(bundled) ? bundled : [];
        let source = features.length > 0 ? "manifest" : "none";
        if (features.length <= 0 && isWaterRuntimeOverpassFallbackEnabled()) {
          try {
            const fallback = await fetchWaterFeaturesFromOverpass(bounds, zoom);
            if (Array.isArray(fallback) && fallback.length > 0) {
              features = fallback;
              source = "osm";
            }
          } catch (fallbackError) {
            manager.failureReasonByKey.set(
              key,
              fallbackError && fallbackError.message
                ? String(fallbackError.message)
                : String(fallbackError)
            );
          }
        }
        if (!Array.isArray(features) || features.length <= 0) {
          manager.failed += 1;
          manager.warning = "Water tile failed: " + key;
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 22000);
          if (!manager.failureReasonByKey.has(key)) {
            manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, "no_data");
          }
          return;
        }
        const built = buildWaterTileGroup({ key, z: zoom, x, y, bounds }, features);
        if (!built || !built.group || built.counts.total <= 0) {
          manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 20000);
          manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, "no_renderable");
          return;
        }
        manager.group.add(built.group);
        manager.tiles.set(key, {
          key,
          z: zoom,
          x,
          y,
          bounds,
          group: built.group,
          counts: built.counts,
          source,
          features,
          lastWantedMs: Date.now(),
        });
        manager.loaded += 1;
        manager.ready = true;
        manager.failureBackoffByKey.delete(key);
        manager.failureReasonByKey.delete(key);
        addWaterStats(manager.featureCounts, built.counts, 1);
        debugLog("water:tile_loaded", {
          key,
          source,
          count: built.counts.total,
        });
      } catch (error) {
        manager.failed += 1;
        manager.warning = "Water tile failed: " + key;
        manager.failureBackoffByKey.set(key, Date.now() + 22000);
        manager.failureReasonByKey.set(key, error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error));
        debugLog("water:tile_failed", {
          key,
          message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
        });
      } finally {
        manager.pending.delete(key);
      }
    }

    function evictWaterLayerTile(tile, reason) {
      const manager = state.waterLayerManager;
      if (!manager || !tile) return;
      try {
        if (tile.group && tile.group.parent) {
          tile.group.parent.remove(tile.group);
        }
        if (tile.group && typeof tile.group.traverse === "function") {
          tile.group.traverse((child) => {
            if (!child || !child.isMesh) return;
            if (child.geometry && typeof child.geometry.dispose === "function") {
              child.geometry.dispose();
            }
          });
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }
      manager.tiles.delete(tile.key);
      addWaterStats(manager.featureCounts, tile.counts || {}, -1);
      debugLog("water:tile_evicted", { key: tile.key, reason: reason || "evict" });
    }

    function clearWaterLayerManager() {
      const manager = state.waterLayerManager;
      if (!manager) return;
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        evictWaterLayerTile(tile, "water_reset");
      }
      manager.tiles.clear();
      manager.pending.clear();
      manager.desired.clear();
      manager.currentZoom = null;
      manager.loaded = 0;
      manager.failed = 0;
      manager.ready = false;
      manager.warning = "";
      manager.featureCounts = {
        river: 0,
        canal: 0,
        stream: 0,
        lake: 0,
        pond: 0,
        reservoir: 0,
        riverbank: 0,
        total: 0,
      };
      if (!(manager.failureBackoffByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureBackoffByKey = new Map();
      }
      if (!(manager.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map)) {
        manager.failureReasonByKey = new Map();
      }
      manager.failureBackoffByKey.clear();
      manager.failureReasonByKey.clear();
      waterLayerTileFeatureCache.clear();
    }

    function chooseWaterLayerZoom(altitudeM, currentZoom) {
      const cfg = WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.tileZoomRange
        ? WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.tileZoomRange
        : TRANSPORT_CONFIG.tileZoomRange;
      return chooseTransportZoom(altitudeM, Number.isFinite(currentZoom) ? currentZoom : Number(cfg && cfg.max));
    }

    function scheduleWaterLayerTiles(nowMs) {
      if (WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.enabled === false) {
        return;
      }
      const manager = buildWaterLayerManager();
      if (!state.camera) return;
      if (nowMs - manager.lastTickMs < manager.requestIntervalMs) return;
      manager.lastTickMs = nowMs;
      const llh = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
      if (!llh || !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) || !Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) return;
      if (!isWithinBounds(llh.lng, llh.lat, TOKYO23 && TOKYO23.bounds ? TOKYO23.bounds : null)) return;
      const suggestedZoom = chooseWaterLayerZoom(llh.altitudeM, manager.currentZoom);
      const availableZooms = getTileIndexZoomLevels(
        WATERWAYS_MANIFEST && WATERWAYS_MANIFEST.tileIndex && typeof WATERWAYS_MANIFEST.tileIndex === "object"
          ? WATERWAYS_MANIFEST.tileIndex
          : null
      );
      const constrainedZoom = constrainZoomToAvailableLevels(suggestedZoom, availableZooms);
      const previousZoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : null;
      manager.currentZoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : constrainedZoom;
      if (manager.currentZoom !== constrainedZoom) {
        manager.currentZoom = constrainedZoom;
        for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
          if (!tile || tile.z === constrainedZoom) continue;
          evictWaterLayerTile(tile, "zoom_change");
        }
        manager.desired.clear();
        debugLog("water:zoom_changed", {
          from: previousZoom,
          to: constrainedZoom,
        });
      }
      const zoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : constrainedZoom;
      const center = lonLatToSlippy(llh.lng, llh.lat, zoom);
      const radius = state.driveMode ? 1 : 1;
      const pendingCap = state.driveMode ? 6 : 4;
      const desired = new Set();
      const maxIndex = Math.pow(2, zoom) - 1;
      for (let dy = -radius; dy <= radius; dy += 1) {
        for (let dx = -radius; dx <= radius; dx += 1) {
          if (desired.size >= manager.maxActiveTiles) continue;
          const tx = clamp(center.x + dx, 0, maxIndex);
          const ty = clamp(center.y + dy, 0, maxIndex);
          const tileBounds = slippyBounds(tx, ty, zoom);
          if (!transportTileRelevantToActiveWards(tileBounds, llh)) continue;
          const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(tx) + "/" + String(ty);
          desired.add(key);
          const existing = manager.tiles.get(key);
          if (existing) {
            existing.lastWantedMs = nowMs;
            continue;
          }
          if (manager.pending.size >= pendingCap) continue;
          loadWaterLayerTile(zoom, tx, ty).catch((error) => {
            debugLog("water:tile_async_error", {
              key,
              message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
            });
          });
        }
      }
      manager.desired = desired;
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        if (desired.has(tile.key)) continue;
        if (nowMs - (tile.lastWantedMs || 0) >= manager.hysteresisMs) {
          evictWaterLayerTile(tile, "outside_desired");
        }
      }
    }

    function collectStreetControlFeatures() {
      const manager = state.streetLayerManager;
      if (!manager || !(manager.tiles instanceof Map) || manager.tiles.size <= 0) {
        return [];
      }
      const out = [];
      for (const tile of manager.tiles.values()) {
        if (!tile || !Array.isArray(tile.assetFeatures)) continue;
        for (const feature of tile.assetFeatures) {
          if (!feature || feature.geometryType !== "Point" || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates)) continue;
          const cls = String(feature.featureClass || "").toLowerCase();
          if (cls === "traffic_signal" || cls === "stop_sign" || cls === "turn_restriction_hint") {
            out.push(feature);
          }
        }
      }
      return out;
    }

    function parseTrafficMaxSpeedMps(attrs, fallbackMps) {
      const value = attrs && attrs.maxspeed ? String(attrs.maxspeed) : "";
      if (!value) return fallbackMps;
      const numeric = Number(String(value).replace(/[^\d.]/g, ""));
      if (!Number.isFinite(numeric) || numeric <= 0) return fallbackMps;
      return numeric > 35 ? numeric / 3.6 : numeric;
    }

    function buildTrafficNodeKey(lon, lat) {
      return Math.round(Number(lon) * 1e6) + ":" + Math.round(Number(lat) * 1e6);
    }

    function buildTrafficGraph(roads, controls) {
      const nodes = new Map();
      const edges = new Map();
      const stopByNode = new Map();
      const signalByNode = new Map();
      const restrictedWayPairs = new Set();

      function ensureNode(lon, lat) {
        const key = buildTrafficNodeKey(lon, lat);
        if (!nodes.has(key)) {
          nodes.set(key, { id: key, lon, lat, out: [] });
        }
        return nodes.get(key);
      }

      function addEdge(fromNode, toNode, coords, attrs, wayId, reverseFlag) {
        if (!fromNode || !toNode || !Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length < 2) return;
        let lengthM = 0;
        for (let i = 0; i < coords.length - 1; i += 1) {
          const a = coords[i];
          const b = coords[i + 1];
          if (!Array.isArray(a) || !Array.isArray(b) || a.length < 2 || b.length < 2) continue;
          lengthM += haversineDistanceM(Number(a[0]), Number(a[1]), Number(b[0]), Number(b[1]));
        }
        if (!Number.isFinite(lengthM) || lengthM <= 1) return;
        const maxSpeedMps = parseTrafficMaxSpeedMps(attrs, 11);
        const edgeId =
          String(fromNode.id) +
          "->" +
          String(toNode.id) +
          ":" +
          String(wayId || "w") +
          ":" +
          String(reverseFlag ? "r" : "f") +
          ":" +
          String(edges.size);
        const edge = {
          id: edgeId,
          from: fromNode.id,
          to: toNode.id,
          coords,
          lengthM,
          maxSpeedMps,
          wayId: Number.isFinite(Number(wayId)) ? Number(wayId) : null,
          attrs: attrs && typeof attrs === "object" ? attrs : {},
        };
        edges.set(edgeId, edge);
        fromNode.out.push(edgeId);
      }

      for (const road of roads) {
        if (!road || !Array.isArray(road.coordinates) || road.coordinates.length < 2) continue;
        const start = road.coordinates[0];
        const end = road.coordinates[road.coordinates.length - 1];
        if (!Array.isArray(start) || !Array.isArray(end) || start.length < 2 || end.length < 2) continue;
        const fromNode = ensureNode(Number(start[0]), Number(start[1]));
        const toNode = ensureNode(Number(end[0]), Number(end[1]));
        const attrs = road.attrs && typeof road.attrs === "object" ? road.attrs : {};
        const oneway = attrs.oneway ? String(attrs.oneway).toLowerCase() : "";
        const canForward = oneway !== "-1";
        const canReverse = oneway !== "yes" && oneway !== "1" && oneway !== "true";
        if (canForward) {
          addEdge(fromNode, toNode, road.coordinates, attrs, road.wayId, false);
        }
        if (canReverse) {
          addEdge(toNode, fromNode, road.coordinates.slice().reverse(), attrs, road.wayId, true);
        }
      }

      if (Array.isArray(controls)) {
        const nodeList = Array.from(nodes.values());
        const nearestNode = (lon, lat, maxDistM) => {
          let best = null;
          for (const node of nodeList) {
            const dist = haversineDistanceM(lon, lat, node.lon, node.lat);
            if (dist > maxDistM) continue;
            if (!best || dist < best.dist) {
              best = { node, dist };
            }
          }
          return best ? best.node : null;
        };
        for (const control of controls) {
          if (!control || !Array.isArray(control.coordinates) || control.coordinates.length < 2) continue;
          const lon = Number(control.coordinates[0]);
          const lat = Number(control.coordinates[1]);
          if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) continue;
          const node = nearestNode(lon, lat, 28);
          if (!node) continue;
          const cls = String(control.featureClass || "").toLowerCase();
          if (cls === "traffic_signal") {
            if (!signalByNode.has(node.id)) signalByNode.set(node.id, []);
            signalByNode.get(node.id).push(control);
          } else if (cls === "stop_sign") {
            if (!stopByNode.has(node.id)) stopByNode.set(node.id, []);
            stopByNode.get(node.id).push(control);
          } else if (cls === "turn_restriction_hint") {
            const attrs = control.attrs && typeof control.attrs === "object" ? control.attrs : {};
            const fromRef = Number(attrs.fromRef);
            const toRef = Number(attrs.toRef);
            if (Number.isFinite(fromRef) && Number.isFinite(toRef)) {
              restrictedWayPairs.add(String(fromRef) + "->" + String(toRef));
            }
          }
        }
      }

      return {
        nodes,
        edges,
        stopByNode,
        signalByNode,
        restrictedWayPairs,
      };
    }

    function collectTrafficRoadFeatures() {
      const manager = state.transportManager;
      if (!manager || !(manager.tiles instanceof Map) || manager.tiles.size <= 0) {
        return [];
      }
      const roads = [];
      for (const tile of manager.tiles.values()) {
        if (!tile || !Array.isArray(tile.features)) continue;
        for (const feature of tile.features) {
          if (!feature || feature.featureClass !== "road" || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) || feature.coordinates.length < 2) continue;
          roads.push(feature);
        }
      }
      return roads;
    }

    function buildTrafficVehicleSpec(size, wheelRadiusM, kind) {
      const rawWidth = Number(size && size.width);
      const rawHeight = Number(size && size.height);
      const rawLength = Number(size && size.length);
      const width = clamp(Number.isFinite(rawWidth) ? rawWidth : 1.7, 1.2, 3.4);
      const height = clamp(Number.isFinite(rawHeight) ? rawHeight : 1.4, 1.1, 4.2);
      const length = clamp(Number.isFinite(rawLength) ? rawLength : 3.8, 2.4, 16);
      const rawWheelRadius = Number(wheelRadiusM);
      const wheelRadius = clamp(
        Number.isFinite(rawWheelRadius) ? rawWheelRadius : (kind === "bus" ? 0.5 : 0.32),
        0.2,
        0.75
      );
      const wheelWidth = clamp(width * (kind === "bus" ? 0.22 : 0.19), 0.2, 0.8);
      const wheelTrackHalfM = Math.max(0.22, width * 0.5 - wheelWidth * 0.58);
      const axleOffsetM = clamp(length * 0.34, 0.9, length * 0.46);
      const bodyBottomM = kind === "bus" ? 0.34 : 0.22;
      return {
        kind,
        width,
        height,
        length,
        wheelRadius,
        wheelWidth,
        wheelTrackHalfM,
        axleOffsetM,
        wheelCenterY: wheelRadius,
        bodyCenterY: bodyBottomM + height * 0.5,
        groundClearanceM: 0.04,
        bodyGeometry: new THREE.BoxGeometry(width, height, length),
        wheelGeometry: new THREE.CylinderGeometry(wheelRadius, wheelRadius, wheelWidth, 14),
      };
    }

    function addTrafficVehicleWheel(root, manager, spec, x, z) {
      if (!root || !manager || !spec) {
        return;
      }
      const wheel = new THREE.Mesh(spec.wheelGeometry, manager.wheelMaterial);
      wheel.rotation.z = Math.PI * 0.5;
      wheel.position.set(x, spec.wheelCenterY, z);
      root.add(wheel);
      if (manager.wheelHubMaterial) {
        const hub = new THREE.Mesh(
          new THREE.CylinderGeometry(
            spec.wheelRadius * 0.42,
            spec.wheelRadius * 0.42,
            spec.wheelWidth * 0.44,
            12
          ),
          manager.wheelHubMaterial
        );
        hub.rotation.z = Math.PI * 0.5;
        hub.position.set(x, spec.wheelCenterY, z);
        root.add(hub);
      }
    }

    function addNavcatCarBody(root, manager, spec) {
      if (!root || !manager || !spec) {
        return;
      }
      const chassisHeight = spec.height * 0.44;
      const chassis = new THREE.Mesh(
        new THREE.BoxGeometry(spec.width * 0.94, chassisHeight, spec.length * 0.9),
        manager.carBodyMaterial
      );
      chassis.position.set(0, spec.wheelRadius + chassisHeight * 0.5 + 0.04, -spec.length * 0.04);
      root.add(chassis);
      const cabinHeight = spec.height * 0.34;
      const cabin = new THREE.Mesh(
        new THREE.BoxGeometry(spec.width * 0.66, cabinHeight, spec.length * 0.42),
        manager.carCabinMaterial || manager.carBodyMaterial
      );
      cabin.position.set(0, chassis.position.y + chassisHeight * 0.34 + cabinHeight * 0.5, -spec.length * 0.02);
      root.add(cabin);
      const nose = new THREE.Mesh(
        new THREE.ConeGeometry(spec.width * 0.36, spec.length * 0.28, 4),
        manager.carBodyMaterial
      );
      nose.rotation.x = -Math.PI * 0.5;
      nose.rotation.y = Math.PI * 0.25;
      nose.position.set(0, chassis.position.y + chassisHeight * 0.18, spec.length * 0.34);
      root.add(nose);
    }

    function addBusBody(root, manager, spec) {
      if (!root || !manager || !spec) {
        return;
      }
      const body = new THREE.Mesh(spec.bodyGeometry, manager.busBodyMaterial || manager.carBodyMaterial);
      body.position.set(0, spec.bodyCenterY, 0);
      root.add(body);
      const roof = new THREE.Mesh(
        new THREE.BoxGeometry(spec.width * 0.82, spec.height * 0.22, spec.length * 0.68),
        manager.carCabinMaterial || manager.busBodyMaterial || manager.carBodyMaterial
      );
      roof.position.set(0, spec.bodyCenterY + spec.height * 0.28, -spec.length * 0.03);
      root.add(roof);
    }

    function createTrafficVehicleMesh(manager, kind) {
      if (!manager || !manager.vehicleSpecs) {
        return null;
      }
      const spec = manager.vehicleSpecs[kind] || manager.vehicleSpecs.car;
      if (!spec || !manager.wheelMaterial) {
        return null;
      }
      const root = new THREE.Group();
      root.name = "trafficVehicle:" + String(spec.kind || "car");
      if (spec.kind === "bus") {
        addBusBody(root, manager, spec);
      } else {
        addNavcatCarBody(root, manager, spec);
      }
      const wheelZ = [spec.axleOffsetM, -spec.axleOffsetM];
      const wheelX = [spec.wheelTrackHalfM, -spec.wheelTrackHalfM];
      for (const z of wheelZ) {
        for (const x of wheelX) {
          addTrafficVehicleWheel(root, manager, spec, x, z);
        }
      }
      root.userData.kind = spec.kind;
      root.userData.groundClearanceM = spec.groundClearanceM;
      root.traverse((obj) => {
        if (obj && obj.isMesh) {
          obj.castShadow = false;
          obj.receiveShadow = false;
        }
      });
      return root;
    }

    function buildTrafficManager() {
      if (state.trafficManager) {
        return state.trafficManager;
      }
      const group = new THREE.Group();
      group.name = "trafficGroup";
      state.scene.add(group);
      const cfg = TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG && typeof TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG === "object" ? TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG : {};
      const carSize = {
        width: Number(cfg.agentSizeM && cfg.agentSizeM.width) || 1.65,
        height: Number(cfg.agentSizeM && cfg.agentSizeM.height) || 1.4,
        length: Number(cfg.agentSizeM && cfg.agentSizeM.length) || 3.8,
      };
      const busSize = {
        width: Number(cfg.busSizeM && cfg.busSizeM.width) || Math.max(2.45, carSize.width * 1.45),
        height: Number(cfg.busSizeM && cfg.busSizeM.height) || Math.max(2.9, carSize.height * 2.05),
        length: Number(cfg.busSizeM && cfg.busSizeM.length) || Math.max(9.8, carSize.length * 2.5),
      };
      const vehicleSpecs = {
        car: buildTrafficVehicleSpec(carSize, Number(cfg.carWheelRadiusM) || 0.36, "car"),
        bus: buildTrafficVehicleSpec(busSize, Number(cfg.busWheelRadiusM) || 0.5, "bus"),
      };
      const manager = {
        enabled: cfg.enabled !== false,
        group,
        graph: null,
        graphSignature: "",
        graphUpdatedAtMs: 0,
        agents: [],
        nextAgentId: 1,
        accumulatorSec: 0,
        tickSec: 1 / Math.max(2, Number(cfg.tickHz) || 10),
        lastSpawnMs: 0,
        vehicleSpecs,
        vehicleBusShare: clamp(
          Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.busSpawnShare)) ? Number(cfg.busSpawnShare) : 0.24,
          0,
          0.95
        ),
        vehicleBusSpeedScale: clamp(
          Number.isFinite(Number(cfg.busSpeedScale)) ? Number(cfg.busSpeedScale) : 0.74,
          0.35,
          1
        ),
        carBodyMaterial: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          color: 0x2f9ef2,
          emissive: 0x041322,
          emissiveIntensity: 0.14,
          roughness: 0.52,
          metalness: 0.2,
        }),
        carCabinMaterial: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          color: 0x9fd6ff,
          emissive: 0x02101a,
          emissiveIntensity: 0.08,
          roughness: 0.36,
          metalness: 0.08,
          transparent: true,
          opacity: 0.92,
        }),
        busBodyMaterial: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          color: 0xff8f2a,
          emissive: 0x4f1f00,
          emissiveIntensity: 0.32,
          roughness: 0.56,
          metalness: 0.08,
        }),
        wheelMaterial: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          color: 0x13161d,
          emissive: 0x060708,
          emissiveIntensity: 0.35,
          roughness: 0.86,
          metalness: 0.03,
        }),
        wheelHubMaterial: new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          color: 0xb8bec8,
          roughness: 0.58,
          metalness: 0.24,
        }),
        stats: {
          active: 0,
          spawned: 0,
          despawned: 0,
          signalizedJunctions: 0,
        },
      };
      state.trafficManager = manager;
      return manager;
    }

    function clearTrafficManager() {
      const manager = state.trafficManager;
      if (!manager) return;
      for (const agent of manager.agents) {
        if (agent && agent.mesh && agent.mesh.parent) {
          agent.mesh.parent.remove(agent.mesh);
        }
      }
      manager.agents = [];
      manager.graph = null;
      manager.graphSignature = "";
      manager.graphUpdatedAtMs = 0;
      manager.stats.active = 0;
      manager.stats.signalizedJunctions = 0;
    }

    function getTrafficPlayerLonLat() {
      if (state.driveMode && state.kart && state.kart.kinematic && state.kart.kinematic.positionLocal) {
        const llh = driveLocalToLonLat(state.kart.kinematic.positionLocal);
        if (llh && Number.isFinite(llh.lng) && Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) {
          return llh;
        }
      }
      if (state.camera) {
        const llh = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
        if (llh && Number.isFinite(llh.lng) && Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) {
          return llh;
        }
      }
      return null;
    }

    function getTrafficSignalState(control, nowMs) {
      const cfg = TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG && TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.signals ? TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.signals : {};
      const cycleMs = Math.max(3000, Number(cfg.cycleMs) || 18000);
      const greenMs = clamp(Number(cfg.greenMs) || 9000, 1000, cycleMs - 500);
      const amberMs = clamp(Number(cfg.amberMs) || 1800, 0, cycleMs - greenMs);
      const id = control && control.id ? String(control.id) : "";
      let hash = 0;
      for (let i = 0; i < id.length; i += 1) {
        hash = (hash * 31 + id.charCodeAt(i)) >>> 0;
      }
      const offset = hash % cycleMs;
      const t = (nowMs + offset) % cycleMs;
      if (t < greenMs) return "green";
      if (t < greenMs + amberMs) return "amber";
      return "red";
    }

    function sampleLinePoint(coords, progress) {
      if (!Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length <= 0) {
        return null;
      }
      if (coords.length === 1) {
        const only = coords[0];
        if (!Array.isArray(only) || only.length < 2) {
          return null;
        }
        return [Number(only[0]), Number(only[1])];
      }
      const t = clamp(Number.isFinite(progress) ? progress : 0, 0, 1);
      const segmentLengths = [];
      let totalLengthM = 0;
      for (let i = 0; i < coords.length - 1; i += 1) {
        const a = coords[i];
        const b = coords[i + 1];
        if (!Array.isArray(a) || !Array.isArray(b) || a.length < 2 || b.length < 2) {
          segmentLengths.push(0);
          continue;
        }
        const len = haversineDistanceM(Number(a[0]), Number(a[1]), Number(b[0]), Number(b[1]));
        const safeLen = Number.isFinite(len) && len > 0 ? len : 0;
        segmentLengths.push(safeLen);
        totalLengthM += safeLen;
      }
      if (totalLengthM <= 1e-6) {
        const a = coords[0];
        const b = coords[coords.length - 1];
        if (!Array.isArray(a) || !Array.isArray(b) || a.length < 2 || b.length < 2) {
          return null;
        }
        return [
          Number(a[0]) + (Number(b[0]) - Number(a[0])) * t,
          Number(a[1]) + (Number(b[1]) - Number(a[1])) * t,
        ];
      }
      const targetM = t * totalLengthM;
      let traversedM = 0;
      for (let i = 0; i < segmentLengths.length; i += 1) {
        const segLen = segmentLengths[i];
        if (segLen <= 0) {
          continue;
        }
        if (traversedM + segLen >= targetM) {
          const a = coords[i];
          const b = coords[i + 1];
          if (!Array.isArray(a) || !Array.isArray(b) || a.length < 2 || b.length < 2) {
            return null;
          }
          const localT = clamp((targetM - traversedM) / segLen, 0, 1);
          return [
            Number(a[0]) + (Number(b[0]) - Number(a[0])) * localT,
            Number(a[1]) + (Number(b[1]) - Number(a[1])) * localT,
          ];
        }
        traversedM += segLen;
      }
      const last = coords[coords.length - 1];
      if (!Array.isArray(last) || last.length < 2) {
        return null;
      }
      return [Number(last[0]), Number(last[1])];
    }

    function sampleTrafficPoint(coords, progress) {
      try {
        if (typeof sampleLinePoint === "function") {
          const sampled = sampleLinePoint(coords, progress);
          if (Array.isArray(sampled) && sampled.length >= 2) {
            return [Number(sampled[0]), Number(sampled[1])];
          }
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // fall through to linear fallback
      }
      if (!Array.isArray(coords) || coords.length <= 0) {
        return null;
      }
      if (coords.length === 1) {
        const only = coords[0];
        if (!Array.isArray(only) || only.length < 2) {
          return null;
        }
        return [Number(only[0]), Number(only[1])];
      }
      const start = coords[0];
      const end = coords[coords.length - 1];
      if (!Array.isArray(start) || !Array.isArray(end) || start.length < 2 || end.length < 2) {
        return null;
      }
      const t = clamp(Number.isFinite(progress) ? progress : 0, 0, 1);
      return [
        Number(start[0]) + (Number(end[0]) - Number(start[0])) * t,
        Number(start[1]) + (Number(end[1]) - Number(start[1])) * t,
      ];
    }
    try {
      if (typeof globalThis !== "undefined") {
        globalThis.sampleLinePoint = sampleLinePoint;
        globalThis.sampleTrafficPoint = sampleTrafficPoint;
      }
    } catch (_error) {
      // no-op
    }

    function pickTrafficSpawnEdge(graph, playerLLH, radiusM) {
      if (!graph || !(graph.edges instanceof Map) || graph.edges.size <= 0 || !playerLLH) {
        return null;
      }
      const candidates = [];
      for (const edge of graph.edges.values()) {
        if (!edge || !Array.isArray(edge.coords) || edge.coords.length < 2) continue;
        const start = edge.coords[0];
        const end = edge.coords[edge.coords.length - 1];
        if (!Array.isArray(start) || !Array.isArray(end)) continue;
        const centerLon = (Number(start[0]) + Number(end[0])) * 0.5;
        const centerLat = (Number(start[1]) + Number(end[1])) * 0.5;
        const dist = haversineDistanceM(playerLLH.lng, playerLLH.lat, centerLon, centerLat);
        if (dist <= radiusM) {
          candidates.push(edge);
        }
      }
      if (candidates.length <= 0) return null;
      return candidates[Math.floor(Math.random() * candidates.length)];
    }

    function removeTrafficAgent(manager, agent, reason) {
      if (!manager || !agent) return;
      if (agent.mesh && agent.mesh.parent) {
        agent.mesh.parent.remove(agent.mesh);
      }
      manager.stats.despawned += 1;
      debugLog("traffic:agent_removed", {
        id: agent.id,
        reason: reason || "remove",
      });
    }

    function spawnTrafficAgent(manager, nowMs) {
      if (!manager || !manager.graph) return;
      const cfg = TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG && typeof TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG === "object" ? TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG : {};
      const maxVehicles = Math.max(0, Number(cfg.maxVehicles) || 40);
      if (manager.agents.length >= maxVehicles) return;
      const playerLLH = getTrafficPlayerLonLat();
      if (!playerLLH) return;
      const edge = pickTrafficSpawnEdge(manager.graph, playerLLH, Math.max(120, Number(cfg.spawnRadiusM) || 350));
      if (!edge) return;

      const progress = Math.random() * 0.35;
      const pos = sampleTrafficPoint(edge.coords, progress) || edge.coords[0];
      if (!Array.isArray(pos) || pos.length < 2) return;
      const vehicleKind = Math.random() < (Number(manager.vehicleBusShare) || 0) ? "bus" : "car";
      const mesh = createTrafficVehicleMesh(manager, vehicleKind);
      if (!mesh) {
        return;
      }
      manager.group.add(mesh);
      const speedCfg = cfg.speed && typeof cfg.speed === "object" ? cfg.speed : {};
      const minMps = Math.max(2, Number(speedCfg.minMps) || 4);
      const maxMps = Math.max(minMps + 0.1, Number(speedCfg.maxMps) || 14);
      const seedSpeed = clamp(minMps + Math.random() * (maxMps - minMps), minMps, maxMps);
      const kindSpeedScale = vehicleKind === "bus" ? Number(manager.vehicleBusSpeedScale) || 0.74 : 1;
      const targetSpeed = clamp(seedSpeed * kindSpeedScale, minMps * 0.45, maxMps);
      const agent = {
        id: "npc_" + String(manager.nextAgentId++),
        vehicleKind,
        visualSpec: manager.vehicleSpecs && manager.vehicleSpecs[vehicleKind]
          ? manager.vehicleSpecs[vehicleKind]
          : (manager.vehicleSpecs ? manager.vehicleSpecs.car : null),
        edgeId: edge.id,
        progress,
        speedMps: targetSpeed * 0.45,
        targetSpeedMps: targetSpeed,
        prevPos: { lon: Number(pos[0]), lat: Number(pos[1]) },
        currPos: { lon: Number(pos[0]), lat: Number(pos[1]) },
        stoppedUntilMs: 0,
        lastStopNodeId: "",
        lastForwardEcef: null,
        lastRightEcef: null,
        mesh,
      };
      manager.agents.push(agent);
      manager.stats.spawned += 1;
      manager.stats.active = manager.agents.length;
      manager.lastSpawnMs = nowMs;
    }

    function chooseNextTrafficEdge(manager, currentEdge) {
      if (!manager || !manager.graph || !currentEdge) return null;
      const toNode = manager.graph.nodes.get(currentEdge.to);
      if (!toNode || !Array.isArray(toNode.out) || toNode.out.length <= 0) return null;
      const options = [];
      for (const edgeId of toNode.out) {
        const candidate = manager.graph.edges.get(edgeId);
        if (!candidate) continue;
        if (candidate.to === currentEdge.from) {
          continue;
        }
        if (
          Number.isFinite(Number(currentEdge.wayId)) &&
          Number.isFinite(Number(candidate.wayId)) &&
          manager.graph.restrictedWayPairs &&
          manager.graph.restrictedWayPairs.has(String(currentEdge.wayId) + "->" + String(candidate.wayId))
        ) {
          continue;
        }
        options.push(candidate);
      }
      if (options.length <= 0) {
        return null;
      }
      return options[Math.floor(Math.random() * options.length)];
    }

    function evaluateTrafficTargetSpeed(manager, agent, edge, nowMs) {
      const cfg = TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG && typeof TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG === "object" ? TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG : {};
      const speedCfg = cfg.speed && typeof cfg.speed === "object" ? cfg.speed : {};
      const baseMin = Math.max(2, Number(speedCfg.minMps) || 4);
      const baseMax = Math.max(baseMin + 0.2, Number(speedCfg.maxMps) || 14);
      let target = clamp(edge.maxSpeedMps || baseMax, baseMin, baseMax);

      const distanceToEndM = Math.max(0, (1 - agent.progress) * Math.max(1, edge.lengthM));
      const signalControls = manager.graph.signalByNode.get(edge.to) || [];
      for (const signal of signalControls) {
        const stateSignal = getTrafficSignalState(signal, nowMs);
        if ((stateSignal === "red" || stateSignal === "amber") && distanceToEndM < 30) {
          target = 0;
          break;
        }
      }
      const stopControls = manager.graph.stopByNode.get(edge.to) || [];
      const stopCfg = cfg.stopControl && typeof cfg.stopControl === "object" ? cfg.stopControl : {};
      const stopLookAheadM = Math.max(5, Number(stopCfg.lookAheadM) || 18);
      const stopDwellMs = Math.max(300, Number(stopCfg.dwellMs) || 1200);
      if (nowMs < agent.stoppedUntilMs) {
        target = 0;
      } else if (stopControls.length > 0 && distanceToEndM < stopLookAheadM && agent.lastStopNodeId !== edge.to) {
        if (distanceToEndM < 2.4) {
          agent.stoppedUntilMs = nowMs + stopDwellMs;
          agent.lastStopNodeId = edge.to;
          target = 0;
        } else {
          target = Math.min(target, 1.2);
        }
      }
      return target;
    }

    const trafficPoseForward = new THREE.Vector3();
    const trafficPoseRight = new THREE.Vector3();
    const trafficPoseCorrectedForward = new THREE.Vector3();
    const trafficPoseMatrix = new THREE.Matrix4();

    function setTrafficMeshPose(agent, alpha, manager) {
      if (!agent || !agent.mesh || !agent.prevPos || !agent.currPos) return;
      const t = clamp(Number.isFinite(alpha) ? alpha : 1, 0, 1);
      const lon = agent.prevPos.lon + (agent.currPos.lon - agent.prevPos.lon) * t;
      const lat = agent.prevPos.lat + (agent.currPos.lat - agent.prevPos.lat) * t;
      if (!Number.isFinite(lon) || !Number.isFinite(lat)) return;

      let heightM = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lon, lat);
      if (!Number.isFinite(heightM)) {
        heightM = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lon, lat, "");
      }
      const visualSpec = agent.visualSpec && typeof agent.visualSpec === "object" ? agent.visualSpec : null;
      const groundClearanceM = visualSpec && Number.isFinite(Number(visualSpec.groundClearanceM))
        ? Number(visualSpec.groundClearanceM)
        : 0.9;
      const ecef = lonLatToECEF(lon, lat, heightM + groundClearanceM);
      agent.mesh.position.copy(ecef);

      const lookHeight = Number.isFinite(heightM) ? heightM + groundClearanceM : groundClearanceM;
      const up = ecef.clone().normalize();
      const forward = trafficPoseForward;
      forward.set(0, 0, 0);

      if (
        Number.isFinite(Number(agent.prevPos.lon)) &&
        Number.isFinite(Number(agent.prevPos.lat)) &&
        (Math.abs(Number(agent.currPos.lon) - Number(agent.prevPos.lon)) > 1e-10 ||
          Math.abs(Number(agent.currPos.lat) - Number(agent.prevPos.lat)) > 1e-10)
      ) {
        const prevEcef = lonLatToECEF(Number(agent.prevPos.lon), Number(agent.prevPos.lat), lookHeight);
        forward.copy(ecef).sub(prevEcef);
      }

      if (forward.lengthSq() < 1e-8 && manager && manager.graph && manager.graph.edges instanceof Map) {
        const edge = manager.graph.edges.get(agent.edgeId);
        if (edge && Array.isArray(edge.coords) && edge.coords.length >= 2) {
          const p = clamp(Number(agent.progress), 0, 1);
          const back = sampleTrafficPoint(edge.coords, clamp(p - 0.015, 0, 1));
          const ahead = sampleTrafficPoint(edge.coords, clamp(p + 0.015, 0, 1));
          if (Array.isArray(back) && back.length >= 2 && Array.isArray(ahead) && ahead.length >= 2) {
            const backEcef = lonLatToECEF(Number(back[0]), Number(back[1]), lookHeight);
            const aheadEcef = lonLatToECEF(Number(ahead[0]), Number(ahead[1]), lookHeight);
            forward.copy(aheadEcef).sub(backEcef);
          }
        }
      }

      forward.addScaledVector(up, -forward.dot(up));
      if (forward.lengthSq() < 1e-8 && agent.lastForwardEcef && agent.lastForwardEcef.isVector3) {
        forward.copy(agent.lastForwardEcef);
      }
      if (forward.lengthSq() < 1e-8) {
        agent.mesh.up.copy(up);
        return;
      }
      forward.normalize();
      if (!agent.lastForwardEcef || !agent.lastForwardEcef.isVector3) {
        agent.lastForwardEcef = new THREE.Vector3();
      }
      agent.lastForwardEcef.copy(forward);

      const right = trafficPoseRight;
      right.crossVectors(up, forward);
      if (right.lengthSq() < 1e-8 && agent.lastRightEcef && agent.lastRightEcef.isVector3) {
        right.copy(agent.lastRightEcef);
      }
      if (right.lengthSq() < 1e-8) {
        agent.mesh.up.copy(up);
        return;
      }
      right.normalize();
      if (!agent.lastRightEcef || !agent.lastRightEcef.isVector3) {
        agent.lastRightEcef = new THREE.Vector3();
      }
      agent.lastRightEcef.copy(right);

      const correctedForward = trafficPoseCorrectedForward;
      correctedForward.crossVectors(right, up);
      if (correctedForward.lengthSq() < 1e-8) {
        agent.mesh.up.copy(up);
        return;
      }
      correctedForward.normalize();

      trafficPoseMatrix.makeBasis(right, up, correctedForward);
      agent.mesh.quaternion.setFromRotationMatrix(trafficPoseMatrix);
    }

    function applyTrafficPlayerPenalty(manager) {
      if (!manager || !state.driveMode || !state.kart || !state.kart.kinematic || !state.kart.kinematic.positionLocal) {
        return;
      }
      const cfg = TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG && TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.playerPenalty ? TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.playerPenalty : {};
      const radiusM = Math.max(1.2, Number(cfg.radiusM) || 3.2);
      const damp = clamp(Number(cfg.speedDamp) || 0.82, 0.1, 0.98);
      const player = driveLocalToLonLat(state.kart.kinematic.positionLocal);
      if (!player || !Number.isFinite(player.lng) || !Number.isFinite(player.lat)) return;
      for (const agent of manager.agents) {
        if (!agent || !agent.currPos) continue;
        const dist = haversineDistanceM(player.lng, player.lat, agent.currPos.lon, agent.currPos.lat);
        if (dist <= radiusM) {
          state.kart.kinematic.speedMps *= damp;
        }
      }
    }

    function updateTrafficManager(deltaSec, nowMs) {
      const manager = buildTrafficManager();
      if (!manager || !manager.enabled) {
        return;
      }
      const roads = collectTrafficRoadFeatures();
      const controls = collectStreetControlFeatures();
      const signature = String(roads.length) + "|" + String(controls.length);
      if (!manager.graph || manager.graphSignature !== signature || nowMs - manager.graphUpdatedAtMs > 3000) {
        manager.graph = buildTrafficGraph(roads, controls);
        manager.graphSignature = signature;
        manager.graphUpdatedAtMs = nowMs;
        manager.stats.signalizedJunctions = manager.graph && manager.graph.signalByNode
          ? manager.graph.signalByNode.size
          : 0;
      }
      if (!manager.graph || !(manager.graph.edges instanceof Map) || manager.graph.edges.size <= 0) {
        if (manager.agents.length > 0) {
          for (const agent of manager.agents) {
            removeTrafficAgent(manager, agent, "no_graph");
          }
          manager.agents = [];
          manager.stats.active = 0;
        }
        return;
      }

      const cfg = TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG && typeof TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG === "object" ? TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG : {};
      const spawnIntervalMs = Math.max(200, Number(cfg.spawnIntervalMs) || 900);
      if (nowMs - manager.lastSpawnMs >= spawnIntervalMs) {
        spawnTrafficAgent(manager, nowMs);
      }

      manager.accumulatorSec += Math.max(0, Number(deltaSec) || 0);
      const tickSec = Math.max(0.05, Number(manager.tickSec) || 0.1);
      const speedCfg = cfg.speed && typeof cfg.speed === "object" ? cfg.speed : {};
      const accelMps2 = Math.max(0.5, Number(speedCfg.accelMps2) || 2.4);
      const brakeMps2 = Math.max(1.0, Number(speedCfg.brakeMps2) || 4.6);

      const playerLLH = getTrafficPlayerLonLat();
      const despawnRadiusM = Math.max(80, Number(cfg.despawnRadiusM) || 500);

      while (manager.accumulatorSec >= tickSec) {
        manager.accumulatorSec -= tickSec;
        const removeIdx = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < manager.agents.length; i += 1) {
          const agent = manager.agents[i];
          const edge = manager.graph.edges.get(agent.edgeId);
          if (!edge) {
            removeIdx.push(i);
            continue;
          }
          if (playerLLH && agent.currPos) {
            const distanceFromPlayer = haversineDistanceM(playerLLH.lng, playerLLH.lat, agent.currPos.lon, agent.currPos.lat);
            if (distanceFromPlayer > despawnRadiusM) {
              removeIdx.push(i);
              continue;
            }
          }

          agent.prevPos = {
            lon: Number(agent.currPos.lon),
            lat: Number(agent.currPos.lat),
          };
          agent.targetSpeedMps = evaluateTrafficTargetSpeed(manager, agent, edge, nowMs);
          const deltaSpeed = agent.targetSpeedMps - agent.speedMps;
          const maxDelta = deltaSpeed >= 0 ? accelMps2 * tickSec : brakeMps2 * tickSec;
          agent.speedMps += clamp(deltaSpeed, -Math.abs(maxDelta), Math.abs(maxDelta));
          agent.speedMps = Math.max(0, agent.speedMps);

          const deltaProgress = edge.lengthM > 1 ? (agent.speedMps * tickSec) / edge.lengthM : 0;
          agent.progress += deltaProgress;
          if (agent.progress >= 1) {
            const carry = agent.progress - 1;
            const nextEdge = chooseNextTrafficEdge(manager, edge);
            if (!nextEdge) {
              removeIdx.push(i);
              continue;
            }
            agent.edgeId = nextEdge.id;
            agent.progress = clamp(carry, 0, 0.999);
            if (nextEdge.to !== agent.lastStopNodeId) {
              agent.lastStopNodeId = "";
            }
          }
          const activeEdge = manager.graph.edges.get(agent.edgeId);
          if (!activeEdge) {
            removeIdx.push(i);
            continue;
          }
          const pos = sampleTrafficPoint(activeEdge.coords, clamp(agent.progress, 0, 0.999));
          if (!pos || !Array.isArray(pos) || pos.length < 2) {
            removeIdx.push(i);
            continue;
          }
          agent.currPos = {
            lon: Number(pos[0]),
            lat: Number(pos[1]),
          };
        }

        for (let idx = removeIdx.length - 1; idx >= 0; idx -= 1) {
          const i = removeIdx[idx];
          const agent = manager.agents[i];
          removeTrafficAgent(manager, agent, "tick_remove");
          manager.agents.splice(i, 1);
        }
      }

      const alpha = tickSec > 1e-6 ? clamp(manager.accumulatorSec / tickSec, 0, 1) : 1;
      for (const agent of manager.agents) {
        setTrafficMeshPose(agent, alpha, manager);
      }
      manager.stats.active = manager.agents.length;
      applyTrafficPlayerPenalty(manager);
    }

    function safeUpdateTrafficManager(deltaSec, nowMs) {
      if (state.trafficDisabledDueToError) {
        return;
      }
      try {
        updateTrafficManager(deltaSec, nowMs);
      } catch (error) {
        const message = error && error.message ? error.message : String(error);
        state.trafficDisabledDueToError = true;
        console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "traffic:disabled_after_error", {
          message,
          stack: error && error.stack ? String(error.stack).split("\\n").slice(0, 3).join(" | ") : "",
        });
        try {
          clearTrafficManager();
        } catch (_clearError) {
          // no-op
        }
        setStatus("Traffic simulation disabled after runtime error: " + message, "error");
      }
    }

    function getDrivePhysicsNumber(name, fallback) {
      const physics = state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.physics ? state.driveConfig.physics : {};
      const value = Number(physics[name]);
      return Number.isFinite(value) ? value : fallback;
    }

    function getDriveEngine() {
      const raw =
        state.driveConfig && typeof state.driveConfig.engine === "string"
          ? String(state.driveConfig.engine).trim().toLowerCase()
          : "";
      return raw === "cannon" ? "cannon" : "mk3_kinematic";
    }

    function dampScalar(current, target, lambda, deltaSec) {
      const c = Number.isFinite(current) ? current : 0;
      const t = Number.isFinite(target) ? target : 0;
      const l = Math.max(0, Number(lambda) || 0);
      const d = Math.max(0, Number(deltaSec) || 0);
      if (l <= 0 || d <= 0) {
        return t;
      }
      return c + (t - c) * (1 - Math.exp(-l * d));
    }

    function getDriveModelString(name, fallback) {
      const model = state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.model ? state.driveConfig.model : {};
      const value = model && typeof model[name] === "string" ? String(model[name]).trim() : "";
      return value || fallback;
    }

    function getDriveModelBoolean(name, fallback) {
      const model = state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.model ? state.driveConfig.model : {};
      if (typeof model[name] === "boolean") {
        return model[name];
      }
      if (typeof model[name] === "string") {
        const lower = model[name].toLowerCase();
        if (lower === "true") {
          return true;
        }
        if (lower === "false") {
          return false;
        }
      }
      return !!fallback;
    }

    function getDriveModelNumber(name, fallback) {
      const model = state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.model ? state.driveConfig.model : {};
      const value = Number(model[name]);
      return Number.isFinite(value) ? value : fallback;
    }

    function getDriveSpawnBoolean(name, fallback) {
      const spawn = state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.spawn ? state.driveConfig.spawn : {};
      if (typeof spawn[name] === "boolean") {
        return spawn[name];
      }
      if (typeof spawn[name] === "string") {
        const lower = spawn[name].toLowerCase();
        if (lower === "true") {
          return true;
        }
        if (lower === "false") {
          return false;
        }
      }
      return !!fallback;
    }

    function getDriveSpawnNumber(name, fallback) {
      const spawn = state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.spawn ? state.driveConfig.spawn : {};
      const value = Number(spawn[name]);
      return Number.isFinite(value) ? value : fallback;
    }

    function resolveAssetUrlCandidates(value) {
      const input = normalizeAssetPath(value);
      if (!input) {
        return [];
      }
      const out = [];
      const seen = new Set();
      const push = (candidate) => {
        const normalized = normalizeAssetPath(candidate);
        if (!normalized) {
          return;
        }
        const key = normalized.toLowerCase();
        if (seen.has(key)) {
          return;
        }
        seen.add(key);
        out.push(normalized);
      };

      push(input);
      const stripped = trimLeadingSlashes(input.replace(/^\\.\\//, ""));
      if (stripped && stripped !== input) {
        push(stripped);
      }
      if (/^(https?:|data:|blob:|file:)/i.test(input)) {
        return out;
      }

      const baseCandidates = [];
      const seenBaseCandidates = new Set();
      const pushBaseCandidate = (candidate) => {
        const normalized = normalizeAssetPath(candidate);
        if (!normalized) {
          return;
        }
        const key = normalized.toLowerCase();
        if (seenBaseCandidates.has(key)) {
          return;
        }
        seenBaseCandidates.add(key);
        baseCandidates.push(normalized);
      };
      const folder = trimLeadingSlashes(
        normalizeAssetPath(
          PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.folder
            ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.folder)
            : "patch_assets"
        ).replace(/^\\.\\/+/, "")
      ) || "patch_assets";
      const explicitBase =
        PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && typeof PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.baseUrl === "string"
          ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.baseUrl).trim()
          : "";
      if (explicitBase) {
        pushBaseCandidate(explicitBase);
      }
      if (typeof window !== "undefined") {
        if (typeof window.__patchAssetsBaseUrl === "string" && window.__patchAssetsBaseUrl) {
          pushBaseCandidate(window.__patchAssetsBaseUrl);
        }
        if (
          typeof window.__supParentOrigin === "string" &&
          window.__supParentOrigin &&
          window.__supParentOrigin !== "*"
        ) {
          pushBaseCandidate(String(window.__supParentOrigin).replace(/\\/?$/, "/"));
        }
        if (typeof window.__supParentUrl === "string" && window.__supParentUrl) {
          pushBaseCandidate(window.__supParentUrl);
        }
        if (typeof window.__supParentHref === "string" && window.__supParentHref) {
          pushBaseCandidate(window.__supParentHref);
        }
      }
      if (typeof document !== "undefined" && typeof document.baseURI === "string" && document.baseURI) {
        pushBaseCandidate(document.baseURI);
      }
      if (typeof document !== "undefined" && typeof document.referrer === "string" && document.referrer) {
        pushBaseCandidate(document.referrer);
        try {
          const refUrl = new URL(document.referrer);
          const refAssetBase =
            refUrl.searchParams.get("patchAssetsBase") ||
            refUrl.searchParams.get("assetBase") ||
            refUrl.searchParams.get("assetsBase") ||
            refUrl.searchParams.get("patchBase");
          if (refAssetBase) {
            pushBaseCandidate(refAssetBase);
          }
          pushBaseCandidate(new URL("./", document.referrer).toString());
        } catch (_error) {
          // no-op
        }
      }
      if (typeof window !== "undefined" && window.location) {
        if (typeof window.location.href === "string" && window.location.href) {
          pushBaseCandidate(window.location.href);
          try {
            const currentUrl = new URL(window.location.href);
            const currentAssetBase =
              currentUrl.searchParams.get("patchAssetsBase") ||
              currentUrl.searchParams.get("assetBase") ||
              currentUrl.searchParams.get("assetsBase") ||
              currentUrl.searchParams.get("patchBase");
            if (currentAssetBase) {
              pushBaseCandidate(currentAssetBase);
            }
          } catch (_error) {
            // no-op
          }
        }
        if (
          typeof window.location.origin === "string" &&
          window.location.origin &&
          window.location.origin !== "null"
        ) {
          pushBaseCandidate(window.location.origin + "/");
        }
      }
      if (typeof window !== "undefined" && window.parent && window.parent !== window) {
        try {
          if (window.parent.location && typeof window.parent.location.href === "string" && window.parent.location.href) {
            pushBaseCandidate(window.parent.location.href);
          }
        } catch (_error) {
          // no-op
        }
      }
      if (typeof window !== "undefined" && window.top && window.top !== window) {
        try {
          if (window.top.location && typeof window.top.location.href === "string" && window.top.location.href) {
            pushBaseCandidate(window.top.location.href);
          }
        } catch (_error) {
          // no-op
        }
      }

      const targets = [];
      const seenTargets = new Set();
      const pushTarget = (candidate) => {
        const normalized = trimLeadingSlashes(normalizeAssetPath(candidate));
        if (!normalized) {
          return;
        }
        const key = normalized.toLowerCase();
        if (seenTargets.has(key)) {
          return;
        }
        seenTargets.add(key);
        targets.push(normalized);
      };
      pushTarget(stripped || input);
      if (stripped && !stripped.startsWith(folder + "/")) {
        pushTarget(folder + "/" + stripped);
      }
      if (stripped && stripped.startsWith(folder + "/")) {
        pushTarget(stripped.slice(folder.length + 1));
      }
      if (input && !stripped && !input.startsWith(folder + "/")) {
        pushTarget(folder + "/" + input);
      }

      for (const base of baseCandidates) {
        for (const target of targets) {
          try {
            push(new URL(target, base).toString());
          } catch (_error) {
            // no-op
          }
        }
      }
      for (const target of targets) {
        push("/" + target);
      }
      return out;
    }

    function getKartModelCandidatePaths() {
      const candidates = [];
      const seen = new Set();
      const pushCandidate = (value) => {
        const resolved = resolveAssetUrlCandidates(value);
        for (const normalized of resolved) {
          const key = normalized.toLowerCase();
          if (seen.has(key)) {
            continue;
          }
          seen.add(key);
          candidates.push(normalized);
        }
      };
      const patchFolder = PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.folder
        ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.folder)
        : "./patch_assets";
      const patchFile = PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG && PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.kartModelFile
        ? String(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG.kartModelFile)
        : "mk3_kart.glb";
      pushCandidate(joinAssetPath(patchFolder, patchFile));
      pushCandidate(patchFile);
      pushCandidate("./" + trimLeadingSlashes(patchFile));
      pushCandidate(getDriveModelString("path", ""));
      pushCandidate(getDriveModelString("fallbackPath", ""));
      if (KART_MANIFEST && typeof KART_MANIFEST.path === "string") {
        pushCandidate("./" + trimLeadingSlashes(String(KART_MANIFEST.path)));
      }
      pushCandidate("./sup/data/kart/mk3_kart.glb");
      if (getDriveModelBoolean("allowRemoteFallback", false)) {
        pushCandidate("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mustache-dev/Mario-Kart-3.js/main/public/models/kart.glb");
        pushCandidate("https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/mustache-dev/Mario-Kart-3.js@main/public/models/kart.glb");
      }
      return candidates;
    }

    function cloneKartTemplateScene() {
      if (!state.kart || !state.kart.modelTemplate) {
        return null;
      }
      if (typeof state.kart.modelTemplate.clone === "function") {
        return state.kart.modelTemplate.clone(true);
      }
      return null;
    }

    function forceKartToonMaterials(root, primaryColor) {
      if (!root) {
        return null;
      }
      const bodyMaterial = new THREE.MeshToonMaterial({
        color: primaryColor,
      });
      const trimMaterial = new THREE.MeshToonMaterial({
        color: 0x2f3847,
      });
      const darkMaterial = new THREE.MeshToonMaterial({
        color: 0x121821,
      });
      root.traverse((obj) => {
        if (!obj || !obj.isMesh) {
          return;
        }
        obj.castShadow = false;
        obj.receiveShadow = false;
        const lowerName = String(obj.name || "").toLowerCase();
        if (lowerName.includes("tire")) {
          obj.material = darkMaterial;
          return;
        }
        if (lowerName.includes("rim") || lowerName.includes("wheel")) {
          obj.material = trimMaterial;
          return;
        }
        obj.material = bodyMaterial;
      });
      return bodyMaterial;
    }

    function getDriveCameraNumber(name, fallback) {
      const cameraCfg = state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.camera ? state.driveConfig.camera : {};
      const value = Number(cameraCfg[name]);
      return Number.isFinite(value) ? value : fallback;
    }

    function ensureCannonModuleLoaded() {
      if (state.cannon && state.cannon.module) {
        return Promise.resolve(state.cannon.module);
      }
      if (state.cannon && state.cannon.loadingPromise) {
        return state.cannon.loadingPromise;
      }
      if (!state.cannon) {
        return Promise.reject(new Error("cannon_state_missing"));
      }
      state.cannon.loadingPromise = loadCannonModule()
        .then((mod) => {
          state.cannon.module = mod;
          state.cannon.ready = true;
          state.cannon.error = "";
          CANNON = mod;
          debugLog("cannon:module_recovered");
          return mod;
        })
        .catch((error) => {
          const message = error && error.message ? error.message : String(error);
          state.cannon.ready = false;
          state.cannon.error = message;
          throw error;
        })
        .finally(() => {
          state.cannon.loadingPromise = null;
        });
      return state.cannon.loadingPromise;
    }

    function createKartWheelMesh(radius, width, accentColor) {
      const wheelGroup = new THREE.Group();
      const tire = new THREE.Mesh(
        new THREE.CylinderGeometry(radius, radius, width, 24),
        new THREE.MeshToonMaterial({ color: 0x111111 })
      );
      tire.rotation.z = Math.PI * 0.5;
      tire.castShadow = false;
      tire.receiveShadow = false;
      wheelGroup.add(tire);

      const rim = new THREE.Mesh(
        new THREE.CylinderGeometry(radius * 0.62, radius * 0.62, width + 0.03, 16),
        new THREE.MeshToonMaterial({ color: 0xd3dae4, emissive: new THREE.Color(accentColor), emissiveIntensity: 0.18 })
      );
      rim.rotation.z = Math.PI * 0.5;
      wheelGroup.add(rim);
      return wheelGroup;
    }

    function createProceduralKartVisualMesh() {
      const palette = [0xff0000, 0x00aa00, 0x0066ff, 0xffdd00, 0xff66aa, 0xff6600];
      const accentColor = palette[0];
      const chassis = new THREE.Group();
      chassis.name = "kartChassis";

      const bodyMaterial = new THREE.MeshToonMaterial({ color: accentColor });
      const darkMaterial = new THREE.MeshToonMaterial({ color: 0x252a32 });
      const trimMaterial = new THREE.MeshToonMaterial({ color: 0x353e4c });

      const body = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(1.9, 0.6, 3.2), bodyMaterial);
      body.position.y = 0.25;
      chassis.add(body);

      const nose = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(1.5, 0.45, 0.8), bodyMaterial);
      nose.position.set(0, 0.12, 1.9);
      chassis.add(nose);

      const bumper = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(1.8, 0.22, 0.25), darkMaterial);
      bumper.position.set(0, 0.05, 2.2);
      chassis.add(bumper);

      const cockpit = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(1.35, 0.35, 1.5), darkMaterial);
      cockpit.position.set(0, 0.62, -0.15);
      chassis.add(cockpit);

      const engine = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(1.1, 0.28, 0.55), trimMaterial);
      engine.position.set(0, 0.18, -1.75);
      chassis.add(engine);

      const spoilerL = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.15, 0.6, 0.15), trimMaterial);
      spoilerL.position.set(-0.6, 0.5, -1.4);
      chassis.add(spoilerL);
      const spoilerR = spoilerL.clone();
      spoilerR.position.x = 0.6;
      chassis.add(spoilerR);

      const wing = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(1.6, 0.1, 0.45), bodyMaterial);
      wing.position.set(0, 0.85, -1.95);
      chassis.add(wing);

      const wheelRadius = getDrivePhysicsNumber("wheelRadius", 0.52);
      const wheelWidth = Math.max(0.24, wheelRadius * 0.86);
      const wheels = [
        createKartWheelMesh(wheelRadius, wheelWidth, accentColor),
        createKartWheelMesh(wheelRadius, wheelWidth, accentColor),
        createKartWheelMesh(wheelRadius, wheelWidth, accentColor),
        createKartWheelMesh(wheelRadius, wheelWidth, accentColor),
      ];
      wheels.forEach((wheel, index) => {
        wheel.name = "kartWheel" + String(index);
      });

      return {
        chassis,
        wheels,
        wheelNodeMap: ["kartWheel0", "kartWheel1", "kartWheel2", "kartWheel3"],
        wheelsAreChildren: false,
        frontWheelGroup: null,
        frontWheelNodes: [wheels[0], wheels[1]],
        wheelBaseRotations: wheels.map((wheel) => wheel ? wheel.rotation.clone() : null),
        wheelBaseQuaternions: wheels.map((wheel) => wheel ? wheel.quaternion.clone() : null),
        visualAlignment: null,
        visualYawOffsetRad: 0,
        modelSource: "procedural",
        palette,
        bodyMaterial,
      };
    }

    function getWheelIndexFromName(name) {
      const lower = String(name || "").toLowerCase();
      const indexedMatch = lower.match(/(?:^|[^a-z0-9])wheel[_-]?([0-3])(?:[^a-z0-9]|$)/);
      if (indexedMatch) {
        return clamp(Number(indexedMatch[1]), 0, 3);
      }
      if (lower === "wheel" || lower.endsWith("_wheel")) {
        return -2;
      }
      return -1;
    }

    function detectKartWheelMeshes(root) {
      const indexed = [null, null, null, null];
      const generic = [];
      if (!root || typeof root.traverse !== "function") {
        return indexed;
      }
      root.traverse((obj) => {
        if (!obj || !obj.isMesh) {
          return;
        }
        const idx = getWheelIndexFromName(obj.name);
        if (idx >= 0 && idx <= 3) {
          if (!indexed[idx]) {
            indexed[idx] = obj;
          }
          return;
        }
        if (idx === -2 || String(obj.name || "").toLowerCase().includes("wheel")) {
          generic.push(obj);
        }
      });

      if (generic.length > 0) {
        let next = 0;
        for (let i = 0; i < indexed.length; i += 1) {
          if (!indexed[i] && generic[next]) {
            indexed[i] = generic[next];
            next += 1;
          }
        }
      }
      return indexed;
    }

    function computeKartBoundsIgnoringWheels(root, wheels) {
      const fallback = new THREE.Box3().setFromObject(root);
      if (!root || typeof root.traverse !== "function") {
        return fallback;
      }
      const wheelSet = new Set((Array.isArray(wheels) ? wheels : []).filter(Boolean));
      const box = new THREE.Box3();
      let has = false;
      root.traverse((obj) => {
        if (!obj || !obj.isMesh || wheelSet.has(obj)) {
          return;
        }
        const geom = obj.geometry;
        if (!geom) {
          return;
        }
        if (!geom.boundingBox) {
          geom.computeBoundingBox();
        }
        if (!geom.boundingBox) {
          return;
        }
        const worldBox = geom.boundingBox.clone().applyMatrix4(obj.matrixWorld);
        if (!has) {
          box.copy(worldBox);
          has = true;
        } else {
          box.union(worldBox);
        }
      });
      return has ? box : fallback;
    }

    function computeKartAlignment(chassis, wheels) {
      const alignment = {
        scale: 1,
        eulerDeg: { x: 0, y: 0, z: 0 },
        localOffset: { x: 0, y: 0, z: 0 },
      };
      if (!chassis) {
        return alignment;
      }
      chassis.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      const localWheelPoints = (Array.isArray(wheels) ? wheels : [])
        .map((wheel) => {
          if (!wheel) {
            return null;
          }
          const world = new THREE.Vector3();
          wheel.getWorldPosition(world);
          return chassis.worldToLocal(world.clone());
        })
        .filter(Boolean);

      // Solve one-time visual orientation so kart stays upright in runtime.
      // This keeps driving logic yaw-only while correcting authoring-axis skew.
      if (localWheelPoints.length === 4) {
        const p0 = localWheelPoints[0];
        const p1 = localWheelPoints[1];
        const p2 = localWheelPoints[2];
        const p3 = localWheelPoints[3];
        const front = p0.clone().add(p1).multiplyScalar(0.5);
        const rear = p2.clone().add(p3).multiplyScalar(0.5);
        const left = p0.clone().add(p2).multiplyScalar(0.5);
        const right = p1.clone().add(p3).multiplyScalar(0.5);

        const forwardAxis = front.sub(rear);
        const rightAxis = right.sub(left);
        if (forwardAxis.lengthSq() > 1e-10 && rightAxis.lengthSq() > 1e-10) {
          forwardAxis.normalize();
          rightAxis.normalize();

          let upAxis = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(forwardAxis, rightAxis);
          if (upAxis.lengthSq() > 1e-10) {
            upAxis.normalize();
            if (upAxis.y < 0) {
              upAxis.multiplyScalar(-1);
              rightAxis.multiplyScalar(-1);
            }

            // Re-orthonormalize basis.
            rightAxis.addScaledVector(upAxis, -rightAxis.dot(upAxis));
            if (rightAxis.lengthSq() > 1e-10) {
              rightAxis.normalize();
            }
            const correctedForward = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(rightAxis, upAxis).normalize();
            if (correctedForward.lengthSq() > 1e-10) {
              const modelBasis = new THREE.Matrix4().makeBasis(rightAxis, upAxis, correctedForward);
              const qModel = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromRotationMatrix(modelBasis);
              const qAlign = qModel.clone().invert();
              chassis.quaternion.premultiply(qAlign);
              const alignEuler = new THREE.Euler().setFromQuaternion(qAlign, "XYZ");
              alignment.eulerDeg = {
                x: Number(toDeg(alignEuler.x).toFixed(3)),
                y: Number(toDeg(alignEuler.y).toFixed(3)),
                z: Number(toDeg(alignEuler.z).toFixed(3)),
              };
            }
          }
        }
      }

      const manualRotXDeg = getDriveModelNumber("alignRotXDeg", 0);
      const manualRotYDeg = getDriveModelNumber("alignRotYDeg", 0);
      const manualRotZDeg = getDriveModelNumber("alignRotZDeg", 0);
      if (
        Math.abs(manualRotXDeg) > 1e-6 ||
        Math.abs(manualRotYDeg) > 1e-6 ||
        Math.abs(manualRotZDeg) > 1e-6
      ) {
        const manualQ = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromEuler(
          new THREE.Euler(toRad(manualRotXDeg), toRad(manualRotYDeg), toRad(manualRotZDeg), "XYZ")
        );
        chassis.quaternion.premultiply(manualQ);
      }

      chassis.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      const boxBefore = computeKartBoundsIgnoringWheels(chassis, wheels);
      const sizeBefore = new THREE.Vector3();
      boxBefore.getSize(sizeBefore);

      let preferredScale = Number.NaN;

      if (getDriveModelBoolean("preferWheelbaseScale", false) && localWheelPoints.length === 4) {
        const front = localWheelPoints[0].clone().add(localWheelPoints[1]).multiplyScalar(0.5);
        const rear = localWheelPoints[2].clone().add(localWheelPoints[3]).multiplyScalar(0.5);
        const wheelbaseM = Math.hypot(front.x - rear.x, front.z - rear.z);
        if (Number.isFinite(wheelbaseM) && wheelbaseM > 0.05) {
          const targetWheelbaseM = clamp(getDriveModelNumber("targetWheelbaseM", 1.85), 1.4, 4.5);
          preferredScale = targetWheelbaseM / wheelbaseM;
        }
      }

      if (!Number.isFinite(preferredScale)) {
        const horizontalLength = Math.max(
          Number(sizeBefore.x) || 0,
          Number(sizeBefore.z) || 0
        );
        if (Number.isFinite(horizontalLength) && horizontalLength > 0.01) {
          const targetLengthM = clamp(getDriveModelNumber("targetLengthM", 3.2), 1.8, 7.5);
          preferredScale = targetLengthM / horizontalLength;
        }
      }

      if (Number.isFinite(preferredScale) && preferredScale > 0) {
        const trimScale = clamp(getDriveModelNumber("scaleMultiplier", 0.72), 0.25, 2.5);
        const scale = clamp(preferredScale * trimScale, 0.1, 12);
        chassis.scale.multiplyScalar(scale);
        alignment.scale = scale;
      }

      chassis.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      const boxAfter = computeKartBoundsIgnoringWheels(chassis, wheels);
      const centerAfter = new THREE.Vector3();
      boxAfter.getCenter(centerAfter);
      const baseHeight = Math.max(0.1, getDrivePhysicsNumber("mk3BaseHeightM", 0.92));
      const targetBottomY = -baseHeight;
      const offsetX = -centerAfter.x;
      const offsetY = targetBottomY - boxAfter.min.y;
      const offsetZ = -centerAfter.z;

      alignment.localOffset = {
        x: Number(offsetX) || 0,
        y: Number(offsetY) || 0,
        z: Number(offsetZ) || 0,
      };
      return alignment;
    }

    async function prepareKartModelTemplate() {
      if (!state.kart) {
        return false;
      }
      if (state.kart.modelTemplate) {
        return true;
      }
      if (state.kart.modelLoadPromise) {
        return state.kart.modelLoadPromise;
      }
      state.kart.modelLoadPromise = (async () => {
        const LoaderClass = await loadGLTFLoaderClass();
        const DracoLoaderClass = await loadDracoLoaderClass();
        const loader = new LoaderClass();
        if (typeof loader.setCrossOrigin === "function") {
          loader.setCrossOrigin("anonymous");
        }
        let dracoLoader = null;
        if (DracoLoaderClass && typeof loader.setDRACOLoader === "function") {
          try {
            dracoLoader = new DracoLoaderClass();
            if (typeof dracoLoader.setDecoderPath === "function") {
              dracoLoader.setDecoderPath("https://www.gstatic.com/draco/v1/decoders/");
            }
            if (typeof dracoLoader.preload === "function") {
              try {
                dracoLoader.preload();
              } catch (_error) {
                // no-op
              }
            }
            loader.setDRACOLoader(dracoLoader);
            debugLog("kart:draco_enabled", { decoderPath: "https://www.gstatic.com/draco/v1/decoders/" });
          } catch (error) {
            debugLog("kart:draco_unavailable", {
              message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
            });
          }
        } else {
          debugLog("kart:draco_unavailable", { message: "module_missing" });
        }
        const fetchArrayBufferWithTimeout = async (url, timeoutMs) => {
          const timeout = Math.max(500, Number(timeoutMs) || 2500);
          const controller = typeof AbortController === "function" ? new AbortController() : null;
          let timer = null;
          if (controller) {
            timer = setTimeout(() => {
              try {
                controller.abort();
              } catch (_error) {
                // no-op
              }
            }, timeout);
          }
          const decodeArrayBufferFromSupResponse = async (response) => {
            if (!response) {
              return null;
            }
            if (response.ok === false) {
              return null;
            }
            if (typeof response.arrayBuffer === "function") {
              return await response.arrayBuffer();
            }
            if (typeof response.bytes === "function") {
              const bytes = await response.bytes();
              if (bytes && bytes.buffer) {
                return bytes.buffer;
              }
            }
            if (typeof response.text === "function") {
              const text = await response.text();
              if (typeof text === "string" && text.length > 0) {
                return new TextEncoder().encode(text).buffer;
              }
            }
            if (response.data && response.data instanceof ArrayBuffer) {
              return response.data;
            }
            if (response.body && response.body instanceof ArrayBuffer) {
              return response.body;
            }
            return null;
          };
          const trySupFetchArrayBuffer = async (rawUrl) => {
            if (!(window.sup && typeof window.sup.fetch === "function")) {
              return null;
            }
            const localCandidates = [];
            const seen = new Set();
            const push = (value) => {
              const normalized = normalizeAssetPath(value);
              if (!normalized) {
                return;
              }
              const key = normalized.toLowerCase();
              if (seen.has(key)) {
                return;
              }
              seen.add(key);
              localCandidates.push(normalized);
            };
            const normalized = normalizeAssetPath(rawUrl);
            const stripped = trimLeadingSlashes(normalized.replace(/^\\.\\//, ""));
            if (!/^(https?:|data:|blob:|file:)/i.test(normalized)) {
              push(normalized);
              push(stripped);
              push("./" + stripped);
              if (stripped && !stripped.startsWith("patch_assets/")) {
                push("patch_assets/" + stripped);
                push("./patch_assets/" + stripped);
              }
            }
            for (const candidate of localCandidates) {
              try {
                const maybe = await Promise.resolve(
                  window.sup.fetch(candidate, {
                    method: "GET",
                    cache: "no-store",
                  })
                );
                const buffer = await decodeArrayBufferFromSupResponse(maybe);
                if (buffer && buffer.byteLength > 0) {
                  debugLog("kart:asset_sup_fetch_ok", { path: candidate, bytes: buffer.byteLength });
                  return buffer;
                }
              } catch (_error) {
                // continue
              }
            }
            return null;
          };
          try {
            let response = null;
            let fetchError = null;
            try {
              response = await fetch(url, {
                credentials: "omit",
                cache: "no-store",
                signal: controller ? controller.signal : undefined,
              });
            } catch (error) {
              fetchError = error;
            }
            if (response && response.ok) {
              return await response.arrayBuffer();
            }
            const supBuffer = await trySupFetchArrayBuffer(url);
            if (supBuffer && supBuffer.byteLength > 0) {
              return supBuffer;
            }
            if (response && !response.ok) {
              throw new Error("http_" + String(response ? response.status : 0));
            }
            if (fetchError) {
              throw fetchError;
            }
            throw new Error("fetch_failed");
          } finally {
            if (timer) {
              clearTimeout(timer);
            }
          }
        };
        const parseBufferAsGltf = (buffer, url) =>
          new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            let resourcePath = "";
            try {
              const parsedUrl = new URL(url);
              const pathname = parsedUrl.pathname || "/";
              parsedUrl.pathname = pathname.endsWith("/") ? pathname : pathname.replace(/[^/]+$/, "");
              resourcePath = parsedUrl.toString();
            } catch (_error) {
              resourcePath = "";
            }
            loader.parse(buffer, resourcePath, resolve, reject);
          });
        const candidates = getKartModelCandidatePaths();
        debugLog("kart:asset_candidates", {
          count: candidates.length,
          first: candidates.slice(0, 6),
        });
        let lastError = "";
        for (const pathCandidate of candidates) {
          try {
            const buffer = await fetchArrayBufferWithTimeout(pathCandidate, 3600);
            const gltf = await parseBufferAsGltf(buffer, pathCandidate);
            const template = gltf && gltf.scene ? gltf.scene : null;
            if (template) {
              state.kart.modelTemplate = template;
              state.kart.modelTemplatePath = pathCandidate;
              state.kart.modelLoadError = "";
              debugLog("kart:asset_resolved", { path: pathCandidate });
              return true;
            }
            lastError = "missing_scene";
          } catch (error) {
            lastError = error && error.message ? error.message : String(error);
            debugLog("kart:asset_candidate_failed", {
              path: pathCandidate,
              message: lastError,
            });
          }
        }
        if (dracoLoader && typeof dracoLoader.dispose === "function") {
          try {
            dracoLoader.dispose();
          } catch (_error) {
            // no-op
          }
        }
        state.kart.modelTemplate = null;
        state.kart.modelTemplatePath = "";
        state.kart.modelLoadError = lastError || "no_candidate_loaded";
        debugLog("kart:asset_fallback", {
          reason: state.kart.modelLoadError,
          candidates: candidates.length,
        });
        return false;
      })()
        .catch((error) => {
          state.kart.modelTemplate = null;
          state.kart.modelTemplatePath = "";
          state.kart.modelLoadError = error && error.message ? error.message : String(error);
          debugLog("kart:asset_fallback", {
            reason: state.kart.modelLoadError,
            candidates: getKartModelCandidatePaths().length,
          });
          return false;
        })
        .finally(() => {
          state.kart.modelLoadPromise = null;
        });
      return state.kart.modelLoadPromise;
    }

    function createKartVisualMeshFromTemplate() {
      const palette = [0xff0000, 0x00aa00, 0x0066ff, 0xffdd00, 0xff66aa, 0xff6600];
      const sourceRoot = cloneKartTemplateScene();
      if (!sourceRoot) {
        return null;
      }
      sourceRoot.name = "kartChassis";
      sourceRoot.updateMatrixWorld(true);

      const bodyMaterial = forceKartToonMaterials(sourceRoot, palette[0]) || new THREE.MeshToonMaterial({ color: palette[0] });
      const hideShapeMesh = getDriveModelBoolean("hideShapeMesh", false);
      if (hideShapeMesh) {
        sourceRoot.traverse((obj) => {
          if (!obj || !obj.isMesh) {
            return;
          }
          const key = String(obj.name || "").toLowerCase();
          if (key === "shape") {
            obj.visible = false;
          }
