        });
      }

      const objectByName = new Map();
      sourceRoot.traverse((obj) => {
        if (obj && obj.name) {
          const key = String(obj.name).toLowerCase();
          if (!objectByName.has(key)) {
            objectByName.set(key, obj);
          }
        }
      });
      const pick = (name) => objectByName.get(String(name).toLowerCase()) || null;
      const strictWheels = [
        pick("wheel_0"),
        pick("wheel_1"),
        pick("wheel_2"),
        pick("wheel_3"),
      ];
      const wheels = strictWheels.slice();
      const wheel0 = wheels[0] || null;
      const wheel1 = wheels[1] || null;
      const wheel2 = wheels[2] || null;
      const wheel3 = wheels[3] || null;

      const visualAlignment = computeKartAlignment(sourceRoot, wheels);
      sourceRoot.updateMatrixWorld(true);

      let visualYawOffsetRad = toRad(getDriveModelNumber("yawOffsetDeg", 0));
      if (getDriveModelBoolean("autoYawFromWheels", false) && wheel0 && wheel1 && wheel2 && wheel3) {
        const p0 = sourceRoot.worldToLocal(wheel0.getWorldPosition(new THREE.Vector3()));
        const p1 = sourceRoot.worldToLocal(wheel1.getWorldPosition(new THREE.Vector3()));
        const p2 = sourceRoot.worldToLocal(wheel2.getWorldPosition(new THREE.Vector3()));
        const p3 = sourceRoot.worldToLocal(wheel3.getWorldPosition(new THREE.Vector3()));
        const front = p0.clone().add(p1).multiplyScalar(0.5);
        const rear = p2.clone().add(p3).multiplyScalar(0.5);
        const forward = front.sub(rear);
        if (forward.lengthSq() > 1e-8) {
          visualYawOffsetRad = forward.z >= 0 ? 0 : Math.PI;
        }
      }

      const mappedCount = wheels.filter((wheel) => !!wheel).length;
      if (mappedCount < 4) {
        debugLog("kart:wheels_missing", {
          mapped: mappedCount,
          expected: 4,
          mode: "strict_names_only",
          path: state.kart.modelTemplatePath || "unknown",
        });
      }
      debugLog("kart:wheel_visual_mode", {
        mode: "mk3_direct_scene",
        mapped: mappedCount,
        scale:
          visualAlignment && Number.isFinite(Number(visualAlignment.scale))
            ? Number(Number(visualAlignment.scale).toFixed(4))
            : null,
      });
      if (visualAlignment) {
        debugLog("kart:alignment_solved", {
          scale:
            Number.isFinite(Number(visualAlignment.scale))
              ? Number(Number(visualAlignment.scale).toFixed(4))
              : null,
          eulerDeg: visualAlignment.eulerDeg || null,
          offset: visualAlignment.localOffset || null,
        });
      }

      return {
        chassis: sourceRoot,
        wheels,
        wheelNodeMap: ["wheel_0", "wheel_1", "wheel_2", "wheel_3"],
        wheelsAreChildren: true,
        frontWheelGroup: null,
        frontWheelNodes: [wheel0, wheel1],
        wheelBaseRotations: wheels.map((wheel) => (wheel ? wheel.rotation.clone() : null)),
        wheelBaseQuaternions: wheels.map((wheel) => (wheel ? wheel.quaternion.clone() : null)),
        visualAlignment: visualAlignment || null,
        visualYawOffsetRad,
        animateWheels: getDriveModelBoolean("animateWheels", false),
        modelSource: "mk3",
        palette,
        bodyMaterial,
      };
    }

    async function createKartVisualMesh() {
      const loaded = await prepareKartModelTemplate();
      if (loaded) {
        const view = createKartVisualMeshFromTemplate();
        if (view) {
          return view;
        }
      }
      return createProceduralKartVisualMesh();
    }

    function buildDriveFrame(anchorLng, anchorLat) {
      const terrainAtAnchor = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(anchorLng, anchorLat);
      const geoidFallback = sampleGeoidOffsetM(anchorLng, anchorLat, "");
      const anchorHeight = Number.isFinite(terrainAtAnchor)
        ? terrainAtAnchor
        : (Number.isFinite(geoidFallback) ? geoidFallback : 0);
      const originECEF = lonLatToECEF(anchorLng, anchorLat, anchorHeight);
      const up = originECEF.clone().normalize();
      const east = new THREE.Vector3(-Math.sin(toRad(anchorLng)), Math.cos(toRad(anchorLng)), 0).normalize();
      const north = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(up, east).normalize();
      const frameBasis = new THREE.Matrix4().makeBasis(east, up, north);
      const frameQuat = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromRotationMatrix(frameBasis);
      return {
        anchorLng,
        anchorLat,
        anchorHeight,
        originECEF,
        east,
        north,
        up,
        frameQuat,
      };
    }

    function ensureDriveFrame() {
      if (state.driveSpawn.frame) {
        return state.driveSpawn.frame;
      }
      state.driveSpawn.frame = buildDriveFrame(state.driveSpawn.anchorLng, state.driveSpawn.anchorLat);
      return state.driveSpawn.frame;
    }

    function ecefToDriveLocal(ecefVec) {
      const frame = ensureDriveFrame();
      const delta = ecefVec.clone().sub(frame.originECEF);
      return new THREE.Vector3(
        delta.dot(frame.east),
        delta.dot(frame.up),
        delta.dot(frame.north)
      );
    }

    function driveLocalToECEF(localVec) {
      const frame = ensureDriveFrame();
      return frame.originECEF
        .clone()
        .addScaledVector(frame.east, localVec.x)
        .addScaledVector(frame.up, localVec.y)
        .addScaledVector(frame.north, localVec.z);
    }

    function driveLocalToLonLat(localVec) {
      return ecefToLonLat(driveLocalToECEF(localVec));
    }

    function lonLatToDriveLocal(lng, lat, altitudeM) {
      return ecefToDriveLocal(lonLatToECEF(lng, lat, altitudeM));
    }

    function lonLatToPlanarMeters(lng, lat, refLng, refLat) {
      const kx = 111320 * Math.cos(toRad(refLat));
      const ky = 110540;
      return {
        x: (lng - refLng) * kx,
        y: (lat - refLat) * ky,
      };
    }

    function planarMetersToLonLat(x, y, refLng, refLat) {
      const kx = 111320 * Math.cos(toRad(refLat));
      const ky = 110540;
      return {
        lng: refLng + (kx !== 0 ? x / kx : 0),
        lat: refLat + (ky !== 0 ? y / ky : 0),
      };
    }

    function nearestPointOnSegment2D(px, py, ax, ay, bx, by) {
      const abx = bx - ax;
      const aby = by - ay;
      const apx = px - ax;
      const apy = py - ay;
      const denom = abx * abx + aby * aby;
      const tRaw = denom > 1e-9 ? (apx * abx + apy * aby) / denom : 0;
      const t = clamp(tRaw, 0, 1);
      const qx = ax + abx * t;
      const qy = ay + aby * t;
      const dx = px - qx;
      const dy = py - qy;
      return {
        x: qx,
        y: qy,
        t,
        distanceM: Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy),
        tangentX: abx,
        tangentY: aby,
      };
    }

    function collectTransportRoadFeatures() {
      const manager = state.transportManager;
      if (!manager || !(manager.tiles instanceof Map) || manager.tiles.size <= 0) {
        return [];
      }
      const features = [];
      for (const tile of manager.tiles.values()) {
        if (!tile || !Array.isArray(tile.features) || tile.features.length <= 0) {
          continue;
        }
        for (const feature of tile.features) {
          if (!feature || !Array.isArray(feature.coordinates) || feature.coordinates.length < 2) {
            continue;
          }
          if (feature.featureClass !== "road") {
            continue;
          }
          features.push(feature);
        }
      }
      return features;
    }

    function findNearestRoadPoint(lng, lat, maxDistanceM) {
      const roads = collectTransportRoadFeatures();
      if (roads.length <= 0) {
        return null;
      }
      const limitM = Number.isFinite(maxDistanceM) ? maxDistanceM : 220;
      const refLng = lng;
      const refLat = lat;
      const p = lonLatToPlanarMeters(lng, lat, refLng, refLat);
      let best = null;

      for (const feature of roads) {
        const coords = feature.coordinates;
        for (let i = 0; i < coords.length - 1; i += 1) {
          const a = coords[i];
          const b = coords[i + 1];
          if (!Array.isArray(a) || !Array.isArray(b) || a.length < 2 || b.length < 2) {
            continue;
          }
          const aM = lonLatToPlanarMeters(Number(a[0]), Number(a[1]), refLng, refLat);
          const bM = lonLatToPlanarMeters(Number(b[0]), Number(b[1]), refLng, refLat);
          const nearest = nearestPointOnSegment2D(p.x, p.y, aM.x, aM.y, bM.x, bM.y);
          if (!Number.isFinite(nearest.distanceM) || nearest.distanceM > limitM) {
            continue;
          }
          if (!best || nearest.distanceM < best.distanceM) {
            const ll = planarMetersToLonLat(nearest.x, nearest.y, refLng, refLat);
            const headingRad = Math.atan2(nearest.tangentX, nearest.tangentY);
            best = {
              lng: ll.lng,
              lat: ll.lat,
              headingRad,
              distanceM: nearest.distanceM,
            };
          }
        }
      }
      return best;
    }

    function applyKartPose(lng, lat, headingRad, sourceLabel, persistAsReset) {
      const kart = state.kart;
      if (!kart) {
        return false;
      }
      const engine = getDriveEngine();
      const terrainH = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(lng, lat);
      const fallbackH = sampleGeoidOffsetM(lng, lat, "");
      const baseHeightM = engine === "mk3_kinematic"
        ? getDrivePhysicsNumber("mk3BaseHeightM", 0.92)
        : 1.35;
      const altitudeM = Number.isFinite(terrainH)
        ? terrainH + baseHeightM
        : (Number.isFinite(fallbackH) ? fallbackH + baseHeightM : baseHeightM);
      const localPos = lonLatToDriveLocal(lng, lat, altitudeM);

      if (engine === "mk3_kinematic") {
        if (kart.kinematic && kart.kinematic.positionLocal) {
          kart.kinematic.positionLocal.copy(localPos);
          kart.kinematic.yawRad = headingRad;
          kart.kinematic.speedMps = 0;
          kart.kinematic.steerValue = 0;
          kart.kinematic.turnInput = 0;
          kart.kinematic.wheelSpinRad = 0;
          kart.kinematic.verticalVelocity = 0;
          kart.kinematic.jumpOffsetM = 0;
          kart.kinematic.groundFilteredY = localPos.y;
        }
      } else {
        const chassisBody = kart.chassisBody;
        if (!chassisBody) {
          return false;
        }
        chassisBody.position.set(localPos.x, localPos.y, localPos.z);
        chassisBody.velocity.set(0, 0, 0);
        chassisBody.angularVelocity.set(0, 0, 0);
        chassisBody.quaternion.setFromAxisAngle(new CANNON.Vec3(0, 1, 0), headingRad);
        if (typeof chassisBody.wakeUp === "function") {
          chassisBody.wakeUp();
        }
        for (const wheelBody of kart.wheelBodies || []) {
          if (!wheelBody) {
            continue;
          }
          wheelBody.velocity.set(0, 0, 0);
          wheelBody.angularVelocity.set(0, 0, 0);
          if (typeof wheelBody.wakeUp === "function") {
            wheelBody.wakeUp();
          }
        }
      }
      kart.controls.jumpCount = 0;
      kart.controls.isGrounded = true;
      kart.speedKmh = 0;
      kart.visualPoseInitialized = false;
      kart.spawnLabel = sourceLabel || "fallback_anchor";
      kart.spawnApplied = true;
      state.driveSpawn.fallbackPose = { lng, lat, headingRad };
      if (persistAsReset) {
        state.driveSpawn.resetPose = { lng, lat, headingRad };
      }
      return true;
    }

    function resolveKartSpawn(force) {
      const nowMs = Date.now();
      if (!force && nowMs - state.driveSpawn.lastSnapAttemptMs < state.driveSpawn.retryIntervalMs) {
        return false;
      }
      state.driveSpawn.lastSnapAttemptMs = nowMs;
      const anchorLng = state.driveSpawn.anchorLng;
      const anchorLat = state.driveSpawn.anchorLat;
      const preferFixedSpawn = getDriveSpawnBoolean("preferFixed", true);
      const fixedHeadingRad = toRad(getDriveSpawnNumber("headingDeg", 82));

      if (preferFixedSpawn) {
        const applied = applyKartPose(anchorLng, anchorLat, fixedHeadingRad, "tokyo_station_plaza", true);
        if (applied) {
          state.driveSpawn.converged = true;
          state.driveSpawn.snapped = {
            lng: anchorLng,
            lat: anchorLat,
            headingRad: fixedHeadingRad,
            distanceM: 0,
          };
          debugLog("kart:spawn_fixed_plaza", {
            lng: Number(anchorLng.toFixed(6)),
            lat: Number(anchorLat.toFixed(6)),
            headingDeg: Number((fixedHeadingRad * 180 / Math.PI).toFixed(1)),
          });
        }
        return applied;
      }
      const snapped = findNearestRoadPoint(anchorLng, anchorLat, 240);
      if (snapped) {
        state.driveSpawn.converged = true;
        state.driveSpawn.snapped = { ...snapped };
        state.driveSpawn.resetPose = { lng: snapped.lng, lat: snapped.lat, headingRad: snapped.headingRad };
        const applied = applyKartPose(snapped.lng, snapped.lat, snapped.headingRad, "tokyo_station_street", true);
        if (applied) {
          debugLog("kart:spawn_snap_ok", {
            lng: Number(snapped.lng.toFixed(6)),
            lat: Number(snapped.lat.toFixed(6)),
            distanceM: Number(snapped.distanceM.toFixed(2)),
          });
        }
        return applied;
      }

      // Ensure road tiles near the fixed spawn anchor are requested even if camera is elsewhere.
      try {
        const manager = buildTransportManager();
        const zoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : 14;
        const center = lonLatToSlippy(anchorLng, anchorLat, zoom);
        const maxIndex = Math.pow(2, zoom) - 1;
        for (let dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy += 1) {
          for (let dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx += 1) {
            const tx = clamp(center.x + dx, 0, maxIndex);
            const ty = clamp(center.y + dy, 0, maxIndex);
            loadTransportTile(zoom, tx, ty).catch(() => {
              // no-op
            });
          }
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }

      if (!state.kart.spawnApplied || force) {
        const fallbackHeading = toRad(90);
        const applied = applyKartPose(anchorLng, anchorLat, fallbackHeading, "fallback_anchor", !state.driveSpawn.resetPose);
        if (applied) {
          debugLog("kart:spawn_fallback", {
            lng: Number(anchorLng.toFixed(6)),
            lat: Number(anchorLat.toFixed(6)),
          });
        }
        return applied;
      }
      return false;
    }

    function cycleKartColor() {
      const kart = state.kart;
      if (!kart || !kart.ready || !Array.isArray(kart.palette) || kart.palette.length <= 0) {
        return;
      }
      kart.colorIndex = (kart.colorIndex + 1) % kart.palette.length;
      const color = kart.palette[kart.colorIndex];
      if (kart.bodyMaterial && kart.bodyMaterial.color) {
        kart.bodyMaterial.color.setHex(color);
      }
    }

    function getKartForwardDirection() {
      const kart = state.kart;
      if (!kart || !kart.chassisMesh) {
        return new THREE.Vector3(0, 0, 1);
      }
      if (getDriveEngine() === "mk3_kinematic" && kart.kinematic) {
        const frame = ensureDriveFrame();
        const yaw = Number(kart.kinematic.yawRad) || 0;
        const localForward = new THREE.Vector3(Math.sin(yaw), 0, Math.cos(yaw));
        const world = frame.east.clone().multiplyScalar(localForward.x).addScaledVector(frame.north, localForward.z);
        if (world.lengthSq() > 1e-10) {
          return world.normalize();
        }
      }
      const frame = ensureDriveFrame();
      const forward = new THREE.Vector3(0, 0, 1).applyQuaternion(kart.chassisMesh.quaternion);
      forward.addScaledVector(frame.up, -forward.dot(frame.up));
      if (forward.lengthSq() <= 1e-10) {
        return frame.north.clone();
      }
      return forward.normalize();
    }

    function applyKartBoost() {
      const kart = state.kart;
      if (!kart || !kart.ready) {
        return;
      }
      if (getDriveEngine() === "mk3_kinematic") {
        const boostImpulse = getDrivePhysicsNumber("boostImpulse", 95);
        const boostMps = clamp(boostImpulse * 0.08, 1.5, 20);
        const current = kart.kinematic && Number.isFinite(kart.kinematic.speedMps) ? kart.kinematic.speedMps : 0;
        const maxRoadSpeed = Math.max(4, getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxRoadSpeedMps", 24));
        if (kart.kinematic) {
          kart.kinematic.speedMps = clamp(current + boostMps, -maxRoadSpeed * 0.5, maxRoadSpeed * 1.25);
        }
        return;
      }
      if (!kart.chassisBody) {
        return;
      }
      const frame = ensureDriveFrame();
      const forwardWorld = getKartForwardDirection();
      const forwardLocal = new THREE.Vector3(
        forwardWorld.dot(frame.east),
        forwardWorld.dot(frame.up),
        forwardWorld.dot(frame.north)
      );
      const boostImpulse = getDrivePhysicsNumber("boostImpulse", 95);
      kart.chassisBody.applyImpulse(
        new CANNON.Vec3(forwardLocal.x * boostImpulse, 0, forwardLocal.z * boostImpulse),
        new CANNON.Vec3(0, 0, 0)
      );
    }

    function tryKartJump() {
      const kart = state.kart;
      if (!kart || !kart.ready) {
        return;
      }
      const maxJumps = Math.max(1, Math.round(getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxJumps", 2)));
      if (kart.controls.jumpCount >= maxJumps) {
        return;
      }
      const impulse = getDrivePhysicsNumber("jumpImpulse", 38);
      if (getDriveEngine() === "mk3_kinematic") {
        if (!kart.controls.isGrounded && kart.controls.jumpCount >= 1) {
          return;
        }
        if (kart.kinematic) {
          kart.kinematic.verticalVelocity = Math.max(kart.kinematic.verticalVelocity, impulse * 0.15);
        }
      } else if (kart.chassisBody) {
        kart.chassisBody.applyImpulse(new CANNON.Vec3(0, impulse, 0), new CANNON.Vec3(0, 0, 0));
      } else {
        return;
      }
      kart.controls.jumpCount += 1;
      kart.controls.isGrounded = false;
    }

    function resetKartPose() {
      const pose = state.driveSpawn.resetPose || state.driveSpawn.fallbackPose;
      if (!pose) {
        resolveKartSpawn(true);
        return;
      }
      applyKartPose(pose.lng, pose.lat, pose.headingRad, state.kart.spawnLabel || "reset_pose", true);
      debugLog("kart:reset", { source: state.kart.spawnLabel || "reset_pose" });
    }

    function applyKartDriveInput() {
      const kart = state.kart;
      if (!kart || !kart.ready || !kart.vehicle) {
        return;
      }
      const roadScale = kart.roadContact ? 1 : 0.72;
      const maxForce = getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxForce", 52) * roadScale;
      const reverseScale = getDrivePhysicsNumber("reverseForceScale", 0.42);
      const maxSteerVal = getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxSteerVal", 0.58);

      let driveForce = 0;
      if (state.keys.KeyW || state.keys.ArrowUp) {
        driveForce = maxForce;
      } else if (state.keys.KeyS || state.keys.ArrowDown) {
        driveForce = -maxForce * reverseScale;
      }
      // Rear-wheel drive.
      kart.vehicle.setWheelForce(driveForce, 2);
      kart.vehicle.setWheelForce(driveForce, 3);

      let steer = 0;
      if (state.keys.KeyA || state.keys.ArrowLeft) {
        steer = maxSteerVal;
      } else if (state.keys.KeyD || state.keys.ArrowRight) {
        steer = -maxSteerVal;
      }
      // Front-wheel steering.
      kart.vehicle.setSteeringValue(steer, 0);
      kart.vehicle.setSteeringValue(steer, 1);
    }

    function updateKartRuntimeKinematic(deltaSec) {
      const kart = state.kart;
      if (!kart || !kart.ready || !kart.kinematic) {
        return;
      }
      const dt = clamp(Number(deltaSec) || 0, 0, 0.05);
      if (dt <= 0) {
        return;
      }

      const roadScale = kart.roadContact ? 1 : 0.9;
      const maxRoadSpeed = Math.max(4, getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxRoadSpeedMps", 24));
      const maxOffroadSpeed = Math.max(3, getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxOffroadSpeedMps", 16));
      const reverseScale = getDrivePhysicsNumber("reverseForceScale", 0.42);
      const speedCap = (kart.roadContact ? maxRoadSpeed : maxOffroadSpeed) * roadScale;

      const forwardPressed = !!(state.keys.KeyW || state.keys.ArrowUp);
      const reversePressed = !!(state.keys.KeyS || state.keys.ArrowDown);
      const accelMps2 = Math.max(1, getDrivePhysicsNumber("mk3AccelMps2", 30));
      const brakeMps2 = Math.max(1, getDrivePhysicsNumber("mk3BrakeMps2", 34));
      const coastDragMps2 = Math.max(0.5, getDrivePhysicsNumber("mk3CoastDragMps2", 10));

      if (forwardPressed && !reversePressed) {
        kart.kinematic.speedMps += accelMps2 * dt;
      } else if (reversePressed && !forwardPressed) {
        kart.kinematic.speedMps -= brakeMps2 * dt;
      } else {
        const dragStep = coastDragMps2 * dt;
        if (kart.kinematic.speedMps > 0) {
          kart.kinematic.speedMps = Math.max(0, kart.kinematic.speedMps - dragStep);
        } else if (kart.kinematic.speedMps < 0) {
          kart.kinematic.speedMps = Math.min(0, kart.kinematic.speedMps + dragStep);
        }
      }
      const maxReverseSpeed = speedCap * reverseScale;
      kart.kinematic.speedMps = clamp(kart.kinematic.speedMps, -maxReverseSpeed, speedCap);

      let turnInput = 0;
      if (state.keys.KeyA || state.keys.ArrowLeft) {
        turnInput -= 1;
      }
      if (state.keys.KeyD || state.keys.ArrowRight) {
        turnInput += 1;
      }
      kart.kinematic.turnInput = turnInput;

      const steerTarget = turnInput * getDrivePhysicsNumber("mk3SteerAngle", 0.8);
      const steerLerp = getDrivePhysicsNumber("mk3TurnLerp", 10);
      kart.kinematic.steerValue = dampScalar(kart.kinematic.steerValue, steerTarget, steerLerp, dt);

      const speedNorm = clamp(Math.abs(kart.kinematic.speedMps) / Math.max(1, speedCap), 0, 1);
      const yawRate = getDrivePhysicsNumber("mk3YawRate", 2.4);
      const directionSign = kart.kinematic.speedMps < 0 ? -1 : 1;
      const lowSpeedTurnFactor = kart.kinematic.speedMps === 0 ? 0 : 0.28;
      const steerFactor = lowSpeedTurnFactor + (1 - lowSpeedTurnFactor) * speedNorm;
      kart.kinematic.yawRad += kart.kinematic.steerValue * yawRate * steerFactor * dt * directionSign;

      const forwardX = Math.sin(kart.kinematic.yawRad);
      const forwardZ = Math.cos(kart.kinematic.yawRad);
      kart.kinematic.positionLocal.x += forwardX * kart.kinematic.speedMps * dt;
      kart.kinematic.positionLocal.z += forwardZ * kart.kinematic.speedMps * dt;

      const gravity = Math.max(1, getDrivePhysicsNumber("worldGravity", 9.82));
      kart.kinematic.verticalVelocity -= gravity * dt;
      kart.kinematic.jumpOffsetM = Math.max(0, kart.kinematic.jumpOffsetM + kart.kinematic.verticalVelocity * dt);
      if (kart.kinematic.jumpOffsetM <= 0) {
        kart.kinematic.jumpOffsetM = 0;
        kart.kinematic.verticalVelocity = 0;
      }

      const wheelSpinFactor = getDrivePhysicsNumber("mk3WheelSpinFactor", 0.08);
      kart.kinematic.wheelSpinRad += kart.kinematic.speedMps * wheelSpinFactor * dt;

      kart.speedKmh = Math.abs(kart.kinematic.speedMps) * 3.6;
    }

    function updateKartRoadContact(nowMs) {
      const kart = state.kart;
      if (!kart || !kart.ready) {
        return;
      }
      if (nowMs - kart.lastRoadCheckMs < kart.roadCheckIntervalMs) {
        return;
      }
      kart.lastRoadCheckMs = nowMs;
      const engine = getDriveEngine();
      const local =
        engine === "mk3_kinematic"
          ? (kart.kinematic && kart.kinematic.positionLocal ? kart.kinematic.positionLocal.clone() : null)
          : (kart.chassisBody
            ? new THREE.Vector3(kart.chassisBody.position.x, kart.chassisBody.position.y, kart.chassisBody.position.z)
            : null);
      if (!local) {
        return;
      }
      const llh = driveLocalToLonLat(local);
      if (!llh || !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) || !Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) {
        kart.roadContact = false;
        return;
      }
      const roadContactRadiusM = Math.max(4, getDrivePhysicsNumber("mk3RoadContactRadiusM", 14));
      const nearest = findNearestRoadPoint(llh.lng, llh.lat, Math.max(roadContactRadiusM + 8, 18));
      kart.roadContact = !!(nearest && nearest.distanceM <= roadContactRadiusM);
      kart.roadContactDistanceM = nearest ? nearest.distanceM : Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY;
    }

    function applyKartGroundClamp(deltaSec) {
      const kart = state.kart;
      if (!kart || !kart.ready) {
        return;
      }
      const engine = getDriveEngine();
      const localPos =
        engine === "mk3_kinematic"
          ? (kart.kinematic && kart.kinematic.positionLocal ? kart.kinematic.positionLocal : null)
          : (kart.chassisBody
            ? new THREE.Vector3(kart.chassisBody.position.x, kart.chassisBody.position.y, kart.chassisBody.position.z)
            : null);
      if (!localPos) {
        return;
      }
      const llh = driveLocalToLonLat(localPos);
      if (!llh || !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) || !Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) {
        return;
      }
      const terrainH = getTerrainHeightAtLonLat(llh.lng, llh.lat);
      if (!Number.isFinite(terrainH)) {
        return;
      }
      const terrainLocal = lonLatToDriveLocal(llh.lng, llh.lat, terrainH);
      const clearance = getDrivePhysicsNumber("terrainClearanceM", 0.08);
      const minY = terrainLocal.y + clearance;
      const clampStrength = clamp(getDrivePhysicsNumber("terrainClampStrength", 0.65), 0.05, 1);

      if (engine === "mk3_kinematic") {
        if (!kart.kinematic || !kart.kinematic.positionLocal) {
          return;
        }
        const dt = Math.max(0, Number(deltaSec) || 0);
        const jumpOffset = Math.max(0, kart.kinematic.jumpOffsetM || 0);
        const baseHeight = getDrivePhysicsNumber("mk3BaseHeightM", 0.92);
        const targetY = minY + baseHeight + jumpOffset;
        const groundFollowLerp = clamp(getDrivePhysicsNumber("terrainClampStrength", 0.65) * 22, 6, 28);
        if (!Number.isFinite(kart.kinematic.groundFilteredY)) {
          kart.kinematic.groundFilteredY = targetY;
        }
        if (jumpOffset > 0.001) {
          kart.kinematic.groundFilteredY = targetY;
          kart.kinematic.positionLocal.y = targetY;
        } else {
          kart.kinematic.groundFilteredY = dampScalar(kart.kinematic.groundFilteredY, targetY, 9, dt);
          kart.kinematic.positionLocal.y = dampScalar(
            kart.kinematic.positionLocal.y,
            kart.kinematic.groundFilteredY,
            groundFollowLerp,
            dt
          );
        }
        if (jumpOffset <= 0.001) {
          const groundGap = Math.abs(kart.kinematic.positionLocal.y - kart.kinematic.groundFilteredY);
          kart.controls.isGrounded = groundGap <= 0.05;
          if (kart.controls.isGrounded) {
            kart.controls.jumpCount = 0;
          }
          kart.kinematic.verticalVelocity = Math.max(0, kart.kinematic.verticalVelocity || 0);
        } else {
          kart.controls.isGrounded = false;
        }
        if (kart.controls.isGrounded && dt > 0) {
          kart.kinematic.verticalVelocity = 0;
        }
      } else {
        if (!kart.chassisBody) {
          return;
        }
        if (kart.chassisBody.position.y < minY) {
          kart.chassisBody.position.y = kart.chassisBody.position.y + (minY - kart.chassisBody.position.y) * clampStrength;
          if (kart.chassisBody.velocity.y < 0) {
            kart.chassisBody.velocity.y = 0;
          }
          kart.controls.isGrounded = true;
          kart.controls.jumpCount = 0;
        } else {
          const distanceAbove = kart.chassisBody.position.y - minY;
          kart.controls.isGrounded = distanceAbove <= 0.18 && Math.abs(kart.chassisBody.velocity.y) <= 0.9;
          if (kart.controls.isGrounded) {
            kart.controls.jumpCount = 0;
          }
        }
      }
    }

    function getKartWheelFallbackLocal(index) {
      switch (index) {
        case 0:
          return new THREE.Vector3(-1.0, -0.55, 1.2);
        case 1:
          return new THREE.Vector3(1.0, -0.55, 1.2);
        case 2:
          return new THREE.Vector3(-1.0, -0.55, -1.0);
        case 3:
          return new THREE.Vector3(1.0, -0.55, -1.0);
        default:
          return new THREE.Vector3(0, -0.55, 0);
      }
    }

    function stabilizeKartPhysics(deltaSec) {
      const kart = state.kart;
      if (!kart || !kart.ready || !kart.chassisBody) {
        return;
      }
      const body = kart.chassisBody;
      const maxRoadSpeed = Math.max(4, getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxRoadSpeedMps", 24));
      const maxOffroadSpeed = Math.max(3, getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxOffroadSpeedMps", 16));
      const maxVerticalSpeed = Math.max(4, getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxVerticalSpeedMps", 16));
      const maxAngularSpeed = Math.max(1, getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxAngularSpeedRad", 5.5));
      const maxSpeed = kart.roadContact ? maxRoadSpeed : maxOffroadSpeed;

      const vx = Number(body.velocity.x) || 0;
      const vz = Number(body.velocity.z) || 0;
      const horizSpeed = Math.sqrt(vx * vx + vz * vz);
      if (horizSpeed > maxSpeed && horizSpeed > 1e-6) {
        const s = maxSpeed / horizSpeed;
        body.velocity.x *= s;
        body.velocity.z *= s;
      }
      body.velocity.y = clamp(body.velocity.y, -maxVerticalSpeed, maxVerticalSpeed);

      const avx = Number(body.angularVelocity.x) || 0;
      const avy = Number(body.angularVelocity.y) || 0;
      const avz = Number(body.angularVelocity.z) || 0;
      const angSpeed = Math.sqrt(avx * avx + avy * avy + avz * avz);
      if (angSpeed > maxAngularSpeed && angSpeed > 1e-6) {
        const s = maxAngularSpeed / angSpeed;
        body.angularVelocity.x *= s;
        body.angularVelocity.y *= s;
        body.angularVelocity.z *= s;
      }

      // Apply mild upright stabilization so the kart recovers instead of tumbling forever.
      const up = body.quaternion.vmult(new CANNON.Vec3(0, 1, 0));
      const uprightTorque = Math.max(0, getDrivePhysicsNumber("uprightTorque", 10));
      if (uprightTorque > 0 && Number.isFinite(up.x) && Number.isFinite(up.y) && Number.isFinite(up.z) && up.y < 0.995) {
        const torqueX = -up.z * uprightTorque * deltaSec;
        const torqueZ = up.x * uprightTorque * deltaSec;
        body.angularVelocity.x += torqueX;
        body.angularVelocity.z += torqueZ;
      }
    }

    function syncKartVisualFromPhysics() {
      const kart = state.kart;
      if (!kart || !kart.ready || !kart.chassisMesh) {
        return;
      }
      const engine = getDriveEngine();
      const frame = ensureDriveFrame();
      let chassisLocal = null;
      let qLocal = null;
      if (engine === "mk3_kinematic") {
        if (!kart.kinematic || !kart.kinematic.positionLocal) {
          return;
        }
        chassisLocal = kart.kinematic.positionLocal.clone();
        qLocal = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromAxisAngle(
          new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0),
          Number(kart.kinematic.yawRad) || 0
        );
      } else {
        if (!kart.chassisBody) {
          return;
        }
        chassisLocal = new THREE.Vector3(
          kart.chassisBody.position.x,
          kart.chassisBody.position.y,
          kart.chassisBody.position.z
        );
        qLocal = new THREE.Quaternion(
          kart.chassisBody.quaternion.x,
          kart.chassisBody.quaternion.y,
          kart.chassisBody.quaternion.z,
          kart.chassisBody.quaternion.w
        );
      }
      const chassisECEF = driveLocalToECEF(chassisLocal);
      const worldQuat = frame.frameQuat.clone().multiply(qLocal);
      if (Number.isFinite(kart.visualYawOffsetRad) && Math.abs(kart.visualYawOffsetRad) > 1e-6) {
        const yawOffset = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromAxisAngle(frame.up, kart.visualYawOffsetRad);
        worldQuat.multiply(yawOffset);
      }
      const worldPos = chassisECEF.clone();
      if (kart.visualAlignment && kart.visualAlignment.localOffset) {
        const localOffset = kart.visualAlignment.localOffset;
        const offsetVec = new THREE.Vector3(
          Number(localOffset.x) || 0,
          Number(localOffset.y) || 0,
          Number(localOffset.z) || 0
        );
        if (offsetVec.lengthSq() > 1e-10) {
          offsetVec.applyQuaternion(worldQuat);
          worldPos.add(offsetVec);
        }
      }

      if (engine === "mk3_kinematic") {
        const poseLerp = state.driveMode ? 0.28 : 0.38;
        if (kart.visualPoseInitialized) {
          kart.chassisMesh.position.lerp(worldPos, poseLerp);
          kart.chassisMesh.quaternion.slerp(worldQuat, poseLerp);
        } else {
          kart.chassisMesh.position.copy(worldPos);
          kart.chassisMesh.quaternion.copy(worldQuat);
          kart.visualPoseInitialized = true;
        }
        if (kart.animateWheels !== false) {
          const spin = kart.kinematic ? Number(kart.kinematic.wheelSpinRad) || 0 : 0;
          const steer = kart.kinematic ? Number(kart.kinematic.steerValue) || 0 : 0;
          for (let i = 0; i < kart.wheelMeshes.length; i += 1) {
            const wheel = kart.wheelMeshes[i];
            if (!wheel) {
              continue;
            }
            const baseQuat = Array.isArray(kart.wheelBaseQuaternions) ? kart.wheelBaseQuaternions[i] : null;
            const baseRot = Array.isArray(kart.wheelBaseRotations) ? kart.wheelBaseRotations[i] : null;
            const isFront = i === 0 || i === 1;
            if (baseQuat) {
              wheel.quaternion.copy(baseQuat);
              if (isFront && Math.abs(steer) > 1e-8) {
                wheel.rotateY(steer);
              }
              if (Math.abs(spin) > 1e-8) {
                wheel.rotateX(spin);
              }
            } else {
              const baseX = baseRot && Number.isFinite(baseRot.x) ? baseRot.x : 0;
              const baseY = baseRot && Number.isFinite(baseRot.y) ? baseRot.y : 0;
              const baseZ = baseRot && Number.isFinite(baseRot.z) ? baseRot.z : 0;
              wheel.rotation.set(baseX + spin, baseY + (isFront ? steer : 0), baseZ);
            }
          }
        }
        kart.speedKmh = Math.abs(kart.kinematic ? kart.kinematic.speedMps : 0) * 3.6;
        return;
      }

      kart.chassisMesh.position.copy(worldPos);
      kart.chassisMesh.quaternion.copy(worldQuat);

      for (let i = 0; i < kart.wheelMeshes.length; i += 1) {
        const wheelMesh = kart.wheelMeshes[i];
        const wheelBody = kart.wheelBodies[i];
        if (!wheelMesh) {
          continue;
        }
        const useProceduralFallback = kart.modelSource === "procedural";
        let wheelLocal = null;
        let wheelQuatLocal = null;
        if (wheelBody) {
          wheelLocal = new THREE.Vector3(wheelBody.position.x, wheelBody.position.y, wheelBody.position.z);
          const offset = wheelLocal.clone().sub(chassisLocal);
          if (useProceduralFallback && offset.lengthSq() > 40) {
            wheelLocal = chassisLocal.clone().add(getKartWheelFallbackLocal(i));
            wheelQuatLocal = qLocal;
          }
        } else if (useProceduralFallback) {
          wheelLocal = chassisLocal.clone().add(getKartWheelFallbackLocal(i));
          wheelQuatLocal = qLocal;
        } else {
          continue;
        }

        wheelMesh.position.copy(driveLocalToECEF(wheelLocal));
        if (!wheelQuatLocal && wheelBody) {
          wheelQuatLocal = new THREE.Quaternion(
            wheelBody.quaternion.x,
            wheelBody.quaternion.y,
            wheelBody.quaternion.z,
            wheelBody.quaternion.w
          );
        }
        wheelMesh.quaternion.copy(frame.frameQuat.clone().multiply(wheelQuatLocal || qLocal));
      }

      const v = kart.chassisBody.velocity;
      kart.speedKmh = Math.sqrt(v.x * v.x + v.y * v.y + v.z * v.z) * 3.6;
    }

    function updateDriveCamera(forceSnap) {
      if (!state.driveMode || !state.kart || !state.kart.ready || !state.camera || !state.kart.chassisMesh) {
        return;
      }
      const frame = ensureDriveFrame();
      const target = state.kart.chassisMesh.position;
      const forward = getKartForwardDirection();
      const distance = getDriveCameraNumber("distance", 10.5);
      const height = getDriveCameraNumber("height", 4.2);
      const smoothness = clamp(getDriveCameraNumber("smoothness", 0.12), 0.01, 1);
      const lookAhead = getDriveCameraNumber("lookAheadDistance", 4.5);
      const upWorld = frame.up;

      const desiredPos = target.clone()
        .addScaledVector(forward, -distance)
        .addScaledVector(upWorld, height);
      if (forceSnap) {
        state.camera.position.copy(desiredPos);
      } else {
        state.camera.position.lerp(desiredPos, smoothness);
      }

      const lookTarget = target.clone()
        .addScaledVector(forward, lookAhead)
        .addScaledVector(upWorld, 1.0);
      if (forceSnap) {
        state.driveCamera.currentLookAt.copy(lookTarget);
      } else {
        state.driveCamera.currentLookAt.lerp(lookTarget, Math.min(1, smoothness * 1.5));
      }

      const driveFov = getDriveCameraNumber("fov", 68);
      if (Number.isFinite(driveFov) && Math.abs(state.camera.fov - driveFov) > 0.01) {
        state.camera.fov = driveFov;
        state.camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
      }

      state.camera.up.copy(upWorld);
      state.camera.lookAt(state.driveCamera.currentLookAt);
    }

    async function setDriveMode(enabled) {
      const next = !!enabled;
      if (state.driveMode === next) {
        if (next && state.kart && state.kart.pendingDriveToggle && state.kart.ready) {
          state.kart.pendingDriveToggle = false;
        }
        return true;
      }
      if (next) {
        state.kart.pendingDriveToggle = true;
      }
      const engine = getDriveEngine();
      if (next && engine === "cannon" && (!state.cannon || !state.cannon.module)) {
        setStatus("Loading kart physics module...", "ok");
        try {
          await ensureCannonModuleLoaded();
        } catch (error) {
          const message = error && error.message ? error.message : String(error);
          state.kart.pendingDriveToggle = false;
          setStatus("Kart mode unavailable: physics module failed (" + message + ").", "error");
          debugLog("kart:mode_toggle_denied", { reason: "cannon_load_failed", message });
          return false;
        }
      }
      if (next && (!state.kart || !state.kart.ready)) {
        const ok = await initKartRuntime();
        if (!ok) {
          state.kart.pendingDriveToggle = false;
          setStatus("Kart mode unavailable. Physics module or spawn not ready yet.", "error");
          debugLog("kart:mode_toggle_denied", { reason: "kart_not_ready" });
          return false;
        }
      }
      state.driveMode = next;
      state.kart.pendingDriveToggle = false;
      state.keys = {};
      state.looking = false;
      state.driveCamera.active = next;
      if (next) {
        if (typeof document.exitPointerLock === "function") {
          try {
            document.exitPointerLock();
          } catch (_error) {
            // no-op
          }
        }
        updateDriveCamera(true);
        setStatus("Kart mode enabled (G to exit).", "ok");
      } else {
        if (state.camera && Math.abs(state.camera.fov - 60) > 0.01) {
          state.camera.fov = 60;
          state.camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
        }
        syncYawPitchFromCamera();
        setStatus("Fly mode enabled (G for kart).", "ok");
      }
      debugLog("kart:mode_toggle", { mode: next ? "drive" : "fly" });
      return true;
    }

    async function initKartRuntime() {
      if (state.kart.ready) {
        return true;
      }
      if (state.kart.initializingPromise) {
        return state.kart.initializingPromise;
      }
      state.kart.initializingPromise = (async () => {
        const engineType = getDriveEngine();
        state.kart.engine = engineType;
        if (engineType === "cannon" && !CANNON) {
          state.cannon.ready = false;
          state.cannon.error = "module_unavailable";
          debugLog("kart:init_fail", { reason: "cannon_missing" });
          return false;
        }
        try {
          const view = await createKartVisualMesh();
          state.kart.group = view.chassis;
          state.kart.visualRoot = view.chassis;
          state.kart.chassisMesh = view.chassis;
          state.kart.wheelMeshes = Array.isArray(view.wheels) ? view.wheels : [];
          state.kart.wheelNodeMap = Array.isArray(view.wheelNodeMap) ? view.wheelNodeMap : [];
          state.kart.wheelsAreChildren = !!view.wheelsAreChildren;
          state.kart.frontWheelGroup = view.frontWheelGroup || null;
          state.kart.frontWheelNodes = Array.isArray(view.frontWheelNodes) ? view.frontWheelNodes : [];
          state.kart.wheelBaseRotations = Array.isArray(view.wheelBaseRotations) ? view.wheelBaseRotations : [];
          state.kart.wheelBaseQuaternions = Array.isArray(view.wheelBaseQuaternions) ? view.wheelBaseQuaternions : [];
          state.kart.animateWheels = view.animateWheels !== false;
          state.kart.visualAlignment = view.visualAlignment || null;
          state.kart.visualYawOffsetRad = Number.isFinite(Number(view.visualYawOffsetRad))
            ? Number(view.visualYawOffsetRad)
            : 0;
          state.kart.modelSource = view.modelSource || "procedural";
          state.kart.visualReady = true;
          state.kart.palette = view.palette;
          state.kart.bodyMaterial = view.bodyMaterial;
          state.scene.add(view.chassis);
          if (!state.kart.wheelsAreChildren) {
            for (const wheel of state.kart.wheelMeshes) {
              if (wheel) {
                state.scene.add(wheel);
              }
            }
          }

          state.kart.chassisBody = null;
          state.kart.wheelBodies = [];
          state.kart.vehicle = null;
          if (engineType === "cannon") {
            const world = new CANNON.World();
            world.gravity.set(0, -Math.abs(getDrivePhysicsNumber("worldGravity", 9.82)), 0);
            world.broadphase = new CANNON.SAPBroadphase(world);
            world.solver.iterations = 10;
            state.cannon.world = world;
            state.cannon.ready = true;
            state.cannon.error = "";

            const wheelMaterial = new CANNON.Material("kartWheel");
            const groundMaterial = new CANNON.Material("kartGround");
            const contact = new CANNON.ContactMaterial(wheelMaterial, groundMaterial, {
              friction: getDrivePhysicsNumber("contactFriction", 1.0),
              restitution: getDrivePhysicsNumber("contactRestitution", 0.01),
            });
            world.addContactMaterial(contact);
            world.defaultContactMaterial = contact;

            const COLLISION_GROUP_GROUND = 1;
            const COLLISION_GROUP_CHASSIS = 2;
            const COLLISION_GROUP_WHEEL = 4;

            const groundBody = new CANNON.Body({ mass: 0, material: groundMaterial });
            groundBody.addShape(new CANNON.Plane());
            groundBody.quaternion.setFromEuler(-Math.PI / 2, 0, 0);
            groundBody.collisionFilterGroup = COLLISION_GROUP_GROUND;
            groundBody.collisionFilterMask = COLLISION_GROUP_CHASSIS | COLLISION_GROUP_WHEEL;
            world.addBody(groundBody);

            const chassisShape = new CANNON.Box(new CANNON.Vec3(1.05, 0.35, 1.65));
            const chassisBody = new CANNON.Body({
              mass: getDrivePhysicsNumber("chassisMass", 16),
              shape: chassisShape,
            });
            chassisBody.allowSleep = false;
            chassisBody.shapeOffsets[0] = new CANNON.Vec3(0, -0.2, 0);
            chassisBody.linearDamping = getDrivePhysicsNumber("chassisLinearDamping", 0.38);
            chassisBody.angularDamping = getDrivePhysicsNumber("chassisAngularDamping", 0.82);
            chassisBody.collisionFilterGroup = COLLISION_GROUP_CHASSIS;
            chassisBody.collisionFilterMask = COLLISION_GROUP_GROUND;

            chassisBody.addShape(new CANNON.Box(new CANNON.Vec3(0.75, 0.22, 0.45)), new CANNON.Vec3(0, -0.18, 1.9));
            chassisBody.addShape(new CANNON.Box(new CANNON.Vec3(0.9, 0.12, 0.18)), new CANNON.Vec3(0, -0.35, 2.2));
            chassisBody.addShape(new CANNON.Box(new CANNON.Vec3(0.55, 0.14, 0.28)), new CANNON.Vec3(0, -0.25, -1.75));
            chassisBody.addShape(new CANNON.Box(new CANNON.Vec3(0.8, 0.05, 0.23)), new CANNON.Vec3(0, 0.35, -1.95));

            const vehicle = new CANNON.RigidVehicle({ chassisBody });
            const wheelRadius = getDrivePhysicsNumber("wheelRadius", 0.52);
            const wheelMass = getDrivePhysicsNumber("wheelMass", 1.0);
            const down = new CANNON.Vec3(0, -1, 0);
            const axle = new CANNON.Vec3(1, 0, 0);
            const wheelPositions = [
              { x: -1.0, y: -0.55, z: 1.2 },
              { x: 1.0, y: -0.55, z: 1.2 },
              { x: -1.0, y: -0.55, z: -1.0 },
              { x: 1.0, y: -0.55, z: -1.0 },
            ];
            const wheelBodies = [];
            for (const pos of wheelPositions) {
              const wheelBody = new CANNON.Body({ mass: wheelMass, material: wheelMaterial });
              wheelBody.addShape(new CANNON.Sphere(wheelRadius));
              wheelBody.allowSleep = false;
              wheelBody.linearDamping = getDrivePhysicsNumber("wheelLinearDamping", 0.3);
              wheelBody.angularDamping = getDrivePhysicsNumber("wheelAngularDamping", 0.5);
              wheelBody.collisionFilterGroup = COLLISION_GROUP_WHEEL;
              wheelBody.collisionFilterMask = COLLISION_GROUP_GROUND;
              vehicle.addWheel({
                body: wheelBody,
                position: new CANNON.Vec3(pos.x, pos.y, pos.z),
                axis: axle,
                direction: down,
              });
              wheelBodies.push(wheelBody);
            }
            vehicle.addToWorld(world);
            state.kart.chassisBody = chassisBody;
            state.kart.wheelBodies = wheelBodies;
            state.kart.vehicle = vehicle;
          } else {
            state.cannon.world = null;
            state.kart.kinematic.positionLocal.set(0, 0, 0);
            state.kart.kinematic.yawRad = 0;
            state.kart.kinematic.speedMps = 0;
            state.kart.kinematic.steerValue = 0;
            state.kart.kinematic.turnInput = 0;
            state.kart.kinematic.wheelSpinRad = 0;
            state.kart.kinematic.verticalVelocity = 0;
            state.kart.kinematic.jumpOffsetM = 0;
            state.kart.kinematic.groundFilteredY = Number.NaN;
          }

          state.kart.controls.maxSteerVal = getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxSteerVal", 0.58);
          state.kart.controls.maxForce = getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxForce", 52);
          state.kart.controls.reverseForceScale = getDrivePhysicsNumber("reverseForceScale", 0.42);
          state.kart.controls.jumpImpulse = getDrivePhysicsNumber("jumpImpulse", 38);
          state.kart.controls.boostImpulse = getDrivePhysicsNumber("boostImpulse", 95);
          state.kart.controls.maxJumps = Math.max(1, Math.round(getDrivePhysicsNumber("maxJumps", 2)));
          state.kart.controls.jumpCount = 0;
          state.kart.controls.isGrounded = true;
          state.kart.ready = true;

          resolveKartSpawn(true);
          syncKartVisualFromPhysics();
          debugLog("kart:init_ok", {
            spawnAnchor: {
              lng: Number(state.driveSpawn.anchorLng.toFixed(6)),
              lat: Number(state.driveSpawn.anchorLat.toFixed(6)),
            },
            engine: engineType,
            modelSource: state.kart.modelSource,
            wheelMap: state.kart.wheelNodeMap,
          });
          return true;
        } catch (error) {
          if (state.kart.chassisMesh && state.kart.chassisMesh.parent) {
            state.kart.chassisMesh.parent.remove(state.kart.chassisMesh);
          }
          if (Array.isArray(state.kart.wheelMeshes)) {
            for (const wheel of state.kart.wheelMeshes) {
              if (wheel && wheel.parent) {
                wheel.parent.remove(wheel);
              }
            }
          }
          state.kart.ready = false;
          state.kart.group = null;
          state.kart.visualRoot = null;
          state.kart.chassisMesh = null;
          state.kart.wheelMeshes = [];
          state.kart.wheelNodeMap = [];
          state.kart.wheelsAreChildren = false;
          state.kart.frontWheelGroup = null;
          state.kart.frontWheelNodes = [];
          state.kart.wheelBaseRotations = [];
          state.kart.wheelBaseQuaternions = [];
          state.kart.visualAlignment = null;
          state.kart.visualYawOffsetRad = 0;
          state.kart.visualReady = false;
          state.kart.chassisBody = null;
          state.kart.wheelBodies = [];
          state.kart.vehicle = null;
          state.kart.engine = "pending";
          state.cannon.world = null;
          state.cannon.error = error && error.message ? error.message : "kart_init_failed";
          if (engineType === "cannon") {
            state.cannon.ready = false;
          }
          debugLog("kart:init_fail", { engine: engineType, message: state.cannon.error });
          return false;
        }
      })().finally(() => {
        state.kart.initializingPromise = null;
      });
      return state.kart.initializingPromise;
    }

    function updateKartRuntime(deltaSec, nowMs) {
      if (!state.kart || !state.kart.ready) {
        return;
      }
      const engine = getDriveEngine();
      updateKartRoadContact(nowMs);
      if (engine === "mk3_kinematic") {
        updateKartRuntimeKinematic(deltaSec);
        applyKartGroundClamp(deltaSec);
      } else {
        if (!state.cannon || !state.cannon.world) {
          return;
        }
        const world = state.cannon.world;
        state.cannon.accumulatorSec += deltaSec;
        const maxSubSteps = 4;
        const fixedStep = state.cannon.fixedStepSec;

        applyKartDriveInput();
        if (state.kart.chassisBody) {
          const damping = state.kart.roadContact
            ? getDrivePhysicsNumber("roadGripDamping", 0.24)
            : getDrivePhysicsNumber("offroadDragDamping", 0.38);
          state.kart.chassisBody.linearDamping = clamp(damping, 0.05, 0.95);
        }

        let steps = 0;
        while (state.cannon.accumulatorSec >= fixedStep && steps < maxSubSteps) {
          world.step(fixedStep);
          state.cannon.accumulatorSec -= fixedStep;
          steps += 1;
        }
        applyKartGroundClamp(deltaSec);
        stabilizeKartPhysics(deltaSec);
      }

      if (!state.driveSpawn.converged && Math.abs(state.kart.speedKmh) < 1.2) {
        resolveKartSpawn(false);
      }

      syncKartVisualFromPhysics();
      if (state.driveMode) {
        updateDriveCamera(false);
      }
    }

    function transportTileRelevantToActiveWards(tileBounds, _cameraLLH) {
      if (!tileBounds) {
        return false;
      }
      const activeWardBounds = getActiveWardBounds();
      if (!Array.isArray(activeWardBounds) || activeWardBounds.length <= 0) {
        return false;
      }
      const tileCenterLng = (Number(tileBounds.west) + Number(tileBounds.east)) * 0.5;
      const tileCenterLat = (Number(tileBounds.south) + Number(tileBounds.north)) * 0.5;
      return isWithinAnyBounds(tileCenterLng, tileCenterLat, activeWardBounds);
    }

    function scheduleTransportTiles(nowMs) {
      const manager = buildTransportManager();
      if (!state.camera) {
        return;
      }
      if (nowMs - manager.lastTickMs < manager.requestIntervalMs) {
        return;
      }
      manager.lastTickMs = nowMs;
      const llh = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
      if (!llh || !Number.isFinite(llh.lng) || !Number.isFinite(llh.lat)) {
        return;
      }
      if (!isWithinBounds(llh.lng, llh.lat, TOKYO23 && TOKYO23.bounds ? TOKYO23.bounds : null)) {
        return;
      }
      manager.lastCameraAltitudeM = Number.isFinite(llh.altitudeM) ? Number(llh.altitudeM) : 0;
      const desiredRenderState = resolveTransportRoadRenderState(manager);
      manager.renderModeActive = desiredRenderState.mode;
      manager.renderModeReason = desiredRenderState.reason;
      manager.laneMeshQuality = desiredRenderState.quality;
      if (desiredRenderState.mode !== manager.renderBuildMode) {
        const now = Number(nowMs) || Date.now();
        const lastSwitch = Number(manager.renderBuildModeSwitchMs) || 0;
        if (now - lastSwitch >= 1800) {
          for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
            evictTransportTile(tile, "render_mode_change");
          }
          manager.desired.clear();
          manager.renderBuildMode = desiredRenderState.mode;
          manager.renderBuildModeSwitchMs = now;
          manager.renderBuildGeneration = (Number(manager.renderBuildGeneration) || 0) + 1;
          debugLog("transport:render_mode_changed", {
            mode: desiredRenderState.mode,
            reason: desiredRenderState.reason,
            generation: manager.renderBuildGeneration,
          });
        }
      }
      const suggestedZoom = chooseTransportZoom(llh.altitudeM, manager.currentZoom);
      const transportZoomLevels = getTileIndexZoomLevels(
        TRANSPORT_MANIFEST && TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.tileIndex && typeof TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.tileIndex === "object"
          ? TRANSPORT_MANIFEST.tileIndex
          : null
      );
      const constrainedZoom = constrainZoomToAvailableLevels(suggestedZoom, transportZoomLevels);
      const previousZoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : null;
      manager.currentZoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : constrainedZoom;
      if (constrainedZoom !== manager.currentZoom) {
        manager.currentZoom = constrainedZoom;
        for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
          if (!tile || tile.z === constrainedZoom) continue;
          evictTransportTile(tile, "zoom_change");
        }
        manager.desired.clear();
        debugLog("transport:zoom_changed", {
          from: previousZoom,
          to: constrainedZoom,
        });
      }
      const simplifyProfile = chooseTransportSimplifyProfile(
        Number.isFinite(llh.altitudeM) ? llh.altitudeM : 0,
        !!state.driveMode
      );
      manager.simplifyProfileKey = simplifyProfile.key;
      manager.simplifyToleranceM = simplifyProfile.toleranceM;
      const zoom = Number.isFinite(manager.currentZoom) ? manager.currentZoom : constrainedZoom;
      const center = lonLatToSlippy(llh.lng, llh.lat, zoom);
      const radius = state.driveMode ? 2 : 1;
      const pendingCap = state.driveMode ? 10 : 6;
      const desired = new Set();
      const maxIndex = Math.pow(2, zoom) - 1;
      for (let dy = -radius; dy <= radius; dy += 1) {
        for (let dx = -radius; dx <= radius; dx += 1) {
          if (desired.size >= manager.maxActiveTiles) {
            continue;
          }
          const tx = clamp(center.x + dx, 0, maxIndex);
          const ty = clamp(center.y + dy, 0, maxIndex);
          const tileBounds = slippyBounds(tx, ty, zoom);
          if (!transportTileRelevantToActiveWards(tileBounds, llh)) {
            continue;
          }
          const key = String(zoom) + "/" + String(tx) + "/" + String(ty);
          desired.add(key);
          const existing = manager.tiles.get(key);
          if (existing) {
            existing.lastWantedMs = nowMs;
            continue;
          }
          if (manager.pending.size >= pendingCap) {
            continue;
          }
          loadTransportTile(zoom, tx, ty).catch((error) => {
            debugLog("transport:tile_async_error", {
              key,
              message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
            });
          });
        }
      }
      manager.desired = desired;
      for (const tile of Array.from(manager.tiles.values())) {
        if (desired.has(tile.key)) {
          continue;
        }
        if (nowMs - (tile.lastWantedMs || 0) >= manager.hysteresisMs) {
          evictTransportTile(tile, "outside_desired");
        }
      }
    }

    function disposeOldTiles() {
      debugLog("tiles:dispose_old");
      state.noVisibleTilesSinceMs = 0;

      try {
        if (state.tiles && state.tiles.group && state.tiles.group.parent) {
          state.tiles.group.parent.remove(state.tiles.group);
        }
      } catch (_error) {
        // no-op
      }

      state.tiles = null;
      state.materialOriginal = new WeakMap();
      state.mirroredModelIds = new Set();
      state.mirrorClonesByModelId = new Map();
      state.mirrorClonesByTileKey = new Map();
      state.localGeoEnabled = false;
      state.localGeoFrame = "none";
      state.localGeoMedianPosNorm = 0;
      state.localGeoAnchor.set(0, 0, 0);
      state.localGeoQuat.identity();
      state.localGeoMatrix.identity();
      state.useMirrorFallback = false;
      if (state.mirrorGroup) {
        while (state.mirrorGroup.children.length > 0) {
          const child = state.mirrorGroup.children.pop();
          if (child && child.parent) {
            child.parent.remove(child);
          }
        }
      }
      if (!state.tilesManager || !state.tilesManager.enabled) {
        if (state.transportManager) {
          clearTransportManager();
        }
        if (state.transitLayerManager) {
          clearTransitLayerManager();
        }
        if (state.transitRealtimeManager) {
          clearRealtimeTransitManager();
        }
        if (state.streetLayerManager) {
          clearStreetLayerManager();
        }
        if (state.parkLayerManager) {
          clearParkLayerManager();
        }
        if (state.waterLayerManager) {
          clearWaterLayerManager();
        }
        if (state.trafficManager) {
          clearTrafficManager();
        }
      }
    }

    async function initTiles(tilesetUrl) {
      debugLog("tiles:init_start", { tilesetUrl });
      disposeOldTiles();

      state.tileProgress = {
        knownTiles: 0,
        loadedModels: 0,
        failedModels: 0,
        seenModelIds: new Set(),
        lastLoggedPercent: -1,
        lastLoggedMs: 0,
        firstModelFocused: false,
        needsAutoFocusCheck: false,
        noModelWarningLogged: false,
        tileInitAtMs: Date.now(),
      };

      const tilesMod = await loadTilesModule();
      debugLog("tiles:module_loaded_keys", Object.keys(tilesMod || {}));
      const TilesRendererClass =
        tilesMod.TilesRenderer ||
        (tilesMod.default && tilesMod.default.TilesRenderer) ||
        tilesMod.default;

      if (!TilesRendererClass) {
        throw new Error("TilesRenderer class missing in loaded module.");
      }

      const tiles = new TilesRendererClass(tilesetUrl);
      tiles.setCamera(state.camera);
      tiles.setResolutionFromRenderer(state.camera, state.renderer);

      const pluginsMod = await loadTilesPluginsModule();
      if (!pluginsMod || typeof tiles.registerPlugin !== "function") {
        throw new Error("GLTFExtensionsPlugin missing; CESIUM_RTC support is required.");
      }
      const GLTFExtensionsPluginClass =
        pluginsMod.GLTFExtensionsPlugin ||
        (pluginsMod.default && pluginsMod.default.GLTFExtensionsPlugin);
      if (!GLTFExtensionsPluginClass) {
        throw new Error("GLTFExtensionsPlugin missing export; CESIUM_RTC support is required.");
      }
      try {
        // Required for CESIUM_RTC on 3d-tiles-renderer >= 0.4.1
        tiles.registerPlugin(new GLTFExtensionsPluginClass({
          rtc: true,
          metadata: false,
        }));
        debugLog("tiles:plugin_enabled", { plugin: "GLTFExtensionsPlugin", rtc: true });
      } catch (error) {
        throw new Error(
          "Failed to register GLTFExtensionsPlugin: " +
          (error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error))
        );
      }

      tiles.errorTarget = LOCAL_ONLY_MODE ? 2 : 7;
      tiles.maxDepth = LOCAL_ONLY_MODE ? 22 : 15;
      // Local standalone mode: bias toward loading more neighborhood geometry.
      if ("displayActiveTiles" in tiles) {
        tiles.displayActiveTiles = true;
      }
      if ("loadSiblings" in tiles) {
        tiles.loadSiblings = true;
      }
      if ("autoDisableRendererCulling" in tiles) {
        tiles.autoDisableRendererCulling = false;
      }
      debugLog("tiles:visibility_config", {
        displayActiveTiles: "displayActiveTiles" in tiles ? !!tiles.displayActiveTiles : "n/a",
        loadSiblings: "loadSiblings" in tiles ? !!tiles.loadSiblings : "n/a",
        autoDisableRendererCulling: "autoDisableRendererCulling" in tiles ? !!tiles.autoDisableRendererCulling : "n/a",
        optimizeRaycast: "deprecated_skipped",
      });

      if (tiles.lruCache) {
        if (Number.isFinite(tiles.lruCache.maxBytesSize)) {
          tiles.lruCache.maxBytesSize = LOCAL_ONLY_MODE
            ? (1024 * 1024 * 1024)
            : (300 * 1024 * 1024);
        }
        if (Number.isFinite(tiles.lruCache.maxSize)) {
          tiles.lruCache.maxSize = LOCAL_ONLY_MODE ? 3000 : 800;
        }
      }

      const UpdateOnChangePluginClass =
        tilesMod.UpdateOnChangePlugin ||
        (tilesMod.default && tilesMod.default.UpdateOnChangePlugin);
      const TilesCompressionPluginClass =
        tilesMod.TilesCompressionPlugin ||
        (tilesMod.default && tilesMod.default.TilesCompressionPlugin);

      if (UpdateOnChangePluginClass) {
        try {
          tiles.registerPlugin(new UpdateOnChangePluginClass());
          debugLog("tiles:plugin_enabled", { plugin: "UpdateOnChangePlugin" });
        } catch (_error) {
          debugLog("tiles:plugin_failed", { plugin: "UpdateOnChangePlugin" });
          // plugin best effort only
        }
      }

      if (TilesCompressionPluginClass) {
        try {
          tiles.registerPlugin(new TilesCompressionPluginClass());
          debugLog("tiles:plugin_enabled", { plugin: "TilesCompressionPlugin" });
        } catch (_error) {
          debugLog("tiles:plugin_failed", { plugin: "TilesCompressionPlugin" });
          // plugin best effort only
        }
      }

      if (typeof tiles.onLoadModel === "function") {
        // If library already wires callback, preserve compatibility.
      }

      const registerTilesEvent = (eventName, handler) => {
        if (!tiles || typeof tiles.addEventListener !== "function") {
          return;
        }
        try {
          tiles.addEventListener(eventName, handler);
          debugLog("tiles:event_hooked", { eventName });
        } catch (_error) {
          // no-op
        }
      };

      const onTileSetLoaded = (event) => {
        const root = extractTilesRoot(tiles, event);
        const count = countTilesInTree(root);
        if (count > 0) {
          state.tileProgress.knownTiles = Math.max(state.tileProgress.knownTiles, count);
        }
        debugLog("tiles:tileset_loaded", {
          knownTiles: state.tileProgress.knownTiles,
          hasRoot: !!root,
        });
        logTileProgress(true);
      };

      const onModelLoaded = (event) => {
        const modelScene =
          (event && (event.scene || event.model || event.modelScene || event.content || event.group)) ||
          null;
        const tile = event && event.tile ? event.tile : null;
        const tileKey = deriveTileKey(event, modelScene);
        const ancestorKeys = getAncestorTileKeys(tile, 12);
        if (ancestorKeys.length > 0 && state.mirrorClonesByTileKey) {
          for (const ancestorKey of ancestorKeys) {
            const ancestorModelId = state.mirrorClonesByTileKey.get(ancestorKey);
            if (ancestorModelId) {
              removeMirrorCloneByModelId(ancestorModelId, "ancestor_replaced_by_child");
            }
          }
        }
        if (modelScene) {
          applyCesiumRtcOffset(modelScene);
          prepareLoadedModelScene(modelScene);
          const hasRtc = !!findCesiumRtcExtension(modelScene);
          debugLog("tiles:model_loaded_event", {
            hasCesiumRtc: hasRtc,
            tileKey: tileKey || null,
            ancestorKeysRemoved: ancestorKeys.length,
          });
        }
        markModelLoaded(modelScene, "event", tileKey, tile);
      };

      const onTileError = (event) => {
        state.tileProgress.failedModels += 1;
        debugLog("tiles:load_error", {
          message:
            event && event.error && event.error.message
              ? String(event.error.message)
              : (event && event.message ? String(event.message) : "unknown"),
          failedModels: state.tileProgress.failedModels,
        });
        logTileProgress(false);
      };

      const onModelDisposed = (event) => {
        if (LOCAL_ONLY_MODE) {
          // Keep local fallback cache stable even if tiles renderer unloads internals.
          return;
        }
        const modelScene =
          (event && (event.scene || event.model || event.modelScene || event.content || event.group)) ||
          null;
        const modelId = modelScene && modelScene.uuid ? String(modelScene.uuid) : "";
        if (!modelId) {
          return;
        }
        removeMirrorCloneByModelId(modelId, "dispose_event");
      };

      registerTilesEvent("load-tile-set", onTileSetLoaded);
      registerTilesEvent("loadTileSet", onTileSetLoaded);
      registerTilesEvent("load-model", onModelLoaded);
      registerTilesEvent("loadModel", onModelLoaded);
      registerTilesEvent("load-error", onTileError);
      registerTilesEvent("loadError", onTileError);
      registerTilesEvent("error", onTileError);
      registerTilesEvent("dispose-model", onModelDisposed);
      registerTilesEvent("disposeModel", onModelDisposed);
      registerTilesEvent("unload-model", onModelDisposed);
      registerTilesEvent("unloadModel", onModelDisposed);

      tiles.onLoadModel = (modelScene) => {
        applyCesiumRtcOffset(modelScene);
        prepareLoadedModelScene(modelScene);
        const hasRtc = !!findCesiumRtcExtension(modelScene);
        if (state.tileProgress && state.tileProgress.loadedModels < 2) {
          debugLog("tiles:model_loaded_callback", { hasCesiumRtc: hasRtc });
        }
        markModelLoaded(modelScene, "callback", "", null);
      };

      state.scene.add(tiles.group);
      if (LOCAL_ONLY_MODE && tiles.group) {
        tiles.group.visible = !state.useMirrorFallback;
        debugLog("tiles:group_visibility", {
          visible: !!tiles.group.visible,
          reason: state.useMirrorFallback ? "local_only_mirror" : "local_tiles_primary",
        });
      }
      state.tiles = tiles;
      debugLog("tiles:init_done", {
        errorTarget: tiles.errorTarget,
        maxDepth: tiles.maxDepth,
      });
      logTileProgress(true);
    }

    async function initTilesWithFallback(primaryUrl, extraCandidates) {
      const urls = [];
      if (primaryUrl && typeof primaryUrl === "string") {
        urls.push(primaryUrl);
      }
      if (Array.isArray(extraCandidates)) {
        for (const candidate of extraCandidates) {
          if (candidate && typeof candidate === "string") {
            urls.push(candidate);
          }
        }
      }

      const ordered = Array.from(new Set(urls));
      if (ordered.length === 0) {
        throw new Error("No tileset URLs provided.");
      }

      async function preflightTilesetUrl(url) {
        if (!url || typeof url !== "string") {
          return {
            ok: false,
            reason: "invalid_url",
            status: 0,
          };
        }
        if (typeof fetch !== "function") {
          return {
            ok: true,
            reason: "fetch_unavailable",
            status: 0,
          };
        }

        let timer = null;
        let controller = null;
        try {
          if (typeof AbortController === "function") {
            controller = new AbortController();
            timer = setTimeout(() => {
              try {
                controller.abort();
              } catch (_error) {
                // no-op
              }
            }, 7000);
          }

          const response = await fetch(url, {
            method: "GET",
            mode: "cors",
            credentials: "omit",
            cache: "no-store",
            signal: controller ? controller.signal : undefined,
          });
          if (!response || !response.ok) {
            return {
              ok: false,
              reason: "http_error",
              status: response ? Number(response.status) || 0 : 0,
            };
          }

          try {
            const payload = await response.clone().json();
            if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object" || !payload.root) {
              return {
                ok: false,
                reason: "invalid_tileset_json",
                status: Number(response.status) || 200,
              };
            }
          } catch (_error) {
            // Some servers may provide non-JSON responses behind redirects; if HTTP is ok, continue.
          }

          return {
            ok: true,
            reason: "ok",
            status: Number(response.status) || 200,
          };
        } catch (error) {
          return {
            ok: false,
            reason: error && error.name === "AbortError" ? "timeout" : "fetch_exception",
            status: 0,
            message: error && error.message ? String(error.message) : String(error),
          };
        } finally {
          if (timer) {
            clearTimeout(timer);
          }
        }
      }

      async function waitForInitialTilesSignal(timeoutMs) {
        const toSafeInt = (value) => {
          const num = Number(value);
          return Number.isFinite(num) ? Math.trunc(num) : 0;
        };
        const maxWait = Number.isFinite(timeoutMs) ? Math.max(500, timeoutMs) : 2500;
        const startedAt = Date.now();
        while (Date.now() - startedAt < maxWait) {
          const progress = state.tileProgress || null;
          if (!progress) {
            return { ok: false, reason: "missing_progress" };
          }
          const knownTiles = toSafeInt(progress.knownTiles);
          const loadedModels = toSafeInt(progress.loadedModels);
          const failedModels = toSafeInt(progress.failedModels);
          const stats = getTileStatsSnapshot();
          const active = toSafeInt(stats.active);
          const downloading = toSafeInt(stats.downloading);
          const parsing = toSafeInt(stats.parsing);

          if (loadedModels > 0 || knownTiles > 0 || active > 0 || downloading > 0 || parsing > 0) {
            return {
              ok: true,
              reason: "activity_detected",
              loadedModels,
              knownTiles,
              stats,
            };
          }
          if (failedModels > 0 && loadedModels <= 0 && knownTiles <= 0) {
            return {
              ok: false,
              reason: "initial_load_error",
              failedModels,
              stats,
            };
          }
          await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 120));
        }

        return {
          ok: true,
          reason: "no_signal_timeout",
        };
      }

      const failures = [];
      for (const url of ordered) {
        try {
          debugLog("tiles:fallback_try", { url });
          const preflight = await preflightTilesetUrl(url);
          if (!preflight.ok) {
            debugLog("tiles:fallback_preflight_fail", {
              url,
              reason: preflight.reason || "unknown",
              status: Number.isFinite(preflight.status) ? preflight.status : 0,
              message: preflight.message || "",
            });
            failures.push({
              url,
              message:
                "preflight " +
                String(preflight.reason || "failed") +
                (Number.isFinite(preflight.status) && preflight.status > 0
                  ? " (" + String(preflight.status) + ")"
                  : ""),
            });
            continue;
          }
          await initTiles(url);
          const signal = await waitForInitialTilesSignal(2600);
          if (!signal.ok) {
            throw new Error(
              "initial signal failed: " +
              String(signal.reason || "unknown") +
              " failedModels=" +
              String(signal.failedModels || 0)
            );
          }
          debugLog("tiles:fallback_success", {
            url,
            preflightStatus: Number.isFinite(preflight.status) ? preflight.status : 0,
            signal: signal.reason || "unknown",
          });
          return url;
        } catch (error) {
          const message = error && error.message ? error.message : String(error);
          failures.push({ url, message });
          console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "tiles:fallback_fail", { url, message });
        }
      }

      throw new Error(
        "All tileset URLs failed: " +
          failures.map((item) => item.url + " (" + item.message + ")").join(" | ")
      );
    }

    function tuneErrorTarget() {
      if (!state.camera) {
        return;
      }

      const llh = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
      let target = 6;
      if (llh.altitudeM < 220) {
        target = 4;
      } else if (llh.altitudeM > 1000) {
        target = 9;
      }

      if (state.tilesManager && state.tilesManager.enabled) {
        state.tilesErrorTarget = target;
        return;
      }
      if (!state.tiles) {
        state.tilesErrorTarget = target;
        return;
      }

      if (state.tiles.errorTarget !== target) {
        state.tiles.errorTarget = target;
      }

      state.tilesErrorTarget = target;
    }

    function updateDistanceMaterials() {
      if (LOCAL_ONLY_MODE) {
        return;
      }
      if (!state.tiles || !state.tiles.group || !state.camera) {
        return;
      }

      if (state.frameCounter % 20 !== 0) {
        return;
      }

      const camPos = state.camera.position;
      state.tiles.group.traverse((obj) => {
        if (!obj.isMesh) {
          return;
        }

        const originalMaterial = state.materialOriginal.get(obj);
        if (!originalMaterial) {
          return;
        }

        const worldPos = new THREE.Vector3();
        obj.getWorldPosition(worldPos);
        const distance = worldPos.distanceTo(camPos);

        if (distance > 1500) {
          obj.material = state.materialFar;
        } else if (distance > 500) {
          obj.material = state.materialMid;
        } else {
          obj.material = originalMaterial;
        }
      });
    }

    function clearOverlay() {
      if (!state.overlayMesh) {
        return;
      }

      if (state.overlayMesh.parent) {
        state.overlayMesh.parent.remove(state.overlayMesh);
      }
      if (state.overlayMesh.geometry) {
        state.overlayMesh.geometry.dispose();
      }
      if (state.overlayMesh.material) {
        state.overlayMesh.material.dispose();
      }

      state.overlayMesh = null;
      state.overlayIds = [];
    }

    function colorForIntent(intent) {
      if (intent === "fire_risk") {
        return 0xff6a63;
      }
      if (intent === "built_before") {
        return 0xf4cb62;
      }
      if (intent === "tallest_near") {
        return 0x63d7ff;
      }
      return 0x89a0bf;
    }

    function updateOverlay(results, intent) {
      clearOverlay();

      if (!Array.isArray(results) || results.length === 0 || !state.scene) {
        return;
      }

      const geometry = new THREE.CylinderGeometry(4, 4, 20, 8, 1, false);
      const material = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({
        color: colorForIntent(intent),
        transparent: true,
        opacity: 0.9,
      });

      const mesh = new THREE.InstancedMesh(geometry, material, results.length);
      const matrix = new THREE.Matrix4();
      const quat = new THREE.Quaternion();
      const pos = new THREE.Vector3();
      const up = new THREE.Vector3();
      const yAxis = new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0);
      const scale = new THREE.Vector3(1, 1, 1);

      const ids = [];

      for (let i = 0; i < results.length; i += 1) {
        const item = results[i];
        if (!Number.isFinite(item.lng) || !Number.isFinite(item.lat)) {
          continue;
        }

        const sourceHeight = Number.isFinite(item.heightM) ? item.heightM : 24;
        const riskBonus = Number.isFinite(item.fireRisk) ? item.fireRisk * 15 : 0;
        const markerHeight = clamp(sourceHeight + riskBonus, 12, 180);

        pos.copy(lonLatToECEF(item.lng, item.lat, sourceHeight * 0.5));
        up.copy(pos).normalize();
        quat.setFromUnitVectors(yAxis, up);
        scale.set(1, markerHeight / 20, 1);

        matrix.compose(pos.clone().add(up.clone().multiplyScalar(markerHeight * 0.5)), quat, scale);
        mesh.setMatrixAt(i, matrix);
        ids[i] = item.id;
      }

      mesh.instanceMatrix.needsUpdate = true;
      mesh.renderOrder = 10;
      state.scene.add(mesh);
      state.overlayMesh = mesh;
      state.overlayIds = ids;
    }

    function clampInt(value, fallback, min, max) {
      const parsed = Number.parseInt(String(value), 10);
      const base = Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : Number(fallback);
      if (!Number.isFinite(base)) {
        return Number(min) || 0;
      }
      return Math.min(Math.max(base, Number(min) || 0), Number(max) || 0);
    }

    function sanitizeClientText(value, maxLen = 140) {
      const text = String(value == null ? "" : value)
        .replace(/[\\u0000-\\u001f\\u007f]/g, " ")
        .replace(/\\s+/g, " ")
        .trim();
      if (!text) {
        return "";
      }
      return text.slice(0, Math.max(1, Number(maxLen) || 140));
    }

    function sanitizeClientUrl(value, maxLen = 900) {
      const text = String(value == null ? "" : value).trim();
      if (!text || text.length > Math.max(60, Number(maxLen) || 900)) {
        return "";
      }
      if (!/^https?:\\/\\//i.test(text)) {
        return "";
      }
      try {
        const parsed = new URL(text);
        if (parsed.protocol !== "https:" && parsed.protocol !== "http:") {
          return "";
        }
        return parsed.toString();
      } catch (_error) {
        return "";
      }
    }

    function decodeClientHtmlEntities(value) {
      return String(value == null ? "" : value)
        .replace(/&quot;/g, '"')
        .replace(/&#34;/g, '"')
        .replace(/&#x22;/gi, '"')
        .replace(/&#39;/g, "'")
        .replace(/&#x27;/gi, "'")
        .replace(/&amp;/g, "&")
        .replace(/&#38;/g, "&")
        .replace(/&lt;/g, "<")
        .replace(/&#60;/g, "<")
        .replace(/&gt;/g, ">")
        .replace(/&#62;/g, ">")
        .replace(/&nbsp;/g, " ");
    }

    function stripClientHtml(value) {
      return String(value == null ? "" : value)
        .replace(/<style[\\s\\S]*?<\\/style>/gi, " ")
        .replace(/<script[\\s\\S]*?<\\/script>/gi, " ")
        .replace(/<[^>]+>/g, " ")
        .replace(/\\s+/g, " ")
        .trim();
    }

    function safeClientParseJson(text, fallback = null) {
      try {
        return JSON.parse(String(text || ""));
      } catch (_error) {
        return fallback;
      }
    }

    function escapeHtml(value) {
      return String(value == null ? "" : value)
        .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
        .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
        .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
        .replace(/"/g, "&quot;")
        .replace(/'/g, "&#39;");
    }

    function normalizeClientMusicAlbums(albums) {
      const rows = Array.isArray(albums) ? albums : [];
      const out = [];
      const seen = new Set();
      for (let i = 0; i < rows.length; i += 1) {
        const row = rows[i] && typeof rows[i] === "object" ? rows[i] : {};
        const albumUrl = sanitizeClientUrl(row.albumUrl || row.url || "", 900);
        if (!albumUrl || seen.has(albumUrl)) {
          continue;
