        }
        seen.add(albumUrl);
        out.push({
          title: sanitizeClientText(row.title || row.name || "Album", 140) || "Album",
          albumUrl,
          artworkUrl: sanitizeClientUrl(row.artworkUrl || row.imageUrl || "", 900),
        });
      }
      return out;
    }

    function normalizeClientMusicTracks(tracks) {
      const rows = Array.isArray(tracks) ? tracks : [];
      const out = [];
      const seen = new Set();
      for (let i = 0; i < rows.length; i += 1) {
        const row = rows[i] && typeof rows[i] === "object" ? rows[i] : {};
        const title = sanitizeClientText(row.title || ("Track " + (i + 1)), 120) || ("Track " + (i + 1));
        const streamUrl = sanitizeClientUrl(row.streamUrl || row.stream || "", 7000);
        const trackUrl = sanitizeClientUrl(row.trackUrl || "", 900);
        const id = sanitizeClientText(row.id || title.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, "-"), 120) || ("track-" + (i + 1));
        const key = id + "|" + title + "|" + streamUrl + "|" + trackUrl;
        if (seen.has(key)) {
          continue;
        }
        seen.add(key);
        out.push({
          id,
          title,
          streamUrl,
          trackUrl,
          duration: Number.isFinite(Number(row.duration)) ? Math.max(0, Number(row.duration)) : 0,
        });
      }
      return out;
    }

    function getCurrentMusicTrack() {
      const tracks = Array.isArray(state.music.tracks) ? state.music.tracks : [];
      if (!tracks.length) {
        return null;
      }
      const idx = clampInt(state.music.trackIndex, 0, 0, tracks.length - 1);
      state.music.trackIndex = idx;
      return tracks[idx] || null;
    }

    function applyMusicVolume(value) {
      const v = clamp(Number.isFinite(Number(value)) ? Number(value) : state.music.volume, 0, 1);
      state.music.volume = v;
      if (state.music.volume > 0) {
        state.music.muted = false;
      }
      if (dom.musicAudio) {
        dom.musicAudio.volume = state.music.muted ? 0 : state.music.volume;
        dom.musicAudio.muted = !!state.music.muted;
      }
    }

    function renderMusicSearchResults() {
      if (!dom.musicSearchResults) {
        return;
      }
      if (state.music.searchLoading) {
        dom.musicSearchResults.innerHTML = "<div class=\\"music-muted\\">Searching Bandcamp albums...</div>";
        return;
      }
      const rows = Array.isArray(state.music.searchResults) ? state.music.searchResults : [];
      if (!rows.length) {
        dom.musicSearchResults.innerHTML = "<div class=\\"music-muted\\">Search albums and click Add.</div>";
        return;
      }
      const html = rows.slice(0, 32).map((row) => (
        "<div class=\\"music-result\\">" +
          "<div class=\\"music-result-title\\">" + escapeHtml(row.title || "Album") + "</div>" +
          "<button class=\\"music-result-add\\" data-album-url=\\"" + escapeHtml(row.albumUrl || "") + "\\" data-album-title=\\"" + escapeHtml(row.title || "Album") + "\\">Add</button>" +
        "</div>"
      ));
      dom.musicSearchResults.innerHTML = html.join("");
    }

    function renderMusicUi() {
      const albums = Array.isArray(state.music.albums) ? state.music.albums : [];
      const tracks = Array.isArray(state.music.tracks) ? state.music.tracks : [];
      const currentTrack = getCurrentMusicTrack();
      if (dom.musicAlbumSelect) {
        const options = albums.map((row, idx) => (
          "<option value=\\"" + String(idx) + "\\">" + escapeHtml(row.title || "Album") + "</option>"
        ));
        dom.musicAlbumSelect.innerHTML = options.join("");
        if (albums.length) {
          dom.musicAlbumSelect.value = String(clampInt(state.music.currentAlbumIndex, 0, 0, albums.length - 1));
        }
        dom.musicAlbumSelect.disabled = state.music.loading || !albums.length;
      }
      if (dom.musicTrack) {
        dom.musicTrack.textContent = state.music.loading
          ? "Loading album..."
          : (currentTrack ? currentTrack.title : "No playable tracks found.");
      }
      if (dom.musicSource) {
        let text = state.music.loading
          ? "Album source: loading..."
          : ("Album source: " + (state.music.source || "fallback"));
        if (state.music.error) {
          text += " (" + state.music.error + ")";
        }
        dom.musicSource.textContent = text;
      }
      if (dom.musicOpen) {
        dom.musicOpen.href = sanitizeClientUrl(state.music.albumUrl || POLYGON_ALBUM_URL, 900) || POLYGON_ALBUM_URL;
      }
      if (dom.musicPlay) {
        dom.musicPlay.textContent = state.music.playing ? "Pause" : "Play";
        dom.musicPlay.disabled = state.music.loading || !tracks.length;
      }
      if (dom.musicPrev) {
        dom.musicPrev.disabled = state.music.loading || tracks.length <= 1;
      }
      if (dom.musicNext) {
        dom.musicNext.disabled = state.music.loading || tracks.length <= 1;
      }
      if (dom.musicSearchBtn) {
        dom.musicSearchBtn.disabled = state.music.searchLoading || state.music.loading;
        dom.musicSearchBtn.textContent = state.music.searchLoading ? "..." : "Search";
      }
      if (dom.musicAddUrlBtn) {
        dom.musicAddUrlBtn.disabled = state.music.loading;
      }
      if (dom.musicMute) {
        const volPct = clampInt(Math.round(state.music.volume * 100), 72, 0, 100);
        dom.musicMute.textContent = state.music.muted ? "Mute" : ("Vol " + volPct + "%");
      }
      if (dom.musicVolume) {
        dom.musicVolume.value = String(clampInt(Math.round(state.music.volume * 100), 72, 0, 100));
      }
      renderMusicSearchResults();
    }

    async function callSupExecWithTimeout(callback, payload, timeoutMs) {
      if (!(window.sup && typeof window.sup.exec === "function")) {
        throw new Error("window.sup.exec unavailable");
      }
      const timeout = clampInt(timeoutMs, 16000, 3000, 45000);
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        let settled = false;
        const timer = setTimeout(() => {
          if (settled) {
            return;
          }
          settled = true;
          reject(new Error(callback + " timeout"));
        }, timeout);
        Promise.resolve()
          .then(() => window.sup.exec(callback, payload || {}))
          .then((result) => {
            if (settled) {
              return;
            }
            settled = true;
            clearTimeout(timer);
            resolve(result);
          })
          .catch((error) => {
            if (settled) {
              return;
            }
            settled = true;
            clearTimeout(timer);
            reject(error);
          });
      });
    }

    function parseBandcampAlbumHtmlClient(html, albumUrl) {
      const output = {
        albumTitle: "Album",
        artworkUrl: POLYGON_DEFAULT_ART,
        tracks: [],
      };
      const source = String(html || "");
      const tralbumMatch = source.match(/data-tralbum="([^"]+)"/i) || source.match(/data-tralbum='([^']+)'/i);
      if (tralbumMatch && tralbumMatch[1]) {
        const raw = decodeClientHtmlEntities(tralbumMatch[1]).replace(/\\\//g, "/");
        const tralbum = safeClientParseJson(raw, null);
        if (tralbum && typeof tralbum === "object") {
          const current = tralbum.current && typeof tralbum.current === "object" ? tralbum.current : {};
          const title = sanitizeClientText(current.title || tralbum.album_title || tralbum.title || "Album", 120);
          if (title) {
            output.albumTitle = title;
          }
          const artId = current.art_id || tralbum.art_id;
          const artUrl = sanitizeClientUrl(tralbum.artFullsizeUrl || tralbum.artUrl || tralbum.artwork_url || "", 900);
          output.artworkUrl = artUrl ||
            (Number.isFinite(Number(artId))
              ? ("https://f4.bcbits.com/img/a" + Math.trunc(Number(artId)) + "_16.jpg")
              : POLYGON_DEFAULT_ART);
          const trackRows = Array.isArray(tralbum.trackinfo) ? tralbum.trackinfo : [];
          for (let i = 0; i < trackRows.length; i += 1) {
            const row = trackRows[i] && typeof trackRows[i] === "object" ? trackRows[i] : {};
            const file = row.file && typeof row.file === "object" ? row.file : {};
            output.tracks.push({
              id: sanitizeClientText(row.track_id || row.id || "", 120) || ("track-" + (i + 1)),
              title: sanitizeClientText(row.title || row.track_title || ("Track " + (i + 1)), 120) || ("Track " + (i + 1)),
              streamUrl: sanitizeClientUrl(file["mp3-128"] || file["mp3-v0"] || file["aac-hi"] || row.streaming_url || "", 7000),
              trackUrl: (() => {
                try {
                  return sanitizeClientUrl(
                    row.title_link ? new URL(String(row.title_link), albumUrl).toString() : "",
                    900
                  );
                } catch (_error) {
                  return "";
                }
              })(),
              duration: Number.isFinite(Number(row.duration)) ? Math.max(0, Number(row.duration)) : 0,
            });
          }
        }
      }
      const ogTitle = source.match(/<meta[^>]+property=["']og:title["'][^>]+content=["']([^"']+)["'][^>]*>/i);
      if (ogTitle && ogTitle[1]) {
        const cleaned = sanitizeClientText(
          decodeClientHtmlEntities(ogTitle[1]).replace(/\\s*\\|\\s*Bandcamp.*$/i, ""),
          120
        );
        if (cleaned) {
          output.albumTitle = cleaned;
        }
      }
      const ogImage = source.match(/<meta[^>]+property=["']og:image["'][^>]+content=["']([^"']+)["'][^>]*>/i);
      if (ogImage && ogImage[1]) {
        output.artworkUrl = sanitizeClientUrl(decodeClientHtmlEntities(ogImage[1]), 900) || output.artworkUrl;
      }
      output.tracks = normalizeClientMusicTracks(output.tracks);
      return output;
    }

    function parseBandcampSearchAlbumsClient(html, searchUrl) {
      const source = String(html || "");
      const rows = [];
      const seen = new Set();
      const resultRegex = /<li[^>]*class=["'][^"']*searchresult[^"']*["'][^>]*>([\\s\\S]*?)<\\/li>/gi;
      let match = null;
      while ((match = resultRegex.exec(source)) !== null) {
        const block = String(match[1] || "");
        if (!/itemtype[^>]*album/i.test(block) && !/item_type[^>]*album/i.test(block) && !/\\/album\\//i.test(block)) {
          continue;
        }
        const hrefMatch = block.match(/href=["']([^"']+)["']/i);
        if (!hrefMatch || !hrefMatch[1]) {
          continue;
        }
        let albumUrl = "";
        try {
          albumUrl = sanitizeClientUrl(new URL(String(hrefMatch[1]), searchUrl).toString(), 900);
        } catch (_error) {
          albumUrl = "";
        }
        if (!albumUrl || seen.has(albumUrl) || !/\\/album\\//i.test(albumUrl)) {
          continue;
        }
        seen.add(albumUrl);
        const titleMatch = block.match(/class=["'][^"']*heading[^"']*["'][^>]*>([\\s\\S]*?)<\\/[^>]+>/i);
        const imgMatch = block.match(/<img[^>]+src=["']([^"']+)["']/i);
        rows.push({
          title: sanitizeClientText(
            stripClientHtml(decodeClientHtmlEntities(titleMatch && titleMatch[1] ? titleMatch[1] : "")),
            140
          ) || "Album",
          albumUrl,
          artworkUrl: sanitizeClientUrl(imgMatch && imgMatch[1] ? imgMatch[1] : "", 900),
        });
        if (rows.length >= 48) {
          break;
        }
      }
      return normalizeClientMusicAlbums(rows);
    }

    async function fetchBandcampAlbumViaProxy(albumUrl) {
      const clean = sanitizeClientUrl(albumUrl, 900);
      if (!clean) {
        return { ok: false, text: "", error: "invalid_album_url" };
      }
      const stripped = clean.replace(/^https?:\\/\\//i, "");
      const candidates = [
        "https://r.jina.ai/http://" + stripped,
        "https://r.jina.ai/http://r.jina.ai/http://" + stripped,
      ];
      for (const endpoint of candidates) {
        try {
          const response = await fetch(endpoint, {
            method: "GET",
            mode: "cors",
            credentials: "omit",
            cache: "no-store",
          });
          if (!response || !response.ok) {
            continue;
          }
          const text = await response.text();
          if (text && text.length > 100) {
            return { ok: true, text, error: "" };
          }
        } catch (_error) {
          // try next endpoint
        }
      }
      return { ok: false, text: "", error: "proxy_fetch_failed" };
    }

    async function fetchBandcampSearchViaProxy(query) {
      const q = sanitizeClientText(query || "", 120);
      if (!q) {
        return { ok: false, text: "", error: "query_required" };
      }
      const searchUrl = "https://bandcamp.com/search?q=" + encodeURIComponent(q) + "&item_type=a";
      const stripped = searchUrl.replace(/^https?:\\/\\//i, "");
      const endpoint = "https://r.jina.ai/http://" + stripped;
      try {
        const response = await fetch(endpoint, {
          method: "GET",
          mode: "cors",
          credentials: "omit",
          cache: "no-store",
        });
        if (!response || !response.ok) {
          return { ok: false, text: "", error: "http_" + String(response && response.status ? response.status : 0) };
        }
        const text = await response.text();
        return { ok: !!text, text: String(text || ""), error: text ? "" : "empty_response", searchUrl };
      } catch (error) {
        return {
          ok: false,
          text: "",
          error: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
          searchUrl,
        };
      }
    }

    async function selectMusicTrack(index, autoPlay) {
      const tracks = Array.isArray(state.music.tracks) ? state.music.tracks : [];
      if (!tracks.length) {
        state.music.playing = false;
        if (dom.musicAudio) {
          try { dom.musicAudio.pause(); } catch (_error) {}
          dom.musicAudio.removeAttribute("src");
          try { dom.musicAudio.load(); } catch (_error) {}
        }
        renderMusicUi();
        return;
      }
      const idx = clampInt(index, state.music.trackIndex, 0, tracks.length - 1);
      state.music.trackIndex = idx;
      const track = tracks[idx];
      const stream = sanitizeClientUrl(track && track.streamUrl ? track.streamUrl : "", 7000);
      if (dom.musicAudio) {
        if (stream) {
          if (String(dom.musicAudio.src || "") !== stream) {
            dom.musicAudio.src = stream;
            try { dom.musicAudio.load(); } catch (_error) {}
          }
          if (autoPlay) {
            try {
              const promise = dom.musicAudio.play();
              if (promise && typeof promise.catch === "function") {
                promise.catch(() => {
                  state.music.playing = false;
                  renderMusicUi();
                });
              }
            } catch (_error) {
              state.music.playing = false;
            }
          } else {
            state.music.playing = !dom.musicAudio.paused;
          }
        } else {
          try { dom.musicAudio.pause(); } catch (_error) {}
          dom.musicAudio.removeAttribute("src");
          try { dom.musicAudio.load(); } catch (_error) {}
          state.music.playing = false;
        }
      }
      renderMusicUi();
    }

    async function playMusicNext(offset, autoPlay = state.music.playing) {
      const tracks = Array.isArray(state.music.tracks) ? state.music.tracks : [];
      if (!tracks.length) {
        return;
      }
      const current = clampInt(state.music.trackIndex, 0, 0, tracks.length - 1);
      const dir = offset >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
      const next = (current + dir + tracks.length) % tracks.length;
      await selectMusicTrack(next, autoPlay);
    }

    async function toggleMusicPlayback() {
      const track = getCurrentMusicTrack();
      if (!track) {
        return;
      }
      const stream = sanitizeClientUrl(track.streamUrl || "", 7000);
      if (!stream && track.trackUrl) {
        window.open(track.trackUrl, "_blank", "noopener,noreferrer");
        return;
      }
      if (!dom.musicAudio || !stream) {
        return;
      }
      if (String(dom.musicAudio.src || "") !== stream) {
        dom.musicAudio.src = stream;
        try { dom.musicAudio.load(); } catch (_error) {}
      }
      if (dom.musicAudio.paused) {
        try {
          const promise = dom.musicAudio.play();
          if (promise && typeof promise.catch === "function") {
            promise.catch(() => {
              state.music.playing = false;
              renderMusicUi();
            });
          }
          state.music.playing = true;
        } catch (_error) {
          state.music.playing = false;
        }
      } else {
        try { dom.musicAudio.pause(); } catch (_error) {}
        state.music.playing = false;
      }
      renderMusicUi();
    }

    async function loadMusicAlbumPlaylist(albumUrl, albumTitle) {
      const cleanAlbumUrl = sanitizeClientUrl(albumUrl || state.music.albumUrl || POLYGON_ALBUM_URL, 900) || POLYGON_ALBUM_URL;
      state.music.loading = true;
      state.music.error = "";
      state.music.source = "loading";
      state.music.albumUrl = cleanAlbumUrl;
      state.music.albumTitle = sanitizeClientText(albumTitle || state.music.albumTitle || "Album", 120) || "Album";
      renderMusicUi();
      try {
        let response = null;
        if (window.sup && typeof window.sup.exec === "function") {
          response = await callSupExecWithTimeout("loadPolygonIslandPlaylist", { albumUrl: cleanAlbumUrl }, 20000);
        } else {
          const fetched = await fetchBandcampAlbumViaProxy(cleanAlbumUrl);
          if (!fetched.ok) {
            throw new Error(fetched.error || "proxy_fetch_failed");
          }
          const parsed = parseBandcampAlbumHtmlClient(fetched.text, cleanAlbumUrl);
          response = {
            ok: true,
            albumUrl: cleanAlbumUrl,
            albumTitle: parsed.albumTitle,
            artworkUrl: parsed.artworkUrl,
            tracks: parsed.tracks,
            source: parsed.tracks.length ? "proxy-live" : "fallback",
            error: parsed.tracks.length ? "" : "No stream URLs found from proxy.",
          };
        }
        if (!response || !response.ok) {
          throw new Error(response && response.error ? response.error : "music_callback_failed");
        }
        state.music.albumUrl = sanitizeClientUrl(response.albumUrl || cleanAlbumUrl, 900) || cleanAlbumUrl;
        state.music.albumTitle = sanitizeClientText(response.albumTitle || state.music.albumTitle || "Album", 120) || "Album";
        state.music.artworkUrl = sanitizeClientUrl(response.artworkUrl || POLYGON_DEFAULT_ART, 900) || POLYGON_DEFAULT_ART;
        state.music.tracks = normalizeClientMusicTracks(response.tracks);
        if (!state.music.tracks.length) {
          state.music.tracks = [
            {
              id: "album-fallback",
              title: state.music.albumTitle || "Album",
              streamUrl: "",
              trackUrl: state.music.albumUrl || cleanAlbumUrl,
              duration: 0,
            },
          ];
        }
        state.music.trackIndex = 0;
        state.music.source = sanitizeClientText(response.source || "fallback", 60) || "fallback";
        state.music.error = sanitizeClientText(response.error || "", 260);
        if (dom.musicOpen) {
          dom.musicOpen.href = state.music.albumUrl;
        }
        await selectMusicTrack(0, false);
      } catch (error) {
        state.music.source = "fallback";
        state.music.error = sanitizeClientText(error && error.message ? error.message : String(error), 260);
        if (!Array.isArray(state.music.tracks) || !state.music.tracks.length) {
          state.music.tracks = [
            {
              id: "album-fallback",
              title: state.music.albumTitle || "Album",
              streamUrl: "",
              trackUrl: state.music.albumUrl || cleanAlbumUrl,
              duration: 0,
            },
          ];
          state.music.trackIndex = 0;
        }
      } finally {
        state.music.loading = false;
        renderMusicUi();
      }
    }

    async function selectMusicAlbumByIndex(index, autoPlay) {
      const albums = Array.isArray(state.music.albums) ? state.music.albums : [];
      if (!albums.length) {
        return;
      }
      const idx = clampInt(index, state.music.currentAlbumIndex, 0, albums.length - 1);
      state.music.currentAlbumIndex = idx;
      const album = albums[idx];
      await loadMusicAlbumPlaylist(album.albumUrl, album.title);
      if (autoPlay) {
        await toggleMusicPlayback();
      }
    }

    async function addMusicAlbumByUrl(rawUrl, explicitTitle) {
      const cleanUrl = sanitizeClientUrl(rawUrl, 900);
      if (!cleanUrl) {
        setStatus("Invalid Bandcamp album URL.", "error");
        return;
      }
      const title = sanitizeClientText(explicitTitle || "", 140) || "Bandcamp Album";
      const albums = Array.isArray(state.music.albums) ? state.music.albums : [];
      const existingIndex = albums.findIndex((row) => row && row.albumUrl === cleanUrl);
      if (existingIndex >= 0) {
        state.music.currentAlbumIndex = existingIndex;
        await selectMusicAlbumByIndex(existingIndex, false);
        return;
      }
      albums.push({
        title,
        albumUrl: cleanUrl,
        artworkUrl: "",
      });
      state.music.albums = normalizeClientMusicAlbums(albums);
      const idx = state.music.albums.findIndex((row) => row && row.albumUrl === cleanUrl);
      state.music.currentAlbumIndex = idx >= 0 ? idx : Math.max(0, state.music.albums.length - 1);
      renderMusicUi();
      await selectMusicAlbumByIndex(state.music.currentAlbumIndex, false);
    }

    async function searchMusicAlbums() {
      const query = dom.musicSearchInput ? sanitizeClientText(dom.musicSearchInput.value || "", 120) : "";
      if (!query) {
        state.music.searchResults = [];
        renderMusicSearchResults();
        return;
      }
      state.music.searchLoading = true;
      renderMusicSearchResults();
      try {
        let rows = [];
        if (window.sup && typeof window.sup.exec === "function") {
          const response = await callSupExecWithTimeout("searchBandcampAlbums", { query }, 18000);
          if (!response || !response.ok) {
            throw new Error(response && response.error ? response.error : "bandcamp_search_failed");
          }
          rows = normalizeClientMusicAlbums(response.albums);
        } else {
          const proxy = await fetchBandcampSearchViaProxy(query);
          if (!proxy.ok) {
            throw new Error(proxy.error || "search_proxy_failed");
          }
          rows = parseBandcampSearchAlbumsClient(proxy.text, proxy.searchUrl || "https://bandcamp.com/search");
        }
        state.music.searchResults = rows.slice(0, 32);
      } catch (error) {
        state.music.searchResults = [];
        state.music.error = sanitizeClientText(error && error.message ? error.message : String(error), 260);
      } finally {
        state.music.searchLoading = false;
        renderMusicSearchResults();
        renderMusicUi();
      }
    }

    async function loadInitialMusicAlbums() {
      state.music.loading = true;
      state.music.error = "";
      state.music.source = "loading";
      renderMusicUi();
      try {
        if (window.sup && typeof window.sup.exec === "function") {
          const response = await callSupExecWithTimeout("loadBandcampArtistAlbums", { artistUrl: BANDCAMP_DEFAULT_ARTIST_URL }, 18000);
          if (response && response.ok) {
            const albums = normalizeClientMusicAlbums(response.albums);
            if (albums.length) {
              state.music.albums = albums;
              state.music.currentAlbumIndex = 0;
              state.music.source = sanitizeClientText(response.source || "artist-live", 60) || "artist-live";
              state.music.error = sanitizeClientText(response.error || "", 260);
            }
          }
        }
      } catch (error) {
        state.music.source = "fallback";
        state.music.error = sanitizeClientText(error && error.message ? error.message : String(error), 260);
      } finally {
        state.music.loading = false;
      }
      renderMusicUi();
      await selectMusicAlbumByIndex(state.music.currentAlbumIndex, false);
    }

    function setupMusicEvents() {
      if (dom.musicPrev) {
        dom.musicPrev.addEventListener("click", () => {
          void playMusicNext(-1, state.music.playing);
        });
      }
      if (dom.musicPlay) {
        dom.musicPlay.addEventListener("click", () => {
          void toggleMusicPlayback();
        });
      }
      if (dom.musicNext) {
        dom.musicNext.addEventListener("click", () => {
          void playMusicNext(1, state.music.playing);
        });
      }
      if (dom.musicAlbumSelect) {
        dom.musicAlbumSelect.addEventListener("change", () => {
          const idx = clampInt(dom.musicAlbumSelect.value, state.music.currentAlbumIndex, 0, 1000);
          void selectMusicAlbumByIndex(idx, false);
        });
      }
      if (dom.musicSearchBtn) {
        dom.musicSearchBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
          void searchMusicAlbums();
        });
      }
      if (dom.musicSearchInput) {
        dom.musicSearchInput.addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
          if (event.key === "Enter") {
            event.preventDefault();
            void searchMusicAlbums();
          }
        });
      }
      if (dom.musicAddUrlBtn) {
        dom.musicAddUrlBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
          const value = dom.musicAddUrl ? String(dom.musicAddUrl.value || "").trim() : "";
          if (!value) {
            return;
          }
          if (dom.musicAddUrl) {
            dom.musicAddUrl.value = "";
          }
          void addMusicAlbumByUrl(value);
        });
      }
      if (dom.musicAddUrl) {
        dom.musicAddUrl.addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
          if (event.key === "Enter") {
            event.preventDefault();
            const value = String(dom.musicAddUrl.value || "").trim();
            dom.musicAddUrl.value = "";
            void addMusicAlbumByUrl(value);
          }
        });
      }
      if (dom.musicSearchResults) {
        dom.musicSearchResults.addEventListener("click", (event) => {
          const target = event.target;
          if (!target || !target.classList || !target.classList.contains("music-result-add")) {
            return;
          }
          const albumUrl = sanitizeClientUrl(target.getAttribute("data-album-url") || "", 900);
          const title = sanitizeClientText(target.getAttribute("data-album-title") || "", 140);
          if (!albumUrl) {
            return;
          }
          void addMusicAlbumByUrl(albumUrl, title);
        });
      }
      if (dom.musicVolume) {
        dom.musicVolume.addEventListener("input", () => {
          const next = clampInt(dom.musicVolume.value, Math.round(state.music.volume * 100), 0, 100) / 100;
          applyMusicVolume(next);
          renderMusicUi();
        });
      }
      if (dom.musicMute) {
        dom.musicMute.addEventListener("click", () => {
          state.music.muted = !state.music.muted;
          applyMusicVolume(state.music.volume);
          renderMusicUi();
        });
      }
      if (dom.musicAudio) {
        dom.musicAudio.crossOrigin = "anonymous";
        dom.musicAudio.addEventListener("ended", () => {
          void playMusicNext(1, true);
        });
        dom.musicAudio.addEventListener("play", () => {
          state.music.playing = true;
          renderMusicUi();
        });
        dom.musicAudio.addEventListener("pause", () => {
          state.music.playing = false;
          renderMusicUi();
        });
        dom.musicAudio.addEventListener("error", () => {
          state.music.error = "Audio stream failed. Try another album/track.";
          state.music.playing = false;
          renderMusicUi();
        });
      }
    }

    async function initMusicPlayer() {
      if (!dom.musicPlayer) {
        return;
      }
      setupMusicEvents();
      applyMusicVolume(state.music.volume);
      renderMusicUi();
      await loadInitialMusicAlbums();
    }

    async function onCanvasClick(event) {
      if (!state.overlayMesh || !state.camera || !state.renderer) {
        return;
      }

      const rect = dom.viewport.getBoundingClientRect();
      state.pointer.x = ((event.clientX - rect.left) / rect.width) * 2 - 1;
      state.pointer.y = -((event.clientY - rect.top) / rect.height) * 2 + 1;

      state.raycaster.setFromCamera(state.pointer, state.camera);
      const hits = state.raycaster.intersectObject(state.overlayMesh, false);
      if (!hits || hits.length === 0) {
        return;
      }

      const hit = hits[0];
      const instanceId = hit.instanceId;
      if (!Number.isInteger(instanceId)) {
        return;
      }

      const buildingId = state.overlayIds[instanceId];
      if (!buildingId) {
        return;
      }
      debugLog("overlay:clicked", { buildingId, instanceId });

      if (!window.sup || typeof window.sup.exec !== "function") {
        debugLog("overlay:missing_exec");
        return;
      }

      try {
        const detail = await window.sup.exec("getBuildingDetails", { id: buildingId });
        debugLog("overlay:detail_response", detail);
        if (!detail || !detail.ok) {
          setDetails("Failed to load detail for " + buildingId);
          return;
        }

        const b = detail.building || {};
        const lines = [
          "id: " + (b.id || "n/a"),
          "year: " + (Number.isFinite(b.year) ? b.year : "n/a"),
          "heightM: " + (Number.isFinite(b.heightM) ? b.heightM.toFixed(2) : "n/a"),
          "floors: " + (Number.isFinite(b.floors) ? b.floors : "n/a"),
          "usage: " + (b.usage || "n/a"),
          "structure: " + (b.structureType || "n/a"),
          "fireproof: " + (b.fireproofClass || "n/a"),
          "fireRisk: " + (Number.isFinite(b.fireRisk) ? b.fireRisk.toFixed(2) : "n/a"),
          "",
          "context prompt:",
          detail.contextualPromptText || "n/a",
        ];
        setDetails(lines.join("\\n"));
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "overlay:detail_error", err);
        setDetails("Detail callback error: " + err.message);
      }
    }

    function getCameraStateForServer() {
      if (!state.camera) {
        return null;
      }

      const llh = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
      return {
        lng: llh.lng,
        lat: llh.lat,
        altitudeM: llh.altitudeM,
      };
    }

    function applyCameraSuggestion(suggestion) {
      if (!suggestion || !Number.isFinite(suggestion.lng) || !Number.isFinite(suggestion.lat)) {
        return;
      }
      const altitude = Number.isFinite(suggestion.altitudeM) ? suggestion.altitudeM : 350;
      focusCameraOn(suggestion.lng, suggestion.lat, altitude);
    }

    async function runQueryFromInput() {
      if (VM_TEMP_DISABLED) {
        setStatus(VM_TEMP_DISABLED_REASON, "error");
        return;
      }

      if (!window.sup || typeof window.sup.exec !== "function") {
        debugLog("runQuery:missing_exec");
        setStatus("window.sup.exec unavailable in this environment.", "error");
        return;
      }

      const queryText = dom.queryInput.value.trim();
      if (!queryText) {
        setStatus("Enter a query first.", "error");
        return;
      }

      setStatus("Running query...", null);
      debugLog("runQuery:start", {
        queryText,
        cameraState: getCameraStateForServer(),
      });

      try {
        const response = await window.sup.exec("runQuery", {
          text: queryText,
          cameraState: getCameraStateForServer(),
        });
        debugLog("runQuery:response", response);

        if (!response) {
          setStatus("No response from runQuery.", "error");
          return;
        }

        state.lastSummary = response.summary || "";
        state.lastStats = response.stats || { totalMatched: 0, displayed: 0 };
        state.lastResults = Array.isArray(response.results) ? response.results : [];

        setSummary(response.summary || "No summary text.");
        setResultsList(state.lastResults);
        updateOverlay(state.lastResults, response.intent || "unknown");
        applyCameraSuggestion(response.cameraSuggestion);

        if (response.ok) {
          setStatus("Query complete.", "ok");
        } else {
          setStatus(response.summary || "Query failed.", "error");
        }
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "runQuery:error", err);
        setStatus("runQuery callback failed: " + err.message, "error");
      }
    }

    async function shareSnapshot() {
      if (!window.sup || typeof window.sup.share !== "function" || !state.renderer) {
        debugLog("snapshot:missing_share");
        setStatus("Snapshot share unavailable in this environment.", "error");
        return;
      }

      try {
        const dataUrl = state.renderer.domElement.toDataURL("image/png");
        debugLog("snapshot:share_start", { dataUrlLength: dataUrl ? dataUrl.length : 0 });
        await window.sup.share({ url: dataUrl, type: "image" });
        debugLog("snapshot:share_done");
        setStatus("Snapshot shared.", "ok");
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "snapshot:share_error", err);
        setStatus("Snapshot share failed: " + err.message, "error");
      }
    }

    async function shareSummary() {
      if (!window.sup || typeof window.sup.exec !== "function" || typeof window.sup.share !== "function") {
        debugLog("summary:missing_exec_or_share");
        setStatus("Summary share unavailable in this environment.", "error");
        return;
      }

      try {
        const payload = await window.sup.exec("shareSummary", {
          summary: state.lastSummary,
          stats: state.lastStats,
        });
        debugLog("summary:payload", payload);
        await window.sup.share(payload || state.lastSummary || "No summary available.");
        debugLog("summary:share_done");
        setStatus("Summary shared.", "ok");
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "summary:share_error", err);
        setStatus("Summary share failed: " + err.message, "error");
      }
    }

    async function runVmHealth() {
      if (VM_TEMP_DISABLED) {
        setStatus("VM health disabled in this temporary geometry-only build.", "error");
        setVmState("VM disabled\\nreason: " + VM_TEMP_DISABLED_REASON);
        return;
      }

      if (!window.sup || typeof window.sup.exec !== "function") {
        setStatus("VM health check unavailable in this environment.", "error");
        return;
      }

      setStatus("Running VM health check...", null);
      try {
        const health = await window.sup.exec("vmHealth", {});
        debugLog("vmHealth:response", health);
        if (health && health.ok) {
          setStatus("VM health check passed.", "ok");
          setVmState(
            [
              "id: " + ((health.vm && health.vm.id) || "n/a"),
              "url: " + ((health.vm && health.vm.url) || "n/a"),
              "elapsedMs: " + (Number.isFinite(health.elapsedMs) ? health.elapsedMs : "n/a"),
              "deleteOk: " + (health.deleteOk ? "yes" : "no"),
              "deleteError: " + (health.deleteError || "none"),
            ].join("\\n")
          );
          return;
        }

        const attempts = health && Array.isArray(health.attempts) ? health.attempts : [];
        const attemptsText = attempts.length
          ? attempts
            .map((a) => {
              const idx = Number.isFinite(a.attempt) ? a.attempt : "?";
              const elapsed = Number.isFinite(a.elapsedMs) ? a.elapsedMs : 0;
              const err = a.error || "unknown";
              return "#" + idx + ":" + elapsed + "ms:" + err;
            })
            .join(" | ")
          : "none";
        setStatus("VM health check failed.", "error");
        setVmState(
          [
            "id: n/a",
            "url: n/a",
            "vmHealthError: " + ((health && health.error) || "unknown"),
            "vmHealthAttempts: " + attemptsText,
          ].join("\\n")
        );
      } catch (error) {
        setStatus("VM health callback failed: " + error.message, "error");
      }
    }

    async function runBootstrap(forceReindex, forceReload, phase, shouldInitTiles) {
      const bootstrapPhase = typeof phase === "string" && phase ? phase : "full";
      const initTilesAfter = shouldInitTiles !== false;
      setStatus("Bootstrapping phase: " + bootstrapPhase + "...", null);
      setVmState("Bootstrapping phase: " + bootstrapPhase + "...");
      debugLog("bootstrap:start", {
        forceReindex: !!forceReindex,
        forceReload: !!forceReload,
        phase: bootstrapPhase,
        shouldInitTiles: initTilesAfter,
        clientSessionId: state.clientSessionId,
      });

      try {
        let response = null;
        const hasExec = !!(window.sup && typeof window.sup.exec === "function");
        if (LOCAL_ONLY_MODE || !hasExec) {
          const fallbackTiles = Array.isArray(INJECTED.tilesetCandidates) ? INJECTED.tilesetCandidates : [];
          const fallbackTileUrl = fallbackTiles[0] || "";
          debugLog("bootstrap:standalone_mode", {
            phase: bootstrapPhase,
            localOnlyMode: LOCAL_ONLY_MODE,
            fallbackTileUrl,
          });
          response = {
            ok: true,
            phase: bootstrapPhase,
            tilesetUrl: fallbackTileUrl,
            centroid: TOKYO23.centroid,
            bounds: TOKYO23.bounds,
            cacheState: "cold",
            indexStats: { buildingCount: 0 },
            semanticEnabled: false,
            warnings: [
              LOCAL_ONLY_MODE
                ? "Running in local-only mode (semantic callbacks disabled by config)."
                : "Running in standalone mode (no Sup runtime callbacks).",
              VM_TEMP_DISABLED_REASON,
            ],
            vm: {
              id: "n/a",
              url: "",
              sessionId: null,
              createdAt: null,
              replacedPrevious: false,
            },
            previousVm: {},
            vmProbe: {
              attempted: false,
              ok: false,
              output: "",
              elapsedMs: 0,
              error: LOCAL_ONLY_MODE ? "local_only_mode" : "window.sup.exec unavailable",
            },
            progressive: {
              phase: bootstrapPhase,
              nextPhase: "none",
            },
            dataset: {
              cityGmlCandidates: Array.isArray(INJECTED.cityGmlCandidates) ? INJECTED.cityGmlCandidates : [],
              tilesetCandidates: fallbackTiles,
              wardTilesets: Array.isArray(INJECTED.wardTilesets) ? INJECTED.wardTilesets : [],
              terrainConfig: INJECTED.terrainConfig || {},
              geoidManifest: INJECTED.geoidManifest || {},
              transportManifest: INJECTED.transportManifest || {},
              transportConfig: INJECTED.transportConfig || {},
              transitManifest: INJECTED.transitManifest || {},
              transitLayerConfig: INJECTED.transitLayerConfig || {},
              transitRealtimeConfig: INJECTED.transitRealtimeConfig || {},
              streetLayersManifest: INJECTED.streetLayersManifest || {},
              streetLayerConfig: INJECTED.streetLayerConfig || {},
              parksManifest: INJECTED.parksManifest || {},
              parkLayerConfig: INJECTED.parkLayerConfig || {},
              waterwaysManifest: INJECTED.waterwaysManifest || {},
              waterLayerConfig: INJECTED.waterLayerConfig || {},
              markingStyleConfig: INJECTED.markingStyleConfig || {},
              trafficConfig: INJECTED.trafficConfig || {},
              driveConfig: INJECTED.driveConfig || {},
              patchAssetConfig: INJECTED.patchAssetConfig || {},
              selectedTilesetSource: fallbackTileUrl ? "fallback_static" : "none",
            },
            debug: {
              currentStage: "standalone_no_exec",
              vmRotationDiagnostics: null,
              vmError: LOCAL_ONLY_MODE ? "local_only_mode" : "window.sup.exec unavailable",
              semanticError: null,
            },
          };
        } else {
          response = await window.sup.exec("bootstrap", {
            forceReindex: !!forceReindex,
            forceReload: !!forceReload,
            phase: bootstrapPhase,
            sessionId: state.clientSessionId,
            patchRunReason: "launch_bootstrap",
          });
          debugLog("bootstrap:response", response);
          if (response && response.debug) {
            debugLog("bootstrap:server_debug", response.debug);
            const vmDiag = response.debug.vmRotationDiagnostics || {};
            debugLog("bootstrap:server_debug_compact", {
              stage: response.debug.currentStage || "n/a",
              vmError: response.debug.vmError || null,
              vmCreateError: vmDiag.vmCreateError || null,
              vmCreateAttempts: Array.isArray(vmDiag.vmCreateAttempts)
                ? vmDiag.vmCreateAttempts
                : [],
            });
          }
        }
        updateVmStateFromBootstrap(response);

        state.boot = response;
        state.semanticEnabled = !!response.semanticEnabled;

        if (!response.ok) {
          const stageText = response.errorStage ? " (stage=" + response.errorStage + ")" : "";
          setStatus("Bootstrap failed: " + (response.error || "unknown error") + stageText, "error");
          return response;
        }

        if (Array.isArray(response.warnings) && response.warnings.length > 0) {
          setStatus(
            "Bootstrap completed with warnings:\\n" + response.warnings.join("\\n"),
            response.ok ? "ok" : "error"
          );
        } else {
          setStatus("Bootstrap complete.", "ok");
        }

        setSummary(
          "cacheState=" + (response.cacheState || "n/a") +
          " | buildingCount=" + ((response.indexStats && response.indexStats.buildingCount) || 0) +
          " | semanticEnabled=" + state.semanticEnabled +
          " | vmId=" + ((response.vm && response.vm.id) || "n/a") +
          " | phase=" + (response.phase || bootstrapPhase) +
          " | stage=" + ((response.debug && response.debug.currentStage) || "n/a")
        );

        const wardManifest =
          response &&
          response.dataset &&
          Array.isArray(response.dataset.wardTilesets)
            ? response.dataset.wardTilesets
            : [];
        if (response && response.dataset) {
          if (response.dataset.terrainConfig && typeof response.dataset.terrainConfig === "object") {
            Object.assign(TERRAIN_CONFIG, response.dataset.terrainConfig);
          }
          if (response.dataset.transportConfig && typeof response.dataset.transportConfig === "object") {
            Object.assign(TRANSPORT_CONFIG, response.dataset.transportConfig);
          }
          if (response.dataset.transitLayerConfig && typeof response.dataset.transitLayerConfig === "object") {
            Object.assign(TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG, response.dataset.transitLayerConfig);
            if (response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.lineOffsetsM && typeof response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.lineOffsetsM === "object") {
              TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.lineOffsetsM = {
                ...(TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.lineOffsetsM || {}),
                ...response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.lineOffsetsM,
              };
            }
            if (response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.lineWidthsM && typeof response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.lineWidthsM === "object") {
              TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.lineWidthsM = {
                ...(TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.lineWidthsM || {}),
                ...response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.lineWidthsM,
              };
            }
            if (response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.markerOffsetsM && typeof response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.markerOffsetsM === "object") {
              TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.markerOffsetsM = {
                ...(TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.markerOffsetsM || {}),
                ...response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.markerOffsetsM,
              };
            }
            if (response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.markerScale && typeof response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.markerScale === "object") {
              TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.markerScale = {
                ...(TRANSIT_LAYER_CONFIG.markerScale || {}),
                ...response.dataset.transitLayerConfig.markerScale,
              };
            }
          }
          if (response.dataset.transitRealtimeConfig && typeof response.dataset.transitRealtimeConfig === "object") {
            Object.assign(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG, response.dataset.transitRealtimeConfig);
            if (response.dataset.transitRealtimeConfig.trainSources && typeof response.dataset.transitRealtimeConfig.trainSources === "object") {
              TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.trainSources = {
                ...(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.trainSources || {}),
                ...response.dataset.transitRealtimeConfig.trainSources,
              };
            }
            if (response.dataset.transitRealtimeConfig.busSources && typeof response.dataset.transitRealtimeConfig.busSources === "object") {
              TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.busSources = {
                ...(TRANSIT_REALTIME_CONFIG.busSources || {}),
                ...response.dataset.transitRealtimeConfig.busSources,
              };
            }
          }
          if (response.dataset.streetLayerConfig && typeof response.dataset.streetLayerConfig === "object") {
            Object.assign(STREET_LAYER_CONFIG, response.dataset.streetLayerConfig);
          }
          if (response.dataset.parkLayerConfig && typeof response.dataset.parkLayerConfig === "object") {
            Object.assign(PARK_LAYER_CONFIG, response.dataset.parkLayerConfig);
            PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.treeEnabled = false;
          }
          if (response.dataset.waterLayerConfig && typeof response.dataset.waterLayerConfig === "object") {
            Object.assign(WATER_LAYER_CONFIG, response.dataset.waterLayerConfig);
          }
          if (response.dataset.markingStyleConfig && typeof response.dataset.markingStyleConfig === "object") {
            Object.assign(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG, response.dataset.markingStyleConfig);
            if (response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.offsetsM && typeof response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.offsetsM === "object") {
              MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.offsetsM = {
                ...(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.offsetsM || {}),
                ...response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.offsetsM,
              };
            }
            if (response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.widthsM && typeof response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.widthsM === "object") {
              MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.widthsM = {
                ...(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.widthsM || {}),
                ...response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.widthsM,
              };
            }
            if (response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.colors && typeof response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.colors === "object") {
              MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors = {
                ...(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.colors || {}),
                ...response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.colors,
              };
            }
            if (response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.dashMeters && typeof response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.dashMeters === "object") {
              MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.dashMeters = {
                ...(MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.dashMeters || {}),
                ...response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.dashMeters,
              };
            }
            if (Array.isArray(response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.dashedClasses)) {
              MARKING_STYLE_CONFIG.dashedClasses = Array.from(
                new Set(
                  response.dataset.markingStyleConfig.dashedClasses
                    .map((item) => String(item || "").toLowerCase())
                    .filter(Boolean)
                )
              );
            }
          }
          if (response.dataset.trafficConfig && typeof response.dataset.trafficConfig === "object") {
            Object.assign(TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG, response.dataset.trafficConfig);
            if (response.dataset.trafficConfig.speed && typeof response.dataset.trafficConfig.speed === "object") {
              TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.speed = {
                ...(TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.speed || {}),
                ...response.dataset.trafficConfig.speed,
              };
            }
            if (response.dataset.trafficConfig.signals && typeof response.dataset.trafficConfig.signals === "object") {
              TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.signals = {
                ...(TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.signals || {}),
                ...response.dataset.trafficConfig.signals,
              };
            }
            if (response.dataset.trafficConfig.stopControl && typeof response.dataset.trafficConfig.stopControl === "object") {
              TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.stopControl = {
                ...(TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.stopControl || {}),
                ...response.dataset.trafficConfig.stopControl,
              };
            }
            if (response.dataset.trafficConfig.playerPenalty && typeof response.dataset.trafficConfig.playerPenalty === "object") {
              TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.playerPenalty = {
                ...(TRAFFIC_SIM_CONFIG.playerPenalty || {}),
                ...response.dataset.trafficConfig.playerPenalty,
              };
            }
          }
          if (response.dataset.driveConfig && typeof response.dataset.driveConfig === "object") {
            Object.assign(DRIVE_CONFIG, response.dataset.driveConfig);
            state.driveConfig = {
              ...(state.driveConfig || {}),
              ...response.dataset.driveConfig,
              spawnAnchor: {
                ...((state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.spawnAnchor) || {}),
                ...((response.dataset.driveConfig && response.dataset.driveConfig.spawnAnchor) || {}),
              },
              spawn: {
                ...((state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.spawn) || {}),
                ...((response.dataset.driveConfig && response.dataset.driveConfig.spawn) || {}),
              },
              camera: {
                ...((state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.camera) || {}),
                ...((response.dataset.driveConfig && response.dataset.driveConfig.camera) || {}),
              },
              physics: {
                ...((state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.physics) || {}),
                ...((response.dataset.driveConfig && response.dataset.driveConfig.physics) || {}),
              },
              model: {
                ...((state.driveConfig && state.driveConfig.model) || {}),
                ...((response.dataset.driveConfig && response.dataset.driveConfig.model) || {}),
              },
            };
          }
          if (response.dataset.patchAssetConfig && typeof response.dataset.patchAssetConfig === "object") {
            Object.assign(PATCH_ASSET_CONFIG, response.dataset.patchAssetConfig);
          }
          if (response.dataset.kartManifest && typeof response.dataset.kartManifest === "object") {
            Object.assign(KART_MANIFEST, response.dataset.kartManifest);
          }
          if (response.dataset.transportManifest && typeof response.dataset.transportManifest === "object") {
            Object.assign(TRANSPORT_MANIFEST, response.dataset.transportManifest);
          }
          if (response.dataset.transitManifest && typeof response.dataset.transitManifest === "object") {
            Object.assign(TRANSIT_MANIFEST, response.dataset.transitManifest);
          }
          if (response.dataset.streetLayersManifest && typeof response.dataset.streetLayersManifest === "object") {
            Object.assign(STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST, response.dataset.streetLayersManifest);
            if (response.dataset.streetLayersManifest.layers && typeof response.dataset.streetLayersManifest.layers === "object") {
              const incomingLayers = response.dataset.streetLayersManifest.layers;
              const currentLayers =
                STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers && typeof STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers === "object"
                  ? STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers
                  : {};
              STREET_LAYERS_MANIFEST.layers = {
                ...currentLayers,
                ...incomingLayers,
                streetAssets: {
                  ...(currentLayers.streetAssets && typeof currentLayers.streetAssets === "object"
                    ? currentLayers.streetAssets
                    : {}),
                  ...(incomingLayers.streetAssets && typeof incomingLayers.streetAssets === "object"
                    ? incomingLayers.streetAssets
                    : {}),
                },
                streetMarkings: {
                  ...(currentLayers.streetMarkings && typeof currentLayers.streetMarkings === "object"
                    ? currentLayers.streetMarkings
                    : {}),
                  ...(incomingLayers.streetMarkings && typeof incomingLayers.streetMarkings === "object"
                    ? incomingLayers.streetMarkings
                    : {}),
                },
              };
            }
          }
          if (response.dataset.parksManifest && typeof response.dataset.parksManifest === "object") {
            Object.assign(PARKS_MANIFEST, response.dataset.parksManifest);
          }
          if (response.dataset.waterwaysManifest && typeof response.dataset.waterwaysManifest === "object") {
            Object.assign(WATERWAYS_MANIFEST, response.dataset.waterwaysManifest);
          }
          if (response.dataset.geoidManifest && typeof response.dataset.geoidManifest === "object") {
            Object.assign(GEOID_MANIFEST, response.dataset.geoidManifest);
            state.geoidManager = null;
          }
        }
        if (initTilesAfter && state.tilesManager && state.tilesManager.enabled && wardManifest.length > 0) {
          state.tilesManager.wardManifest = wardManifest;
          clearTokyoTilesManager();
          clearTerrainManager();
          clearTransportManager();
          clearTransitLayerManager();
          clearRealtimeTransitManager();
          clearStreetLayerManager();
          clearParkLayerManager();
          clearWaterLayerManager();
          clearTrafficManager();
          disposeOldTiles();
          if (response && response.centroid && Number.isFinite(response.centroid.lng) && Number.isFinite(response.centroid.lat)) {
            focusCameraOn(response.centroid.lng, response.centroid.lat, 1600);
          }
          scheduleTokyoWardActivation(Date.now());
          scheduleTerrainTiles(Date.now());
          scheduleTransportTiles(Date.now());
          scheduleTransitLayerTiles(Date.now());
          scheduleStreetLayerTiles(Date.now());
          scheduleParkLayerTiles(Date.now());
          scheduleWaterLayerTiles(Date.now());
          debugLog("bootstrap:init_tokyo_manager", {
            wards: wardManifest.length,
            terrainConfig: response.dataset && response.dataset.terrainConfig ? response.dataset.terrainConfig : null,
            geoidManifest: response.dataset && response.dataset.geoidManifest ? "available" : "missing",
            transportManifest: response.dataset && response.dataset.transportManifest ? "available" : "missing",
            transitManifest: response.dataset && response.dataset.transitManifest ? "available" : "missing",
          });
        } else if (initTilesAfter && response.tilesetUrl) {
          const fallbackList =
            response &&
            response.dataset &&
            Array.isArray(response.dataset.tilesetCandidates)
              ? response.dataset.tilesetCandidates
              : [];
          debugLog("bootstrap:init_tiles", { tilesetUrl: response.tilesetUrl, fallbackList });
          try {
            const loadedUrl = await initTilesWithFallback(response.tilesetUrl, fallbackList);
            debugLog("bootstrap:init_tiles_loaded", { loadedUrl });
          } catch (tileError) {
            const message = tileError && tileError.message ? tileError.message : String(tileError);
            console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "bootstrap:tiles_failed", message);
            setStatus("Bootstrap complete, but tiles failed to load: " + message, "error");
            disposeOldTiles();
          }
        } else {
          if (!initTilesAfter) {
            debugLog("bootstrap:tiles_deferred", { phase: bootstrapPhase });
          } else {
            debugLog("bootstrap:no_tileset_url");
            clearTokyoTilesManager();
            clearTerrainManager();
            clearTransportManager();
            clearTransitLayerManager();
            clearRealtimeTransitManager();
            clearStreetLayerManager();
            clearParkLayerManager();
            clearWaterLayerManager();
            clearTrafficManager();
            disposeOldTiles();
          }
        }
        return response;
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "bootstrap:error", err);
        setVmState("Bootstrap failed before VM response.");
        setStatus("Bootstrap callback failed: " + err.message, "error");
        return null;
      }
    }

    async function runProgressiveBootstrap(forceReload) {
      debugLog("bootstrap:progressive_start", { forceReload: !!forceReload });

      if (VM_TEMP_DISABLED) {
        debugLog("bootstrap:geometry_only_mode", { reason: VM_TEMP_DISABLED_REASON });
        await runBootstrap(false, false, "geometry_only", true);
        return;
      }

      const vmPhase = await runBootstrap(false, !!forceReload, "vm_probe", false);
      const vmHealthy = !!(vmPhase && vmPhase.vmProbe && vmPhase.vmProbe.ok);
      debugLog("bootstrap:progressive_vm_phase", {
        vmHealthy,
        vmPhase: vmPhase ? vmPhase.phase : "none",
      });

      await runBootstrap(false, false, "geometry_only", true);

      if (!vmHealthy) {
        debugLog("bootstrap:progressive_skip_semantic", {
          reason: "vm_probe_not_ready",
        });
        return;
      }

      setTimeout(() => {
        runBootstrap(false, false, "semantic_only", false).catch((error) => {
          console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "bootstrap:progressive_semantic_error", error);
        });
      }, 150);
    }

    function updateHeadsUp() {
      if (!state.camera) {
        return;
      }

      const loadedPercent = computeTileLoadedPercent();
      const llh = ecefToLonLat(state.camera.position);
      const manager = state.tilesManager || null;
      const terrain = state.terrainManager || null;
      const stats = getTileStatsSnapshot();
      const tierDist = manager && manager.tierDistribution
        ? manager.tierDistribution
        : { A: 0, B: 0, C: 0 };
      const cachePressure = Number.isFinite(stats.cached) && Number.isFinite(stats.active) && stats.cached > 0
        ? Math.min(1, stats.active / Math.max(1, stats.cached))
        : 0;
      const geoid = state.geoidManager || null;
      const ground = manager && manager.groundCalibration ? manager.groundCalibration : null;
      const transport = state.transportManager || null;
      const transitLayer = state.transitLayerManager || null;
      const transitRt = state.transitRealtimeManager || null;
      const streetLayers = state.streetLayerManager || null;
      const parks = state.parkLayerManager || null;
      const water = state.waterLayerManager || null;
      const traffic = state.trafficManager || null;
      const transportFailSample =
        transport && transport.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map && transport.failureReasonByKey.size > 0
          ? (() => {
            const first = transport.failureReasonByKey.entries().next().value;
            if (!first) return "";
            return String(first[0]) + "=" + String(first[1]).slice(0, 52);
          })()
          : "";
      const streetFailSample =
        streetLayers && streetLayers.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map && streetLayers.failureReasonByKey.size > 0
          ? (() => {
            const first = streetLayers.failureReasonByKey.entries().next().value;
            if (!first) return "";
            return String(first[0]) + "=" + String(first[1]).slice(0, 52);
          })()
          : "";
      const parksFailSample =
        parks && parks.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map && parks.failureReasonByKey.size > 0
          ? (() => {
            const first = parks.failureReasonByKey.entries().next().value;
            if (!first) return "";
            return String(first[0]) + "=" + String(first[1]).slice(0, 52);
          })()
          : "";
      const waterFailSample =
        water && water.failureReasonByKey instanceof Map && water.failureReasonByKey.size > 0
          ? (() => {
            const first = water.failureReasonByKey.entries().next().value;
            if (!first) return "";
            return String(first[0]) + "=" + String(first[1]).slice(0, 52);
          })()
          : "";
      const transportTotal = transport && transport.featureCounts
        ? Math.max(1, Number(transport.featureCounts.total) || 0)
        : 1;
      const rtWarnCount = transitRt && Array.isArray(transitRt.warnings) ? transitRt.warnings.length : 0;
      const sidewalkCoverage = transport && transport.featureCounts
        ? (
          (
            (Number(transport.featureCounts.sidewalk) || 0) +
            (Number(transport.featureCounts.crosswalk) || 0) +
            (Number(transport.featureCounts.pedestrian) || 0)
          ) / transportTotal
        )
        : 0;
      const kartWheelMapCount =
        state.kart && Array.isArray(state.kart.wheelNodeMap)
          ? state.kart.wheelNodeMap.filter((entry) => !!entry).length
          : 0;
      const lines = [
        "lng=" + llh.lng.toFixed(6),
        "lat=" + llh.lat.toFixed(6),
        "alt=" + llh.altitudeM.toFixed(1) + "m",
        "mode=" + (state.driveMode ? "drive" : "fly"),
        "geoMode=" + state.navigationMode,
        "errorTarget=" + state.tilesErrorTarget,
        "tilesLoaded=" + formatPercent(loadedPercent) + "%",
        "activeWards=" + (manager ? manager.activeWardIds.size : 0),
        "tiers=A:" + (tierDist.A || 0) + " B:" + (tierDist.B || 0) + " C:" + (tierDist.C || 0),
        "kartEngine=" + (state.kart && state.kart.engine ? state.kart.engine : getDriveEngine()),
        "cannon=" + (getDriveEngine() === "cannon" ? (state.cannon && state.cannon.ready ? "ok" : "error") : "n/a"),
        "kartModel=" + (state.kart && state.kart.modelSource ? state.kart.modelSource : "procedural"),
        "kartVisualReady=" + (state.kart && state.kart.visualReady ? "yes" : "no"),
        "kartWheelMap=" + String(kartWheelMapCount) + "/4",
        "speedKmh=" + (state.kart && Number.isFinite(state.kart.speedKmh) ? state.kart.speedKmh.toFixed(1) : "0.0"),
        "kartGrounded=" + (state.kart && state.kart.controls && state.kart.controls.isGrounded ? "yes" : "no"),
        "kartRoadContact=" + (state.kart && state.kart.roadContact ? "yes" : "no"),
        "spawn=" + (state.kart && state.kart.spawnLabel ? state.kart.spawnLabel : "pending"),
        "terrainTiles=" + (terrain ? terrain.tiles.size : 0),
        "terrainPending=" + (terrain ? terrain.pending.size : 0),
        "terrainFailed=" + (terrain ? terrain.failed : 0),
        "terrainReady=" + (terrain && terrain.ready ? "yes" : "no"),
        "terrainWarn=" + (terrain && terrain.warning ? "yes" : "no"),
        "datumState=" + (ground && ground.datumState ? ground.datumState : (geoid && geoid.datumState ? geoid.datumState : "pending")),
        "geoidMode=" + (geoid && geoid.geoidOffsetMode ? geoid.geoidOffsetMode : "pending"),
        "cachePressure=" + (cachePressure * 100).toFixed(0) + "%",
        "frameMs=" + (Number.isFinite(state.frameTimeAvgMs) ? state.frameTimeAvgMs.toFixed(2) : "n/a"),
        "rtcPlugin=" + (manager && manager.rtcPluginReady ? "ok" : "missing"),
        "wardWarns=" + (manager && Array.isArray(manager.warnings) ? manager.warnings.length : 0),
        "semantic=" + (state.semanticEnabled ? "on" : "off"),
        "inTokyo23=" + (isWithinBounds(llh.lng, llh.lat, TOKYO23 && TOKYO23.bounds ? TOKYO23.bounds : null) ? "yes" : "no"),
        "transportTilesLoaded=" + (transport ? transport.tiles.size : 0),
        "transportZoom=" + (transport && Number.isFinite(transport.currentZoom) ? transport.currentZoom : "n/a"),
        "transportPending=" + (transport ? transport.pending.size : 0),
        "transportFailed=" + (transport ? transport.failed : 0),
        "transportReady=" + (transport && transport.ready ? "yes" : "no"),
        "transportMode=" + (transport ? (transport.renderModeActive || "ribbon") : "ribbon"),
        "transportQuality=" + (transport ? (transport.laneMeshQuality || "off") : "off"),
        "transportWarn=" + (transport && transport.warning ? "yes" : "no"),
        "sourceMix=" + (transport
          ? ("plateau:" + (transport.sourceMix.plateau || 0) + ",osm:" + (transport.sourceMix.osm || 0))
          : "plateau:0,osm:0"),
        "transitTilesLoaded=" + (transitLayer ? transitLayer.tiles.size : 0),
        "transitFeaturesLoaded=" + (transitLayer && transitLayer.featureCounts ? (transitLayer.featureCounts.total || 0) : 0),
        "transitPending=" + (transitLayer ? transitLayer.pending.size : 0),
        "transitFailed=" + (transitLayer ? transitLayer.failed : 0),
        "rtTrains=" + (transitRt ? transitRt.trainById.size : 0),
        "rtBuses=" + (transitRt ? transitRt.busById.size : 0),
        "rtLastUpdate=" + (transitRt && transitRt.lastUpdateIso ? transitRt.lastUpdateIso : "n/a"),
        "rtWarn=" + String(rtWarnCount),
        "sidewalkCoverage=" + (sidewalkCoverage * 100).toFixed(1) + "%",
        "streetTilesLoaded=" + (streetLayers ? streetLayers.tiles.size : 0),
        "streetZoom=" + (streetLayers && Number.isFinite(streetLayers.currentZoom) ? streetLayers.currentZoom : "n/a"),
        "streetPending=" + (streetLayers ? streetLayers.pending.size : 0),
        "streetFailed=" + (streetLayers ? streetLayers.failed : 0),
        "streetReady=" + (streetLayers && streetLayers.ready ? "yes" : "no"),
        "streetWarn=" + (streetLayers && streetLayers.warning ? "yes" : "no"),
        "streetAssetsLoaded=" + (streetLayers && streetLayers.featureCounts ? (streetLayers.featureCounts.street_asset || 0) : 0),
        "streetTreesLoaded=" + (streetLayers && streetLayers.featureCounts ? (streetLayers.featureCounts.street_tree || 0) : 0),
        "markingsLoaded=" + (streetLayers && streetLayers.featureCounts ? (streetLayers.featureCounts.marking || 0) : 0),
        "trafficControlsLoaded=" + (streetLayers && streetLayers.featureCounts ? (streetLayers.featureCounts.traffic_control || 0) : 0),
        "markingShaderMode=" + (state.markingShaderMode || "legacy_solid"),
        "streetInstancing=" + (state.streetInstancingEnabled ? "on" : "off"),
        "parksEnabled=" + (PARK_LAYER_CONFIG && PARK_LAYER_CONFIG.enabled === false ? "no" : "yes"),
        "parksTilesLoaded=" + (parks ? parks.tiles.size : 0),
        "parksFeaturesLoaded=" + (parks ? (Number(parks.featureCount) || 0) : 0),
        "parkTreesLoaded=" + (parks ? (Number(parks.treeCount) || 0) : 0),
        "waterEnabled=" + (WATER_LAYER_CONFIG && WATER_LAYER_CONFIG.enabled === false ? "no" : "yes"),
        "waterTilesLoaded=" + (water ? water.tiles.size : 0),
        "waterFeaturesLoaded=" + (water ? (Number(water.featureCounts && water.featureCounts.total) || 0) : 0),
        "waterPending=" + (water ? water.pending.size : 0),
        "waterFailed=" + (water ? water.failed : 0),
        "waterWarn=" + (water && water.warning ? "yes" : "no"),
        "npcVehiclesActive=" + (traffic && traffic.stats ? (traffic.stats.active || 0) : 0),
        "signalizedJunctionsActive=" + (traffic && traffic.stats ? (traffic.stats.signalizedJunctions || 0) : 0),
        "trafficTickMs=" + (traffic && Number.isFinite(traffic.tickSec) ? (traffic.tickSec * 1000).toFixed(1) : "n/a"),
      ];
      if (transportFailSample) {
        lines.push("transportFailReason=" + transportFailSample);
      }
      if (streetFailSample) {
        lines.push("streetFailReason=" + streetFailSample);
      }
      if (parksFailSample) {
        lines.push("parksFailReason=" + parksFailSample);
      }
      if (waterFailSample) {
        lines.push("waterFailReason=" + waterFailSample);
      }
      if (transitRt && Array.isArray(transitRt.warnings) && transitRt.warnings.length > 0) {
        lines.push("rtWarnMsg=" + String(transitRt.warnings[0]).slice(0, 72));
      }
      if (manager && manager.syncByWard && manager.syncByWard.size > 0) {
        const applied = [];
        let appliedCountTotal = 0;
        for (const [wardId, sync] of manager.syncByWard.entries()) {
          if (sync && sync.biasApplied && Number.isFinite(sync.biasM)) {
            appliedCountTotal += 1;
            if (applied.length < 4) {
              applied.push(wardId + ":" + (sync.biasM >= 0 ? "+" : "") + sync.biasM.toFixed(1));
            }
          }
        }
        const totalWards = manager.wardManifest ? manager.wardManifest.length : 0;
        lines.push("biases=" + (applied.length > 0 ? applied.join(",") : "pending"));
        lines.push("biasConverged=" + appliedCountTotal + "/" + totalWards);
      } else {
        lines.push("biases=pending");
        lines.push("biasConverged=0/0");
      }
      if (ground && ground.gapStats) {
        lines.push(
          "gapMedian/p95=" +
          (Number.isFinite(ground.gapStats.medianAbsM) ? ground.gapStats.medianAbsM.toFixed(3) : "n/a") +
          "m/" +
          (Number.isFinite(ground.gapStats.p95AbsM) ? ground.gapStats.p95AbsM.toFixed(3) : "n/a") +
          "m"
        );
        lines.push(
          "residualBiasState=" +
          (ground.residualBiasState || "pending") +
          " (" +
          (Number.isFinite(ground.gapStats.sampleCount) ? ground.gapStats.sampleCount : 0) +
          " samples)"
        );
      } else {
        lines.push("gapMedian/p95=n/a/n/a");
        lines.push("residualBiasState=pending (0 samples)");
      }
      if (DEBUG_LOCAL_CONTROLS) {
        lines.push("mirrorFallback=" + (state.useMirrorFallback ? "on" : "off"));
        lines.push("levelMode=" + state.localLevelMode);
        lines.push("levelTilt=" + state.localLevelTiltDeg.toFixed(2) + "deg");
      }
      dom.headsUp.textContent = lines.join("\\n");
    }

    function getTilesUpdateCamera() {
      if (!state.camera) {
        return null;
      }
      if (!LOCAL_ONLY_MODE || !state.useMirrorFallback || !state.mirrorGroup) {
        return state.camera;
      }

      state.camera.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      state.mirrorGroup.updateMatrixWorld(true);

      const mirrorWorld = state.mirrorGroup.matrixWorld || state.mirrorGroup.matrix;
      if (!mirrorWorld || !mirrorWorld.elements || mirrorWorld.elements.length < 16) {
        return state.camera;
      }

      let inverseMirror = null;
      try {
        inverseMirror = mirrorWorld.clone().invert();
      } catch (_error) {
        return state.camera;
      }
      if (!inverseMirror) {
        return state.camera;
      }

      const proxy = state.tilesProxyCamera || new THREE.PerspectiveCamera();
      state.tilesProxyCamera = proxy;
      proxy.matrixAutoUpdate = false;
      proxy.fov = state.camera.fov;
      proxy.aspect = state.camera.aspect;
      proxy.near = state.camera.near;
      proxy.far = Math.max(state.camera.far, 100000000);
      proxy.updateProjectionMatrix();

      const proxyWorld = new THREE.Matrix4().multiplyMatrices(inverseMirror, state.camera.matrixWorld);
      proxy.matrix.copy(proxyWorld);
      proxy.matrixWorld.copy(proxyWorld);
      proxy.matrix.decompose(proxy.position, proxy.quaternion, proxy.scale);
      proxy.up.set(0, 1, 0).applyQuaternion(proxy.quaternion).normalize();
      proxy.matrixWorldNeedsUpdate = true;
      proxy.updateMatrixWorld(true);
      return proxy;
    }

    function animate() {
      requestAnimationFrame(animate);
      if (!state.renderer || !state.scene || !state.camera) {
        return;
      }
      try {
        const dt = Math.min(0.05, state.clock.getDelta());
        const nowMs = Date.now();
        updateFlyMode(dt);
        updateKartRuntime(dt, nowMs);
        state.frameCounter += 1;
        state.frameTimeAvgMs = state.frameTimeAvgMs <= 0
          ? (dt * 1000)
          : (state.frameTimeAvgMs * 0.92 + dt * 1000 * 0.08);

        if (state.tilesManager && state.tilesManager.enabled) {
          tuneErrorTarget();
          state.camera.updateMatrixWorld(true);
          updateTokyoTilesManager(nowMs);
          scheduleTerrainTiles(nowMs);
          scheduleTransportTiles(nowMs);
          scheduleTransitLayerTiles(nowMs);
          scheduleStreetLayerTiles(nowMs);
          scheduleParkLayerTiles(nowMs);
          scheduleWaterLayerTiles(nowMs);
          pollRealtimeTransit(nowMs).catch((error) => {
            debugLog("transit:realtime_poll_async_error", {
              message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
            });
          });
          safeUpdateTrafficManager(dt, nowMs);
          if (state.frameCounter % 20 === 0) {
            logTileProgress(false);
          }
        } else if (state.tiles) {
          tuneErrorTarget();
          state.camera.updateMatrixWorld(true);
          const tilesCamera = getTilesUpdateCamera() || state.camera;
          state.tiles.setCamera(tilesCamera);
          state.tiles.setResolutionFromRenderer(tilesCamera, state.renderer);
          state.tiles.update();
          updateDistanceMaterials();
          scheduleTransportTiles(nowMs);
          scheduleTransitLayerTiles(nowMs);
          scheduleStreetLayerTiles(nowMs);
          scheduleParkLayerTiles(nowMs);
          scheduleWaterLayerTiles(nowMs);
          pollRealtimeTransit(nowMs).catch((error) => {
            debugLog("transit:realtime_poll_async_error", {
              message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
            });
          });
          safeUpdateTrafficManager(dt, nowMs);
          if (
            state.tileProgress &&
            state.tileProgress.needsAutoFocusCheck &&
            !state.tileProgress.firstModelFocused
          ) {
            maybeAutoFocusFromModel(state.tiles.group || null, "animate", false);
            if (state.tileProgress.firstModelFocused) {
              state.tileProgress.needsAutoFocusCheck = false;
            }
          }
          if (state.frameCounter % 30 === 0) {
            if (
              state.tileProgress &&
              !state.tileProgress.firstModelFocused &&
              state.tileProgress.loadedModels > 0
            ) {
              maybeAutoFocusFromModel(state.tiles.group || null, "periodic", false);
            }
            if (
              state.tileProgress &&
              state.tileProgress.loadedModels > 0
            ) {
              const stats = getTileStatsSnapshot();
              const zeroFrustum =
                Number.isFinite(stats.inFrustum) && stats.inFrustum === 0 &&
                Number.isFinite(stats.visible) && stats.visible === 0;
              if (zeroFrustum) {
                if (!state.noVisibleTilesSinceMs) {
                  state.noVisibleTilesSinceMs = Date.now();
                }
                debugLog("tiles:zero_frustum_detected", {
                  loadedModels: state.tileProgress.loadedModels,
                  stats,
                });
              } else {
                state.noVisibleTilesSinceMs = 0;
              }
            }
            logTileProgress(false);
          }
          if (
            state.tileProgress &&
            !state.tileProgress.noModelWarningLogged &&
            state.tileProgress.loadedModels === 0 &&
            state.tileProgress.tileInitAtMs > 0 &&
            Date.now() - state.tileProgress.tileInitAtMs > 7000
          ) {
            state.tileProgress.noModelWarningLogged = true;
            debugLog("tiles:no_models_visible_yet", {
              elapsedMs: Date.now() - state.tileProgress.tileInitAtMs,
              stats: getTileStatsSnapshot(),
              note:
                "Tileset initialized but no model callbacks seen yet. Camera/transform mismatch is likely.",
            });
            setStatus(
              "Tiles connected but no model geometry visible yet. Check debug log for load stats.",
              "error"
            );
          }
        }

        if (state.sky && state.camera && state.sky.position && typeof state.sky.position.copy === "function") {
          state.sky.position.copy(state.camera.position);
        }
        advanceRealtimeTransitMarkers(nowMs);

        updateHeadsUp();
        onResize();
        state.renderer.render(state.scene, state.camera);
      } catch (error) {
        const message = error && error.message ? error.message : String(error);
        const decision = shouldLogGlobalError("animate_error", message);
        if (decision.allow) {
          console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "animate:error", {
            message,
            stack: error && error.stack ? String(error.stack).split("\\n").slice(0, 3).join(" | ") : "",
          });
          if (decision.flushSuppressed > 0) {
            console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "animate:error_suppressed", {
              message,
              suppressed: decision.flushSuppressed,
            });
          }
        }
      }
    }

    dom.runQuery.addEventListener("click", runQueryFromInput);
    dom.bootAgain.addEventListener("click", () => runProgressiveBootstrap(false));
    dom.forceReindex.addEventListener("click", () => {
      if (VM_TEMP_DISABLED) {
        setStatus("Force Reindex disabled while VM features are temporarily off.", "error");
        return;
      }
      runBootstrap(true, false, "full", true);
    });
    dom.shareSnapshot.addEventListener("click", shareSnapshot);
    dom.shareSummary.addEventListener("click", shareSummary);
    dom.vmHealth.addEventListener("click", runVmHealth);

    dom.queryInput.addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
      if (event.key === "Enter" && (event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey)) {
        event.preventDefault();
        runQueryFromInput();
      }
    });

      if (VM_TEMP_DISABLED) {
        dom.queryInput.placeholder = "Semantic queries temporarily disabled; geometry viewer only.";
        dom.runQuery.disabled = true;
        dom.forceReindex.disabled = true;
      dom.vmHealth.disabled = true;
      dom.detailBox.textContent = "Semantic building details are temporarily unavailable.";
      setVmState("VM disabled\\nreason: " + VM_TEMP_DISABLED_REASON);
      }

      let manifestLoadState = null;
      for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 3; attempt += 1) {
        manifestLoadState = await loadExternalPatchAssetManifests();
        if (
          manifestLoadState &&
          manifestLoadState.transport &&
          manifestLoadState.transit &&
          manifestLoadState.streetLayers &&
          manifestLoadState.parks
        ) {
          break;
        }
        await sleepMs(260 * (attempt + 1));
      }
      debugLog("assets:external_manifest_summary", manifestLoadState || {});

      initThree();
      animate();
      void initMusicPlayer().catch((error) => {
        debugLog("music:init_error", {
          message: error && error.message ? error.message : String(error),
        });
      });

    dom.queryInput.value = "Show me all buildings in Tokyo built before 1980";
    runProgressiveBootstrap(false);
    clearTimeout(startupWatchdogId);
    }

    startApp().catch((error) => {
      console.error(CLIENT_DEBUG_PREFIX, "startup:fatal", error);
      if (dom.status) {
        dom.status.textContent = "Startup failed. See Debug Log.";
        dom.status.classList.add("error");
      }
      if (dom.vmBox) {
        dom.vmBox.textContent = "Startup failed before VM init.";
      }
    });
  </script>
</body>
</html>`;
}

function renderChatApp() {
  const callbacks = LOCAL_ONLY_MODE
    ? ["loadTransitRealtime"]
    : [
        "bootstrap",
        "runQuery",
        "getBuildingDetails",
        "shareSummary",
        "vmHealth",
        "loadTransitRealtime",
        "loadPolygonIslandPlaylist",
        "loadBandcampArtistAlbums",
        "searchBandcampAlbums",
      ];
  return sup.html(buildClientHtml(), {
    width: 1200,
    height: 900,
    tailwind: false,
    inline: true,
    callbacks,
  });
}

function main() {
  return renderChatApp();
}
